Ukwengeza , umthetho wenziwe mayelana nokwakhiwa kwamakomidi wamawadi , njengemikhakha eyelelisako efaka abajameli bakamasipala nebomphakathi ukobana bakhambise iindingo zomphakathi neemphakamiso bazise kumkhandlu . Ikambiso ekabili yokujameleka kumawadi nokujameleka ngokweengcenye itjho bona imiphakathi ikhethe abajameli bunqopha abaziphendulela kibo , ukukhambisa nokutjheja imibonwabo . Hlathulula iindlela ezahlukahlukeneko zokusebenza ngenturhu . iimali ezibulungelwa umhlalaphasi kanye nesikhala seenzuzo zeengozi kufanele sivalwe ngamatjhuguluko , kufaka hlangana iimali ezikhutjhwa ngokukatelelwa , ngokutjheja indaba yokufaka ezinye iimali zokwehlisa iindleko zeemalezi ezikhutjhwa basebenzi abarhola imirholo ephasi nanyana basebenzi abasebenza ngeenkhathi zoke . Imithombo yangaphakathi : ikhiqizwa ngumasipala ngokwakhe , isib . iimali zomthelo nezeenlinganiso begodu neensetjenziswa ezifana nokuqatjhiswa kwezindlu begodu memithelo yokusetjenziswa kwazo namkha ngehlelo lemali okutheliswa kwepahla namkha yendawo yokulala . Ukwakhiwa lwelandelaniso lezehlakalo zomphakathi , icozululo leenqhelo zeenkhathi ezithize zonyaka neleenqhelo eziragela phambili kwenza bonyana umphakathi ukwazi ukukhomba iinkambiso eziqakathekileko ezenzeka njalonjalo begodu kwenza bonyana umphakathi ukwazi ukukhomba nokucozulula ukuphumelela nokubhalelwa kweendlela ezahlukeneko zokusiza ezisetjenziswe ngomnqopho wokuthuthukisa umphakathi . i-Venn diagram , icozululo leendlela zokuziphilisa , umtletlana wendawana eyisampula kanye nemisebenzi yokutlama ikhiqiza isithombe esingasisihle mayelana nobujamo bakhathesi obukhona emphakathini . Begodu igandelela amatshwayo wobujamo bephasi , webhoduluko , wesikhala , kanye necozululo leendlela zokuziphilisa nemisebenzi yomphakathi . Ukutjheja iragelo phambili lephrojekthi kuqakathekile ukuqinisekisa bona ihlala isemtlhaleni nokobana ubungozi namtjhana amatjhuguluko ayatjhejwa ekwenziweni komsebenzi okulandelako . Iinqhema zamaphrojekthi zisebenzisa iinkomba ukutjheja iragelo phambili . Iinkomba zimiqothelwa etjengisa bona iminqopho iphunyelelisiwe nanyana njani . Kwesinye isikhathi amalogfremu abiza iinkomba ' iinkomba eziqinisekiseka kwamambala ' . Iinkomba kufanele zifaneleke , zanele , zinqophe , zimedeke , zonge imali begodu zitholakale . Ama-CDW adzimelele eensetjenzisweni zomphakathi abantu abasebenza emphakathini lapho bakhethelwe khona , lapha bahlala khona nakiloyo abamphendulako mayelana nomsebenzabo . Asekelwa minyango eminengi karhulumende khulukhulu urhulumende wekhaya . UmZombe wokweThulwa kweenSetjenziswa kuboniswe etheyibuleni elisekhasini lama-28 . Libonisa iingaba zomzombe nobuzibophelela welinye nelinye izinga lakarhulumende . Isigaba sokuqalelelwa kweensetjenziswa kukulapha itjhejo nomsebenzi kwenzeka khona okuyindawo yamambala yokunikelwa kweensetjenziswa . Ivikele ibhoduluko lemvelo ebujameni obunye nobunye , ikwazi nokho ukutjhiyela iinzukulwana zangomuso igugu lemvelo ubuncani bakhona elilinganako ngokuqakatheka . I-MFMA , yomnyaka we-2003 idinga bonyana ibhajedi kamasipala ifane neye-IDP . Ukuhlobanisa ibhajedi kamasipala naleyo ye-IDP kuqinisekisa bonyana amalunga womkhandlu azibophelele emphakathini womkhandlu newomphakathi begodu neendingo zalabo ababajameleko ziyafezekiswa begodu ziba nezinto ezikhona . Izinto eziqakathekileko kunezinye ezikhonjiweko ku-IDP kumele zibotjhelelwe ebhajedini ekulu kamasipala . UmThethosisekelo weSewula Afrika unikela itlhatlha loke zombelele imithetho nemithetjhwana okumele yenzelwe ngaphakathi kwalo . Linikela amalungelo , ikululeko , amandla nevikeleko kibo boke abantu enarheni . Liveza kuhle imikhakha emithathu karhulumende ekungeyenarha- welizwe , wephrovinsi nawendawo . UmThethosisekelo ukatelela urhulumende wendawo ukobana uthathe indima yokuthuthukisa ngokunikela urhulumende wendawo eminye imisebenzi yokuthuthukisa . Ilawulo letjhuguluko mazombe : Ukubona amandla wamatjhuguluko kanye nokubambisana kwamatjhuguluko weendawo eziqakathekileko nokobana kufanele ngenzeni ngazo . Ukutlama ngendlela efaneleko kwenza bonyana amalunga womphakathi akwazi ukuveza tjhatjhalazi iintjisakalo zawo ezakhako malungana nomphakathi . Begodu kuba namandla khudlwana , njengemsebenzini olandelako , lokha nangabe kweyame phezu kokubuyekezwa kwepahla nemisebenzi enikelwako . Lokhu kugcugcuzela abantu bonyana bakhe umbono wamambala , ongaphunyeleliswa kanye namagadango wokufikelela embonweni lowo . Mnengi umsebenzi ekusafanele wenziwe ukugandelela iimbopho zezakhamuzi ekuzithuthukiseni zona ngokwazo nekusebenzisaneni nabanye emphakathini ukurarulula ukutjhuba kommoya kanye neentjhijilo . Ukuzibeka kwacaca , " uphuthe imikhono uthi umbuso uzasenzela " kufanele kutjhijilwe - lokho akusilo iqiniso begodu akukhambisani nerherho lombuso weSewula Afrika . Khuyini imiphumela yephrogremu ngehlangothini lokuthuthukisa iintlabagelo zobuntu nokwakha umthamo wabomma na ? Yabobaba yona ke ? Indawo nobujamo babomma buthuthukile yini ngebanga lephrogremu le na ? Amakhetho anande abanjwa amahle , atjhaphulukileko enziwa siphathimandla esingabandakanyekiko ekhethweni anikela izakhamuzi ithuba lokuzikhethela ngokwazo . Umsebenzi 2 Njengesiqhema cocani ngamalunga aqakathekileko womtlamo wewadi begodu nikhombe ngeengaba okumele zakhe umtlamo . Tjhijila enye nenye indlela yokumorosa imali kamasipala abezwa ngayo begodu babawe nephenyo ngayo . Abahlanganyeli bahlukana ngeenqhema ezincazana begodu baqale imiphumela emithathu abayikhethe njengaleyo edinga itjhejontangi emsebenzini ogadungileko . Abahlanganyeli bazijayeza igadango elinye nelinye lokwakha umtlamo wewadi ngokusebenzisa indlela yokufunda bulingisa . Abakghonakalisi abathunywe ukwenza umsebenzi lowo kuba ngibo abasizako , iinqhema zirekhoda ilwazi lazo efliphutjhadini begodu isiqhema ngasinye siyakhonjelwa bonyana sizokwenza isethulo emhlanganweni wamalunga woke . Hlela ingcoco encwadini ucoce ngeempendulo zabahlanganyeli begodu nangabe bangakghona ukusebenzisa iimphakamiso erhelweni lokuhlola bese baqala ezinye iindlela abangazisebenzisa ukukghonakalisa ukuhlanganyela komphakathi . Iinkomba zemiphumela zilinganisa ' lokho okuphuma kuphrojekthi . Iinkomba kumele zikhethwe ngokuya kwekhathelelo lesitjhabeso . Iinkomba ziyezwakala kwaphela nangabe ngezifaneleko ngokuya kwekhathelelo labantwabo . Inani labantu ababuya eenqhemeni eziqothelweko zokulingana kwemisebenzi eqatjhwe emalevelini amathathu aphezulu wokuphatha ngokuthobela umtlamo wokulingana komsebenzi ophasisiweko kamasipala . Yenza isiqiniseko sokobana amalunga womphakathi ayezwisisa isirhunyezo sebhajedi begodu nezinto eziphathelene newadi . Imihlahlandlela ayisiyo imithetho , kodwana ilitlhatlha elingasiza abomasipala ekuhlomeni amaKomidi wamaWadabo . Abomasipala bendawo bahlukene begodu batlhoga ukobana babe nobukghwari nanyana nekghono lokuzitholela zabo iinsombululo zemiraro ebahlangabezana nayo emiphakathinabo . Abomasipala kutlhogeka bona bathuthukise umgomo weKomidi yeWadabo okufanele uphumeleliswe Mkhandlu kaMasipala . IKomidi yeWadi inayo yini indlela emajadu yokukhuthaza abomma ukuhlanganyela ngokusebenzisa amaKomidi wamaWadi , namaqhinga wokwandisa ubujameleki emalevelini wokuthathwa kwenqunto na ? Nangabe zikhona ngiziphi ? UmTlamo wokuThuthukisa weliZwe Loke unqophe ukurarha ubuchaka nokuphungula ukungalingani ungakafiki umnyaka wee-2030 . ISewula Afrika ingakwazi ukuphumelelisa iminqopho le ngokusebenzisa amandla wabantu bayo , ngokwakha umnotho ozakwazi ukuhlomulisa boke abantu bayo , ngokwakha amakghono , ngokungezelela amandla wombuso , begodu nangokuthuthukisa amakhwalithi woburholi obuhle kanye nokusebenza ngokuhlanganyela emphakathini woke . Ukuphunyeleliswa ngepumelelo komtlamo lo kutlhoga uburholi obuqinileko bombuso , bekoro yamabhizinisi , bekoro yabasebenzi kanye nomphakathi woke . Icozululo lababambisani liyinto ekufanele ivakatjhelwe njalo ephrojektheni . Kufanele kuqalwe ngokuhlanganiswa nokucozululwa komraro , kunokobana kube yinto ehlukanisiweko . Itsengo yebhajedi yobulili isiza urhulumende ukobana athathe isiqunto sokobana imithethokambiso idinga ukuhlaliswa njani , begodu nokobana iintlabagelo zidinga ukwabiwa kuphi godu . Itsengo yebhajedi yobulili inikela abomma ikomba yokuzibophelela kukarhulumende ekulungiseni iindingo ezinqophileko zabomma nelungelo lezetlhogomelo kwezepilo , ifundo nomsebenzi . Imihlangano emibili yokutjheja ebanjwa qobe nyanga iqakathekile ekomidini ngemva kokwakhiwa komtlamo njengendlela yokugcugcuzela abantu malungana nokuphunyeleliswa komtlamo kanye nokubenza babenesibopho malungana neragelo phambili . Khuthaza umphakathi ukuthatha igadango begodu nependulo , ukuqinisekisa umkhandlu ngombiko obuyako . Ukungezelela ukukhula komnotho ukufikela ngaphezu kwamaphesende amahlanu ngomnyaka kuzokufuna bonyana ikoro yamabhizinisi neyabasebenzi zisekele umbono ohlanganyelweko . Inarha le ithome mhlapha nje ukukhulumisana ngamaphuzu anomfakela ekohlakalweni . Umlando weSewula Afrika wokulawula ukuqatjhwa kwabasebenzi okusekelwa mbuso ngeemali nawo utjharaganisa amazinga wokuziphatha ukuya phambili . Ilemuko leentjhabatjhaba likhombisa bonyana ngokusebenzisa amandla wepolotiki nangokusebenzisa amaqhinga alungileko ngendlela eragela phambili , ikohlakalo ingaphunguka ngendlela ebonakalako begodu nethemba lomphakathi lingabuyela esigeni . Khetha abantu abafaneleko mayelana nesehlakalo esithileko . Isibonelo nangabe yindaba emayelana namaphilo , abasebenzi bezamaphilo , iingulani , imikhandlu etlhogomela ekhaya , abayelelisi bomphakathi njll . Kungaba babantu okutlhogeka bona babandakanyeke . Ukujanyelwa kweenqhema ezinekareko - Ziyini iinkambiso ezikhona zokobana ngithole umbono obuya eenqhemeni ezinerhuluphelo ? Ingabe kudinga bona ngenze umhlangano nesiqhema esinerhuluphelo ? Yenza isiqiniseko sokobana uthethe isikhathi sokwethula iKomidi yeWadi esiqhemeni esinye nesinye esinerhuluphelo bese usinikela imininingwana yokuthintana . Umkghonakalisi nguye orholako begodu ulawula ikambiso . AmaKomidi weWadi angabizwa bona alawule umhlangano benzelele ukuthola umbono womphakathi umTlamo wokuThuthukisa oHlanganiswe ngokuZeleko namtjhana ekwenzeni iRherho lokuLawula ukwEnza . Imiphakathi imumethe abantu abanezendlalelo ezihlukileko , abaneenkareko ezihlukileko , abanamasiko ahlukileko , abaneenkolo ezihlukileko , bemihlobo ehlukileko kanye nalabo abarhola imirholo ehlukileko . Ukubhalansa nokutjheja ngefanelo leziinkareko ezihlukileko kusitjhijilo esikhulu kwamanikelela . Amaphuzu anjengemithombo enganeliko nengafumaneki lula kanye nokungalawuleki kuhle kwemithombo kungokhunye okungezelela kileziintjhijilo . Abakghonakalisi be-CBP kufuze baqinisekise bonyana abantu bajameleka ngendlela efaneleko lokha nakutlanywako begodu babonelele ngamathuba azakwenza bonyana abantu bakwazi ukuveza iinkareko zabo ezihlukileko , kukhulunyisanwe begodu kuzwanwe ngazo . Indima ekufuze bayidlale ngeyokwakha ibhoduluko elizakuqinisekisa bonyana iinqhema zihlanganyela ngobunengi lokha nakutlanywako . Ngimaphi amarherho nemithetjhwana yeendlela zekambiso yokuthathwa kweenqunto : ithoma iphezulu iye phasi na ? Iyakuvumela yini ukuhlanganyela na ? Akhona yini amathuba wabasebenza ngaphandle , abaphethe iindaba eziphathelene nomphathi , begodu abangasibo abaphathi abathoma ukunikela eenquntweni eziqakathekileko zeKomidi yeWadi na ? Kuhlanganyela okubonwa maphiko wombuso njengento esiza ekuphumeleliseni iminqopho yephrojekthi , khulukhulu iindleko eziphunguliweko . Abantu bangahlanganyela ngokwakha iinqhema ezizakwazi ukuhlangabezana neminqopho ebekiweko ehlobene nephrojekthi . Ukuzibandakanya okunjalo kuvamise ukuba khona ngemva kobana abasebenzeli bangaphandle bathethe iinqunto ezikulu . Umkhandlu okhethiweko uyiforamu yokugcina ethatha iinqunto zama-IDP . Indima yobuhlanganyelo bedomokhrasi kukwazisa , ukukhulumisana begodu nokubeka umbono eenquntwenezo , ngesikhathi sekambiso yomtlamo wokuthatha iinqunto . Hlathululela abahlanganyeli woke amanothi wekhoso asekhasini lama-75-76 . Abahlanganyeli balungisa i-ajenda yomhlangano weKomidi yeWadi neyomhlangano womphakathi . Umkhandlu ukhangise ithendara lokusabalalisa amaphaselana wokudla emphakathini . Ithendara lelo lakontragiswa umuntu wangaphandle , kanti abanye bacabanga bona kukhona abantu abangakghona ukwenza umsebenzi lowo khona ekhayapha . Ikontraga nayo yasebenzisa abantu bangaphandle abangakajayeli indawo esikhathini esinengi amaphasela wokudla akafiki ebantwini abafaneleko . Kunokuthintana okungasikuhle hlangana kwekontraga , iKomidi yeWadi kanye nomphakathi . Sele kunemiraro evelako begodu umphakathi unombono wokobana iKomidi yeWadi kufanele ibe nokuthileko ekwenzako ngomraro lo . Nakufika umnyaka wee-2030 , abantu abahlala eSewula Afrika kufanele baphile ngokuphepha begodu bangasabi ubulelesi . Abomma , abantwana nezinye iinqhema ezingathinteka lula kufanele bavikelwe . Kufanele babe nethemba lokobana irherho lobulungiswa bezobulelesi lizakubopha belitjhutjhise ngepumelelo zoke izelelesi ezenza okuphambene nevikeleko labantu kanye nemiphakathi . IButho lamaPholisa weSewula Afrika namapholisa wemethro kufanele abe maziko asebenza ngobuthakgha aneensebenzi ezinamakghono , abazilawula ngefanelo , abantu abaziphatha kuhle begodu abathanda umsebenzabo nabasebenzela umphakathi . AmaKomidi weWadi asebujameni obumbi bokuqinisekisa ukuhlanganyela komphakathi wekhaya ekusebenzeni kwakamasipala . Lokhu kufaka hlangana ukutjheja ukwenza kwakamasipala kanye nokunikela ku-PMS . Kunesifuneko sangokomthetho sokobana umasipala afake amakomidi wekhaya ngamaKomidi weWadi , ekubekeni ama-KPS nabomqothelwa bokwenza begodu nokuqinisekisa ukubandakanyeka komphakathi ekutjhejeni nekubuyekezeni iinkomba . Kungaba neenkghuluphelo eziphalisanako emawadini ngokuhlukahlukana kumasipala begodu iinkghuluphelwezi kufanele zithathelwe phezulu lokha nakulungiswa i-PMS . IKomidi enye nenye yeWadi kumasipala izokubeka indlebe ekuzweni bona iinrhuluphelo zabo ziyatjhejwa . Isibonelo , iwadi enefemu encani kanye nabantu abanengi abangasebenziko izokubona kungcono ukwenza ibhoduluko lokugcugcuzela ifemu ekulu . Enye iwadi ingaba nedoyelo leemphaphamtjhini bese isinghonghoyilo sabo kube litjhada nokusilaphazeka . I-PMS ngalokho kufanele ifake iinkghuluphelo ezinengi itjheje lokho okungokwamambala komphakathi . Urhulumende wendawo kufanele wenze isiqiniseko sokobana kunelawulo elifaneleko lokuvikela imali-ngeniso , ipahla nemali kamasipala kunokobana imoroswe , ilahleke nanyana yetjiwe . Kuqakathekile ukuthola iindingo zomphakathi ngaphambi kokwenza iphrojekthi namtjhana ukuthuthukisa umsebenzi endaweni . Idayagramu ephepheni elilandelako itjengisa izinto eziqakathekileko ekufanele zitjhejwe . Iphrogremu iphendule njani ezintweni eziqakathekileko kunezinye zeenqhema eziqothelweko ezinqophileko hlangana nesitjhaba sabengubo nabembaji abanendaba na ? Umlaleli - ukukghonakalisa kudinga amakghono wokulalela , qala isAhluko 2 ukuthola ilwazi elingezelelweko lamakghono wokulalela . Indlela ejayelekileko yokwethula umraro nabonobangela bakhona , ukusebenzisa umfanekiso womraro . Ihloso yalomdwebo kutjengisa izinto ababambisani abafisa ukuzahlula bese zisizwa ukuthuthukisa iminqopho eyimiphumela yephrojekthi . Imigomo yombuso yokuthengwa kwepahla nemisebenzi ngiyo etjharaganisako eendabeni zekohlakalo , begodu irherho lombuso lokuthenga ipahla nemisebenzi linobubhyurokhrasi obunengi khulu bekambiso yombuso . Ukugandela ukuthobela ngokutshwaya ibhoksi kwenza bonyana irherhweli libize imali enengi , libe litshwenyo , lingasebenzi ngepumelelo begodu libe nobukhwabaniseke lula . Siphakamisa bonyana ukwelusa okuphakathi okukhudlwana kwamathenda amakhulu newesikhathi eside , okwenza bonyana kungabi semthethweni ukobana abasebenzi bombuso benze eminye imihlobo yamabhizinisi nokwenza bonyana abantu babe nesibopho mayelana namalahlekelo wemilandu yekohlakalo . Ukufuduka kulindeleke bonyana kungezeleleke ngamaphesende ahlangana ne-0.1 ne-0.2 ngomnyaka esilinganisweni sokukhula kwesitjhaba ukufikela emnyakeni wee-2030 . Ukungabikhona kwesikhathi -Amalunga womphakathi esikhathini esinengi kufanele angeze isikhathi nomzamo ekutheni arhole begodu akakakulungeli ukukhambela imighlangano . Kanengi lokhu kwenzeka kibomma nakulawo malunga womphakathi angasebenziko . I-PMS ne-IDP zisebenza ndawonye njengomasipala njengobana zilinganisa bona ukwethula kwakamasipala mayelana ne-IDP kuphumelelisa kangangani , njengobana I-IDP iyisisekelo sokwethulwa kweensetjenziswa nokuphakanyiswa komphakathi . I-PMS kufanele iqalane khulukhulu namajamo kamasipala . Kufanele ibe nobudlelwana neensetjenziswa zakamasipala begodu inqophane nalokhu okuqakathekileko kunokhunye , iminqopho , iinkomba kanye nabomqothelwa abaku-IDP . UNgqogqotjhe kaRhulumende weKhaya newesiFunda ubeke ama-KPI akatelelekileko kawokewoke . Abomasipala kufanele bafake lokhu hlangana kanye , namanye ama-KPI afanelekileko kuma-PMS wabo . Lokha umtlamo womphakathi nawuzakuba yipumelelo , kufuneka bonyana kufakwe boke ababambisani ekambisweni yokutlama njengabahlali , amakhansela , iinkhulu zakamasipala , amalunga wezakhiwo zomphakathi njengamaKomidi weWadi nama-CBO , abarholi bendabuko , iinqhema zendawo ezinekareko kanye namabhizinisi wendawo . Omunye nomunye umbambisani udlala indima ku-CBP . Ngaphezu kwamandla wepolotiki , ikohlakalo kufanele kulwisanwe nayo emahlangothini amathathu : ngokuvimbela bonyana abantu bangalelesi ngokubethusa ngemiphumela yobulelesobo , ngokukhandela nangefundo . Ukuvimbela bonyana abantu bangalelesi ngokubethusa ngemiphumela yobulelesobo kusiza abantu bonyana bezwisise bonyana kungenzeka babanjwe bese bayajeziswa . Ukukhandela kuphathelene namarherho ( ilwazi , ukuhlolisisa nokhunye ) enza bonyana kube budisi ukuzibandakanya ezenzweni zekohlakalo . Amahlangothi wezehlalakuhle wekohlakalo kufanele bonyana asetjenzwe ngokuqalana neenkambisolawulo , ngokusebenzisa ifundo . Kufanele kuqedwe ubuthakathaka bezakhiwo ezimbalwa nangabe i-Afrika ifuna ukutjhugulula ukukhula ngokurhaba nefuneko ephezulu yepahla yokurhweba ukobana kukhuphule imisebenzi namazinga wokuphila . Okuqakatheke khulu , kukobana itjhebiswano lezokuthutha elingasilihle namathungelelwano wemithangalasisekelo angasimahle , kanye neenqabo zemithelo nalezo ezingakaphathelani nemithelo , zikhuphula iindleko zokwenza ibhizinisi begodu zikhinyabeze ukusisa nokurhwebelana kwangaphakathi . Iinhlangano zomthetho ezinganamandla begodu , lapho khunye ukubusa kumbi kukhuphula iingozi zokusisa . Kodwana isithombe esimbeso sithoma ukuba ngcono , kodwana kusese neentjhijilo , ezifaka hlangana lezo zeHlangano yokuThuthukisa amaZwe we-Afrika engeSewula ( SADC ) , eqalene nobudisi mayelana nemithangalasisekelo , iinqabo kwezokurhwebelana kanye nokubusa . Njengombana iSewula Afrika izokuba nobudisi bokuphalisana ngemikhiqizo efuna amakghono aphasi ngenca yesakhiwo sayo seendleko eziphezulu , kodwana iinarha ezinengi enarhakazini le zingakghona ukuphalisana njengombana iindleko zemikhiqizo zikhuphuka ePumalanga ye-Asia . Amarherho weendlela zokwenza eziphumelelisako zidinga ukuhlolwa ukobana umehluko ungamukelwa bewugugubazwe njani ukwenzela bonyana woke amalunga womphakathi akwazi ukufakwa hlangana ngendlela engarhelebha umphakathi ukufeza iminqopho yawo ngokuqinisekisa ukwethulwa komsebenzi okuphumelelisako ngokuhlanganyela nomphakathi . Kodwana , ukukhuthaza nokumukela ukuhlukana akusikho kwaphela ukubeka abomqothelwa , namkha nokufunda ukwenza ubugugu ngomehluko wabantu kodwana kufuneka wakhe ukwamukeleka nokudzimelelisa ukubekezelelana nehlonipho . Funda ifundo-sehlakalo esesAhlukweni 5 , 5,6 bese uzijayeza eenqhemeni bona uyokusebenza bunjani ngesigaba ngasinye . Abahlanganyeli baya edayagrameni esekhasini le-15 banqophise esigabeni esinye nesinye sekambiso yokuthintana . AmaKomidi weWadi akakafaneli bona abe namalunga akhethiweko angaphezu kwali-10 ajamele amakareko ahlukahlukileko emphakathini . Umkhandlu omunye nomunye wenza umthetho wokukhetha amalunga weKomidi yeWadi . Nokho-ke , amalunga ayakhethwa , kungaba mabhaloti ayifihlo emhlanganweni womphakathi namtjhana ngokutjengisa ngezandla namtjhana ngokuvumelana , kufanele kuvunyelwane nabahlanganyeli boke begodu imibiko ecacileko yekambiso kufanele ibe khona ukuze umphakathi uziqalele nangabe unesidingo . Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi kufanele abe bavowudi abarejistariweko begodu kufanele babe ngabakhutheleko , abathembekako nabahloniphekako ikakhulukazi iinqhema abazijamelako . Abakghonakalisi bewadi - bangathathwa emalungeni weKomidi yeWadi nanyana kungaba malunga ahloniphekileko womphakathi njengabomazithandela , abarholi bezekolo nabanemibono , nanyana abantu abayisika abanamakghono wokwenza izinto emphakathini njengabantu abasebenza umbuso esele bafumana umhlalaphasi , abotitjhere , umrholi wesiqhema sabomma , njll . Kibo boke ubujamo kufuze babe namandla kanye netjisakalo yokusiza ukwakha nokuphumelelisa imitlamo yomphakathi . Emsebenzini olandelako imiphumela efuneka eenqhemeni zehlalakuhle ihlanganiswa neSWOT yazo zoke iinqhema ezahlukeneko zehlalakuhle . Ngokwenza bunjalo kuzabe kwakhiwa umbono omkhulu womphakathi . Begodu lokhu kusiza ekutjhejeni ntangi imiphumela eqakathekileko . Sikhathi esingangani esidingekako ukuqedelela amahlelo kanye namajima ewadini labo ? Ifundo ephakemeko . Umsebenzi wamaziko akhona uthoma kiloyo osezingeni elihle khulu loke ukuya kilelo elingasilihle nakancani . Ukwenziwa ngcono kwekhwalithi ngazo zoke iinkhathi kuyadingeka ngombana irherho likhula ngebelo elilingeneko . Isitjhijilo esikhulu ngesokobana ifundo engasiyihle yesikolo ingezelela iindleko zokukhiqiza iimfundiswa ezineziqu , begodu inani eliphasi khulu labafundi abanzima lifumana iziqu zemayunivesithi . Ukungezelela ukuhlanganyela kanye neenlinganiso zokufumana iziqu , ngokukhetha idigri yeyunivesithi ethatha iminyaka emine , ngokuyihlanganisa namakhoso ayamisako kanye nokusekelwa khudlwana kwamayunivesithi ukusekela abafundi abanzima abegade badinywe amathuba ngaphambilini , kungenzeka kube namakhakhazela aseqophelweni eliphezulu . IKomidi yeWadi kufuze ibe nehlelo lomnyaka elendlala ngokucacileko lokho elikubona kuqakathekile nokuthi ihlose ukuzuza ini . Lokho kuzokusiza iKomidi yeWadi ukubona bonyana ingabe ikwazile ukuzuza lokho ebeyikuhlosile . Begodu kuzokusiza iKomidi yeWadi ukubika kumasipala , njengombana ingabika qobe nyanga ngalokho esele ikuzuzile ukuya ngokomtlamo wayo . Nangabe usebenzisa iinsetjenziswa ezifana ne-overheard projector , namtjhana ifliphutjhadi , zijayeze ukuyisebenzisa ngaphambili . Ukutlama - Ikomidi yeWadi isebenzisana khulu nekhansela ukuqala lokho okufunwa mphakathi qangi nokwenza isiqiniseko sokobana okunyulwakokhu kuyafakwa eemphakamisweni zebhajede nemitlameni yamaphrojekthi . Ikomidi yeWadi itlhoga ukobana ibe nomtlamo womnyaka oveza kuhle lokho ekunyulako nalokho elindele ukukuzuza . Lokhu kuzakusiza iKomidi yeWadi ukobana itlame umhlangano okhethekileko msinyazana ukuthuthukisa umtlamo wokwenza . Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi kufanele enze isiqiniseko sokobana umtlamawo ungewamambala begodu uyazuzeka . Umtlamo ulithulusi lokuhlathulula bonyana umphakathi ufuna ukuya kuphi , lokwenza iimphakamiso ku-IDP , lokutjheja iragelo phambili ekuphunyelelisweni komtlamo , begodu lingenziwa bonyana likhambisane nesikhathi qobe mnyaka lokha amaphrojekthi nakaragela phambili , nalokha nakuvela amatjhejontangi amatjha . Lokha nakwakhiwa umtlamo , ubunikazi bawo bungenziwa ngcono ngokutjheja ezinye iindlela zokwazisa iinqhema ezahlukahlukeneko zomphakathi ngalokho okumumethwe mtlamo lowo , lokho kufaka hlangana iinrhunyezo zamalimi wendawo , amaphosta , idrama . Lokhu kufuze kukhulunywe emhlanganweni womphakathi wokuqedelela . Kuqakathekile bonyana amatshwayo aqakathekileko anjengombono kanye neminqopho itjhugululelwe elimini elikhulunywa babantu bendawo leyo . Begodu ukutjhugulula irherho lezomnotho kutjho ukutjhugulula amaphethini wobunikazi nokulawula . Ukufikela namhlanjesi , imizamo yokudlulisa ubunikazi bepahla yengeniso ibhalelwe kuletha imiphumela efunekako , begodu iinkimu zobunikazi bamatjhere zabasebenzi zidlala indima encani khulu . Kutlhogeka iqhinga elibonakalako kanye neenqothelwa ezicacileko . Iinsetjenziswa zemigomo zokugcugcuzela ikoro yangeqadi ukobana itjhugulule amaphethini wobunikazi zifaka hlangana amakarada wokuzithandela wetuthukomsebenzi , imithetho yokuthengwa kwepahla nemisebenzi , amalungiselelo wokukhutjhwa kwamalayisense ( njengakumathintaniswanoliqha nemisebenzini yokurhweba ngezenjiwa ) nemali ethuthukisako . Ikghono leenhlangano liqakatheke khulu ekuphumeleleni kweqhingeli , kufaka hlangana ukubuyekezwa kwemithetho yokurarulula ubudlelwano obungasimnandi phakathi kweenhlangano zendabuko kanye neenhlangano ezakhiwe ngokweenjamiso zomthethosisekelo . Ukuhlunga ( nokutjheja ) nerhelo lokuhlola lizakufaka yini phakathi iimfuneko nelwazi lerhemiso-mvama elicacileko begodu nelwazi elingakahlanganiswa kobulili na ? Ukuphungula iindleko zokuphila mayelana nemindeni esebenzako begodu erhola imali encani . Ukungalingani nobuchaka kungararululwa ngokungezelela imirholo ngokukhuliswa kwemikhiqizo nangokuphungula iindleko zokuphila . Ukuzibophelela ezingeni elamukelekako lokuphila kuzakuqinisekisa bonyana yoke imindeni ihlanganyela ngokubonakalako erherhweni lezomnotho . Iindleko zokudla , zeenthuthi zabakhambi ngeenkhwelo nokwakhelwa izindlu kufanele bonyana ziphungulwe , begodu kufanele kukhutjhulwe ikhwalithi yefundo yasimahla nanyana yeendleko eziphasi neyetjhejo lezamaphilo . IKomidi yeWadi ingahloma amakomidi angaphasi ibe yinye nanyana zibe zinengi bese ifaka hlangana iinhlangano zomphakathi kilamakomidi angaphasi . Boke ababambisani eWadini bayakhuthazwa ukobana bahlanganyele emakomidini angaphasi akhambisana nemisebenzabo . Indlela yokusebenza eyame phezu kwamakghono yindlela ebalekela ukutlama okweyame phezu kwemiraro , okuyindlela eqalene neenqintelo . Indlela eyame phezu kwamakghono iqalene khulu nokutlama ngendlela efaneleko nokuthi umphakathi ufuna ukuzibona ukuphi nokobana ungafika bunjani lapho . UmTlamo wokuHlanganisa ngokuZeleko ( i-IDP ) ukhomba iinhloso zakamasipala begodu amaphrojekthi athathwako alinganiswa ngehlelo . Ngendlela efanako , umtlamo wewadi ngokuvamileko unikela iinlinganiso zesiqunto zamaphrojekthi ezikhethwa yiKomidi yeWadi . Ukuvikelwa kwehlalakuhle kuletha ibumbano nokuzwana komphakathi mayelana nepilo begodu kuqinisekisa bona kube nezinga lepilo elamukelekako . Begodu kudlala indima eqakathekileko ekusizeni imindeni nemizi ukulawula iingozi zepilo , begodu kwenza lula amatjhuguluko wemakethe yabasebenzi , begodu lokho kusiza ekutheni irherho lezomnotho likwazi ukutjhuguluka khudlwana ukuya ngokobujamo . Umkhandlu wewadi Z wenze imihlahlandlela yokukhetha amaKomidi weWadi . Umasipala ukhangise ema-ofisini womkhandlu , iinkolo , iinhlangano zekolo , imitholapilo yekhaya kanye nezinye iindawo zomphakathi lapho iKomidi yeWadi izokubekwa khona nokobana uyini umsebenzayo . Isaziso sihlathululwe ephetjhaneni elinanyathiselweko lelwazi bona ihlangano namtjhana iziko ( begodu yendlala ngamaziko ) lingathumela abongikhethani emkhandlwini wekhaya . Iphetjhaneli linikela godu ilanga lamakhetho , indawo nesikhathi begodu limema abavowudi abarejistariweko bona beze . Emhlanganweni kufundwe amagama waboonkhetheni begodu ungikhethani omunye nomunye wethuliwe emhlanganweni begodu babakiwa bona bazazise bebatjho nokobana bajamele liphi iziko . Bekunabongikhethani abama-28 . Amagama waboonkhetheni bekatlolwe ephepheni lebhalodi begodu abahlanganyeli emhlanganweni babakwe bona bavowudele abali-10 . Aboonkhetheni aba-10 abathole amavowudu amanengi benza iKomidi weWadi . Okwesibili , umasipala kufanele alinganise imisebenzi okufanele ikhuliswe namtjhana ithuthukiswe . Ingabe ezinye iindawo zomphakathi zineensila khulu begodu aziphathwa kuhle ? Umphathi kamasipala ukhethwa mkhandlu eminyakeni emihlanu yekontraga yokwenziwa komsebenzi . Uyihloko yokuphathwa komkhandlu begodu unomsebenzi wokulawula iimali , ukuqatjha nokujezisa iinsebenzi . Iinkhulu zakamasipala zisebenzela ukuphatha nokwenza imithethokambiso yomkhandlu . Umphumela wesigabesi kuba yi-IDP kamasipala esele ithole imvumo . Ukwenza ilandelela - IKomidi yeWadi ingabawa imibiko njalo ngamaphrojekthi kanye nangemisebenzi eyenziweko . Ukulawulwa kwerherho lokufunda . Ukuphungula amalarha webhyurokhrasi kuzakwenza bonyana kube nemithombo eminengana yokusekela iinkolo nabotitjhere . Indlela yelemuko lamambala ngethi amangenelelo , asekelako nalungisako , kufanele alamane ngokupherhuliweko nomsebenzi kwesikolo . Ngalendlela , iinkolo ezisebenza ngconywana zinganikelwa ikululeko yokuragela phambili nomsebenzi , ikani kunobungcono obulinganisekako . Senza iimphakamiso ezinqophileko ngokuqala isekelo elingconywana elinikelwa iinkolo , ukwethulwa kweendingo ezisisekelo zefundo ehle nangokulinganisa izinto ezilungileko . Ziphakamisa bonyana kube nejima lokwenza ngcono imithangalasisekelo yeenkolo ezitlhagako , khulukhulu eendaweni zemakhaya . Ekupheleni kwalomhlangano osemthethweni , umphakathi uzokuba nombono ohlanganyelweko ekubonisenwe ngawo ophathelene nokuthuthukiswa komphakathi . URhulumende weKhaya : UmThetho wokuLawula iimali zakaMasipala ( MFMA ) , we-2003 uhlanganiswe nomThetho wamaRherho kaMasipala ( MSA ) , we-2000 njengoba yomibili isebenza ngamarherho wangaphakathi kurhulumende wekhaya ; ukwenziwa kweendlela zokuthintana ; amarherho wokwenza neendlela zokuthuthukisa ukuziphendulela . I-MFMA ihlathulula bona irherho leemali zakamasipala lisebenza bunjani nokobana indima endlalwa malunga womkhamdlu ngiyiphi eyenza isebenze . Lalela bewuhloniphe abanye , ngokungakhathaleli iinkolelo zabo , amagama namtjhana ukuziphatha . Kunobujamo obuqakathekileko bokuloba nokuzuza ekufuze butjhejwe mayelana nokwenjiwa kanye nokuzuza emkhiqizweni wezenjiwa . ISewula Afrika iloba itjhere yemakethe yephasi loke emikhiqizweni enjengeferokhromu . Kodwana , isigaba sokuthoma sokusetjenzwa kwayo nanyana sokuyincibilikisa sisebenzisa igezi nemali enengi khulu , begodu kuyenzeka bonyana sisebenzise igezi nemali yeenkoro ezinye . ISewula Afrika kufanele bonyana ikwazi ukukhetha imikhakha enqophe ukusekela isigaba sokuthoma sokwenjiwa nokusetjenzwa kwezenjiwa . Imikhakha ekufanele bonyana itjhejwe ntangi kufanele ifake hlangana leyo esele inamakghono afaneleko , nanyana leyo ekungenzeka bonyana ukwenjiwa nokusetjenzwa kwezenjiwa kungarholela eenkambisweni eziza ngemva kokukhiqiza . Ukwemba nokusebenza zoke izenjiwa zenarha akukghonakali begodu akukaqakatheki mayelana nokuthuthukisa ikoro ekudlwana yokukhiqiza . Mukela ukukwata kwakho . Cabanga ngakho . Ungali ukuba khona kokukwata kwakho namtjhana ubalekele ukusebenza ngakho . Nangabe uyakwenza lokho kungaya endaweni engasingiyo begodu kuye ebantwini okungasingibo . Itsengo yebhajedi eyipendulo yobulili itjho ukutsengwa kwamambala kweendleko zakarhulumende begodu nengeniso-mali kibomma nabentazana nakumadaniswa nakubaba nabesana . Amabhajedi wobulili akusiwo amabhajedi ahlukileko wabomma begodu akakanqophi kwaphela ekwandiseni iindleko kumaphrogremu wabomma . Akwenzako kuqinisekisa bonyana iindingo zabomma zifakwe phakathi begodu ziyaphiwa . Lo mtlamo weSewula Afrika . Unikela umleyo ophumelelisako nonabileko wokuhlahla izinto eziqakathekileko ekufanele zikhethwe namagadango ekufanele athathwe . Ukuphumelela kwawo kweyame kiwo woke amaSewula Afrika ekutheni azibophelele ekuphumeleliseni umtlamo lo orholwa nguMengameli neKhabinethi . AmaKomidi weWadi ajamele iinkareko ezahlukahlukeneko ezifaka hlangana iindaba ezimayelana nedorobha nanyana imikhandlu yababhadeli beenlinganiso , iinhlangano zezetuthuko , bamayuniyoni weensebenzi , iinhlangano zezerhwebo , iinqhema zabomma , ilutjha kanye neenhlangano zezekolo . Ilawulo lephrojekthi libandakanya ukulawula ukuphunyeleliswa komtlamo , okufaka hlangana ukuhluza kobana izinto zikhamba njani nokubuyekeza imitlamo ekuphenduleni iintjhijilo namtjhana amatjhuguluko wobujamo angavela endleleni . E-Egypt kade , abobaba bebahlala ekhaya beluka . Abomma batlhogomele imindeni . Abomma bebathola ipahla njengelifa abobaba bebangatholi litho . Amaphepha womqondo wephrojekthi akhuluma ' ngomsebenzi wamaphepha ' ekufuze ulungiswe begodu udluliselwe emkhandlwini nanyana eminyangweni yeenkoro . Lamaphepha alirekhodi lalokho ekuvunyelenwe ngakho okuzakuqinisekisa bonyana boke ababambisani bazinikela ekwaluseni iragelo phambili . Imithombo ethembakeleko yenturhu emawadini wabahlanganyeli . Ukuhloma iindlelakambiso ezitja kanye nomleyo welizwe loke wokufakwa kwabantu eendaweni zokuhlala . Amatjhebiswano neenhlangano zendawo ezifana nalezo okungasizo iinhlangano zikarhulumende , iinhlangano ezitjheja zinganikela indawo yeendawo nelwazi okumele linikelwe umphakathi nelibuya emphakathini . Umsebenzi 2 khomba iinkambisolawulo eziqakathekileko zokuhlanganyela komphakathi . UMBUZO 2 Ungayirarulula njani imiraro yokwethulwa komsebenzi ? Amathulusi enza i-LFA angasetjenziselwa ukwakha kabutjha namtjhana ukuphula iphrojekthi ephakanyisiweko , nokuragela phambili ngokuhlahluba ukukhambelana nokukghonakala . Ebujameni bamaKomidi wamaWadi abadlali-ndima bangathuthukisa umthethokambiso omajadu nobonakalako werhemiso-kambiso okuyindlela yobunjalo bokubonakala kobulili kiyo yoke imithethokambiso namaphrogremu , ukwenzela bonyana ngaphambi kobana iinqunto zithathwe itsengo yokuphumelela kwabomma nabobaba iyenziwa . I-PCM idzimelele emzombeni wephrojekthi begodu iqalelela kabutjha zoke iingcenye zephrojekthi esikhathini sasafuthi sephrojekthi . Lokhu kutjho bona amatjhuguluko namtjhana iintjhijilo zihlangana ekwenziweni nekuhlelweni kwegadango elilandelako . Ku-LFA iinkomba ngezinye iinkhathi zibizwa ' iinkomba eziqinisekiseka kwamambala ' . Lokhu kungombana omunye nomunye kufanele amede iinkomba ngendlela yamambala engathathi ihlangothi begodu afinyelele emphumeleni ofanako , akukakhathaleki bona umuntu ozimedako ubona njani . Ubulwele obuthathelwanako be-HIV / AIDS butjengise ikghono leSewula Afrika lokwenza imitjhapho emikhulu yezehlalakuhle nepolotiki - kanye nekghono layo lokuyilungisa nokuphumelelisa ihlelo elibudisi ngepumelelo . Ipumelelo yerherho lezamaphilo ekulawuleni ukurhatjheka kobulwelobu iminyaka emihlanu egadungileko iyathokozisa . Kodwana akukafaneli bonyana zithokoziswe ngilokho bese siphutha imikhono . Kunefuneko eragela phambili yefundo , ukukhandela , ukuhlolela ubulwele nokwelatjhwa . Ukwehlisa isilinganiso sokutshwayeleka okutjha ngobulwelobu kuzakuphungula ifuneko yerherho lezamaphilo lombuso . Kodwana nanyana kungekho ukutshwayeleka okutjha ngobulwelobu , basazokuba khona abanye abantu abanomulwana we-HIV abadinga ukwelatjhwa , bese lokho kubangele iintjhijilo eziragela phambili zesilinganiso sokutshwayeleka ngobulwele bamaphahla kanye nengozi yokubonakala kwamatshwayo athileko we-HIV ebhalela imitjhoga . Ubulwele obuthathelwanakobu kanye nemithelela yabo mayelana nomgomo wombuso kungenzeka buphikelele bubambe ubuncani bakhona esinye isizukulwana esizako - kungenzeka zibe mbili . Abanesabelo / Abahlanganyeli kumele kuvunyelwane ngekambiso begodu amarekhodi abonakalako atloliweko wekambiso kufuze atholakale ukuze azokuqalisiswa . Ubulili kuba mcabango ongenelela woke amahlangothi wobujamo bepilo . Ubujamo bobulili obulinganako abuvimbeli ukuhlanganyela kwabobaba , ngakwelinye ihlangothi , bavumela ubungcono begodu nomsebenzi olinganiseke ngokweqileko phakathi kwabobaba nabomma , ukungabuye kudosele emiphumeleni eyenziwe ngcono yetlhogomelo . Amagadango wokulungisa lokho okungakhange kukhambe kuhle ngaphambilini emisebenzini kufanele bonyana atjheje khulu ukuthuthukiswa kwamabhizinisi , ukufumaneka kwebandulo , ukuthuthuka ngokwebizelo begodu nokweluleka . UmThetho oHlongozwako uliphahla lokuthoma lomgomo / lomthethokambiso welizweloke kuboRhulumende beKhaya / besiGodi ngesikhathi sangemva kwebandlululoUmThetho oHlongozwako wendlala ukuqakatheka kwaborhulumende bekhaya ukuqalelela ituthuko . Ubeka ukuthuthukisa njengombono ophambili , umbono waborhulumende bekhaya / besigodi . Ukuzwisisa ubulili nokusetjenziswa kwesisekelo setsengo lobulili aqakathekileko aqakathekileko wamaKomidi wamaWadi ngehlangothini letuthuko . Awudingi ukobana ube mumuntu okhuthalele ukwenza izinto zobulili , zenzeke , ofuna ukusebenzela ukutjhaphulula nokufana kwabomma ukusebenzisa itsengo lobulili . Omunye nomunye osebenza endaweni yetuthuko yomphakathi ofuna ukwenza ngcono iimpilo zabantu kumele bakwazi ukusebenzisa amathulusi la . Ngokutjhiwoko abomma , khulukhulu esiqhemeni seminyaka esuka kweli-15 ukuya kwema-24 inikuvama okukhulu ukuphathwa yi-HIV begodu nentumbantonga , itjhejo elikhethekileko lidinga ukunikelwa ukuqinisekisa bonyana amaphrogremu namaphrojekthi akhonjwe mphakathi athatha lokhu ngendlela enobuziphendulelo . Umhlangano wokutlama okwandulelako kufuze ubanjwe iveke nanyana iimveke ezimbili ngaphambi komhlangano oqakathekileko wokutlama . Kufuze kugcugcuzelwe abarholi abavela eengcenyeni ezahlukeneko zomphakathi bonyana bazokwenza amalungiselelo weveke yokutlama bebaqinisekise bonyana kuba mphakathi ngokwawo odlala indima eqakathekileko nowamukela ubunikazi bendlelakambiso . Isirhunyezo esingaphasi sendlala amatshwayo aqakathekileko womhlangano wokutlama okwandulelako kanye nendlelakambiso . Yakha ibhoduluko lapha kungazokuba khona ukuphazamiseka khona , lapha abantu bazokunqopha kilokho abakhulumisana ngakho begodu bebakghone nokulalelisisa . Ilawulo lephrojekthi lisebenzisa ithulusi lokwakha ukusiza ababambisani bona bathole ilwazi elidephileko lokuzwisisa isidingo esiqakatheke ukudlula esinye nokuzwisisa imiphumela yomraro . Ngokwenza umfanekiso womraro boke abonobangela kanye nemiphumela ingaqalelelwa . Ukuzindla mbono ocatjangwe ngaphambi kwesikhathi namkha kubandlulula okubuye kuhlathululwe ngendlela yokuziphatha ephikisako , ukudlumbana okunganabuhle emuntwini namkha emalungelweni womuntu . IKomidi yeWadi yenza ilandelela eendabeni zombili nekomidi etjhayelako begodu kwathi ngemva kweenyanga ezi-3 amakhandlela wendlela afakwa bese iKomidi yeWadi yasebenzisana neForamu yesiPholisa somPhakathi ukupatrola indawo . Abantu bahlanganyela ngokuzisungulela imizamo bona ngakwabo ngaphandle kokusizwa ziinhlangano zangaphandle ukufumana imithombo yesizo kanye neenluleko zobuthekhiniki abazidingako , kodwana bahlala banelawulo ziinkoro imithombo yesizo isetjenziswa bunjani . Ingabe zikhona iindawo zamanzi eziqakathekileko nezazisako ze-ikholoji , ekufuze zitlhogonyelwe nanyana abantu bazithabise ngazo , isib . iintete , amatsha , imilomo yemilambo , amadamu , imilambo ? Kuqakathekile ukukhumbula bona ama-KPI asebenza kumayunidi wokuphatha kumasipala neensebenzi , kanye nenye nenye nenye ibhizinisi kamasipala nonikela ngokwenza umsebenzi loyo umasipala anesivumelwano naye sokwenza umsebenzi . I-Luckytown lidorobha elincani elitholakala ePumalanga Kapa ( nanyana kwesinye nesinye isifunda ) . Kwenye ingcenye yedorobheli , abantu bahlala ezindlini ezakhiwe kuhle emaplodini amakhulu wendawo . Abanye bazibhorele imigodi yamanzi begodu kwamanye amaplodi , abanikazi banemithi embalwa yemirorho neenthelo . Ngaphambi komnyaka ka-1994 , lengcenye yedorobha begade ihlala amakhuwa kwaphela kodwana kwathi ngemva kwalokho kwaba nemizi embalwa evela esikomplasini esiseduze eyagcina sele ifudukele kilo . Ukubumbana komphakathi kufanele bonyana kusekele iqhingeli . Nangabe iSewula Afrika iyaphumelela ukuqeda ubunikazi bepahla obunikelwa abantu bobuhlanga obuthileko nokulawulwa komnotho ngaphandle kokuphungula ubuchaka nokungalingani , itjhuguluko lizabe lingekho . Ngokufanako , nangabe izinga lobuchaka nokungalingani liphungulwa ngaphandle kweendlela ezingatjengisi ukutjhuguluka kobunikazi , ituthuko yenarha izakuhlangahlangana begodu ilimale lula . Ikambiso emahlangothi mabili yewadi nokujameleka ngokwengcenye kutjho bona imiphakathi izikhethele bunqopha abajameli abaziphendulela kibo , ukukhambisa nokutjheja iimphakamiso zabo . Ukutjhejwa begodu nokuhlanganiswa kokwethulwa kweensetjenziswa kuyindlela yekambiso yokuhlola ikambiso yeragelo phambili ekutholakaleni kweminqopho esele ibekiwe begodu iyadingeka kwenye nenye ingcenye eqakathekileko yevowudi yebhajedi ekhambisana nesigaba sama-27 ( 4 ) se-PFMA . Imiphumela yokwenziwa komsebenzi ibekelwe bonyana yenze ngcono ukuphumelela kweendleko ukuba nekghono lokwenza begodu kunakho koke ukuphumelela kweendlela zokwethulwa kweesetjenziswa . Indlela yekambiso yokuhlola iragelo phambili ingasetjenziswa njengethulusi lokuzihlola ngokwakho ubeke iminqoppho , utjheje iragelo phambili begodu ukghonakalise ukukhulumisana namakhastama wangaphandle . UMSEBENZI 1 khomba abadlali bendima abahlukeneko neembopho zabo eziphathelene nomtlamo womsebenzi . Ubuhlanganyeli bunikela amandla lakha abantu nabenza zabo iinqunto nokuzikhethela . Ubuhlanganyeli obumajadu bokutlama ngabamukelifa abanqotjhiweko , abangilaba , imiphakathi eyadinywa amathuba , iinhlangano zabomma , iinqhema zetja , iinhlangano zomphakathi , abahlali njll , buqakathekile . Ukutlama kokuhlanganisa ngokuzeleko kuyindlela ebandakanya umasipala woke nemiphakathi ekutholeni iinsombululo ezingcono zokuphumelelisa ukuthuthukiswa kwesikhathi eside . I-IDP lithulusi eliqakathekileko lokusebenzisa iinsetjenziswa ezikhona ukwenzelela ukuhlangana neendingo ezinengi zendawo . Isiza umasipala ekuqaleni bona ziyini iindingo emaphikweni ahlakahlukeneko- njengezepilo , amanzi , iinthuthi , ukuvikeleka komphakathi , ukurhweba- nokobana kungenziwani bunjani ngendlela ehlelekileko . Hlola imisebenzi ye-CBP uyimadanise naleyo ephakanyiswe ku-IDP ukwenzela bonyana ukwazi ukutjho bonyana imumethe okufanako nanyana njani . Nanyana ingakamumathi okufanako , kodwana kungabayinto ekghonakalako nefaneleko bonyana kuvakatjhelwe ngokunqophileko abanye abasekeli ngeemali . Zijayeze ngalokhu ozokutjho ngaphambi kwesikhathi - umndenakho namtjhana abangani namtjhana abalingani balaleli ongazijayeza kibo . Tlama ikhambo leenyawo elingakahleleli kuhle ewadini elifaka hlangana amaphuzu aqakathekileko wendawo . Lokha nawukhamba ngeenyawo , yelela amatshwayo aqakathekileko nokobana enzeka kuphi . Kuyasiza ukuthatha ilwazeli ulibeke esithombeni esibumuda utjengise amanye namanye amatshwayo aphathelene nokwephasi nanyana iindaba ezithuthukisako kinanyana ngisiphi seemphande , bese ngemva kwalokho unikele ubujamo ewadini ngendlela isibonelo esingaphasi ezokubonisa ngayo . Sebenzisa irherho lokuhlola lebhduluko ukuqinisekisa bonyana woke amaphuzu afakiwe . Umsebenzi katitjhere . Iimphakamiso zethu zifaka hlangana ibandulo , umrholo , iinhlohlomezelo , isikhathi somsebenzi , isilinganiso somsebenzi , kanye nesekelo lokumunyethweko nokufundisa . Amazinga aphezulu weenkambisolawulo zebizelomsebenzi kanye nemibandela ekhuphula ukuziphatha ngendlela etjengisa ukuhlonipha ibizelomsebenzi kufanele yakhiwe ngobutjha . Lokhu kutjho bonyana ukuthuthukiswa kwebizelomsebenzi , ukubuyekezwa kwabalingani ngesikhundla , imithangalasisekelo yeenkolo , ukunikelwa kwabafundi amamatheriyali wokubasekela kanye namarherho wokusekela abotitjhere kufanele aqiniswe . Abotitjhere , ngamunye begodu ezingeni lesikolo , kufanele babe nokuziphendulela mayelana nomsebenzi womfundi , ngokwamukela ibhoduluko lokufunda . Idayagramu elandelako itjengisa bona imiphumela yesigaba yesigaba selawulo lephrojekthi ifike bunjani ezenzekweni zokobana zihlolwe godu nokobana umzombe awukaqondi ngokwemvelo . I-Masincedana Development Coiporation yahlonywa njengekhamphanini yesiGaba sama-21 . Beyinqophe ukubuthelela begodu nokuphathwa Kweemali begodu nokwenza amaqhinga we-LED ngokwesiqunto . Ngokulandela umlandelande weemfundobandulo , umphakathi wakhomba amaqhinga aphathekako iMasincedane engakwazi ukulandelela . Elinye nelinye ilunga lomphakathi livunyelwe ukubeka iingcenye ezintathu ngokuzinqophanisa nomphumela omunye nomunye owodwa nanyana engaphezulu . Umnyombo womThethosisekelo yiVikelomalungelo . Ivikelomalungelo isekela amalungelo wazo zoke izakhamuzi nabahlali ukobana baphathwe ngokulinganako begodu baphathwe ngesithunzi kungaqalwa umbalabo , ubulili , ubunjinga nanyana iinkhundla zabo . inani lamalungelo wehlalakuhle nomnotho ivikeliwe kuVikelomalungelo , okufana nelungelo lokuhlala ebhodulukweni elinepilo , ukufikelela ekutholeni izindlu ezifaneleko , ukufikelela imisebenzi yetlhogomelo lezamaphilo nokudla okwaneleko kanye namanzi . Kumsebenzi karhulumende wendawo , kanye neminye imikhakha karhulumende , ' ukuhlonipha , ukuvikela , ukuthuthukisa nokwenza bona amalungelo la asebenze ' . I-CBP ilihlanganyelo lomphakathi , umasipala namakhansela . Abakghonakalisi be-CBP kufuze basebenze begodu batlame namakhansela malungana negadango elinye nelinye lendlelakambiso . Nangabe iYunivesithi yeTshwane inqophe ukunikela ngemfundaze lapha abafundi abavela ePumalanga Kapa neGauteng bangaphalisana khona , ukungalingani ngekhe kwabazamela abafundi abavela ePumalanga Kapa . Isibonelo , akusibo boke abakhuluma isitayela sesiNgisi esifanako , namkha abanekghono elifanako lokufumana iindlela zokuthintana . Khuyini ihlanganyelo lemisebenzi kamasipala ? URhulumende weKhaya : UmThetho wamaReyiti wePahla kaMasipala , we-2004 unikela ilwazi lokuthelisa ipahla bomasipala boke begodu nokuthinta iimpahla ezatjhiywa ngaphandle komkhawulo kamasipala phambilini . Kuqakathekile kibomasipala bona bazi lapho kutholakala khona ilwazeli njengobana amareyiti wepahla zizinto ezivame ukuphakanyiswa bahlali . Inengi lemisebenzi ekhonjwe nabegade kwenziwa i-CBP liphunyeleliswa maKomidi weWadi , kodwana eminye ingafuna iinsetjenziswa ezinengi ezivela ngaphandle nanyana ingeziwa ngepumelelo kumasipala kwaphela . Lokho kufaka hlangana ukuthatha isiqunto malungana nomuntu ekufuze abe nesibopho sephrojekthi begodu enze amalungiselelo wokufumana iinsetjenziswa zokuphumelelisa . Lokha nasele umtlamo ukhona , kuqakathekileko bonyana kube nendlelakambiso yokutjheja , yokulinganisa kanye nokubuyekeza umtlamo . Imitlamo kufuze ibuyekezwe emhlanganweni omunye nomunye weKomidi yeWadi begodu qobe nyanga nanyana ngeenyanga ezimbili kufuze ubuyekezwe emhlanganweni womphakathi newadi / nesiyingi / nomasipala . AmaKomidi weWadi kufuze abike ngetuthuko esele yenziwe begodu ahlathulule ngokuzeleko imiraro eminye neminye evelileko . Lemibiko kufuze ifake hlangana ingcenye yeemali enikela yoke imininingwana yeemali ezisetjenzisiweko . Umkhandlu kumele wenze ngcono ibhajedi ngaphambi kobana kuthome umnyaka omutjha weemali , emva kokutlama okufaneleko begodu nokubonisana namaKomidi weWadi begodu nezinye iinqhema zababambisani endaweni le . AmaKomidi wamaWadi aqakathekile ekugegisweni kwebhajedi emphakathini begodu nokukghonakaliswa kombiko obuyako ovela emphakathini oya kwamasipala . Nangabe amaKomidi wamaWadi ayabandakanyeka ekuquntweni bonyana yimalini okumele umasipala ayisebenzise begodu kumaphi amaphrojekthi , lokhu kungatjho bonyana amawadabo azakuzuza bunqopha . Kunekghonokalo yokobana ukukhula komnotho wephasi eminyakeni elitjhumi ezako kuzokuba phasi kunangendlela ebegade kungayo eminyakeni elitjhumi egadungileko . Lokhu kuzokutlhogeka ukuqalisiswa khudlwana komgomo , ukuphunyeleliswa kwemigomo yamabubulo ngendlela efaneleko kanye nokuthuthukiswa kwamakghono okwenziwe ngcono . Ubujamo obuhle bomzimba nanyana bengqondo yomuntu buqakathekile mayelana nepilo enemiphumela emihle begodu eyanelisako . UmBiko wokuHlahluba utjengisa iintjhijilo ezihlobene khulu ezibangelwa lirherho elifadalalako lezamaphilo kanye nobudisi bokwanda kwamalwele . Irherho lezamaphilo womphakathi elonakeleko leSewula Afrika kufanele lilungiswe . Nanyana ukusetjenziswa khudlwana kwetjhejo lezamaphilo lekoro yangeqadi , elibhadalwa basebenzisi balo nanyana elibhadalwa yitjhorensi yezamaphilo , kuyingcenye yesisombululo , kodwana lokho akujamiseleli ukwenziwa ngcono kwetjhejo lezamaphilo womphakathi . Kufuneka umzamo opheleleko wokwenza ngcono ikhwalithi yetjhejo , khulukhulu ezingeni eliphasi . Qinisekisa bonyana imibono yomphakathi iyezwakala . Indima edlalwa yiKomidi yeWadi kuqinisekisa bona labo abanesibopho sokutlama iphrojekthi babandakanya umphakathi begodu baqinisekisa bona umphakathi uhlanganyela ngokuzeleko ephrojekthini . UkuZwisisa nokuLungisa - umnqopho wesigabesi kukwenza ithuba leenqhema zoke ezibandakanyekako bona ' zizwiwe ' begodu zivunyelwe ukutjho indabazo . Omunye nomunye umuntu unethuba lokuhlathulula ubujamo bakhe . Emva kobana isiqhema sihlathulule ubujamo baso umlamuli urhunyeza amaphuzu bese uhlola neenqhema bona uzwile lokhu abakutjhwileko . Iinqhema bese zivumelana ngeendaba ekufanele zirarululwe bese zenza ibhoduluko elizokuba lihle ekurarululeni umraro . Lokhu kungadinga bonyana abakghonakalisi be-CBP babambe imihlangano embalwa nomasipala ntangi ukwenzela bonyana bakwazi ukuvumelana nokukhulumisana ngelwazi elingaphezulu . Bobani abamphakathi wethu begodu basebenzisa ziphi iindlela zokuziphilisa ? ' Abakghonakalisi ' kufuze bafumane ilwazeli esiqhemeni sabo bese bayalirekhoda . Isiqhema kufuze sihlathulule isiqhema saso , begodu sitjheje inani lamalunga wesiqhema saso , siqale bonyana ayasebenza nokobana asebenza msebenzi bani , nangabe akasebenzi siqale bonyana mangaki angasebenziko , kufuze siqale nebunjo lesiqhema eliphathelene nobuzwe . UMSEBENZI KARHULUMENDE KUKWENZA LOKHU : ' kukwakha imisebenzi yomphakathi emayelana nabantu begodu elethwa babantu , etjengiswa kulingana , ikhwalithi , ukwenziwa ngesikhathi nemithetho yokuziphatha enamandla , ukuhlelwa kuhle nokwenzelwa imisebenzi emihle esezingeni eliphezulu ' . Izakhamuzi zinesibopho sokudosa abarholi ngendlebe bonyana bangathathi iinqunto ezingazisiko , ezineboneloduze nekunqotjhwe ngazo ukuphumelelisa iimfiso neenrhuluphelo ezincani . Ukucocisana ngokudephileko komphakathi kanye nesiko lokuveza iinghonghoyilo ngendlela enokuthula kuzakusiza ekuzwisiseni khudlwana iintjhijilo imiphakathi eqalene nazo begodu lokho kuzakuqinisa ukuziphendulela kweenkhulu ezikhethiweko . Isibonelo , Nangabe imiphumela yokufunda esikolweni ingaphasi kwaleyo ezwakalako elindelwe miphakathi , umphakathi ungasiza ukulungisa ubujamo ngokuqinisa ukulawulwa kweenkolo , ngokuqinisa bonyana abafundi nabotitjhere bafika ngesikhathi , nangokuqinisa bonyana izakhiwo ezisekelako zeenkhulu zombuso zisebenza ngepumelelo . Kukwenza iimpilo zabomma zibe lula . Iindimabo ekhiqizako ibanikela itshwenyo elikhulu . Ngokutjheja amaphrojekthi akhuluma ngokutjhejwa kwabentwana , itjhejo lezepilo elifumanekako , ukufumaneka kwamanzi negezi begodu neenthuthi zomphakathi ezinekghono , netorho lomsebenzi ukutlhlogomela umndeni begodu umndeni ungehliswa ube mncani . Umsebenzi 3 Qala kumThethosisekelo , begodu utjengise indima kanye nomsebenzi wakarhulemende welizweloke . Ukwenza ngcono amandla weembaseli zokukhambisa umsebenzi wokwemba emayini kanye namaminerali ngamaphesende ali-15 ungakafiki umnyaka wee-2030 . Lokhu kufaka hlangana ukuvalwa kwamaziko amanengi angasebenzisi amandla weembaseli ngendlela enekghono . Abahlanganyeli bathalela amagama-mmongo wesitatimende esinye nesinye saleziintatimende , isib . malungana nomrholo owenziwe ngcono - igama-mmongo elingathalelwa ngelithi ' umrholo ' , malungana nobulelesi kungaba ngelithi ' phephileko nelithi vikelekileko ' bese bawatlola efliphutjhadini . Ukwakha ngobutjha amadorobha amakhulu weSewula Afrika , amadorobha amancani neendawo zemakhaya zokuhlaliswa kwabantu kuyiphrojekthi ebudisi nezokuthatha isikhathi eside , edinga ukubuyekezwa okukhulu kwemithetho netjisakalo yepolotiki . Kodwana kuyiphrojekthi etlhogekako lokha nasiqala iindleko ezikulu zehlalakuhle , zebhoduluko neemali ezibangelwe kuhlukaniswa kwabantu ngokweendawo zokuhlala . Ukuphepha nokuvikeleka komphakathi kutlhoga itjhebiswano nephiko labavikela indawo begodu lilawulwa kukobana umphakathi usizane ukobana urarulule imiraro yevikeleko lamalunga womphakathi . Ukulawulwa kokwenziwa komsebenzi kutjhidelene eduze nokwethulwa kweensetjenziswa , kokubili kuhlathululeka kuhle ngeqhinga leBatho Pele elethulwa ngonyaka we-1997 . Khulukhulu , abantu abatjha kufanele bafumane amathuba angcono wezefundo nomnotho , begodu kutlhogeka imizamo enqophileko yokuphelisa ukungalingani ngokobulili . Ukuthuthukisa ukulingana ngokobulili namathuba angezelelweko wabantu abatjha kumimongo ehlanganisiweko netholakala kiwo woke umtlamo lo . Abosopolitiki banesibopho sokuqinisekisa ukwenziwa kwelandelela nokuphunyeleliswa kwemitlamo begodu ukuzibophelela kwabo ekambisweni kuqakathekile . Ngebanga lalokho , ukuhlanganyela kwabo kuqakathekile . UmThetho wamaHlelo waboMasipala unqophe kumahlelo wangaphakathi kanye nokuphathwa kwakamasipala . Kungani kumele amaKomidi weWadi akuzwisise bekayisebenzise ikambiso le ? OMUNYE NOMUNYE UMASIPALA UFUNEKA NGOKOMTHETHO ATHUTHUKISE IRHERHO LOKUPHATHWA KOKWENZIWA KOMSEBENZI ( I-PMS ) OKUZAKWENZA NGCONO UKUZIPHENDULELA NOKUPHUMELELA NGOKWEHLANGANO KOKUSETJENZISWA KWEENTLABAGELO ZAKAMASIPALA NOKUTJENGISA IPUMELELO YEMIPHUMELA . I-PMS GODU IYAKGHONA UKUVEZA ISIYELELISO SAMSINYA NJENGOBANA ITJENGISA UKUNGASEBENZI NOFANA UKUSEBENZA OKUNGANELISIKO , BESE IVUMELA UKUNGENELWA PHAKATHI KWETUTHUKO . Boke abomasipala kulindeleke kobana balungise umTlamo oHlanganiswe ngokuZeleko ( i-IDP ) . I-IDP ibeka ekufuze kuthonywe ngakho endaweni . I-IDP isetjenziswa esikhathini esiminyaka emihlanu bese ubuyekezwa qobe mnyaka . UmThetho wePhahla lobuDlelwana kaRhulumende wangaPhakathi , we-2005 wenzelwe ukuthuthukisa nokukghonakalisa ukuzwana kokuthathwa kwesiqundo hlangana neenkhundla ezintathu zakarhulumende ukuze imithetholawulo nemisebenzi kizo zoke iinkhundla igcugcuzele ukwethulwa kweensetjenziswa bese kutholakala iindlela zokuhlangabezana neendingo zabahlali ngendlela etshwayelekileko . Iinkhundla ezintathu zakarhulumende zibotjhelelwa Mthethosisekelo ukuzwananisa nokukhulumisana ngeendlela zokuvumelana ngokuphatha , iindaba zezepolotiki nezeemali . Qala incwajana Working Together for Development . Nikela abonobangela bokutjhejula imisebenzi ngendlela owenze ngayo bese utjengisa lokhu ngendlela yetjhejuli , yetjhadi lebha namtjhana ngokunikela iimbonelo . Ukwakha ikambiso yokuthutha ipahla phakathi kweThekwini ne-Gauteng , kufaka hlangana isitetjhi semikhumbi esenjiwe kuhle ebaleni ledoyelo leemphaphamtjhini elidala leThekwini . Lokha umtlamo womphakathi nawuzakuba yipumelelo , kudingeka bonyana kufakwe boke ababambisani ekambisweni yokutlama . Nanyana kungeze kwakghonakala bonyana umphakathi ungahlanganyele i-100% , kodwana kuqakathekileko ukuqinisekisa bonyana kubandakanywa zoke iinqhema eziqakathekileko zehlalakuhle nezinekareko emphakathini . Akukafaneli bonyana kuhlanganyele abarholi bendawo kwaphela nanyana labo abavamise ukukhambela nanyana ukuphatha imihlangano yomphakathi . I-CBP itjho bonyana kufuze kwenziwe imizamo yokufikelela nakilabo abasemphakathini abangadlali indima ebonakalako . Idinga isikhathi , umzamo nokuzibophelela . Umtlamo womphakathi kufuze urholele esenzweni esibandakanya imiphakathi ngokwayo , ngokuhlanganyela nabomasipala . Umsebenzi 2 Qala kumThethosisekelo , begodu kanye nomsebenzi wakarhulumende wesifunda netjhebiswano lawo kurhulumende wekhaya . Ukukhuthwa kwencwadi nokwabiwa kwelwazi lerhubhululo kumele kutlanywe ngokutjhejisisa ukusukela esigabeni sokutlama iphrojekthi . Isahlukwesi siqale eemfunekweni ze-PMS begodu sihlathulula iinKomba eziQakathekileko zokwEnziwa komSebenzi ( KPI ) ngokuzeleko , nokobana kuhlaliswa begodu kwenziwa bunjani ama-KPI nokobana kukhethwa bekulinganiswa bunjani ukwenza . Sibuye sihlathulule indima eqakathekileko edlalwa miphakathi , amaKomidi weWadi ekubuyekezweni kokwenziwa nekambiso yokuhlola ukwenza . Kunemihlobo eyahlukahlukeneko yokuphathwa kwamaphrojekthi esetjenziswako esigabeni sokuthuthukisa . Amaphrojekthi la angehluka kumamodlhela asetjenziswa emaphasini wezerhwebo . Ebujameni beSewula Afrika ayikho imodlhela esezingeni esigabeni somphakathi begodu kuzokuba nemehluko nahlangana kwamamodlhela asetjenziswa kweminye iminyango yakarhulumende / yombuso . Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi kumele azijayeze ngomzombe wokuphathwa kwephrojekthi njengombana le kuyimodlhela esetjenziswa kanengi . Ukwehlukaniswa kanye namabizo weengaba zomzombe wephrojekthi zingehluka kuye ngokuphakelwa kweemali yi-ofisi nanyana mnyango karhulumende / wombuso . Khetha indlela engcono yokwethula ilwazi . Ungafuna ukulitlola etjhadini , namtjhana abahlanganyeli bahlanganyele nawe ngokuphakamisa izandla kutlolwe amaphuzu aqakathekileko . Ikhansela lekhaya lingakusiza ngokwenza amakhophi . Esahlukweni lesi siqala iindlela ezivamileko ezisetjenziswako , indlela yokurarulula umraro . UMSEBENZI 1 AmaKomidi wamaWadi angawurherha njani umTlamo weLizwe wokuThuthukisa iiNdawo ? ISAHLUKWESI SINQOPHE BONA AMAPHROJEKTHI AKHONJWA BUNJANI hlangana nomasipala namtjhana yiKomidi yeWadi . Izokuba mphumela esivumelwaneni sokuraga ngephrojekthi , namtjhana kungatholakala bona iphrojekthi ayikghonakali begodu angeze yenziwe . Ukukhonjwa kwephrojekthi , amarhubhululopumelelo , ukucozululwa kwemiraro nabambambisani koke kumatshwayo walesisiteji . Abahlanganyeli babeka amadayagramabo begodu namaphephabo alengiswako phezulu emaqadi woke wekamuru . Mema abahlanganyeli bonyana bazokuqala , amadayagramu begodu namaphepha alengiswako . Khetha yinye yamadayagramu begodu umeme nesiqhema ukwenzela bonyana usihlathululele ngokuzeleko ngomnqopho womtlamo . AmaKomidi weWadi angasebenzisa isibonelwesi bona sibasize ekulinganiseni ukwenza kwakamasipalabo . Ihlanganyelo yomphakathi embusweni yingcenye eyisisekelo kwakuyinamtjhana ngiyiphi idemokhrasi . Lokhu kutjengiswe kumThethosisekelo , isiGaba 152 esithi umphakathi kufuze uzibandakanye eendabeni zombuso wekhaya , ikhomba bona omunye weminqopho yombuso wekhaya " kugcugcuzela ukuzibandakanya kwemiphakathi neenhlangano zomphakathi eendabeni zombuso wekhaya " . Indlela yekambiso ye-CBP kuyo yoke indawo kamasipala kufanele ngokwemibandela yokuphelela kweemfanelo ezifunekako yenzeke ngaphambi kwegadango lokuthoma lomtlamo we-IDP begodu nendlela yekambiso yayo yokubuyekeza . UmThetho kaMasipala wemiKhawulo we-1998 ubeke iinkambiso neendlela zokulinganisa imikhawulo kamasipala . IBhodo yemiKhawulo njengomthetho ozijameleko ubeke ukwenza lo msebenzi . Nakulinganiswa ngemikhawulo , iBhodo izokutjheja abonobangela abanengi abafaka hlangana ukukghonakala kweemali kwendawo , ukuhlanganisa kwamaphiko wobuhlanga nokuhlela ngokunqophisa namaphiko kamasipala lokha nakwenziwa isiqundo sokulinganisa umkhawulo kamasipala . Abantu bahlanganyela ngokukhulumisana nangokuphendula imibuzo . Abasebenzeli bangaphandle bahlathulula imiraro kanye neendlelakambiso zokubuthelela ilwazi , begodu ngokunjalo balawula icozululo . Indlelakambiso enjalo yokukhulumisana ayivumi bonyana kube nokwabelana ekuthatheni iinqunto , begodu akukakateleleki bonyana amaphrofetjhinali amukele imibono yabantu . Ukutlama : Izakhamuzi , ama-NGO , ama-CBO neenhlangano zepolitiki ziyasebenzisana ukuthuthukisa isibawo sesiphakamiso ukobana umkhandlu usiqale , kanye nokukhuthaza umasipala ukobana usebenzise amakghono akhona ekusebenziseni umthangalsisekelo , nokusekela amatjhebiswano neenhlangano ezisemiphakathini okungenzeka zibe namakghono wokukghonakalisa amahlelo athuthukiswako . Nanyana ngimuphi umsebenzi othintana nezeemali kumele uhlathululwe begodu uphasiswe ebhajedini . Nanyana ngisiphi isiqunto seemali esinesithintela seendleko namkha sengenisomali kumele siqinisekiswe . Ukuzibophelela kuyakhambisana nesibopho eenquntweni ezenziweko . Imisebenzi emunyethweko neendlela zokwenza ezisetjenziswako zizakuba ngezifaneleko begodu zihlangabeze iindingo zabobaba nabomma yini , ngaphandle kobuzwe bazo , ikolo nesendlalelo sezomnotho na ? Ingabe amahlelo la ayaphumelela ? Ekupheleni kwalomhlangano osemthethweni , abahlanganyeli kufuze khibe sebalungise isirhunyezo samaphrojekthi / semisebenzi abafuna ukusethula ukwenzela bonyana umasipala nanyana abanye abanikeli ngemisebenzi bakwazi ukusisekela ngeemali , begodu basifake naku-IDP . Soloko kwangomnyaka ka-1994 uRhulumende wenze imigomo namaphahla afuna ukuthuthukisa ukubusa ngokuhlanganyela . Iphahleli livezwe kuhle emfanekisweni ongenzasi . I-PMS ibeka iinkombiso zokwenza umsebenzi begodu yenza bonyana urhulumende wemakhaya nezakhamuzi zikghone ukulinganisa ipumelelo ukuphikisana neentjengiso lezi . Lapho itjengisa khona ukungasebenzi , ikghonakalisa ukungenelela phakathi okufunekako . Ifaka hlangana neengaba zokuhlela , ilandelelo nombiko obuyako begodu neembuyekezo zokusebenza konyaka nonyaka . Yenza amalunga womkhandlu aziphendulele ukulwisana nobukhohlakali namkha nokumoroswa kweemali zakamasipala . Nanyana abomma bavame ukuba yingcenye yomphakathi ebandlululwa ngokweqileko , ukubonokhu , kwehlela thina soke esikubona njengokuhlukileko ' namkha ' okungafani nathi ' . Khuyini okuwumehluko emasinariyweni ? Ingcenye le yebhajedi ingilokhu umasipala azakusisa ekuthuthukisweni kwezinto ezitja eziphathekako , umthangalasisekelo namkha amanye amafa amakhulu afana nokwakhiwa kweendlela nezindlu . Amaphrojekthi la angatathwa njengamaphrojekthi amakhulu . Urhulumende wekhaya kumele azi bonyana iimali ezifakwe ebhanga zizakuba yimalini unyaka nonyaka begodu nokuthi zizakubuyaphi . Zenze bonyana umbuso , amabhizinisi nabo boke abarholi emphakathini baziphendulele malungana nezenzo zabo . Amaziko anamakghono kanye namakghonofundwa anjengePhiko lomVikeli womPhakathi kanye nePhiko eliPhenya ngobuLelesi obuKhethekileko kufanele asizwe ngeemali ezaneleko kanye nabasebenzi abalingeneko begodu angacajelwa babantu abangaphandle . Ukuze ube mthintanisi othintanisa ngokwepumelelo kufanele utjheje indlela okhuluma ngayo . Ukuhlela ama-KPI uwahlelela iminqopho ebekwe yi-IDP ( isib . Ukunikela abaninimizi abazi-10 0 ngesoritjhi emnyakeni weemali ozako ) ukutjheja begodu nokulinganiswa kokwenziwa kwemisebenzi . Ungathikamezi , lisa okhulumako aqede ukutjho imibonwakhe ngokuzeleko . Indlela enzinze emandleni - lokhu kukulokha isiqhema sisebenzisa isikhundla saso segunya ukuzama nokukatelela imbangi bona yenze ngendlela ethile . Lendlela yeyame emandleni namtjhana ekukateleleni ukufuna umphumela . Isibonelo , abonogada babopha abatjengisi abavimbe indlela , namtjhana umuntu osemthethweni emsebenzini wenza isiqunto abanye beensebenzi abangasithandiko kodwana bayahluleka ukutjho imibonwabo ngonobangela wesikhundla esikhulu somuntu owenza isiqunto . Izenzeko ezivamileko zendlela enzinze emandleni zingafaka hlangana ukunghala , iintrayigi , ukutjengisa , ukulwa kwemasi , ukusetjenziswa komrhatjho ukulwa nembangi , ipi . Lokhu kusisa ebujameni BOKUTHUMBA / BOKULOBA . Ngiwaphi amalanga wokugcina abekelwe ukuqedelela imisebenzi ? Umsebenzi wokuthoma uvumelanisa imiphumela emihlanu eqakatheke kwamanikelela , begodu uyaqinisekisa bonyana loke ilwazi lokutlama lirekhodwe ngendlela efaneleko . Umtlamo lo uphakamisa iqhinga labasebenzi boke elimahlangothi-mathathu elibandakanya iqhinga lokubandula lesikhathi eside , imiphumela engconywana yekoro yefundo ephakemeko kanye nokwabiwa kwemithombo etlhogekako . Ukujanyelwa ngokobujamo bephasi kufuze kutjhejwe ukuqinisekisa bonyana ikambiso ihlanganisa imiphakathi ikwazi ukubumbana . Imihlangano yokuhloma neyokunikela imibiko ebuyako kufuneka bonyana ibanjelwe endaweni engaphezu kweyodwa ukwenzela bonyana kufunyanwe boke abantu . Ukubumbanisa woke amaSewula Afrika ukobana ahlanganyele ehlelweni elilodwa lokufumana ipumelelo nokulingana . Ezinye izinto zisiwa emakomidini wephothifoliyo womkhandlu ukuze kwenziwe ikulumiswano eragela phambili neemphakamiso . Qedelela ngokuhlathulula ngokuzeleko imiNqopho yokuThuthukisa yeMileniyamu nokobana abomasipala bendawo , kanye nomphakathi , kufuze bazifumane bunjani iindlela zokusebenza ukuze bahlangabezane naleminqopho . Kilesi sigaba sokuthoma ukuba semthethweni nokuvunyelwa komphakathi makomidi wamawadi kungaba mraro ngesimanga sokukhetha okunganamandla neendlela zemibiko ebuyako . Isibonelo ilunga lingaba sekomidini ngombana libuya ephikweni lezekolo , kodwana kungenzeka lingabi nokuhlangana kuhle nezinye iinkolo zamanye amasondo . Umuntu lo angeze abonwa njengomjameli wephiko lezekolo nangabe abatjheji itjhebiswano lokuziphendulela ephikwenelo . Umzamo wethu wokwakha isitjhaba ube budisi khulu eenkhathini zokutjhitjhiriza kwezinga lokukhula komnotho . ISewula Afrika angeze yavumela ukwehla komnotho okukhuphula ukutjhuba kommoya womphakathi . Kutlhogeka uburholi obuqinileko ukugcugcuzela umbono womThethosisekelo . Isivumelwano esihlelekileko somphakathi singasiza ukuqinisa inqophiso phakathi kokukhula , ituthuko nokwakha isitjhaba , begodu lokho kungakha umzombetuthuko . Indlela yokusebenza kwe-IDP ibonelela ngokuhlanganyela njengengcenye yekambiso yokutlama ngokusebenzisa izakhiwo ezinqophileko . Lokhu kufaka hlangana iForamu yabaJameli , iinhlangano zemisebenzi yamaphrojekthi kanye nezehlakalo zamaqhinga . Begodu umThetho uyihlathulula ngokucacileko ifuneko yokukhulumisana ezingeni lewadi . Iyiveza ngokunqophileko ifuneko yokufaka isandla komphakathi emitlameni eyenziwako kanye nokuveza amazizo mayelana nokusebenza kukamasipala . Ukutjheja ukuhlanganyela kweenqhema okusisenzo serhubhululo elenziwa ngokubambisana nama-NGO kanye nama-CBO kungangenisa ilwazi elizeleko elimayelana neendingo ezinengi ezihlukeneko mayelana neendingo ezithileko kanye nobungako . Ngokunabileko , ukusebenzisana nephasi loke kutjho ukukhuphuka kwezinga lokurhwebelana nephasi loke nokukhamba ngokukhululeka kwabantu okungeziweko , ukusiselana ngokukhululeka , ukubonisana kanye nokurhwebelana ngetheknoloji neenarha ezinye eminyakeni ematjhumitjhumi egadungileko . Amatjhuguluko la asekele ukuthuthuka kweenarha ezitlhagako kanye nalezo ezifumana ingeniso ephakathi , begodu lokho kuzenze zakghona ukufumana amamakethe , ipahla , imisebenzi , itheknoloji kanye namakghono . Begodu ukusebenzisana nephasi loke kusize khulu mayelana " nobudlelwano " obukhulako obuphungule iinqabo zokungena eenarheni ezinye begodu banabisa nokufumaneka kwelwazi . Esikhathini esiphakathesi , iSewula Afrika kufanele ithathe igadango mayelana netjhugulukweli ngokusekela ukukhiqizwa nokuthengiswa kwepahla kanye nokusisa emabubulweni afumana ingeniso ephezulu begodu nangokungezelela inani lezenjiwa ezithengiselwa amanye amazwe . Esikhathini eside esizako , kufanele bonyana iSewula Afrika isebenze ngconywana ekukhuphuleni izinga lokukhiqizwa nokuthengiswa kwepahla emikhakheni ezakwazi ukuqatjha abantu abanengi . Ngokwenza ngcono isakhelo samakghono nangokungezelela ukukhiqizwa nokuthengiswa kwepahla , irherho lezomnotho lingakghona ukuhluka , begodu lokho kungaletha ukulingana phakathi kweentengo zepahla yokurhwebelana eziphezulu kanye neranda . Ukuzibandakanya ecaleni lebhajedi ehlangothini lomphakathi . Amacala webhajedi aqinisekisa bona iimfuneko ze-MFMA ziyahlangatjezwa ngokuya ngokokuhlanganyela komphakathi ekambisweni yebhajedi . Amacala webhajedi kamasipala avumela amaKomidi weWadi ukuhlanganyela ekuthuthukisweni kwebhajedi kamasipala . Ukunikela amandla wamakghono emalungeni wekomidi yeWadi ukwenzela bonyana bakwazi ukusebenza njengeengorho zokuthuthukiswa kwekhaya begodu bakwazi nokusebenzisana na bo begodu nokuthuthukissa umphakathi ngobubanzi . Iindlela zekambiso ze-IDP ne-CBP nemiphumela zakhelwa phezu kokuthize , zimzombe begodu ziyazibuyekeza . Ilwazi elimunyethwe yi-IDP le ekhona kumele lisetjenziswe ukuhlahla indlela yekambiso ye-CBP ngesikhathi imiphumela ye-CBP izabe ihlahla indlela yokubuyekeza i-IDP yomnyaka ozako . Itsengo lobulili lenziwa begodu lawurarulula umraro . Kwaba sepepeneneni bonyana abomma babalimi , banokuncani banokuncani abangakutjho emndenini namkha emphakathini . Ukuboleka abomma imali , ukusekelwa kwemisebenzi namaforomu wokuthatha iinqunto ezihlanganyelweko zabekwa begodu yayisetjenziselwa yayisetjenziselwa ukutjhugulula abalimi abachakileko abangakwaziko ukuphumelela babe ngilabo abakhiqizako . Ezinye iindawo zokumeda kungaba kuthintana , itjhebiswano nomkhandlu , nanyana iindawo zomsebenzi ohlelwa yikomidi yewadi ezihlelela wona ukwenza isiqiniseko sokobana amalungayo enza iimbopho zawo njengombana kutjho umthetjhwana omayelana nokubandakanyeka komphakathi . Abantu bahlanganyela ekwenzeni icozululo ngokuhlanganyela , ekwakhiweni kwemitlamo yokusebenza kanye nekubumbeni nanyana ekuqiniseni iinhlangano zekhaya . Lendlelakambiso ibandakanya iindlela zokusebenza eziphathelene nemikhakha eyahlukeneko yelwazi ezidinga imibono eminengi nezisebenzisa iindlelakambiso zokufunda ezihlelekileko nezijanyisiweko . Njengombana iinqhema zithatha iinqunto zendawo begodu zitjho nokobana imithombo yesizo ekhona isetjenziswa bunjani , ngalokho kutjho bonyana zinesabelo ekugcineni izakhiwo nanyana izenzo ezinjalo . Ukwakha iimvumelwano zebhoduluko zokufakwa kwabantu eendaweni zokuhlala ngomnqopho wokuhlanganisa umphakathi , ikoro yamabhizinisi nombuso ekurarululeni imiraro . ISAHLUKWESI SIHLATHULULA INDIMA EDLALWA MAKOMIDI WEWADI kanye namanye amalunga womphakathi emtlameni womphakathi . IsAhluko 1 sihlathulule ngokuzeleko bonyana umtlamo womphakathi kufuze ulungiswe babantu bendawo leyo malungana newadi labo , kufuze ube ngewomphakathi begodu kufuze uqinisekise bonyana umphakathi uhlanganyela ngokukhuthala ekuwuphumeleliseni . IKomidi yeWadi idlala indima eqakathekileko ekuqinisekiseni nekufumaneni ukuhlanganyela komphakthi . Ukusebenza komuntu ngamunye , iinqhema nabalingani abanetjhebiswano bomPhakathi waNgasese osiza bona kuzuzwe amaqhinga weminqopho yomnyango nanyana umasipala kufanele abekwe ilihlo ukuqinisekisa bona wenza imisebenzi esezingeni eliphezulu . Ukusebenza komuntu ngamunye kuzakuhlolwa ngokukhambisana nekambiso yokuphatha ukwenziwa komsebenzi eyenziwe ngumasipalabo . Ukuzihlola komuntu ngokwakhe nokuhlolwa mngani kuziinsetjenziswa esisetjenziswako nakuhlolwa umuntu ngamunye . Ukutlama iinsetjenziswa : Ukulinganisa bona ngiziphi iinsetjenziswa ( abantu , isisetjenziswa , amamatheriyali ) nokobana ngasinye kuzokudingeka bona sibe ngangani ukwenzela bona sikwazi ukwenza imisebenzi yephrojekthi . I-CBP ihloma indlelakambiso ehlanganyelweko ukwenzela bonyana ikwazi ukuthola imifakela yomphakathi kanye nokutlama ngokutjheja khulu iindaba zabantu abajayelekileko emphakathini nokuqala bonyana ilwazeli ungalihlobanisa bunjani nendlelambono enabileko yomtlamo kamasipala . Lokhu okungaphasi sibonelo samaphuzu aqakathekileko najayelekileko womtlamo wewadi begodu nokufaneleka kwawo ekusetjenzisweni ku-IDP . Hlathululani imikhakha emithathu ( 3 ) yakamasipala bese nibuza abahlanganyeli kobana batjho bonyana umasipala abahlala kuye ungena kuphi . Basizeni nabanganasiqiniseko . Imisebenzi yombuso kufanele bonyana inabe , begodu kufanele kuqalwe khudlwana ilutjha nabomma . Kulindeleke bonyana imisebenzi yombuso inikele ukulingana kweengidi ezimbili zemisebenzi yeenkhathi zoke ungakafiki umnyaka wee-2020 . Imiphakathi , iinhlangano kanye nabantu bahlanganyela ngeenzathu ezahlukeneko begodu baletha amakghono namalemuko angasiza kilokhu . Ithebula elisekhasini lama-21 lendlala umhlobo wokuhlanganyela nalokho okubandakanyekako . Ukuhlobanisa imiphumela ye-CBP neye-IDP kuyindlelakambiso ezombelezako . Kudingeka bonyana umzombe wemisebenzi owendlalwe ku-CBP ukhambelane nomzombe we-IDP . Lokhu kuqakathekile ngombana i-CBP ilinga ukuqinisekisa bonyana iindingo zomphakathi ziyakhonjwa begodu zifakwa ku-IDP . Njengombana i-IDP yenzelwe ukuveza amatjhejontangi womphakathi , lokha nangabe lemizombe ayikhambelani , imiphakathi ingagcina sele idanile begodu ingasanathemba malungana nendlela yokutlama esetjenziswa yi-CBP . Umasipala angajamisa ituthuko yehlanganiso yombambisani lapho bangaletha abantu kuma-CBO nama-NGO ; abosorhwebo bekhaya ; Ama-SMME , zokulima njll . Ihlangniso le ingaluleka umasipala ekuthuthukisweni komnotho wekhaya kanye neendaba ze-IDP . Irherho lehlanganyela yombambisani lizokuzalisa iqhinga lomhlanganyeli elihlangana nomasipala ; lijulise ubuhlanganyeli bedemokhrasi begodu bukhulise inani labantu abanesithintela ekuthatheni ubunikazi eenqundwini zakamasipala . Ukugcugcuzela bona kube noburholi obuqinileko emphakathini woke obuzakwazi ukusebenzisana ekurarululeni imiraro . Embusweni othuthukisako , iinhlangano ezijamele abasebenzi nazo zinesibopho mayelana nekhwalithi yemisebenzi eyenziwako , mayelana nokwenza ngcono umsebenzi wombuso , begodu mayelana nokulwisana nekohlakalo nokungabi namakghono . Loke ilwazi elitlolwe ngaphasi kweNdlela yokwEnza linanyathiselwa ebodeni ukwenzela bonyana woke amalunga wesiqhema akwazi ukulibona . Umkghonakalisi womhlangano ufunda loke ilwazi bese ukhombela isiqhema bonyana singezelele ngeminye imifakela . Njengombana lomhlangano kufuze unikele imiphumela ezokwakha umtlamo wewadi , isiqhemesi kufuze kufuneka bonyana sizwane bonyana ngikuphi lokho ekufuze kutjhejwe ntangi . Kufanele kucace bonyana kunini lapho iinqhema ezingaphandle kombuso ziba nesibopho khona sokuphumelelisa iingcenye zomtlamo lo . Ikoro yamabhizinisi , ikoro yabasebenzi kanye nomphakathi kuziinqhenyana ezingafaniko begodu akukavami nakancani bonyana zikhulume ngalizwi linye . Nanyana kunjalo , imizombe ecacileko yeembopho nokuziphendulela , kufaka hlangana iinhlangano ezijamele abasebenzi nabaqatjhi , iqakathekile ekuphumeleliseni umtlamo lo . Emikhakheni eminengi , ikoro yamabhizinisi , ikoro yabasebenzi kanye nomphakathi ziyakghona ukutjho bonyana zingasifaka njani isandla kumatjhejontangi womtlamo lo . Kodwana , ebujameni obunye kuyadingeka bonyana indima ihlelwe ngokusemthethweni . Ukusebenzisana ekuphumeleliseni iminqopho ethileko kungasiza ekwakheni ukuthembeka ngaphakathi naphakathi kweenkoro ngokwazo . Ngebanga lalokho , ukutlama komphakathi kumhlobo womtlamo ohlanganyelweko otlanyelwe ukuthuthukisa ukuzibandakanya komphakathi nokuwuhlobanisa nomTlamo wokuThuthukisa oHlanganiswe ngokuZeleko ( i-IDP ) . UMBUZO 4 . Ngiyiphi imiphumela eqakathekileko elindelweko ( ama-KRA ) ? Njengombana umtlamo lo utlanyelwe ukuletha itjhuguluko esikhathini esingaba minyaka ematjhumi amabili , udinga ukungatjhuguluki komgomo ohlanganisa amatjhuguluko eburholini bombuso , ekorweni yamabhizinisi nekorweni yabasebenzi . Inengi lamaphuzu womtlamo lizokuthatha iminyaka eminengi ekuzameni ukuletha imiphumela . Isibonelo , ukutjhugulukela erherhweni lomnotho elisebenzisa ikhabhoni ephasi kuzokutlhoga imigomo yesikhathi eside begodu imithetjhwana yokutlama ephathelene nokufaka abantu eendaweni zokuhlala izokuthatha amatjhumitjhumi weminyaka ukuphelisa ukwahlukana ngokobujamo beendawo obabangelwa libandlululo . Amatjhuguluko wemigomo kufanele enziwe ngokucophelela nangokusebenzisa ilemuko nobufakazi ukwenzela bonyana inarha le ingakhohlwa iminqopho yayo yesikhathi eside . Ukuhlanganyela okuhlelekileko : Inengi labomasipala abatjha bakhulu bakhulu nakuqalwa ubunengi babantu nendawo ukuvumela bona kube nokubandakanyeka bunqopha kwenengi lezakhamuzi eenkambisweni ezihlangahlangeneko zokutlama . Ukuhlanganyela ekuthuthukiseni ukutlama okuhlanganisiweko , yeke , kufuna imithetho etjhatjhalazi neenkambiso eziveza bona ngubani okumele azibandakanye nanyana okufanele athintwe , awenzele bani lokho , ngayiphi indaba , lapha ngokweendlela ezihlelekileko , ezingaba namphumela muphi . Iimphakamiso nemibono kufanele zitjengiswe eqadi kweenkomba itjengise imiphumela egade ingakalindelwa ekholomini leemphakamiso nemibono . Begodu indlela imibono ihlangatjezwe ngayo kufanele itlolwe . Ingabe ikhona imibono onayo yokuthuthukisa ? Ukuhlanganyela eForamini yomTlamo wokuThuthukisa oHlanganiswe ngokuZeleko- ukugcugcuzela ihlanganyelo eforamini kungaba bunqopha namtjhana ngobujameli beKomidi yeWadi nangabe iinhlangano ezinye zakamasipala zokuhlanganyela azikho . Irhubhululo netuthuko ( R&D ) . Ukuqalana ne-R&D kanye nekghono lokufundisa ngesikhathi esisodwa kungenza ngcono ikhwalithi yefundo ephakemeko , kodwana ngaphandle kokunaka , ukungabi namakghono alingeneko kwabasebenzi kungakhinyabeza ukukhiqizwa kwelwazi kanye nemibono emitjha . Amayunivesithi kufanele abe masentha wefundo ehle khulu ebujameni obuphambili betheknoloji . Ngokurherha abafundi bangaphetjheya kwamalwandle , amayunivesithi angazingenisela imali begodu angezelele ibuthelelo lamakghono . Abafundi bangaphetjheya kwamalwandle abafumana iziqu zabo emayunivesithi weSewula Afrika kufanele bonyana banikelwe ilungelo lokusebenza iminyaka elikhomba ukubagcugcuzela bonyana bahlale lapha . Nanyana iSewula Afrika kufanele bonyana isebenzise imali enengana ku-R&D yoke , kodwana indlela amaziko ahleleke ngayo kufanele bonyana yenze ngcono ukuhlangana kweemfuneko zemibono emitjha kanye namabhizinisi . Umbuso kufanele uhlanganyele nekoro yangeqadi ukukhuphula izinga le-R&D , begodu imithombo kufanele iqothelwe ekwakheni imithangalasisekelo yerhubhululo efunwa lirherho lezomnotho lesimodeni . ISewula Afrika inehlangano ethuthuke khulu nenamandla netjisakalo ejamele abasebenzi . Ngokomlando , iinhlangano ezijamele abasebenzi zidlale indima epolotikini , ngokuzwisisa bonyana iindaba ezithinta amalunga wazo azipheleli esangweni lebubulo . Iinhlangano zabasebenzi zithuthukisa iinrhuluphelo zamalunga wazo begodu zikhulumela abasebenzi abalimala lula , njengabasebenzi bemaplasini , abasebenzi bemakhwitjhini nanyana abasebenzi bamatorho . Amalungelo neenzuzo ezifunyenwe basebenzi kanye nokukhuphuka kwamazinga wokuphila okubonwe linengi labasebenzi ukusukela ngomnyaka we-1994 kwakha inzuzo ebonakalako enarheni le . Ukutjheja ukwenza imisebenzi yezakhamuzi njengombana umasipala aziphendulela eendingweni zomphakathi kunokukatelela imibonwakhe emphakathini . Lokha nakwenziwa umtlamo okhomba lokho okufunwa mphakathi , kufuze kwakhiwe umtlamo wokusebenza ophathelene nemisebenzi erhabekileko ukwenzela bonyana umphakathi ngokwawo ukwazi ukuphumelelisa ituthuko yawo . Lokhu kungabandakanya ukwabiwa kweemali ezigade isimetjhe esele zikhona , amagadango ekufuze athathwe mphakathi ukuphumelelisa amanye amaphrojekthi , kanye nemisebenzi yendawo enjengokuhlela ifestivali , umsebenzi wokuhlanzekisa indawo ngokudobha okulahliweko njll . Indlelakambiso ye-CBP kufuze yenzeke ngaphambi kokuthathwa kwamagadango wokuthoma womtlamo we-IDP kanye nendlelakambiso yokubuyekeza ukwenzela bonyana i-IDP yendawo enye nenye kamasipala ikwazi ukusebenzela phezu kwayo . Kudingeka bonyana ukutlama kukamasipala omunye nomunye kunqotjhiswe begodu kutlolwe ngokunabileko . Ehlathululweni yetjhejuli yokuthoma i-CBP njengengcenye yomzombe wokutlama , isabelo seemali sitjengisiwe besahlathululwa ngokuzeleko . Lokhu kungebanga ziinkoro isabelo seemali asitjhuguluki ekuhlelweni kwaso kwaqobe mnyaka . UKUBANEKGHONO LOKWENZA- kutjho bonyana iintlabagelo azimoroswa emsebenzini namkha etlayentini elilodwa ekusoziseni omunye . Isiqhema esikghonakalisako kufuze sitjheje bonyana loke ilwazi elitjha elivezwako likhambisana nesikhathi begodu sense iinlungiso ukwenzela bonyana ilwazi elifakwe emtlameni liba ngilelo elamukelwe ngokusemthethweni siqhema esibanzi somphakathi . Abantu , imiphakathi , amaziko neenqhema bahlukile mayelana nekareko nangokukhetha izinto eziqakathekileko kunezinye . Abonobangelaba bamunikelo emphakathini onamandla nohlakaniphileko . AmaKomidi weWadi kufanele azizwe azithemba begodu abe nekghono lokuphatha Imibono eyahlukahlukeneko ezokuba lisizo emphakathini . Kunetlhogeko ekulu yeendlela , amanzi , igezi , begodu akunamasoritjhi . Iindlela zokubika kufanele zicaciswe kwelinye nelinye ilawulo . Kuqakathekile bona abantu kufanele bazi bona kubikwa kubani nokobana kunini lapho kufanele indaba isiwe kumphathimandla . Enye nenye indaba kufanele ihlathululwe bese kuyakhethwa ekuthomeni kwesigaba somzombe wephrojekthi . Imitlamo namaqhinga wokuphumelelisa angekhe athathele ehloko bonyana abobaba nabomma baneendingo ezehlukeneko , iinkareko , ilwazi nendlela yokuziphatha begodu namaphrojekthi , ukuloba ukubona okujulileko , ilwazi ilemuko , amathungelelwano neentlabagelo ezikhona ngokwendabuko eenhlanganweni zomphakathi wabomma . Njengekomidi yeWadi ibuye isebenze njengomsebenzeli olungiselela igadango lomphakathi kuqakathekile ukuba nelemuko lerhemiso-kambiso lobulili emitlamenabo yamagadango namaqhinga .
