UmThetho wePhahla wobuDlelwano baboRhulumende , we-2005 uthi iinkhundla ezintathu zakarhulumende kufanele zisebenze ndawonye ukuphumelelisa ukuphakama komphakathi . Eenqhemeni zabahlanganyeli abane dweba itheyibula lamakholomu amabili phezu kwephepha begodu batjhukatjhukane neendlela amaKomidi wamaWadi angakwazi ukubandakanyeka ngayo eenteyijini ezahlukeneko zebhajedi , ukumerega imibono ekholomini yesibili . INTURHU IYINGCENYE YEPILO YANGAMALANGA . Yenzeka ezingeni elilula neliphasi , lokha nakufanele wenze isiqunto ngalokhu ozokwembatha namtjhana okuqakathekileko okufanele ukuhlele ngelanga , ukulwa nesihlobo , ukurarana komngani namtjhana umlingani , ukwahluka ngokwepolotiki namtjhana ukulwela iinsetjenziswa okungarholela ekulweni namtjhana ekufeni . Njengobana amaKomidi weWadi ahlala akhulumisana nabantu abaneendingo ezahlukahlukeneko nokulindelekileko kanye nabomasipala abahlukahlukana ngeensetjenziswa , inturhu-ke ivamile ukuba khona . amaKomidi weWadi kufanele aphendule inturhu ngendlela ethe tjha . Isahlukwesi sikhomba imihlobo yenturhu engavela okufanele iKomidi yeWadi iyitjheje . Iphenyisisa ngeendlela zelawulo zenturhu begodu zinikela isingeniso emakghonweni welawulo asisekelo . Tjheja iindatjana ezisekhasini lama-68 bese usebenza nomnganakho ekukhombeni indlela yenturhu esetjenziswe enturhwini ngayinye . Umtlamo lo uqalene namakghono aqakathekileko nadingekako ekutjhugululeni umnotho nomphakathi . Ukuphumelelisa amakghono la akuzenzakaleli , begodu angeze atholakala nangabe inarha le iragela phambili nokusebenza ngalendlela esebenza ngayo njenganje . Ukuphakama kwamazinga wokuhlangahlangana nokuphela ihliziyo kuzizinto ezitjengisa bonyana isikhathi siqakatheke kwamanikelela : ukubhalelwa kuthatha igadango kungalimaza iinzuzo ezifunyenweko zentando yenengi . Khulukhulu , iSewula Afrika kufanele ifumane iindlela ezirhabekileko zokuphungula amazinga ahlubayezako wokungasebenzi kwabantu abatjha nezizokunikela abantu abatjha amathuba anabileko . Sebenzisa ifundo-sehlakalo ukuzijayeza ngesigaba esinye nesinye . Banikele isikhathi esaneleko sokwenza lokhu bese ukhetha esinye isiqhema ukutjengisa bona basebenze bunjani ngesigaba ngasinye . Emva kwesigaba ngasinye , biza ezinye iinqhema zizokutjho bona khuyini okusebenze kuhle bese banikela iimphakamiso sokuthuthukisa . Bobani abaSebenzi abaThuthukisa umPhakathi , ( ama-CDW ) , ewadini begodu ngiyiphi indima ayenzako ukusekela amaKomidi weWadi ? Amaphrojekthi kufanele abe nobudlelwano obunqophileko mayelana neendaba eziqakatheke ukudlula ezinye kanye neminqopho etjengiswe ekambisweni yokutlama . Indlela enzinze emalungelweni -Lokhu kukulokha isiqhema senturhu sikholwa bona elinye lamalungelwaso liphuliwe bese iya ehlanganweni mayelana nesiqunto esingathathwa sokuphulwa kwelungelo . Indlela yokulungisa ifaka hlangana amakhotho , ihlelo lokulwa ( ilithigetjhini ) , ukulamula . Isibonelo , abahlali be-Moutse batjhijile ekhotho ngomkhawulo wesahlulelo sokususwa esifundeni seMpumalanga basiwe eLimpopo . Lokhu kube nomphumela wobujamo BOKUTHUMBA / BOKULOBA . ISewula Afrika kufanele isungule amaqhinga amatjha begodu iragele phambili nokufaka isandla ekuthuthukiseni isayensi netheknoloji ephasini loke . Lokhu kutlhoga ukufakwa kweemali erhubhululweni netuthukweni , ukusetjenziswa ngconywana kwemithombo ekhona , neenhlangano ezikghonakalisa ukusungulwa kwamaqhinga amatjha nokusebenzisana okungezelelweko phakathi kweenhlangano zombuso zesayensi netheknoloji kanye nekoro yangeqadi . Iindleko eziphezulu zenarha le ezimayelana nokusatjalaliswa kwemibiko eminengi ngesikhathi esisodwa ngokusebenzisa ithintano lethungelelwanohlanganiso zisese siqabo esikhulu . Woke amaSewula Afrika kufanele akwazi ukufumana nokusebenzisa ilwazi ngepumelelo . Mayelana nalokhu , amalungiselelo weenhlangano wokulawula ibhoduluko lelwazi , amathintano netheknoloji kufanele ahlelwe ngconywana ukuqinisekisa bonyana iSewula Afrika ingazifumani ingungazimbi wokusalela " ngelwazi , ukuthintana netheknoloji " . Umkghonakalisi kufuze aqinisekise kobana iinqunto ziyathathwa , imitlamo iyathuthukiswa kanye nokuzibophelela kwabo boke . Umkghonakalisi omuhle uyacabanga ngalokho okuzokukhulunywa ngakho emhlanganweni nanyana kusifundobandulo kanye nesitayela sawo . Ukukhuphula amakhakhazela " wenzuzo engezelelweko yedemografi " , inarha le itlhoga ukondlela okungcono netjhejo lezamaphilo , amazinga wefundo enziwe ngcono , amathuba angezelelweko wefundo yokuzithuthukisa nephakemeko , ukungena lula emsebenzini nokufika lula emsebenzini ( ikghono lokuya lapho imisebenzi itholakala khona ) . Woke amaphuzu la kufanele bonyana atjhejwe emtlameni welizwe loke . Ingabe ngiyiphi indlela esetjenziswe yiKomidi yeWadi ? Layela abahlanganyeli ehlelweni lokwenza nelogfremu abayithuthukisileko mayelana nengeniso abalenzileko lephrojekthi yengadi ( emsebenzini 2.2 no-3.1 ) . Umfanekiso womraro sewungaqedelelwa kwanjesi ngokudweba imida ejame rwe ukutjengisa ubudlelwana hlangana nonobangela ( kusuka enzasi kuze kube phakathi nesihlahla ) kanye nobudlelwana bemiphumela ( isiquntu sangaphezulu esiseleko ) . Imida evundlako kufanele idwetjwe ukutjengisa lapho kunabonobangela abahlangeneko namtjhana imiphumela ehlanganisiweko . Amaphrojekthi asebenzisa ukulingana kobulili nathuthukisa umtlamo wegadango lokuqinisekisa ukufaka phakathi iminikelo yabomma emaKomidini wamaWadi gade kuphumelelisa begodu kubhalansa . Yenza isiqiniseko sokobana imvelo yeendingo zendawo ethize zikhulunyiswene nomasipala . UMBUZO 1 . Uyini umnqopho werherho lokuphathwa kokwenziwa komsebenzi ? Zisebenzisane nabanye emphakathini ukukhuphula ituthuko , ukurarulula imiraro nokuveza ukutshwenyeka kwalabo abangakwazi ukuzikhulumela nabegade badinywe amathuba . AmaKomidi wamaWadi akanawo amandla ahlelekileko ngaphandle nje kokuthumela abakuthumela bunqopha kukhansela yewadi . Abanamandla asemthethweni ukuthatha iinqunto ezibopha omunye nomunye kumasipala . Ikhansela yewadi imjameli wewadi kumkhandlu begodu yoke imigomo namahlelo weenqunto enziwa yikhansela . IFundo eRagela phambili nokuBandula ( FET ) . Irherho le-FET alisebenzi kuhle . Lincani khulu begodu ikhwalithi yomphumela yimbi . Ukwenziwa ngcono kwekhwalithi ngazo zoke iinkhathi kuyadingeka ngombana irherho liyakhula . Ikhwalithi nokukhambelana kwamakhoso kutlhoga itjhejo elirhabako . Lokha ikhwalithi nayithoma ukuba ngcono begodu ukungatjhejwa kweemfundiswa ezineziqu kuthoma ukwanda , ifuneko yemisebenzi ye-FET izozikhuphukela yona ngokwayo . Ukukhulisa ikoro le ngaphandle kokuqala ikhwalithi kungenza kubize imali enengi begodu kuqede abantu abatjha amandla , begodu lokho kunganikela irherho lezefundo isithunzi esimbi ukuya phambili . Nakufika umnyaka wee-2030 , ikoro ye-FET kufanele ibe sele imumethe pheze amaphesende ama-25 wesiqhema sabafundi esineminyaka yobudala ekhambelanako , lokho kutjho ukungezeleleka kwabafundi pheze abama-300 000 namhlanjesi ukufikela esigidini si-1.25 ngomnyaka wee-2030 . Ukusetjenziswa kwesisomali eSewula Afrika kwehle ukusukela ku-avareji pheze emaphesende ama-30 we-GDP ekuthomeni kweminyaka ye-1980 ukufikela pheze emaphesendeni ali-16 we-GDP ekuthomeni kweminyaka yee-2000 . Begodu ukusetjenziswa kwemithangalasisekelo yombuso kusemazingeni aphasi nakuqalwa amazinga womlando . Eqinisweni , iSewula Afrika ilobe isikhathi sokusisa iimali ekorweni yeendlela , yeentimela , yemikhumbi , yegezi , yamanzi , yehlwengiso , yeenthuthi zomphakathi , yokwakha izindlu . Lokha inarha le nayizakukhula msinyana nangendlela ebandakanya boke abantu , kufanele bonyana ibe nezinga eliphezulu lokusebenzisa imali . Ingeniso epheleleko yepahla kufanele bonyana ifike pheze emaphesendeni ama-30 we-GDP ngomnyaka wee-2030 , begodu isisomali lombuso kufanele lifike emaphesendeni alitjhumi we-GDP , nayizakwazi ukuba negalelo eliragela phambili ekukhuleni nemisebenzini yemindeni . Emsebenzini olandelako amalunga womphakathi akha ilandelaniso lezehlakalo alandele umkhondo womlando womphakathi . Ngokukhomba amaphetheni kanye neenqhelo eziragela phambili , lomsebenzi kufuze uqininisekise bonyana umphakathi uzwisisa khudlwana ubujamo bawo begodu kufuze uwenze bonyana ucabange ngokuphumelela kwesizo elifunyenwe esikhathini esigadungileko . I-Seymour yiSentha encani yokusebenzela esemaphandleni okwakusisabelo se-Ciskei ngaphambili . Indawo le inesitjhaba somhlobo munye wabantu esilinganiselwa e-3000 . Pheze amaphesenthi ama-80 wabantu endaweni le abasebenzi begodu izinga lalabo abangakafundi pheze libe maphesenthi ama-60 . Ukwakha umbuso onekghono nothuthukisako . Iintjhijilo ezimbalwa zitlhoga itjhejo , kufaka hlangana ukutlhayela okukhulu kwamakghono , irherho elinabileko laborhulumende abahlukeneko , amazinga aphezulu wekohlakalo , iindlela ezibuthakathaka zokuziphendulela , ukuhlolisiswa nokweluswa okutlhayelako kwemisebenzi yeembethamthetho kanye nomlando omude wokungacaciswa kuhle kwemisebenzi yesiqhema nombuso . Lezi ziindaba ezibudisi , ezitlhoga ukutjhejwa ngokuthembeka , ukutlama ngokucophelela kanye noburholi obunekghono lokuthatha iinqunto . Khomba abomazinikela ababili ukwenza ukudlalwa kwendima okuthatha amaminidi amathathu , begodu ubanikele imizuzu embalwa ukobana bacabange bonyana bazayidlala njani indimabo . Ungavumeli abalingisi abanye namkha abahlanganyeli babone iindimezo . Tjheja isiqhema bonyana sizabe sibukele ukudlalwa kwendima . Bakhumbuze bonyana abalingisi abethuli imibonwabo , kodwana imibono leyo ababawiwe bayidlale bayidlale . Ukuziphendulela kungenye yeenkambisolawulo eziqakathekileko zokuhlanganyela begodu iKomidi yeWadi njengamakhansela akhethiweko , anokuziphendulela emphakathini abawusebenzelako . Ukutjheja nokuhlunga amaphrojekthi womphakathi nokubika qobe emphakathini ngeragelo phambili lokwenziwa kwezinto , kuyindlela ethe tjha yokuhlola . Ukukhulumisana okunqophileko hlangana komkhandlu nomphakathi , nahlangana nababambisani boke , kuqakathekile . Ilwazi elingakalungi lingabanga inturhu hlangana neenhlangano . Lingagcugcuzela ukurhatjheka kwamala bese enza ihlangahlangano kubahlali . Lokhu ngakwelinye ihlangothi kungaliya ituthuko neragelo phambili mayelana ne-IDP namtjhana amanye amaphrojekthi . AmaKomidi weWadi asebenzisana nabasebenzisani abanengi . Lokhu kufaka hlangana ikhansela lewadi , iinkhulu zakamasipala okufaka hlangana usodorobha , umphathi kamasipala , isisebenzi sakamasipala , iinsebenzi ezithuthukisa umphakathi , abarholi bendabuko nemiphakathi eyenziwe ngedlanzana labantu beenqhema ezinekareko njengeenhlangano zekolo , irhwebo lomphakathi , iinqhema zetja , iinhlangano zabalimi kanye nezinye iinhlangano neenqhema . Ukufana - imiphakathi ingahluka ngokuya ngokwemvelaphi yobuzwe , ikolo , imvelaphi yamaphasi okungabanga inturhu . Irhirikelo labantu abanengi ababuya elizweni elithile elihluka ngelimi namasiko namtjhana ngesifunda namtjhana ngedorobha kungabanga inturhu . Imiphakathi le ' ingabonwa ' ngamanye amalunga ngendlela engasingiyo . Ukwakhiwa kwezindlu : Isibawo seemali esibuya eBhodini yeLizwe yeziNdlu ukusiza ngomraro orhagele kangaka wokutlhogeka kwezindlu endaweni le siphasisiwe . Kodwana , ukuriyada ekutholakaleni kweemali , umbango wenarha ngehlangothini letuthuko begodu nokuriyada emphakathini wekhaya ivimbele khulu ukwenziwa kwephrojekthi le ngendlela okumele yenziwe ngayo . AmaKomidi weWadi kulindeleke kobana andise ukuzibandakanya kwezakhamuzi kurhulumende wekhaya . Anikela ngokuhlanganisa hlangana komphakathi kanye nomkhandlu . Amakomidi weWadi angenza iimphakamiso kukhansela lewadi , nalo ekumele libuye lidlulisele iimphakamiso lezo kuSpikha / kuSomlomo wakamasipala ngemigomo / ngemithethokambiso ethinta iwadi . Nakufika umnyaka wee-2030 , irherho lezamaphilo kufanele ibe lisezingeni lokunikela boke abantu itjhejo lekhwalithi , elitholakala simahla , nanyana elibhadalwa yitjhorensi yombuso nanyana yitjhorensi yangeqadi . Irherho lezamaphilo lemitholapilo nesiyingi kufanele bonyana lisize boke abantu , begodu kufanele kuqalwe khulu ukukhandela , ifundo , ukulawulwa kwamalwele nokwelatjhwa . Iimbhedlela kufanele zisebenze ngekghono nangepumelelo , zinikele itjhejo lekhwalithi elitholakala eembhedlela nemazikweni akhethekileko ebantwini abalitlhogako . Kufanele kuhlale kunabosobizelomsebenzi abanengi , khulukhulu emiphakathini etlhagatlhagako . NDLELA YEKAMBISO YOKUHLOLA UKUBANDAKANYEKA KWABOMMA NABOBABA KWELINYE NELINYE IGADANGO ELITLANYIWEKO , ELIFAKA PHAKATHI UMTHETHO , IMITHETHOKAMBISO NAMKHA AMAPHROGREMU KWENYE NENYE INDAWO BEGODU NAKIWO WOKE AMALEVELI KULIQHINGA LOKWENZA IINKHATHALELO ZABOMMA NABOBABA , AMALEMUKO OKUSIMEDO ESIDINGEKAKO SOMTLAMO , UKWENZIWA KOMSEBENZI NGOKWESIQUNTO , UKUTJHEJA NOKUHLUNGWA KWEMITHETHOKAMBISO BEGODU NAMAPHROGREMU KIYO YOKE IMIKHAKHA YEZEPOLOTIKI , ZOMNOTHO NEPHATHELENE NOMPHAKATHI UKWENZELA BONYANA ABOMMA NABOBABA BAKWAZI UKUZUZA NGOKULINGANA BEGODU UKUNGAFANI AKUSIYO INTO ETHUWELELISWAKO . EKUGCINENI UMNQOPHO KUKUPHUMELELISA UKUFANA NOBULILI . Ukuphumelelisa lamatjhejontangi wemithangalasisekelo , kuqakathekile ukuqinisekisa bonyana imiphakathi yemakhaya iyahlomula kumithangalasisekelo eminengi yezakhiwo zeentambo namaphayiphu nokobana ukubekwa kweentengo zalomthangalasisekelo kutjheja iindingo zemiphakathi yemakhaya . Abakghonakalisi kufuze basekelwe bosiyazi be-CBP . Abosiyazi kufuze banikele isizo lezobuthekhiniki neleensetjenziswa begodu kufuze bahlinzekelwe ngesibopho samawadi anqophileko . Isayensi netheknoloji ziragela phambili nokutjhugulula indlela ekukhiqizwa nekuthengiselanwa ngayo ipahla nemisebenzi . Njengenarha yengeniso ephakathi , iSewula Afrika kufanele isebenzise ilwazi layo kanye nemikhiqizo yayo emitjha ekuphalisaneni . Endleleni yayo , iintengo eziphasi zemikhiqizo angeze zanela ukunabisa ukuba khona kwebubulo leSewula Afrika ephasini loke . Lokhu kuphathelene namabubulo amatjha neenkoro zendabuko , ezinjengomsebenzi wokurhweba ngamaminerali . Imibono emitjha iyadingeka ekuthuthukiseni inarha yengeniso ephakathi . ' UBUSO ' BAKARHULUMENDE BUBUSO BEGODU / NANYANA ILIZWI LABANIKELA NGEMISEBENZI ABANGAPHAMBILI . UmTlamo kaMasipala nemiThetjhwana yokwEnza , we-2001 ubeka ubumvelo bamaRherho wokuLawula ukwEnza . Njengobana amaKomidi weWadi adlala indima ekutjhejeni nekwenzeni kukamasipala , amalunga kufanele atjheje okumumethwe mthetholawulo . Ngemva kweminyaka elitjhumi nobunane sifumene umbuso wentando yenengi , iSewula Afrika isesemphakathi ongalinganiko lapho inengi labantu lisabhodwe mtlhago begodu lapho kunedlanzana labantu abasebenzako . Ikhwalithi yefundo yesikolo yenengi labafundi abanzima ayazisi . Ibandlululo lokuhlukana ngokweendawo zokuhlala lisaragela phambili nokukhungatha inarha . Inengi labantu abatjha libona ngasuthi angeze laphumelela epilweni . Begodu ubumbi obudalwe libandlululo busaragela phambili nokuba nomthelela emathubeni wabantu abanengi . Iintjhijilo ezikulwezi zingararululwa kwaphela ngokutjhugulula igadango lendlela inarha le esebenza ngayo . Kufuze kutjhejwe indaba yokufaka hlangana umnqopho odinga ukutjhejwa ntangi ovela eenqhemeni ebegade zidinywe amathuba khulu ngaphambilini . Ukuhloma itheknoloji yamathungelelwano wenarha , wesiphande nomasipala wokusabalalisa ilwazi ngeentambo zeplastiki nanyana zefayibha ukwakha isakhelo sokufumaneka kwezizwambiko zeentetjhi zommoya ezinabileko . Isisomali langeqadi kufanele lidose phambili kilomkhakha , begodu kufanele lingezelelwe ngeemali zombuso ezifunekako ukuhlangabezana neminqopho yehlalakuhle . Imigomo , umthetjhwana namalungiselelo amahle weenhlangano wokuphumelelisa lokhu afuneka ngokurhaba . Ukutjhugulula irherho lezomnothweli kuyiphrojekthi etjhijilako nethatha isikhathi eside . Ngokufitjhani , siphakamisa bonyana sikhuphule amakghono , ilwazi nelemuko labantu , amandla wokukhiqiza nemithangalasisekelo ukukhuphula inani lepahla ethengiselwa iinarha zangaphandle , ukwenzela bonyana sikwazi ukungezelela imithombo yesisomali nokuphungula ukuthembela eemalini ezivela eenarheni zangaphandle . Isisomali eliphezulu , elisekelwa mithangalasisekelo yombuso kanye namakghono , lizokwenza bonyana umnotho ukwazi ukukhula msinyana begodu ukhiqize khudlwana . Ukukhuphuka kwezinga lemisebenzi nemikhiqizo kuzakurholela ekukhuphukeni kwemirholo namazinga wokuphila nekwehleni kwezinga lokungalingani . Ukutjhugulula irherho lezomnotho libe ngilelo eligcugcuzela isisomali nokungasetjenziswa butjhulweni kweensetjenziswa kuyinto eqakathekileko ekuphumeleliseni umnotho isikhathi eside . Nasele i-IDP iqediwe , kumele inikelwe umkhandlu kamasipala ukunikelwa itjhejo begodu nemvumo . Umkhandlu kumele uqale bonyana i-IDP ifanisa zoke iindaba ( imiraro ) ezithinta indawo begodu nendlela amaqhinga begodu namaphrojekthi azakusiza ukurarulula iimiraro na . Umkhandlu godu kumele uqinisekise bonyana i-IDP iyavumelana netlhogakalo langokomthetho ngaphambi kokuthoal imvumo . Ukuthintana kuzizincambili . Kukukhamba ngokutjhaphuluka nokudlhegana kwelwazi nemibono elisuka komunye umuntu liye komunye . Kuyikambiso lapho umuntu , OMTHUMELI athumela umlayezo komunye umuntu owamukela umlayezo , OMUMAMUKELI . Nasingakhulumi ngepumelelo kungarholela ekutjhubeni kwezinto , ukungavumelani nenturhu engavela . Njengalokhu amaKomidi weWadi ayindlela eqakathekileko yokuthintana ezingeni lekhaya , kufanele aqinisekise bona ilwazi abalinikela umphakathi linqophile begodu lizwisiswa ngomunye nomunye umuntu begodu nabo ngokunjalo bakhuluma ilwazi elinqophileko emkhandlwini nemakhanseleni . Khumbuza abahlanganyeli bona i-logfremu lithebula ekufanele libasize begodu lingabaliyi . Kufanele libonakale njengomtlolo ophilako ongatjhugululwa begodu ohlaliswe kuhle njalo njalo njalo . Ngokubonakalako iBatho Pele izakuthinta indlela umsebenzi owenziwa ngayo ngokukatelela iKambiso yokuPhatha ukwEnziwa komSebenzi ebeka iintjengisi ezimayelana nokwenza umsebenzi begodu yenza bona urhulumende wendawo nezakhamuzi zikghone ukumeda lokho ezikuzuzileko ngeentjengisezi . Lapha kutjengisa ukungasebenzi kuhle , ikghonakalisa ukubandakanyeka okufunekako . Ifaka hlangana iingaba zokutlama , ilandelela nemibiko ebuyako kanye nokubuyekezwa kwemisebenzi eyenziwe ngonyaka . Ukutjhuguluka kweSewula Afrika kuthintwa ngilokho okwenzeka esiphandeni nephasini . Ukuphumelela kuyame ekutheni inarha izwisisise begodu kube nalokho ekwenzako mayelana namatjhuguluko anjalo . Ngaphandle kwehlolo ezeleko yamatjhuguluko wedemografi , umtlamo lo ukhuluma ngamatjhuguluko amahlanu aqakathekileko : amatjhuguluko wezomnotho wephasi loke , itheknoloji , ukusebenzisana nephasi loke , ukutjhugutjhuguluka kwetlayimethi nokukhula komnotho we-Afrika . UMSEBENZI 2 ngiziphi iindlela zokusebenzisana nabadlali beendima bangaphandle . Imithetho embalwa iphasiswe yiPalamende , ngemva kwamakhetho wedemokhrasi we-1994 , la asekela bekaqinise amandla kamasipala wokulawula iindaba zabo nokwenza imisebenzabo ngendlela yokuhlanganyela nokuhlanganisa koke . Ukwakha ukuhlanganyela komphakathi . Iinhlangano zehlalakuhle yomphakathi nokuhlanganyela komphakathi kuzizinto ezifunekako ekwakheni imiphakathi ephephileko . Amasentha wokuphepha komphakathi kufanele atjhejwe . Izulu elinamandla lenze bona ihlabathi engehla yengadi ikhambe namanzi . Amanzi akhiwe ngamatanka begodu azokuba lisizo eenyangeni ezilandelako kodwana kufanele kusetjenzwe nzima ukubuyisela iphrojekthi emtlhaleni . Yembe umnotho wezenjiwa ngomnqopho wokwakha imithombo yokukhuphula amazinga wokuphila , amakghono nemithangalasisekelo ngendlela ebambelelako . Okucatjangwako nakho kuvumela ' ubungako bokuqakatheka ' kwabo boke abantu . Lokhu kutjho bona omunye nomunye umuntu unomnikelo okumele awenze kiyo yoke imikhakha yeempilo zabo . Ithatha godu amakomidi wamawadi njengehlangano ehlanganisa abadosiphambili nabantu . Irherhohlanganisela lokuqatjha iinhloko zeminyango kufanele lethulwe , lifake amatshwayo wepolotiki nokulawula . Iindaba eziqakatheke khulu zomphakathi . IKomidi yeWadi ingenzani ukusiza ? Ngesikhathi nakuthoma ukwenziwa lokhu , kungenzeka kufake ama-elemende amanengi wendlelakambiso . Kodwana , kuzakuthi lokha nakunande kwethulwa lokhu emhlanganweni omunye nomunye weKomidi yeWadi , kukuthome ukuzwakala khudlwana lokha nakuthoma umsebenzi . Ukuze iphrojekthi iphumelele kuqakathekile bona iindima nemisebenzi yelunga ngalinye lesiqhema ihlathululwe ngokutjheja okukhulu . Ilunga elinye nelinye ephrojekthini linomsebenzi ekufanele liwenze ukuthuthukisa iminqopho yephrojekthi nokuqinisekisa ipumelelo yayo . Ubungako : Qatjha amatjhifu amabili wabasebenzi abajamisa iinkoloyi / abogadi beenkoloyi abahlanu . IBatho Pele iveza bona iminyango kiwo womabili amazinga lelizwe nelephrovinsi kufanele abe neenkambiso zokuphatha ukwenziwa kwemisebenzi efaka hlangana stipulates that departments at both national and provincial level must have performance management systems that include the setting of service delivery indicators and the measurement of performance . ISewula Afrika kufanele ibe nalokho ekwenzako mayelana nesehlakalo esiliqiniso sokobana iingidigidi zabantu abaphilileko nabaqinileko bafuna ukusebenza . Esikhathini esifitjhani , irherho lezomnotho kufanele bonyana livuelele amaSewula Afrika angasebenziko amathuba wemisebenzi , inengi labo babantu abasesebatjha begodu abanamakghono aphasi , begodu kufanele bonyana lithuthukise amakghono nelwazi ukwenzela bonyana kube nerherho lezomnotho elihlukileko ngomuso . Ukukhuphula amazinga womsebenzi kuzokuba neenzuzo ezidlula ukuhlonyiswa ngelemuko lokuba nomsebenzi . Kuzokusiza abantu ukobana basise efundweni yabantababo , benze ngcono imizabo begodu bakwazi ukulawula ubungozi obungahle behlele emaphilwenabo . Umsebenzi nefundo zizakwenza bonyana izakhamuzi zenze ngcono amaphilwazo . Ubujamo nabuvelako buphendulwa ukuziphatha okukhambelana nendlela yokuthatha nokubona izinto . Ukulinganisa ngokutjhejisisa / ukurhubhulula ngokwesisekelo kuyakufaka yini phakathi ukuhlungwa umlomo nomlomo kwabomma nabobaba begodu kuyawujamela umphakathi ofaka boke abantu ( abatjha / abadala , bemakhaya / bemadorobheni nangokweenqhema zobuzwe na ? ) abobaba nabomma bazakwenza ukuhlungwa umlomo nomlomo begodu nokubuthelelwa kwemininingwana na ? Ukutlhogonyelwa : Ingabe inani lommango nanyana lendawo yemvelo likhuphukile nanyana lehlile ? Kubayini ? Ingabe zikhona iindawo ezivikelweko ezihlonyiweko ? Ingabe zikhona iindawo ezinobujamo obuphathelene nejiyoloji , nehlabathi nanyana nomehlela nanyana umkhuphukela ezenza bonyana kube budisi ukwakha , isib . iindawo ezehlela nanyana ezikhuphukela khulu , ihlabathi ezele amanzi , kanye nedwala elingakanzinzi elingaphasi ? Kuqakathekile ukwehlisa iindleko zokuphila zemindeni etlhagako . Amanye amatshwayo womtlamo azakuba nomthelela wokukhuphuka kweendleko mayelana nezomnotho . Khulukhulu , ukwenziwa ukuba ngokwesimodeni kwemithangalasisekelo ngemva kwamatjhumitjhumi weminyaka wesisomali eliphasi kungadinga amatharifu aphezulu . Ukulinganisa ukukhuphukokhu , kufanele bonyana umgomo uqalane nokungezelela amakghono wokukhiqiza nokurhwebelana ngepahla kanye nokusisa kumithangalasisekelo emitjha emikhakheni ethinta ngokunqophileko abantu abatlhagako , njengokuqakatheka komadlano , iinthuthi zomphakathi , ifundo nezamaphilo kanye nethintaniswanoliqha . Begodu ukusebenza ngepumelelo khudlwana kombuso kuzakurholela esakhiweni seendleko eziphasi serherho lezomnotho . Yenza isiqiniseko sokobana amaphrojekthi akhonjiweko anesihlanganiso esibunqopha eendabeni eziqakathekileko kunezinye begodu neminqopho leyo ekhonjwe eengabeni ezigadungileko . KUNESIDINGO SANGOKOMTHETHO SOKOBANA OMUNYE NOMUNYE UMASIPALA ATHUTHUKISE irherho lokulawulwa kokwenza ( i-PMS ) . Umnqopho we-PMS kukuziphendulela ngokusetjenziswa kweentlabagelo zakamasipala , ukwenza ngcono ikghono lokwenza begodu nokuphumelela kweenhlangano begodu nokubonisa ukuzuzwa kwemiphumela . Ukugcugcuzela izakhamuzi ezikhutheleko ezizakwazi ukuqinisa ituthuko , intando yenengi nokuziphendulela . Umhlangano wesiqhema esikhulu nesiqhema esibanzi somphakathi lapho imiphumela yomsebenzi weveke ifaka hlangana iNdlela yokuSiza ukuPhumelelisa , imiphumela ehlanganisiweko kanye nelwazi eliphathelene nomphumela ngamunye , kufuze kukhulunywe ngawo begodu kuzwanwe nangezinto zomphakathi ekufuze zinikelwe itjhejontangi . Hlathulula bonyana lokha nakwenziwa lokhu emphakathi , nangabe kuyadingeka , umuntu onikela ihlathululo angasebenzisa ilwazi alifumene emizuzwini yakanobhala , emarekhodini womphakathi kanye nemanothini wabakghonakalisi . Khambelanisa iindaba nesiqhema abafuna ukukhuluma ngaso ngokuzeleko . Lokhu kungaba kuzithwala kwabantwana abasesebancani , i-HIV ne-AIDS nanyana ezinye nezinye iindaba umphakathi ozithatha njengeziqakathekileko . Ukuhlola igalelo nanyana ukuvela komraro , tlola iminyaka efliphutjhadini bese urekhoda ngaphsi komnyaka ngamunye bonyana umraro ube mkhulu kangangani . Ingabe abomasipala basebenzisana njani norhulumende welizweloke kanye nowesifunda kumikhakha yakarhulumende . Ungumma . Utjala imirorho bonyana umndeni udle . Umyenakho usebenza ethresteni begodu ulilunga leKomidi yeWadi yeKhaya . Umndenakho udla eminye yemirorho begodu woke omunye uwuthengisa emakethe begodu lokhu kukunikela imali ongayisebenzisa nakungasinjalo awunayo imali okungeyakho . Umyenakho akakunikeli imali , uletha nje ukudla nezinye iindingo ezivela ethresthini . Udinga bonyana ube nemali ukwenzela bonyana ukwazi ukuthenga izipho ezincani zabantabakho namkha yokubhadela emtholapilo nakunesidingo sokobana uye khona . Umyenakho uza ekhaya akutjele bonyana umnganakhe uthembise ukukuthengisela umrorhwakho edorobheni elikhudlwana . IKhomitjhini yamaLungelo woBuntu inamandla wokuphenya nokubika ngamalungelo wobuntu , ukuthatha amagadango wokukhuluma ngokuhlukunyezwa kwamalungelo wobuntu , ukurhubhulula nokufundisa ngamalungelo wobuntu . Ukwamukela iqhinga elihlanganisiweko . Ukuphumelela ekubeni nomphakathi ophephileko kutjho ukurarulula abonobangela abasisekelo sobulelesi , obudinga imithombo ebanzi nehlukahlukeneko yomphakathi kanye nombuso . Yenze bonyana abantu nomnotho bakwazi ukubuyela ebujameni obuhle bangaphambilini nangabe kunokutjhuguluka kobujamo betlayimethi . Isigaba 29(b) somThetho sikhuluma ngendlelakambiso ekufuze ilandelwe ekwakhiweni kwe-IDP begodu siveza ngokunqophileko bonyana kufuze kukhulunyisanwe nomphakathi wendawo malungana neendingo zokuthuthukisa kanye namatjhejontangi we-IDP begodu sithi umphakathi kufuze uhlanganyele ekutlanyweni kwe-IDP . AmaKomidi weWadi kufanele enze iqhinga lokuqiniseka bona umphakathi uyatjelwa ngeendaba eziphathelene nomkhandlu begodu nomkhandlu nawo uyatjelwa ngeendaba zomphakathi kanye nokuphendula kwawo malungana nemitlamo neenqunto zomkhandlu . Ukuthintana- lezi ziincwadi ezitlolelwe ikomidi nanyana ezatlolwa yikomidi . Zoke iincwadi ezitlolwako kumele ziyelelwe malunga wekomidi njengombana zithunyelwa ngokujamela wona nje . Omunye wemisebenzi eqakatheke khulu kamasipala kukuthola iindingo zezakhamuzi zakhe begodu nokuthi angazifezekisa njani . AmaSewula Afrika woke kufanele agcugcuzelwe bonyana afunde ilimi lesiNtu begodu amahlelo wombuso kufanele asebenzele ukuphumelelisa lokhu . Ukuthuthukisa amabubulo afana nalawo akhiqiza imikhiqizo yezelimo , wezamavakatjho , weendawo zokuthiya iinhlambi namabhizinisi amancani lapho kunamakghono khona . Yabelana imibono nesiqhema esihlelako . Ukutjheja ukwenza namtjhana ukusebenza kweenkhulu . Umfuziselo wokurarulula umraro lithulusi elinesizo lokusiza amaKomidi weWadi . Akhe siqale isibonelo esingenzasi nokobana singenziwa bunjani ngokuphathekako . Iba nento oyenzako / phendula - uphendula bunjani inturhu ? Okuqakatheke khulu kukobana , kungenzeka bonyana ilwazi elinengi libuthelelwe bosiyazi be-CBP , kodwana qinisekisa neKomidi yeWadi kanye nekhansela bonyana ingabe ikhona imithombo yelwazi elisizo begodu engasetjenziswa . Isiqothelwa senani lenarha namalwandlekazi avikelekileko ( njenganje amahagere wenarha pheze aziingidi ezili-7.9 , umthala weligu omakhilomitha ama-848 kanye nelwandlekazi elimakhilomitha azii-4 172km2 kuvikelekile ) . Ikhansela lakamasipala lifuze lihlole kobana liyifinyelela njani iminqopho eliyibekileko . Lenza lokhu ngokubonisana nomphakathi kanye neenhlangano ngomsebenzi walo . Khumbula : Ababambisani bangaba yingcenye yesiqhema engaphezu kweyodwa begodu ababambisani akusibo labo abenza itjhada khulu namtjhana abakhuluma khulu ! Indima yamaKomidi weWadi godu yenabela ekuphumeleliseni kanye nekwengezeleleni imizamo yemiphakathi ukufinyelela iminqopho kumaphrojekthi ethembise ukuwenza . Iinqhema zomsebenzi nanyana amakomidi ahlela nomphakathi ukuqedelela amaphrojekthi athileko azokuzuza kulwazi elisisekelo lokuphatha iphrojekthi . Ukuqinisa amakghono wokutlama wombuso . Qinisekisa ukujameleki okungibo bababambisani emakomidini amancani wamaphrojekthi . Usiyazi kwezobulili , namkha umuntu onelwazi ngezinto eziphathelene nobulili , kumele abe yingcenye yazo zoke iinqhema zokuhlunga iphrogremu ekulu . Imizamo kumele yenziwe ukwenzela bonyana abobaba nabomma bajameleke eenqhemenezi . Iingcenye zokuthuthukisa urhulumende wendawo ngokwendlela yebhajede nangekamiso yemithetho , ukuphatha okuqalene nendawo , ukungaphathi kuhle kweensebenzi zakamasipala nokuthuthukisa umtlamo ohlangeneko ( i-IDP ) ngayinye inikela amathuba wokubandakanyeka komphakathi ekambisweni kamasipala . Ukuphumelelisa nokugcina isilinganiswesi kutlhoga ukuhlangana kwamaphuzu ambalwa , begodu amanye wawo akaweli ngaphasi kwelawulo lombuso . Ukukhula komnotho , ukukhuphuka kwemisebenzi nemirholo , ukwehla kokungalingani , ukuthuthuka kwerherho lezefundo , ubujamo obuhle bokusungula amabhizinisi nokuthuthuka ngokwebizelo kuzokusiza khulu ekubumbaniseni abantu beSewula Afrika . Amahlelo anjengehlelo lokulungisa , ukuthuthukiswa kwabanzima ngokomnotho nokubuyekezwa kwemithetho yenarha aphumelela khulu nangabe umnotho uyakhula begodu irherho lefundo liba ngcono . Ngaphandle kwebhoduluko elinjalo , lamagadango angakhuphula izinga lokutjhuba kommoya womphakathi . Umtlamo lo wenza kunendawo ezimbalwa zokwenza ngcono ukuphumelela kwamahlelo wokulungisa lokho okungakhange kukhambe kuhle ngaphambilini , khulukhulu lawo aphathelene nokunabisa amathuba womnotho walabo ebegade badinywe amathuba ngokomlando . Ukubonisana nombiko obuyako - iKomidi yeWadi yenza amaplatfomu , isibonelo , ukuhlela umhlangano womphakathi , ukukhuluma emhlanganweni wesitokfela , ukukhuluma emhlanganweni wetlabha yezemidlalo njll . Ukunikela ilwazi kanye nombiko obuyako emphakathini mayelana nesiqunto sekhansela kanye neendaba ezikhulunywe mphakathi ezibikwe elungeni lomkhandlu namtjhana ikhansela . Veza imibono eyahlukahlukeneko mayelana nemihlobo ehlukeneko yelwazi elikumasipala wabo ekungaba lisizo ukuba nalo lokha nawutlamako . Yamukela iimpendulo bese uzitlola efliphutjhadini ukwenzela bonyana boke bakwazi ukuzibona . Indlela ye-WID yokwenza izinto yathatha ihlangothi lokuqala abomma njengabemukeli besizo letuthuko abathe du kunokobana babe basebenzeli betjhuguluko abamajadu namkha ekujugululweni komnothwabo , okuphathelene nomphakathi , kwepolitiki begodu namaqiniso wamasiko . Umphumela oqakathekileko kube kukobana izinto abomma abazikhuthalelako ziqaleka zizodwa njengezinto ezahlukanisiweko edosela ekubekelweni kwabo ngeqadi erherhweni lombuso nezinye izakhiwo zomphakathi . Ngokwenzekako , indlela ye-WID iphatha izinto zabomma njengalezo ezinesisekelo esingakahlobani nezinto eziqakathekileko zetuthuko ezifana namalungelo wobuntu , urhulumende wedemokhrasi , ukuvikeleka kwebhoduluko , idlhobhalizetjheni , ukuthula , nokubeka phasi iinkhali , njll . Ihloko elawula imisebenzi yombuso kufanele yakhiwe , ibe nesibopho sokuphatha iragelo phambili lamabizelo weenhloko zeminyango , kufaka hlanga ukubiza iinqhema zokuhlunga abasebenzi abatjha , zokuhlola imisebenzi yabasebenzi neenkambiso zokukhalima . Ukuba khona emihlanganweni yekhansela - ukwenza irosta yamalunga weKomidi yeWadi bona kwabelwe ilunga elinye nelinye umhlangano elifanele ukuwukhamba . Imitlamo ye-IDP yenziwa ngokuthintana hlangana neminyango kanye nomunye nomunye nomunye onerhuluphelo lomphumela . Ukuthatha isiqunto kwenziwa ngendlela evulekileko neyedemokhrasi . Iinsetjenziswa zemisebenzi zatjiwa ngendlela ezokuzalisa ukuthuthukiswa kweminqopho kamasipala . Indlela le yomnqopho yenziwe ukuletha umphumela wemisebenzi enikela ekuthuthukisweni mazombe kwendawo okuzokuba lisizo kiwo woke umuntu . AmaKomidi weWadi ayindlela ehleliweko yokuthintana hlangana komphakathi nomkhandlu . Unayo ibhajedi yomndeni / yekhaya begodu ifaka hlangana ini ? Bawa abahlanganyeli banikele iimbonelo zalokho ebangakufaka ebhajedeni yekhaya nabenza ibhajedi . Tlola izinto ezisetjenziswakwezo etjhadini ngaphasi kwamakholomu amabili , WEENDLEKO NENGENISO . Iindleko zingafaka , umrhala , igezi , imali yesikolo . Ingeniso ingafaka umrholo , irende ( nangabe babhadela irende ekhaya namtjhana enye nje ipahla ) , umsebenzi ongezelelako ongenisa imali . Ukwehlisa - kuza igama elithi ' placate ' elitjho ukwehla uzothe nanyana ukulibalelana . Umkhandlu wenza ' itjhatjha ' mehlweni emibonweni neemphakamisweni zomphakathi ukuzenza bona zithabe kodwana ayenzi litho nanyana itjheje ezinye nezinye iimphakamiso nanyana imibono evezwako . Iphesentheji yomndeni isisekelo seleveli yamanzi , isanithetjhini , igezi nokuthuthwa kweenzibi eziqinileko . Kulisizo ukuzwisisa ilimi elisetjenziswa ku-PCM , nokobana eminye imifuziselo isebenzisa maphi amagama , njengobana kungenzeka bona amalunga weKomidi yeWadi asebenze ngamathemu la ngezinye iinkhathi . Ilimi elisetjenziswa kilemojuli ngelivame ukusetjenziswa ebujameni bakarhulumende wekhaya weSewula Afrika . Kufanele kuhlathululwe izinga elamukelekako lokuphila , kufaka hlangana lokho okufunekako ekwenzeni bonyana abantu bakghone ukuthuthukisa amakghonwabo . Imojuli le yahlukaniswe ngezahluko ezine ; sokuthoma sethula umqondogama wokulawula iphrojekthi bese kuba sisahluko ngasinye eentejini ezintathu ezahlukahlukeneko . Yamukela iimpendulo ezivela eenqhemeni . Nangabe isiqhema esingaphezu kwesisodwa sinombuzo ofanako , yenza isiqiniseko sokobana isiqhema esinye nesinye sifaka isandla . Isibonelo , ungakhombela isiqhema esisodwa bonyana siphendule umbuzo owodwa bese ukhombela esinye isiqhema bonyana siphendule umbuzo wesibili . Nanyana okhunye ongakwenza , kukwamukela iimpendulo ezimbalwa zesiqhema esinye nesinye bese uragela phambili uya kwesinye isiqhema . Amamatheriyali neensetjenziswa - kuyasiza ukwenza irhelo ukuthoma ngokwenza irhelo nokukhomba ama-ayithemu afunekako , ubungako bawo nomsebenzi azowenza . Lokhu kungafaka hlangana ama-ayithemu asisekelo anjengamaphepha namapeni kanye namaforomo , imitjhiningqondo ephathwako namadathaphrojektha . Ukuvumelanisa - inturhu ingavela njengeqhinga elifaneleko elingasetjenziswa ukuphumelelisa umnqopho . Isibonelo , boke ababambisani bangavumelana bona iinkhulu zomphakathi zidinga ukunikela imisebenzi yekghono . Kanti abanye abahlali bangabona kungcono bona iimali zisetjenziselwe ukubandula , kanti abanye bangabona bona amakhomphyutha amanengi angasiza ekurarululeni ukwethulwa kweensetjenziswa okubuthakathaka . Ukuhlobanisa i-CBP ne-IDP kwakha ithuba lokuqinisekisa bonyana i-IDP inzinza phezu kobujamo bendawo ekufuze kusetjenzelwe kibo begodu kuveza ukuqakatheka kweemfuneko zokusebenza ngokuhlanganyela zomThetho wamaHlelo kaMasipala , ka-2000 . Zibandakanye ekulumiswaneni ehleleke ngokungakapheleli nomuntu / nabantu abanamakghono wokwenza izinto ubagcugcuzele bonyana babuze imibuzo . Sebenzisa iinkulumiswano ekusizeni ukukhomba iinqhema ezilamala lula . Ukujanyiswa kwemikhandlu yekhaya ye-AIDS kizo zoke iimfunda zekhaya zakamasipala . Ikoro yangeqadi iqatjhe pheze amakota amathathu wabasebenzi beSewula Afrika begodu yakha iingcenye ezimbili kwezintathu zesisomali kanye neendleko ze-R&D . ISewula Afrika itlhoga ikoro yangeqadi ephumelelako begodu esisa emakghonweni wokukhiqiza . Nanyana ikoro yezamabhizinisi iqalane khulu nokufumana inzuzo , kodwana amakhampani angeze akhula nangabe akasebenzi ebhodulukweni lokukhula kwamazinga wemisebenzi nengeniso . Umthetho ufuna bonyana ikoro yamabhizinisi itjheje indaba yokulingana emsebenzini , ukuthuthukiswa kwabanzima ngokomnotho , ibhoduluko , ukuthuthukiswa kwamakghono , imikhiqizo ekhiqizwa ngaphakathi kwenarha , ukuthuthukiswa kwamabhizinisi amancani , indima edlalwa mphakathi kwezehlalakuhle nezinye izinto ezimbalwa eziqakathekileko ezitholakala endaweni ethileko . Ebujamenobu beengcenye ezahlukahlukeneko , kuyirhuluphelo yesikhathi eside yawo woke amabhizinisi ukobana inarha ithuthuke ngokurhaba nokobana kuqatjhwe abantu abanengi . Itheyibula esekhasini langaphambili iyithempledi engasetjenziswako ukutjengisa iindawo eziqakathekileko zokwenza umsebenzi . Ama-KRA ahlahlelwe enziwa imisebenzi enamazinga womsebenzi woBUNGAKHO , IKHWALITHI , ISIKHATHI neeNDLEKO ezinanyathiselwe kiwo . Ama-KPI begodu nalabo abanesibopho semisebenzi eyahlukaneko kumele babuye batjengiswe ukwenzela ukobana kube nendlela yokwenza bonyana kube netjhejo leragelo phambili . Amaphuzu atjhiwo ngenzasi . Ngonobangela wokwahluka kwamaphrojekthi neentjhijilo ezingavela , isigabesi siqakatheke khulu . Umphumela wesigabesi umtlamo wesenzo esihleliweko esizokunikela isiqhema sephrojekthi umhlahlandlela egadangweni elinye nelinye lephrojekthi . Ukuhlukana ngaphakathi kumumatha umehluko phakathi kwabobaba , abomma , amasiko neenhlanga ukwenzela ukukhuthaza ukubekezelelana ngomehluko okhona ukwenzela bonyana ukuhlukanokha kungamunyathwa ngiwo umehluko lo . Lokhu kukukalukanela ukuhlanganyela ngokuzwana , ukwenzela bonyana ihlangano namkha umphakathi ukwazi ukusebenza ndawonye begodu nokwenza iminqophabo yokugcina . Umsekeli ngeemali kufanele atholwe akwazi ukurholela abatlhogomeli begodu akwazi ukubhadela iindleko zelori . Umsekeli ngeemali kufanele athole imali yokubhadela amaphasela wokudla . Itjhejuli ilithulusi elinesizo elizokusiza umkghonakalisi / abakghonakalisi ukutlama amagadango azokusetjenziswa ekuphumeleliseni umtlamo wewadi . Kungenzeka bonyana itjhejuli ye-CBP ihluke , kodwana lokho kuya ngomphakathi umkghonakalisi asebenzisana nawo . Isibonelo , endaweni yokulima yerhwebo , kungafuneka bonyana kube nemisebenzi eminengana eyenziwa ntambama ebandakanya umphakathi , kodwana emini kubanjwe imihlangano neKomidi yeWadi . Emphakathini lapho inengi labahlali lisebenza imisebenzi yephrofetjhini nanyana emabhizinisini , kungaba budisi ukuhlanganyela nomphakathi ngenca yamagandelelo womsebenzi . Kungadingeka bonyana abakghonakalisi benze umtlamo wokuhlangana amahlandla amabili ntambama ukwenzela bonyana bakwazi ukuhlanganisa abahlali . Okhunye ukutlama kungenziwa emini . Ubude besikhathi esifuneka malungana nokutlama bungaphungulwa nangabe icozululo lobujamo bendawo lenziwe ngokupheleleko nanyana alikenziwa ngokupheleleko ngombana lokhu kungonga isikhathi malungana naleliphuzu . Umkhandlu kamasipala ungathumela kobana wenzelwe imisebenzi ethileko kanye namandla maKomidi weWadi . Umkhandlu kufuze uqinisekise kobana kunamalungiselelo afaneleko ukwenzelela kobana amaKomidi weWadi enze imisebenzi yawo ngepumelelo . ImiHlahlandlela yokuJamisa nokuSebenza kwamaKomidi wamaWadi kaMasipala , iGazede kaRhulumende No 27699 , kuMgwengweni 2005-ImiHlahlandlela ihlathulula iKomidi yeWadi njengezibusako , ihlangano elulekako begodu kufanele ibekezele ekwenzeni imisebenzayo ngaphandle kokusaba , ukubinga namtjhana ukuzindla kanye nendima eqakathekileko edlalwa yiKomidi yeWadi njenge-ejenti emobhilayizako ekuqinisekiseni ukuhlanganyela komphakathi . Khathesi indima edlalwa burholi bendabuko ehlelweni elitjha lakarhulumende wemakhaya ayikahlathululwa ngokucacileko . Izakhiwo zendabuko zisaqakatheke khulu eendaweni zemakhaya . Isibonelo , KwaZulu-Natal ibandla lendawo loburholi bendabuko ladlala indima eqakathekileko ephrojekthini yamanzi nehlwengiso ebizwa i-Isulabasha / Mvunyane , kanye nekomidini yokuTlama ebizwa i-Maluti yesiYingi Nanyana iindima kanye nemisebenzi eyenziwa mabandla wabarholi bendabuko ingakabi ukucaca kuhle , kodwana kufuze kube nendima ayidlalako eendaweni zemakhaya . Asebenza njengabalethitjhuguluko begodu njengamangeno lokha nawufuna ukukhulumisana nomphakathi ngombana umphakathi uwahlonipha kwamanikelela begodu ayakghona ukukhulumisana nanyana ukuthonya abantu . UKUHLUKANA KUFANA NE-MOSAIC : boke abantu abenza ihlangano bafana neentokana ze-mosaic ; zoke zihlukene kodwana zihlanganisiwe njengento eyodwa . Ukusebenza ngepumelelo kwerherho laborhulumende abahlukahlukeneko kuyikulumo ekuphikisanwa ngayo khulu . Imikhakha ehlukeneko yombuso iyamelene begodu kufanele bonyana sifumane iindlela zokuqinisekisa bonyana isebenzisana ngepumelelo . Umtlamo lo uphakamisa bonyana kutjhugululwe indlela yokusebenza bonyana ingasabi ngileyo elinga ukufumana amalungiselelo amatjha wezakhiwo , ngombana yenza bonyana kungabi nokunzinza mayelana nokukhonjwa kanye nokurarululwa kobuthakathaka obuthileko bokuthintanisa namakghono . Umbuso kufanele wenze ngcono indlela olawula ngayo irherho , kufaka hlangana iimvumelwano zokulamula phakathi kwabomasipala besiyingi nabekhaya lapho kunebuyelelomsebenzi nanyana ukutjhayisana mayelana nokwabiwa kweembopho nemithombo . Iimfunda kufanele ziqalane nemisebenzi ezihlonyelwe ukuyenza begodu zithuthukise amakghono wazo ukwenzela bonyana zikwazi ukusekela nokwelusa aborhulumende bekhaya . Ibandlululo lokuhlukanisa abantu bemihlobo engafaniko litjhiye umphumela omumbi wokubekwa kwabantu eendaweni zokuhlala . Nanyana pheze imindeni eziingidi ezi-3.2 ihlomule kangaka ehlelweni elitjha lokwakhelwa izindlu , [ 1 ] begodu izenzelo nemithangalasisekelo ihlinzekelwe imiphakathi eminengi kangaka , kodwana yincani khulu ituthuko eyenziweko ekulungiseni ngobutjha ukungalingani okungenelelekokhu . Kobunye ubujamo , kutholakele bonyana imigomo yangemva komnyaka we-1994 iqinise ukuhlukaniswa kwabantu ngokweendawo zokuhlala ngokuhlalisa abantu abarhola imirholo ephasi eendaweni ezisemikhawulweni yamadorobha amakhulu . Umbuzo 2 Umtlolo lo wephrojekthi uyayiveza yini iminqopho ezuzekako , ecacileko neneempendulo zobulili , imiphumela begodu noneenkomba zokwenza umsebenzi okukhambisana nehlelo lezinto eziqothelwe yituthuko yeentjhabatjhaba na ? Indlela ehle yokuthoma ngeyokumema umuntu omdala kunabo boke esiqhemeni bonyana abelane ngezehlakalo zangaphambilini azikhumbulako . Sebenzisa isehlakalweso njengegadango lokuthoma lelandelaniso lezehlakalo . Thoma ngokudweba ilandelaniso lezehlakalo ephetjhaneni bese ulinamathisela ebodeni . Kuyasiza ukukhombela abantu bonyana batlole izehlakalo emakaradeni begodu balandelanise amakarada lawo ngokwezehlakalo . Lokha nangabe ukutlola kuba mraro , umkghonakalisi angasiza abahlanganyeli besiqhema ngokurekhoda izehlakalwezo ngokuzilandelanisa . Ilandelaniso lezehlakalo kufuze lihlale litjengiswa ukwenzela bonyana kufakwe nokhunye okungafakwa begodu lihlale lilirekhodi lomphakathi . Ngokusebenzisa amanothi wekhoso ukuthoma ekhasini lama-87 ukufikela ekhasini lama-92 ngezelela ngokunikela elinye ilwazi elingezelelako . Gandelela umehluko phakathi komkghonakalisi wewadi , umkghonakalisi kamasipala kanye nelunga leKomidi yeWadi begodu uqinisekise bonyana abahlanganyeli bayayizwisisa indima edlalwa yi-CBP kanye nokuhlobana kwayo namaKomidi weWadi . Iforamu le yabona ukuncipha kwamandlawo begodu yathoma yadosa iseluleko sangaphandle , isekelo begodu neemali . Ngomnyaka we-1992 babawa i-Corplan , okuyihlangano yomphakathi ( i-NGO ) edzimelele emphakathini etholakala e-East London , ukubasiza ngokutlama begodu nokwenza ngokwesiqunto iqhinga elifaneleko le-LED . Bakwazi ukuvala amatjhuba amanengi ngehlangothini lobutheknikhi begodu nomthamo kwezokuphathwa kweendaba zomphakathi ngaphakathi kwedorobha begodu nokufumaneka kweemali zeentjhabatjhaba . Libe khona yini ibandulo lokobana umhlahlandlela ofaka phakathi ubulili usetjenziswa njani kibo boke abasebenzi bokuphathwa kwephrojekthi na ? Bawa abahlanganyeli bafunde ifundo-sehlakalo esingenzasi bese bazijayeza ngeengaba ezahlukahlukeneko emfuziselweni wokulamula , hlathulula bona kwenzakalani esigabeni ngasinye ngokuqala esigabeni 5.6 samanothi . Ukwakha ibhoduluko elifanele ukubandakanyeka komphakathi . Isibonelo ngokunikela umphakathi amabizo wabantu abangathintwako kanye nemininingwana emayelana nemisebenzi efana nokuthuthwa kweenzibi , amatlinigi kanye namabizo weemphathiswa lezo okungathunyelwa kizo iinghonghoyilo . Malungana neenqhema ezingathandi okutloliweko , umhlahlandlela we-AICDD uveza indaba yokusetjenziswa kweembewu , amatje nanyana iingodo emakaradeni ukwenzela bonyana abahlanganyeli bakwazi ukubona ngamehlo bonyana umraro sewukhule kangangani . Lokhu kubekwa phezu kwekarada elikhombisa umnyaka . Iindima ezibustiriyothayiphu ezidlalwa bulili zizakuthuweleliswa begodu ongabhalansiko ongabhalansiko phakathi kwabobaba nabomma uzakweqiswa amehlo . Lokhu kuzakuba netjhayiswano elilandulako phezu kwemiphumela yephrojekthi . Ummongo oragela phambili womtlamo ngothi umzombe wokuziphendulela kufanele uqiniswe . Umphakathi kufanele uzwisise kuhle bonyana ngubani ekufanele aziphendulele mayelana nani . Kufanele kube namarherho enza bonyana boke abarholi emphakathini bakwazi ukuziphendulela mayelana nokuziphatha kwabo . Ngesikhathi sehlelo lokutlama bawa iIunga linye lesinye nesinye isiqhema ukobana liphendule munye wemibuzo , nangabe uneenqhema ezingaphezulu kwezintathu , iinqhema eziseleko kumele zingezelele izinto kwaphela ezingakenziwa esikhathini esigadungileko . AmaKomidi weWadi ajamela iinqhema neenrhuluphelo ezahlukahlukeneko . isibonelo , amanye amalunga angajamela isiqhema sababhadeli bamareyiti , amanye isiqhema sabomma , amanye iinqhema ezithuthukisako amanye iinhlangano zerhwebo . AmaKomidi weWadi kufanele asebenze ndawonye ukuqinisekisa bona imibono yomphakathi inendawo yokuzikhulumela nokobana imibono yawo ithathelwa ehloko ngendlela esiza umphakathi . Angekhe kwenzeke ukuphendula zoke iindingo , kodwana amaKomidi weWadi kufanele azame ukufuna umphumela ofaneleko nosiza umphakathi . AmaKomidi weWadi angazithola ebujameni obunamandla wenturhu lapho kunababambisani abanengi bakarhulumende wekhaya abasebenza nabo begodu babe namakghono wokuphungula namtjhana ukususa namtjhana ukurarulula inturhu ekuzobasiza bona benze imisebenzabo . Iphahla lomgomo lifuna ukuthuthukisa imiphakathi emajadu begodu ababandakanyeka ekulawuleni iintuthukiso zabo , batlewyime amalungelwabo benze neembopho zabo , banikele ezakhiweni zamazinga ahlukeneko zokuphatha , ngokutjhejekako ezingeni lewadi nelikamasipala . Inani elithileko labomasipala lizibumbele imigomo , nanyana amatlhatlha wemithetjhwanabo , mayelana namaKomidi wamaWadabo kibomasipala babo . Imigomo leyo ilawula ukuhlonywa , ukusebenza nokusebenza kwamaKomidi wamaWadi kibomasipala babo bese iveza kuhle iinkambiso neendlela ezizakusiza amaKomidi wamaWadi ukobana asebenze ngepumelelo . Imigomo kufanele itjhugululwe ngombana omunye nomunye umasipala uhlukile begodu kufanele azame ukwenza imigomo ekhambisana kuhle neendingo zawo ukuze usebenzele umphakathi kuhle . URHULUMENDE WEKHAYA UTHATHWA njengesikhundla sakarhulumende esibandamelene nabantu . Ukubandakanya umphakathi lokha nakukhonjwa iindingo begodu nalokha nakwenziwa imithetjhwana namahlelo , kuyindlela ephumelelisako yokuphendula iindingo zomphakathi . Njengobana kungenzeki bona woke umuntu angabandakanyeka bunqopha kodwana amaKomidi weWadi akhona njengehlangano yokulawula ukuthintanokhu . Ngalokho iinkambiso ziyadinga bona zikhanjiswe ngendlela ehlelekileko . Isahlukwesi siqale indima edlalwa makomidi wewadi eenkambisweni zokuthatha isiqunto somkhandlu nokobana ayizalisa bunjani indimawo yokwenza bona umkhandlu uziphendulele ekwenzeni nekuphenduleni iindingo zomphakathi . Amakhansela weWadi akhethwa njengamalunga womkhandlu kamasipala bavowudi abatloliswe kuwadi kungaba ngerherho lesilinganiso lehlangano , lawo-ke makhansela we-PR namtjhana njengamakhansela wewadi . Amalunga womphakathi namtjhana ajamele isiqhema esinerhuluphelo , njengehlangano yababhadeli bamareyiti . Indlela yokusebenza kwe-CBP ibonelela amaKomidi weWadi ngendlelakambiso yokutlama nokuphumelelisa okuhlelekileko ukudlala iindima kanye nokwenza iimbopho zawo . Ane-ajenda - umtlamo wewadi - begodu ukuphumelelisa kanye nokutjheja nokuhlunga umtlamo wewadi uwanikela indima eya phambili ekufuze ayidlale umnyaka woke . Ikhansela yewadi mgcinisihlalo nanyana mphathiintambo weKomidi yeWadi . Angakhetha loyo okhambisa umhlangano ukuyokufika engcenyeni yabajameli bekhansela nanyana elinye nelinye ilunga leKomidi yeWadi . IBatho Pele yindlela yokuziphatha komuntu hlangana nabanye , kumalungiselelo wokuthokoza amalungelwabo neendingo nokuzimisela kwabo ekubasizeni bona bangezelele ubungako beempilo zabo . IBatho Pele isibopho kwabanye abantu esizibuyelelako eminyakeni yokutlhogomela abantu . Ukusebenza njengomgcugcuzeli wokuzibandakanya komphakathi , khulukhulu ngokusebenzisa indlelakambiso ye-IDP kanye nendlelakambiso yokwabiwa kweemali zakamasipala . AmaKomidi weWadi akukafaneli aqabhele ukusebenza kwekhansela , lokhu kufaka hlangana ukunikela imilayelo eenkhulwini zomsebenzazo ekuwukuthatha iinqunto zomthethokambiso wekhansela . Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi ngiwo aphumelelisa khulu nangabe abelwe imisebenzi ukuya ngokwezakhiwo zawo nanyana iingcenye esele akhuthele kizo . Ngokwesibonelo , ilunga elijamele abalimi linganikelwa umsebenzi kwezokuLima , nanyana ilunga leKomidi yeWadi elingutitjhere lingasebenza kumsebenzi omayelana nezeFundo . Lokhu kanengi akuphumeleli kumawadi aphadlhaleleko . Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi anganikelwa umsebenzi ongaphezu kowodwa . Umnqopho we-IDP kuqinisekisa bonyana iintlabagelo ezikhona kumasipala zinqotjhiswa ekwethulweni kwamaphrojekthi nokobana amaphrogremu wamahlelo wetuthuko ngokuqakatheka kwawo kuyahlangatjezwana nawo ngokuya ngokwesivumelwano . I-IDP ilithulusi eliqakathekileko eliqinisekisa bonyana amaphrojekthi akhonjiweko begodu enziwa ngumasipala ayahlangana neendingo zomphakathi . Lokha nasifuna bonyana boke abantu bafumane imisebenzi ehloniphekileko , kufanele itjhejontangi lesikhathi esifitjhani kube kukhuphula imisebenzi nokukhuthaza abantu abatjha bonyana bangene ekorweni yabasebenzi , begodu kufanele sikhandele ukujanyiselelwa nanyana ukwehliswa kwamazinga wokusebenza akhona . Amanye amathuba womsebenzi kungenzeka abhalelise abantu ukobana baphile amaphilo abawafisako msinyana . Ukugcugcuzela ukuziphilisa ngendlela eragela phambili , kuqakathekile ukobana abantu nanyana imindeni , ngaphandle kokuqala umrholo , bakwazi ukufumana izenzelo ezifana nefundo yekhwalithi , itjhejo lezamaphilo nanyana iinthuthi zomphakathi . Begodu kuqakathekile bonyana umuntu olahlekelwa msebenzakhe akwazi ukufumana umsebenzi emahlelweni wemisebenzi yombuso nanyana eenkimini zemisebenzi yomphakathi . Ngaleziindlela , umgomo wombuso kanye negadango lomphakathi kuzizinto ezingezelela umzamo womuntu ekorweni yezemisebenzi , ngokunikela abantu abasebenzako kodwana abasatlhaga iindlela zokuziphilisa ngconywana neziragela phambili . Ukuthintana yikambiso ebudisi ngombana kubandakanya abantu ababuya emabhodukulweni ahlukahlukileko . Ngakho-ke ikhwalithi yokuthintana iqakathekile . Ukuthintana kubandakanya iingcenye ezimbalwa ezahlukahlukeneko . Ukuthintana kuneengcenye ezinengi ezinjengokukhuluma , ukutlola , ukukhulumisana nokulalela . IKomidi yeWadi ingakhuphula ukuthuthuka komnotho wekhaya ngokuhlala ubikela umphakathi njalo ngalokho okuzokuthonywa kanye namathuba . Angayelelisa amakhansela ngemiraro amalunga womphakathi afuna ukuzithomela amarhwebo amancani ahlangabezana nayo . Umtlamo womphakathi uqalene nombono namakghono / namathuba ingasi imiraro . Lokhu kutjho bonyana imitlamo yakhiwa ukuya ngokwemiphumela umphakathi ofuna bonyana inikelwe itjhejontangi , ingasi ukuya ngokwemiraro yawo umphakathi ofuna bonyana inikelwe itjhejontangi . UmThetho oHlongozwako ukhomba amaforamu ' ukuvumela iinhlangano ezihleliweko bonyana zisungule imithethokambiso begodu / nanyana zibe negalelo ekwakhiweni kwemithethokambiso , begodu zihlanganyele ekutjhejeni nekuhlungeni kanye neensungulweni zokwabiwa kweemali okuhlanganyelweko okunqotjhiswe ekuhlobaniseni amatjhejontangi womphakathi namahlelo wokusiswa kweemali ' . Kilesisigaba umlamuli uyazazisa bese ubeka imithetjhwana ezokulandelwa . Ukwenza umsebenzi ngokwehlelo kanye nokuhlaziya - lesi siteji lapho iphrojekthi yenzeka khona begodu sibandakanya ukuhlaziya okungatjhugulukiko nokuhlela kabutjha ukuqinisekisa iragelo phambili . Amakhansela weWadi anelungelo lokubamba imihlangano yomphakathi begodu ngiwo aphatha umhlangano . Amakhansela aletha ubudlelwana hlangana komphakathi kanye nomkhandlu begodu anokuziphendulela emawadinawo . AmaKomidi weWadi anikela ubudlelwana hlangana komphakathi kanye namakhansela . Ukuqinisekisa ukuhlanganyela okuseqophelweni eliphezulu neragelo phambili eliya esisombululweni umlamuli kufanele ahlole ubumajadu bobujamo besiqhema esinye nesinye : khetha indlela yokukhuluma ngeendaba , khetha bona ingabe imihlangano yeenqhema ehlukeneko iqakathekile nomlamuli akhona , qala eenkanukweni zesiqhema esinye nesinye kanye nokulindelweko , ingasi ubujamo ( ubujamo ababuthathako ) ; ukwenza koke okungenzeka bese kuyarekhodwa ; ukugcugcuzela ukuhlangana ; isibonelo : ukujanyiswa komtholapilo wokuthumela umuntu lapha angathola khona ipilo kanye neendlwana zokuzithumela ezitholakala kwaphela erenkeni yamateksi bese i-IDP elandelako ifaka iindlwana zokuthengisela kanye nomtholapilo osebenza ngokuzeleko ; ukwakha iindawo zesivumelwano . Umtlamo wewadi usisekelo sendlelakambiso ye-CBP esiqinisekisa ukuhlanganyela komphakathi ku-IDP . Kuqakathekile bonyana kube khona umtlolo wekhwalithi nozwakalako okhiqizwako ukwenzela bonyana umtlamo ukwazi ukusiza ekuphumeleliseni i-IDP . I-CBP ikhuthaza umphakathi bonyana uvele nemiphumela ngokwawo . Inqophe ukuthuthukisa imitlamo yokuthatha amagadango okungeyamambala ngokubeka iimbopho zokutlama emahlombe wezakhamuzi . . . Ngiwaphi amakghono wendawo yokubekeka kokuthile , ubuthakathaka , amathuba kanye neensabiso ( ezikhonjiswe ephepheni ledatha yebhoduluko neyendawo yokubekeka kokuthile ) ? Khetha abanye badlale indima yamalunga wekomidi , usihlalo , unobhala . Isibonelo : Abantu abama-54 bahlanganyele ekambisweni yokutlama . Iinqhema zifake hlangana abantu abasebenzako - abafukuzi nabasebenzi bema-ofisini , abazisebenzako , abangasebenziko , abomma abangakatjhadi abanabantwana . Ilunga leKomidi yeWadi , uMm . Mofolo kanye nekhansela lendawo , uMm . Smith , bakhambele yoke imihlangano esemthethweni . Abakghonakalisi begade kunguNom . Jones noMm . Mpefu . UNom . Mars ovela ku-dplg begade akhona begodu nomtlami wedorobha uNom . Zungu naye begade akhona . Amalogfremu mathebula azaliswa ngilabo abalawula iphrojekthi . Amathebula lawo anikela isirhunyezo semitlamo yephrojekthi . Ukuzaliswa kwamalogfremu kungaqaleka kuhlangahlangene kodwana kunikela ilwazi eliqakathekileko begodu liyazwisiseka . Aqakathekile mayelana nepumelelo yephrojekthi . Khonapho amalogfremu asiza ekwakheni ukubambelela kanye nokufunda kilabo ababandakanyeka ephrojekthini . Ukulawula iinkambiso - ikambiso ifaka hlangana ukutjheja kanye nokulinganisa ituthuko ukuqinisekisa kobana iminqopho yephrojekthi iyafinyelelwa , ukuveza ukwehluka kumtlamo ukuze kuthathwe igadango lokulungisa . Begodu kufaka hlangana amagadango wokukhandela imiraro engalindelwa , ukumadanisa ukusebenza kokuthoma kanye nokusebenza okuhleliweko / okutlanyiweko . Umtlamo womthetho kamasipala ugadangiselwa ukulethwa kweemphakamiso ezibuya emphakathini . Ngokuqinisekisa bona boke abahlanganyelako bandakanyekako ekambisweni ye-CBP ezehlakalweni ezikhambelanako ne-IDP ngokwezakhiwo neenkambiso njenganje ezifakiweko eendleleni ze-IDP ezimunyethwe epakaneni yomhlahlandlela ye-IDP ( kuhlekuhle umJameli weForamu ye-IDP kanye nePhrojekthi yeenqhema zalokho okwenziwako ) . I-KPI enye nenye kufanele ifake hlangana ukwenza okuqothelweko . ImiThetjhwana inikela iindlela ezimbalwa zokwenza okuqothelweko begodu ingasiza amaKomidi weWadi lokha nakahlola ukwenza okuqothelweko namtjhana abomqothwelwa . Iindlelezi zidzubhula ukuqakatheka kwebhajedi ekhona . Lokhu kungesibanga sokobana i-PMS ayizijameli ngokwayo . I-IDP kufanele ibe mhlahlo wokubeka ama-KPI . Lokha i-KPI ibeka abomqothelwa abangathembakaliko angeze yakghona ukuwahlangabeza . Ukuthuthukisa umbuso wendawo kugandelela ukutlhogeka kokwenza izinto pepenene , ngokuzibophelela , ngokubonisana , ukukghonakalisa ukubandakanyeka komphakathi namatjhebiswano . Kuqakakathekile ukutlola phasi yoke imininingwana yomtlamo ukwenzela bonyana kurekhodwe umbono womphakathi begodu kuqinisekiswe nokobana umtlamo lowo uyakghona ukusetjenziswa baphathi abasezingeni eliphezulu nabanye abanikeli ngemisebenzi . Umasipala kufanele abonane nomphakathi ngaphambi kokuthuthukiswa kweenkomba zokwenza bese avumele umphakathi ahlanganyele nekambiso yokubuyekeza . Iphrojekthi enye nenye ayifani nenye begodu inesede yayo yeentjhijilo nezinto okumele zitjhejwe . Umtlamo ongafaniko neminye ngebanga lalokho uyadingeka ukukghonakalisa ukuqedelelwa kwephrojekthi enepumelelo . Ngaso leso sikhathi itjhejo elikhethekileko kumele linikelwe ukuqinisekisa ukulingana kobulili ekutlameni iphrojekthi . Nikela ipendulo nombono ekambisweni yomkhandlu ukuqinisekisa ukwethulwa kweensetjenziswa . Lo msebenzi owenziwa ngendlela ebonakalako ngokukhamba endaweni leyo . Umkghonakalisi / abakghonakalisi nguye orhola ikhambo leenyawo nababiki abayisika abangaba sithandathu abavela emphakathini . Lokhu kufuze kuthathe isikhathi esingaba li-iri elilodwa nanyana ama-iri amabili ngombana abantu angeze babanaso nesikhathi isikhathi sokukhamba ngeenyawo ukudlula lapho . Imiphumela - ibe yini imiphumela yento oyenzako ? Amalunga wekomidi ngayinye angaba nomsebenzi / iphothfoliyo ekhethekileko ukuwasiza ukujamela umphakathi . Ngaleyondlela , amalunga anendima ecacileko ayidlalako ngaphakathi ewadini begodu afunyana ilemuko bekazwisise iindaba ezimayelana namaphothfoliyo wawo . Amalunga wamaphothfoliyo avela kiwo woke amawadi , ( aneembopho zokwenza umsebenzi / amaphothfoliyo efanako ) ahlangana neminyango yakamasipala efaneleko kanye namakomidi wamaphothfoliyo ukubonisana ngeendaba ezithinta amaphothfoliyo wawo . Umphakathi weSeymour bewuzibandakanye emarherhweni abanzi wamaphrojekthi wetuthuko solo kwangomnyaka we-1992 koke kunezinga elehlukileko lepumelelo . Iphrojekthi eqakathekileko neyathenjiswako solo kwangomnyaka we-1992 ihlathululwe ngenzasi . Nanyana kungasiwo woke amaphrojekthi akhombisa bonyana akhe aba nokuzuza bunqopha kwezomnotho , kumele abonakale njengalawo anikela umsebenzi begodu nerhelebho ebantwini abanethemba lokungaqatjhwa namkha abenethemba lokungathoma iphrojekthi yokuzithuthukisa . Khumbula bona ibhajedi ingafuna imininingwana ezeleko namtjhana engaphasi kodwana lokhu kuya ngokobana inikelwa bani . Abasekeli ngeemali angeze bafune imininingwana efanako neyesiqhema sephrojekthi . Okukholwekako : lokhu kutjho bonyana sineendlela zokuqinisekisa ( ukuba khona kwemininingwana , nokwenzeka ngesikhathi , njll ) ukobana ayatholakala begodu asebenziseka lula . Umthethokambisi ngomnyaka we-1994 bewuthi urhulumende uzokunikela ngeemali iindleko zemali zokusungula imisebenzi emitjha kanye nezakhiwo , ngesikhathi sokutjheja kanye neentengo zizokuvalwa basebenzi . Ngomnyaka we-2001 , kwavunyelwana kobana ubuncani bakhona imisebenzi esisekelo izokunikelwa kiyo yoke imindeni . Lokhu kufaka hlangana ukuthuthwa kweenzibi , amanzi , ukuhlanzeka kwendawo kanye negezi . Ituthuko ehle sele yenziwe ukuphakela ngamanzi kanye negezi . UmThetho weenHlangano zakaMasipala we-1998 kanye nomThetho wamaRherho kaMasipala we-2000 usekela umThethosisekelo begodu utjengise ukuqakatheka kokuhlanganyela begodu unikele nephahla lomthetho lokujamisa amaKomidi weWadi . Amalunga wamaKomidi wamaWadi kufanele azijayeze ngemiThetho le . Isibonelo , umThetho wamaRhelo kaMasipala we-2000 wendlala iindlela zokubusa njengokuthuthukisa kwemiTlamo yokuThuthuka ngokuZeleko ( etjhiwo ngehla ) kanye namaRherho wokuLawula ukwEnza . UMBUZO 3 . Ziyini iindlela zekambiso eziqakathekileko zokutjheja nokuhlungwa ezidingekako ukuqinisekisa ukwethulwa kwesetjenziswa , begodu khuyini amakghonakalo wenzuzo okungalinganiswa ngawo iragelo phambili ? AmaKomidi weWadi angasiza amakomidi ngokuwanikela ilwazi leenhloko ezithize nangabe kunesidingo . Kunefuneko yokwenza ngcono ukusebenza ngepumelelo kweensetjenziswa ezivezwe ngaphezulu , ngokuzwisisa ubujamo obukhona bokuloba nokuzuza . Ngaphezu kwalokho , kufanele kugandelelwe khudlwana indaba yokusekelwa kwamabhizinisi amancani , yokugcugcuzela umbuso nekoro yangeqadi bonyana bathenge ipahlabo nemisebenzi emafemini amancani , neyokuthuthukiswa kwabaphathi abaziimfundiswa zabomma abanzima . Irherho lezomnotho elikhula ngokurhaba begodu elihlukako libe ziinkoro ezitja lizokuvula amathuba wamafemu wabantu abanzima namabhizinisi amancani , begodu lokho kuzokugcugcuzela ukukhula komnotho ozuzisa boke abantu . ISewula Afrika ayinasandla ekukhutjhweni kwerhasi esilaphaza ibhoduluko nebanga ukutjhisa kwaphela - kodwana imiphumela yokutjhugutjhuguluka kobujamo betlayimethi mayelana nezamaphilo , ukuziphilisa , amanzi nokudla inegalelo elimbi nelingalinganiko ebantwini abatlhagako , khulukhulu abomma nabantwana . Nanyana silinga ukuzijayeza amatjhuguluko la , kodwana amabubulo nemindeni kufanele aphungule igalelo elimbi analo phezu kwebhoduluko . Lokhu kuzokutlhogeka amatjhuguluko anomthelela omkhulu mayelana nendlela abantu abaphila nabasebenza ngayo . IMITHETHO EJANYISIWEKO YAKARHULUMENDE WEMAKHAYA ijanyiselwe ukwenza bonyana iSewula Afrika ikwazi ukusebenza ngendlela enesizo nezakwazi ukuqalelela izakhamuzi ngemisebenzi esisekelo nangendlela ezakwazi ukwenza ngcono amaphilwazo kwezomnotho nezehlalakuhle . Njengombana urhulumende wemakhaya aliphiko lombuso eliphakela iinsetjenziswa emphakathini , kuqakathekile ukuqinisekisa bonyana imiphakathi iyasekela begodu iyahlanganyela . Isahlukwesi sendlala iminqopho neenkambisolawulo zomtlamo womphakathi ( i-CBP ) . Abahlanganyeli abenze imida emibili baqalane . Umuda omunye awube ngu-A bese kuthi omunye ube ngu-B . Bawa abahlanganyeli benze ubungani nabantu abaqalene nabo . Bawa boke abo-B baphumele ngaphandle . Ukubuthelelwa kwelwazi elingezelelako emalungeni womphakathi libuthelelwa bakghonakalisi kanye nabajameli bomphakathi . Lokhu kungathatha amalanga ambalwa nanyana kwenziwe ngeengaba ezithile , kodwana kufuze kwenziwe ngaphakathi kwesikhathi esitlanyiweko . IsAhluko 3 seyame phezu komHlahlandlela 2 womTlamo womPhakathi ne-IDP : UmHlahlandlela wabaKghonakalisi kanye nomHlahlandlela wabaThathiinqunto owakhiwe yi-AICDD nemiSebenzi yokuThuthukisa . Amatjhuguluko wesikhathi eside nokurhwebelana kweenarha zephasi loke kanye nokusisa abumba ngobutjha ihlelo lezomnotho wephasi nepolotiki yeentjhabatjhaba . Okuqakatheke khulu kilamatjhuguluko kubonakala kwamahlelo wezomnotho akhula ngokurhaba , khulukhulu i-China , i-India ne-Brazil . Pheze ngemva kwamakhulumnyaka amathathu wokwehluka , ukungalingani phakathi kweenarha kuyaphunguka . Ukuhlala kwabantu emadorobheni kanye nokwakhiwa kwamabubulo e-China ne-India kungenzeka kwenze bonyana kube nefuneko ekulu yemithombo yemvelo eminyakeni elitjhumi nanyana engaphezulu . Ukubonakala kwabasebenzisipahla abanengi eenarheni ezithuthukako kuzokunabisa amathuba wawo woke amahlelo wezomnotho . Umzabalazo olwisana nebandlululo ekuthomeni wabe umayelana nokwakhiwa komphakathi ongabandlululani ngokobuhlanga nangokobulili , lapho boke abantu banamalungelo alinganako khona . Nanyana kube netuthuko enzinzileko ukusukela emnyakeni we-1994 , kodwana iSewula Afrika isesemphakathi ohlukeneko , begodu obandlululana khulu ngokobuhlanga . Ukubandlululana kwabantu ngokobuhlanga nangokobuzwe kwandile begodu ukungaphathwa kwabantu ngendlela efanako kusaragela phambili . Umleyo weenhlangano wenarha kanye namatjhuguluko wayo anabileko wezomnotho nehlalakuhle usizile ekuqedeni ubuhlanga kancani kancani kancani , kodwana ituthuko ayikaneli begodu ayikangeneleli ngokwaneleko . Nanyana kunetuthuko eyenziweko mayelana nokwenza ngcono amaphilo wabomma ; kodwana ukungaphathwa kwabantu ngendlela efanako , ummoya wokulawula kwabobaba babodwa nokungafumani ifundo yekhwalithi efaneleko kusaragela phambili . Umtlamo lo usebenza ngamaphuzu la ngokupheleleko , begodu uyabona bonyana amatjhejontangi aqakathekileko anjengefundo nanyana ukuthuthukiswa kweendawo zemakhaya azokuba negalelo elikhulu kwamanikelela kibomma abatlhagako . UmTlamo wokuThuthukiswa kweliZwe Loke uzokujamisa ngomumo ukwabiwa kwemithombo eminyakeni ematjhumi amabili ezako , kodwana angeze wabeka izabelo zeemali zomnyaka . Indlela ehle yokwakha imithombo yokuphumelelisa umtlamo lo ngeyokuthuthukisa umnotho ngokurhaba . Lokha umnotho nawukhula ngamaphesende angaphezu kwamahlanu ngomnyaka , ingeniso yombuso kanye neenzuzo zamafemu wangeqaqi zizakuba ngaphezu kokubuyelelwa kabili eminyakeni ema-20 ezako . Ukuhlanganisa iimali ezitholakalako zokusiza ezisetjenziselwa iminqopho eyahlukeneko zibe sikhwama esisodwa seemali ezisetjenziswa ekuhleleni ngobutjha ukufakwa kwabantu eendaweni zokuhlala . Ukubandakanyeka kwezakhamuzi okhunye godu kusiza ekuqinisekeni bona umbuso unokuziphendulela begodu wenza umsebenzawo . Ukuba zizakhamuzi akupheleli ekukhetheni iimphathiswa zomphakathi . Iimphathiswa zomPhakathi nazo angeze zalindelwa bona zithathele izakhamuzi iinqunto ezifaneleko nangabe izakhamuzi azibatjeli ngeendingo zabo . Izakhamuzi zazi kuhle bona zifunani begodu kuqakathekile ukobana zizibandakanye ekwenzeni iinsombululo zeendingwezi . Izakhamuzi zidinga ukusebenza ngokubambisana nombuso ukobana sisizwe etuthukweni . Lapha kulapha amaKomidi wamaWadi angina khona njengombana adlala indima eqakathekileko ekambisweni yokukghonakalisamayelana nokubandakanyeka komphakathi . Imihlahlandlela yathuthukiswa ngombana abomasipala abanengi bebalifuna ilwazi elinengi elibahlahlako ngokuthi amaKomidi weWadi ahlonywa njani . Imihlahlandlela le iphakamisa iindlela abomasipala bangahlangabezana neemfuneko zomThetho wezAkhiwo zakaMasipala , we-1998 kanye nomThetho wamaHlelo wakaMasipala we-2000 . Ukwenza ngcono ukuzibophelela okuvela kubaphathi nabadosiphambili bamaphrogremu nokusebenza njengesiqhema ukwenzela ukwenza ngcono irhubhululo nokuphathwa kwerhubhululo eliphumelelisako . Abomasipala baneenkareko ezahlukeneko begodu bangathola bonyana baphalisana babodwa . Irherho lokuphathwa kokwenziwa komsebenzi kumele ingenise iinkareko ezinengi njengombana zingezikghonako ukwenza ngepumelelo begodu zingezigcinekako . Khonapho kuzakuba neendingo ezehlukileko emphakathini wemakhaya kulabo babomasipala abasemadorobheni . Iinlinganiso zokubeletha kwamaSewula Afrika amakhuwa zathoma ukwehla eminyakeni ye-1950 neminyakeni ye-1960 , kwathi iinlinganiso zokubeletha kwama-Afrika zathoma ukwehla eminyakeni yokuphela yangemva komnyaka we-1970 neminyakeni yokuthoma yangemva kewe-1980 . Ezehlakalwenezi zombili , ukwenyuka kwezinga labantu abahlala emadorobheni namazinga angcono wefundo kwaba zizinto ezihlukanisako . Namhlanjesi , isitjhaba seSewula Afrika sikhula ngephesende linye ngomnyaka begodu kulindeleke bonyana ngomnyaka wee-2030 , lizabe likhule ngephesende elili-0.5 ngomnyaka . AmaKomidi weWadi amleyo wehlangano ( kanye neenhlangano zababambisani ) begodu kufuze ajanyelwe eForamini yabaJameli be-IDP kanye nesiqhemeni semisebenzi ye-IDP . Nawuzwa ngomutjhwana othi , iRherho lokuLawula ukwEnza ingabe kutjho ukuthini kuwe ? Umbuso wentando yenengi utlhoga ukuzibandakanya ngokwedemokhrasi ngokwelizwi labo boke abantu emphakathini abakumgomo neendlela zekambiso okuphatha . Lokhu kufuna indlela evulekileko yokuthatha iinqunto nendlela yokubonisana nabantu . Ifuna godu nokobana izakhamuzi ezikghona ukwahlulela , ukuzibandakanya kukulumo-pendulwano enamandla eempilweni zabo nelemuko leentjhijilo ezisemiphakathinazo kanye namakghono nelwazi bathola iinsombululo zeentjhijilwezi . Ukuzibandakanya kuyingcenye eqakathekileko yokuphatha okuhle njengombana kuvumela ukukhamba kuhle kwelwazi phakathi kwezakhamuzi kanye nabadosiphambili abakhethiweko nokuziphendulela . Kunikela godu nelizwi kuzakhamuzi ezithintwe khudlwana mgomo wombuso . Ukwakha umthangalasisekelo wokuthenga irhasi yemvelo encibilikisiweko nokungezelela ihlolo yokufumana imatheriyali engakasetjenzwa yerhasi yangekhaya ( kufaka hlangana ukufunisisa ngezabelo ze-shale nedwala lamalahle le-methane ) ukuhlukanisa ukuhlanganiswa kwamandla weembaseli nokuphungula ukukhutjhwa kwekhabhoni . Esiqhemeni senu esincani cocani ngeendlela lezo okumele umnyango lo usebenzise iBatho Pele ukuze sizuze ukwenzelwa umsebenzi ngendlela eqalwe ngurhulumende . Ungathathi ihlangothi - lisa imibono ikhulunywe mantanzi bese ungezelela yakho . Amanye amatshwayo wepilo yomphakathi akhambisana neenkhathi ezithize zomnyaka , njengamaphetheni wamalwelwe , ukusetjenziswa kwabasebenzi , imizombe yezelimo , kanye nokondleka . Lemisebenzi emibili elandelako ithuthukisa ukuzwisiswa kweenqhelo ezenzeka ngeenkhathi ezithize zomnyaka kanye neenqhelo eziragela phambili . Ngokuhlathulula kabanzi lamaphetheni kanye neenqhelo , abatlami bayakghona ukubonela phambili ezinye izehlakalo begodu bahlalise imitlamo namaqhinga wabo ngendlela efaneleko . Ingcenye yamaSewula Afrika ahlala eendaweni zemakhaya yehle pheze ngamaphuzu amaphesende alitjhumi ukusukela ngowe-1994 . Namhlanjesi , pheze amaphesende ama-60 wesitjhaba ahlala eendaweni zemadorobheni . Ngokukhambisana namatjhuguluko wephasi loke , ukusuka kwabantu beendawo zemakhaya bayokuhlala emadorobheni amakhulu kulindeleke bonyana kuragele phambili , begodu ngaphambi kokuphela komnyaka wee-2030 , pheze amaphesende ama-70 wesitjhaba azabe ahlala emadorobheni . I-Gauteng kanye namadorobha amakhulu iThekwini neKapa kuziimphande zamadorobha amakhulu ezikhula msinyana khulu , begodu lokho kwenza bonyana kube nesidingo sokutlama nokunikela ngeensiza ezisisekelo . Hlathulula bonyana isigaba esilandelako sibandakanya icozululo elingeneleleko kanye nokuhlanganiswa kwelwazi elibuthelelwe esiGabeni soku-1 . Ama-KPI abuyekezwa qobe ngonyaka ngumasipala njengengcenye yekambiswayo yokubuyekeza kokwenziwa . Nangabe umasipala wenza itjhuguluko ku-IDP yakhe kufanele godu abuyekeze ama-KPI wakhe . Umbiko obuyako obuya emphakathini ngamaKomidi weWadi kufanele uthathelwe ehloko nakubuyekezwa ama-KPI . Ngalendlela umphakathi uyithatha njengento ethembekileko i-PMS . Zelimo : Ingabe kube khona amatjhuguluko malungana nemihlobo yesivuno esitjaliweko ? Kubayini ? Ingabe kube khona amatjhuguluko malungana namanani wefuyo eminyakeni egadungileko ? Kubayini ? Ingabe abe khona amatjhuguluko malungana nokufumaneka kwendawo yokudlisela ifuyo nanyana malungana nobukhona bendawo yokudlisela ifuyo ? Ngubani okwazi ukuyifumana ? Ukubotjhwa-sikhathi : lokhu kutjho bonyana umphumela olinganiswako unelanga eliqothelweko . Iphrojekthi iyazibophelela ukufikelela emnqopheni ngelanga lokugcina elibekwe ngaphambili . Ukuqeda indlela yokusebenza ngokwesijoni esipholiseni . Isiqunto sokuqeda indlela yokusebenza ngokwesijoni esipholiseni , yokubalekela umlando waso wesihluku , kwaba mnqopho oqakathekileko wetjhuguluko ngemva komnyaka we-1994 . Ukusetjenziswa ngobutjha kweendlela zesijoni sipholisa eminyakeni embalwa egadungileko kubhalelwe kufumana ihlonipho enengi esipholiseni nanyana kufumana iinlinganiso eziphezulu zokuthweswa imilandu kwezelelesi . Eqinisweni kube nomthelela emigurugurwini . Isipholisa kufanele silise iindlela zokusebenza ngokwesijoni begodu siphathwe ngendlela ezakwazi ukusiza umphakathi ngendlela ephrofetjhinali . Umasipala we-ABC ulungiselela i-IDP yakhe . Ikhansela nekomidi yewadi batjele umphakathi bona umhlangano uzokuba mzukwana amalanga ama-20 kuVelabahlinze nge-iri le-7 ntambama eHolweni yeDorobha eliKhulu . Isaziso sathunyelwa iimveke ezimbili ngaphambili kanye namaphuzu aqakathekileko okuzokukhulunywa ngawo emhlanganweni , amaphuzu aqakathekileko we-IDP . Emhlanganweni ikhansela lewadi lanikela ihlathululo efitjhazana ye-IDP bese labawa iimpendulo neemphakamiso . Umhlangano wavumelana bona iinqhema ezinerhuluphelo kufanele zihlangane ukukhulumisana nge-IDP neemfunda zokubusa bese zibuye evekeni elandelako ukuletha umbiko obuyako . Boke abantu emhlanganweni bavumelana ngelanga nesikhathi . ImiThetjhwana ithi ama-KPI kufanele alinganiseke , anqophe , abe nomnqopho begodu abe mafitjhani . Enzeka eensebenzini nemayunidini wokuphathwa kwakamasipala , ebunyeni bakamasipala omunye nomunye kanye nomnikeli womsebenzi umasipala enze naye isivumelwano . Abantu bahlanganyela ngokutjelwa ngesiqunto esithethweko nanyana ngalokho esele kwenzekile . Kubandakanya izaziso zesiqhema esisodwa ezenziwa baphathi nanyana baphathi bephrojekthi ngaphandle kokulalela iimpendulo zabantu . Njengombana indlelakambiso yokutlama isungulwa begodu ihlanganiswe ngumasipala , i-CBP ilihlanganyelo lewadi nomasipala . Umtlamo ngewewadi , elijanyelwa yiKomidi yeWadi . Umasipala unikela amakhanselakhe wewadi kanye namakomidi amandla wokukghonakalisa indlelakambiso yokutlama ezakwenza bonyana ikomidi elinye nelinye likghone ukufumana igunya lokusebenza ngesikhathi sokuphatha kwalo . Ukukhomba kanye nokusebenzisana malungana neensombululo zeendingo namatjhejontangi womphakathi kusiza amakhansela namaKomidi weWadi bonyana akwazi ukwenza imisebenzi yawo .
