UMTHETHO WEENHLANGANO ZAKAMASIPALA , WE-1998 ufuna abomasipala bona babuyekeze woke umsebenzi owenziwa ngumasipala njalo ngonyaka . Isahluko 6 somThetho wamaRherho kaMasipala , we-2000 unikela iphahla lomthetho elimayelana nokulawulwa kokwenza kwabomasipala . Ilawulo lokwenza kufanele libe yingcenye yomTlamo oThuthukiswe ngokuZeleko . Ukulalelwa kwebhajedi kuqiniseka bonyana iindingo ze-MFMA , zomnyaka we-2003 zifezakele ngokuya kokuhlanganyela komphakathi ekambisweni yokwenziwa kwebhajedi . Ukulalelwa kwebhajedi kamasipala kuvumela amaKomidi wamaWadi bonyana ahlanganyele ekuthuthukisweni kwebhajedi kamasipala . Kukwenzanjani ukuphatha iphrojekthi ? Ukutjheja imibiko ngokwethulwa kweensetjenziswa - I-MFMA idinga abomasipala bona baveze imibiko emayelana neragelo phambili leendawo zabo . Imibiko le inikela imiphakathi iqhinga lokutjheja ituthuko . Ngesikhathi seenkulumiswano ngebhajedi , amalunga womkhandlu , ngamaKomidi weWadi , kufanele aluleke umphakathi ngomphumela ongahle ube khona ngeenqunto eziqakathekileko . Kunesidingo esiqinileko ukobana zombili iindlela , ukubusa ngokubambisana begodu nokusebenzisana hlangana kwengcenye zakarhulumende ezahlukeneko . Iinkambisolawulo zitlanyelwe ukuqiniseka ukunikela amandla ihlangano yezebhoduluko ukobana ikwazi ukunikela umthangalasisekelo kamasipala indlela yokusebenzisana ngokwehlangano . Iinzibi endaweni yangekhenu azithathwa njalo . Izakhamuzi zendawo sezilile kanengi kukhansela lakamasipala , nanyana kunjalo ikinga iragela phambili . Umasipala naye uthi esinye isizathu kukobana izakhamuzi azibhadeli iimali kanye nentela begodu lokhu kuthinta ukuphakelwa kwemisebenzi , khulukhulu njengombana ezinye iindawo zedorobha kuziindawo ezibhadela kuhle begodu umasipala ubona kuqakathekile ukuqinisekisa kobana iindawo lezo ziphakelwa kuhle ngemisebenzi . Amarherho abuthakathaka nangasebenzi kuhle enza bonyana kube budisi ukutjho bonyana ngubani onesibopho , begodu lokho kuvamise ukubangela bonyana kungabi nomuntu oziphendulelako . Umtlamo lo uveza isibonelo sokobana kwenzekani nangabe kutholakala bonyana amanzi wedorobheni akaseleki . Iimbikiindaba zisola uNgqongqotjhe wezaManzi . Umphakathi usola usodorobha . Usodorobha usola ihloko yemisebenzi yamanzi . Ihloko yemisebenzi yamanzi isola usonjiniyera wezobuthekniki . Usonjiniyera uthi isabelo seemali zetjhejo siquntwe eminyakeni emithathu egadungileko begodu njenganje amanzi akaseleki . Ihloko yezeemali kumasipala ithi isabelo seemali saquntwa ngombana iindleko zabasebenzi besele zidlula iindleko zetjhejo . Usodorobha uveza bonyana isakhiwo semirholo vane iHlangano yaboRhulumende bemaKhaya yeSewula Afrika ( i-SALGA ) ikhulumisane ngaso ezingeni lombuso welizwe loke . I-PMS ithi abomasipala bangakhetha ukungazibandakanyi kileziimvumelwano nangabe ziyababhalela . Begodu balinge amanye amaqhinga angabasebenzela , njalonjalo . Abarholi bomphakathi bajamele izakhamuzi mayelana neendaba ezizithinta khulu begodu kufanele zithathelwe phezulu . Abarholaba banesibopho sokuqinisekisa bonyana izenzo zokuhlaba nokuphikisa zenziwa ngehlonipho nangokuvuthwa . Nanyana kwesinye isikhathi abarholi bomphakathi bajamela kwaphela iinrhuluphelo ezithileko emphakathini obanzi nongafaniko , kodwana nabo bayingcenye eqakathekileko yombuso wentando yenengi onamandla netjisakalo obandakanya abantu abazithuthukisa bona ngokwabo . Isivumelwano namtjhana indlela enzinze ekarekweni - lendlela iqala inturhu njengengcenye yobudlelwana bobuntu . Indlela le ayiqali bona ngubani ' olungileko ' nokobana ngubani ' ongakalungi ' ebujameni benturhu kodwana ifuna isisombululo esilisizo kizo zoke iinqhema . Lendlela ilwela isisombululo SOKUTHUMBA / THUMBA isebenzisa isisombululo mraro kanye nokukhulumisana begodu iqale ekusebenzeni ngenturhu ngendlela erholela emphumeleni omuhle kibo boke . Lapho kufanele khona mayelana nemibuzo engaphezulu , buza bonyana ingabe akhona amatjhuguluko abe nomthelela ohlukileko eenqhemeni ezahlukeneko nokobana kube matjhuguluko anjani ( sizakunikela ilwazi elingezelelako elimayelana nokuhluka kwezehlalakuhle ) . Umbono karhulumende wokuthuthukisa urhulumende wendawo kukwakha umasipala osebenzisa ngendlela efaneleko iimali okhambisana nokuhlangabezana neendingo zehlakaluhle , zomnotho neendingo ezisisekelo zabantu babo ngendlela yokuhlanganyela neneragelo phambili . Indima yokuthuthukisa urhulumende wendawo ifakwe kuhle ngaphakathi komthethosisekelo begodu nangaphakathi kwemitlolo ehlukeneko yemigomo , okucocwa ngayo kilesisahluko . Ngokubona kwakaNom . Nkosi kukobana abantu emphakathini bayazikhukhumeza begodu abamcabangeli . Umphakathi wona ubona sengathi uNom . Nkosi ubukhali begodu uyazikhakhazisa . Imihlangano yomphakathi - la maforamu alisizo wokwabelana ngemibono nelwazi . Imikhandlu ingabiza umhlangano ngeendaba ezithize namtjhana ukubika ngomphumela womhlangano namtjhana umnyanya ; ngokunikela ngombiko wangamalanga emphakathini omayelana nemihlangano yomkhandlu kanye nemihlangano yeKomidi leWadi nakungasinjalo nekhansela lewadi , ehlangothini leKomidi yeWadi , angabiza umhlangano ukuzokubika ngesihloko esithize ukuze athole imibono yabahlali ngendaba ethize . Iphrojekthi msebenzi omunye nomunye owenziwako wokuthuthukisa umsebenzi namtjhana umkhiqizo hlangana nesikhathi esithileko esitjhiwoko . Ngenye indlela kufanele ilethe itjhuguluko namtjhana ingezelele ubugugu . Iphrojekthi -inesikhatjhana esincani kunokobana ibe yinto eyenzeka safuthi , inebhajedi ehlathululiweko begodu ivame ukuba msebenzi wesikhathi esisodwa . Imibuso angeze yajamela iindingo zazo zoke izakhamuzi . Lokha izakhamuzi naziyokuvowuda zivowidela ihlangano eziyithandako ukobana ijamele kuhle lokho ezikufunako , abantu bahlukene , begodu baneendingo ezihlukeneko . Nalokha umbuso ungazama njani akukghoneki bona ufikelele kizo zoke izakhamuzi . Ukubandakanyeka kwezakhamuzi kungasiza ukuvala isikhalesi njengombana bazakungezelela emizameni yombuso ngokwabo begodu ngalindlela baveze imizwabo . Kungebangeli amaKomidi wamaWadi ahlonyiwe ukuze asize umbuso ekwenzeni isiqiniseko sokobana izakhamuzi ziyanikela ekuthatheni iinqunto ezibathintako . IVikelomalungelo lifaka hlangana amalungelo wezemnotho nezehlalakuhle , njengelungelo lokuphila ipilo ehle ebhodulukweni , ukukghona ukufunyana indlu ekulingeneko , ukukghona ukuphakelwa ngemisebenzi yokunyangwa begodu nokuba nokudla kanye namanzi aneleko . Ikombamphandemitato yeembikiindaba - imirhatjho yomphakathi wekhaya kanye namaphephandaba wekhaya amithombo eqakathekileko yokusabalalisa ilwazi . Yenza isiqiniseko sokobana unemininingwana yokuthintana yomrhatjho wekhaya nokobana uhlale uthintana nabo njalo . IsAhluko 1 nesAhluko 4 zinikela ilwazi mayelana nemihlobo yabakghonakalisi ababandakanywa ekwakhiweni kweNdlela yokuSiza ukuPhumelelisa i-CBP kanye nababambisani abahlukeneko ekufuze bathintwe . Ukuba zizakhamuzi ezikhutheleko nabatjhotjhozeli bezehlalakuhle kuyafuneka ekuphumeleliseni intando yenengi kanye netuthuko . Umbuso akukafaneli bonyana usebenzele abantu bawo kwaphela - kufanele bonyana usebenze nabantu bawo , ngokusebenzisana nezinye iinhlangano ukunikela amathuba wokuthuthukisa yoke imiphakathi . Qinisekisa imibono yomphakathi begodu nokuvuselelwa kwamaqhinga wokusebenza ukwenzela bonyana kubonakalise okulindelweko komphakathi wekhaya . Ama-KPI kufanele abuyekezwe ngumasipala qobe mnyaka njengengcenyakhe yokubuyekeza ikambiso yokwenza umsebenzi begodu nangabe umasipala utjhugulula i-IDP yakhe kufanele godu atjhugulule nama-KPI wakhe . Imibiko ebuya kumaKomidi wamaWadi kufanele itjhejwe nakubuyekezwa ama-KPI . Ikambiso le yenza isiqiniseko sokobana kuba khona ukuziphendulela begodu ithuthukisa ukuzwana phakathi komphakathi nomkhandlu . isebenzela godu nokwenza isiqiniseko sokobana ama-PMS umphakathi uwathatha njengento eliqiniso ethembekako . Ukukhutjhwa kwekhabhoni-dayoksayidi nezinye iinrhasi ezisilaphaza ibhoduluko nezibanga ukutjhisa kutjhugutjhugulula ubujamo betlayimethi yephasi , begodu lokho kuba nemiphumela emimbi ebantwini abatlhagako . Amazinga wokutjhisa akhuphukako , ukuna kwezulu ngeenkhathi ezingakajayeleki kanye nezehlakalo ezingasizihle zobujamo bezulu kungenzeka zikhuphuke khulu e-Afrika , begodu lokho kungabangela ukurhatjheka okungezelelweko kwamalwele weenarha ezitjhisa khulu kanye nokulahleka ( kwabantu nemali ) ngenca yesomiso kanye neenkhukhula . Ukutjhugutjhuguluka kobujamo betlayimethi kunamandla wokuphungula ukukhiqizwa kokudla nokuba khona kwamanzi adliwako , begodu lokho kungaba nemiphumela yokufuduka kwabantu kanye namazinga wokungezwani . Kuqakathekile ukuqinisekisa bonyana abantu abayisika abanamakghono wokwenza izinto kanye nazo zoke iinqhema ezilimala lula ziyahlanganyela kilekambiso ukwenzela bonyana lokhu kube yinto yomphakathi nelawulwa ngiwo . Tlola imibuzo elandelako efliphutjhadini bese ukhombela abahlanganyeli bonyana bayiqedelele eenqhenyaneni zabo ngokusebenzisa ilwazi lamanothi wekhoso . Umbuso kanye nekoro yangeqadi ungadlala iindima eziqakathekileko ekwakheni imithangalasisekelo , kufakwa hlangana imithangalasisekelo eminengi . Ngemva kwesikhathi sokwehla komnotho somnyaka wee-2009 , ikoro yangeqadi ibonakele idonda ukusisa iingeniso zayo ezihle emandleni akhiqizako . Begodu khonapho , umbuso ubonakele wenyula ukusebenzisa ipahla kunokusisa , okuyifuneko yokuthoma efunekako ebujameni obumasikizobu . Ngokukhamba kwesikhathi , isisomali lombuso lingasiza ekuvumeleni ukukhula kwesisomali lekoro yangeqadi . Umasipala wendawo kuWadi ABC unephosta ekulu eveza kuhle imisebenzi ayenzako . UNom . Jones uqeda ukuthuthela kilomasipala begodu uya e-ofisini uyokunghonghoyila ngokuthi isitrada sakhe asinawo umkhanyo owaneleko . Utjelwa bona athabe ngombana indlu yona unayo . Iinqhema zehlalakuhle kufuze ingathana zikhonjwe ngesikhathi nakwenziwa umtlamo owandulelako begodu zamukelwa ngokusemthethweni emhlanganweni wokuhloma womphakathi . Kodwana ezinye iinqhema ezingezelelako zingakhonjwa lokha nakutlanywako . Funda indatjana bese wenza inembo-mbono nemitjhini yakamasipalakho bese uhlela umhlahlandlela wokuhlanganyela komphakathi ukuhlangabezana nenembo-mbonweli . Kulungiswe i-ajenda ngaphambi komhlangano . Lo msebenzi wakasiHlalo kanye nonobhala . Nokusebenzisana namabhizinisi wombuso aphatheleneko bonyana abike ngetuthuko yeminqopho . I-MFMA , yomnyaka we-2003 idinga bonyana abomasipala baveze imibiko ephathelene nendlela yekambiso yokwethulwa kweensetjenziswa eendaweni zabo . Imibiko le inikela umphakathi iindlela zokutjheja ituthuko . Iindawo zemakhaya zineentjhijilo ezithileko . Iingcenye ezimbili kwezintathu zabahlali beSewula Afrika zihlala eendaweni ezazibizwa " ngezabelo " , begodu inengi lesiqhemesi alitjhejwa mumuntu ngokomnotho . Kufuneka bonyana kwenziwe imigomo yokuletha imindeni eseendawenezi ngaphasi kwerherho lezomnotho elamukelwa linengi labantu . Nokho , zikhona iindawo zemakhaya lapho ukuhlangana kweenthuthi kukuhle khona begodu lapho ukuhlangana kwenzeka khona ngaphandle kokuphatha okuhle kokusetjenziswa kwenarha kanye nokubuswa kweendawo zemadorobheni . Lokhu kutlhoga ukungenelela okurhabako . Abantu bahlanganyela ngokusiza ngemithombo yesizo , isibonelo , ngokusebenza ukwenzela bonyana bakwazi ukufumana ukudla , imali esesandleni nanyana ezinye iinhlohlomezelo ezibonakalako . People participate by contributing resources , for example , labour in return for food , cash or other material incentives . ISewula Afrika yenze iragelo phambili elikarisako nelingakavami ngokutjhiya phasi umbuso webandlululo begodu yamukele umbuso wentando yenengi . Itjhugulukweli lenzeke ngokuthula nanyana umlando wenarha le begade kungilowo onokulwa okukhambisana nemiguruguru kanye nokudinywa amalungelo . Ibandulo elaneleko : Isiqhema sabantu ababili iwadi ngalinye kufuze sibandulwe ukuze sikwazi ukusebenza ngokubambisana neKomidi yeWadi lendawo . Ihlelo lokubandula lingathatha amalanga angaba li-15 , kodwana lokho kuzakuya ngelemuko langaphambili kanye namakghono wokukghonakalisa . Ngokuya kweembalobalo ezidzimelele erhubhululweni , ama-67 womsebenzi wephasi , ekugcineni bathola amaphesende ali- 10 wengeniso-mali lephasi . Tlola phasi okuvunyelenwe ngakho ; zoke iinhlangano azitlikitle ; kuse bunqopha eForamini yabaJameli be-IDP . Imithangalasisekelo ayikaqakatheki kwaphela ekukhuliseni umnotho ngokurhaba nekuvuleni amathuba wemisebenzi amanengi . Begodu igcugcuzela ukukhula okubandakanya boke abantu , ngokunikela izakhamuzi iindlela zokwenza ngcono amaphilwazo nokukhuphula imirholwazo . Imithangalasisekelo iqakatheke khulu etuthukweni . Igalelo lokutjhugutjhuguluka kobujamo betlayimethi lithinta iphasi loke begodu kufanele kufunyanwe iinsombululo zephasi loke , kodwana kufanele kutjhejwe ubujamo beemphande nebamazwe . Umsebenzi 1 Qala kumThethosisekelo , begodu utjengise iingaba ezintathu ezithuthukisa urhulumende wedemokhrasi bewuhlathulule kobana iingaba eziveziweko ziwuthuthukisa njani urhulumende wedemokhrasi . Ukuziphendulela emabhizinisini wombuso kuhlangahlanganiswe kuqatjhwa kwabantu ngeendlela ezingakacaci begodu , eenkhathini ezinye , kucabhela kwepolotiki ngendlela engakafaneli . Siphakamisa bonyana kuhlathululwe iindlela zokuziphendulela ngokwakha amagunya atjheja ukwenziwa kwemisebenzi yomphakathi begodu ahlathulula bonyana ibhizinisi lombuso lizowusiza bunjani umphakathi , neliqinisekisa bonyana iindlelakambiso zokuqatjha zitjheja amakghono nepumelelo begodu zitjhatjhalazi , nokwenza ngcono ukuthintana phakathi kweminyango yemigomo neminyango yabanikazizabelo . Ukutjhejwa mahlangothi womabili kwalezizinto ezirhabeke kangaka kuzizinto eziqakathekileko ekuphumeleliseni ituthuko yelizwe loke . Ukubumbanisa iSewula Afrika kumfakela oqakathekileko ekambisweni yokuphungula ubuchaka nokungalingani begodu kumphumela onqophileko wokuphungula ubuchaka ngepumelelo . Ukwakha umphakathi obumbene ngokwehlalakuhle , iSewula Afrika kufanele iphungule ubuchaka nokungalingani ngokunabisa amathuba nomsebenzi ngokubandakanya boke abantu kwezomnotho , ngokusebenzisa ifundo namakghono , nangokuthatha amagadango anqophe ukulungisa lokho okungakhange kukhambe kuhle ngaphambilini ; ukugcugcuzela ihlonipho ebantwini boke nangokubandakanya boke abantu ngokwenza okukhambisana nomthethosisekelo ukobana iSewula Afrika ingeyabantu boke abahlala kiyo , nokobana boke abantu bayalingana phambi komthetho ; nangokuqinisa ukuthokozelelanwa kokuziphendulela nokuzibophelela kwezakhamuzi . Iindleko zamatjhejuli zivumela ukubandakanyeka kwemali engenako nesetjenziswako efanele ihlolwe ( okufaka hlangana iminikelo yababambisani abahlukahlukeneko ) , kanye nobubanzi beemVumelwano zeeMali ezifanele ukulinganiswa . Itsengo yobulili lithulusi lokuthola umrabhu womehluko phakathi kwabomma nabobaba mayelana nemisebenzabo enqophileko , ubujamo , iindingo , ukukghona ukufumana , nelawulo leentlabagelo begodu nokukghona ukufumana iinzuzo zetuthuko nokuthathwa kweenqunto . Lifunda ngokuhlangana kwalokhu namanye amafektha ebujameni obukhudlwana obuphathelene nomphakathi , nomnotho , nepolotiki begodu nobujamo bezebhoduluko . Itsengo yobulili ifaka hlangana , kokuthoma nokuqakathekileko , ukubuthelelwa kwemininingwana yobulili obungahlanganiselekiko , ilwazi elizwelana nobulili ngesitjhaba esithintekako . Itsengo yobulili ligadango lokuthoma ekutlameni ngezinto ezizwelana nobulili ekuthuthukiseni ukufana kobulili . Yenza umsebenzi ongenzasi nabahlanganyeli bese ukghonakalisa ikulumiswano ngokuya ngemibuzo . INDLELA YOKWENZA YE-CBP INIKELA AMAKOMIDI WEWADI UMTLAMO OBURHERHO BEGODU NENDLELA YEKAMBISO YOKWENZA UMSEBENZI NGOKWESIQUNTO UKUDLALA INDIMA NEEMBOPHO ZAWO . BANEHLELO / UMTLAMO WEWADI- BEGODU NENDLELA YOKWENZA UMSEBENZI NGOKWESIQUNTO , UKUTJHEJA BEGODU NOKUHLUNGWA KOMTLAMO WEWADI KUBANIKELA INDIMA ERAGELA PHAMBILI UMNYAKA WOKE UKULUNGISA IZINTO OKUCATJANGWA BONYANA ZINGEZIQAKATHEKILEKO KUNEZINYE ZOMPHAKATHI ABAKHELWE BONYANA BAWUSEBENZELE . Abahlanganyeli baphendula imibuzo etlolwe ngezansi , yesigaba leso abatjelwe sona . Iinkomba eziqakathekileko zokwenza zisiza urhulumende wekhaya nabahlali bona balinganise iintuthuko . Ama-KPI minqopho ' eyenzekako ' nelinganisekako leyo umasipala avumelene ukuyiphumelelisa ngesikhathi esithile . Isiza ekukhulumisaneni nekulinganiseni bona ikhansela nomasipala wethule kuhle kangangani ngokuya ngemitlamo endlalwe ku-IDP begodu ngalendlela abahlali bakghona ukubamba ukuziphendulela kwakamasipala . Ilogfremu inikela isisekelo lapho amakontraka angalungiswa khona ngokutjho iminqopho elindelweko . Isiza godu ekukhombeni ileveli yomsebenzi kanye nokuziphendulela kwabaphathi bephrojekthi nabanye ababambisani . Abakghonakalisi kufuze balungiselelwe ukusebenza ngombiko obuyako ovela emkhandlwini omalungana nesabelo seemali ezigade isimetjhe . Kungenzeka bonyana umphakathi uhlangahlangane lokha nangabe amanye amatjhejontangi wabo azange akhethelwe ukusekelwa ngeemali . Isede yamazinga womsebenzi iyayihlangabeza yini indlela yokwenza i-SMART na ? Ngimaphi amaphrojekthi amaKomidi weWadi afisa ukuwenza ? Cabangani ngezinto ezifana namaphrojekthi wokuthuthukisa umnotho wesigodi , ukubandula abatjheji abanikela ngesizo emakhaya . Cabangani kobana ingabe amaphrojekthi lawo angenziwa kanye nezinye iinhlangano zomphakathi ? Khambela imihlangano yomphakathi : Imihlangano le ingabizwa likhansela lendawo , iKomidi yeWadi nanyana isigungu . Emihlanganweni kungakhulunywa , ngomTlamo wokuHlanganisa oZeleko ( i-IDP ) , ngebhajede yakamasipala nanyana iindaba ezikhambisana nayo . UmTlolo weemBopho , owenziwe mNyango wezeFundo esiSekelo neminye , kufanele waziswe begodu wenziwe bonyana uthandwe ngibo boke abantu , begodu kufanele kugcugcuzelwe omunye nomunye umuntu bonyana akhambisane nemithethokambiso yomThethosisekelo . Ungubaba . Unomsebenzi ethrestenapha . Umkakho utjala imirorho . Umnganakho uthembisa ukuyokuthengisa imirorho le edorobheni elikhudwana ngemali ehle ufuna ukwenza lokhu ngombana udinga imali ephezudlwana ngombana ufuna ukuthenga isudu etja ozayembatha emhlanganweni womkhandlu kamasipala ozako . Phendula kulokhu begodu unikele umbiko obuyako ngesitatimende senembo-mbono , ukuthuthukiswa kweminqophobegodu namaqhinga wokuphumelelisa okuthize begodu nokukhonjwa kwamaphrojekthi we-IDP ukuqinisekisa bonyana lokhu kuveza ubujamo iKomidi yeWadi begodu nomphakathi abathanda bonyana indawo yabo ibe khona . Ukunikelwa kwezindlu kufanele kuhlanganiswe neembawo zamasabsidi , ukubonisana ngokwezomthetho nokunikelwa kwezindlu kuphakheji yinye , ngokwenza njalo kusizwe ikhastama ukobana lifikelele imisebenzi yoke begodu ingasi ngokweenkhewukhewu nangokweengcenye ezihlukeneko neentokana . Ukuhlanganiswa komnotho wesiphande kungakhuphula ukukhula komnotho eenarheni zoke ze-Afrika engeSewula . Isiphande sikhule ngokurhaba eminyakeni elitjhumi egadungileko , begodu isebenze ngokuzikhandla emkhakheni wezenjiwa , wezelimo , wezethintaniswanoliqha newezamavakatjho . Ukuphumelelisa ukuhlanganiswa komnotho kutlhoga ukukhomba amathuba abonakalako lapho ukusebenzisana kungahlomulisa khona amahlangothi woke , kungadala isisomali kumithangalasisekelo ; kungaqinisa iimvumelwano zemibuso yesiphande zokuphungula nanyana zokuqeda iinqabo zokurhwebelana ; kungehlisa amatharifu ; begodu kungatjheja iinqabo ezingakaphathelani namatharifu , njengeenkhala zemisebenzi yemkhawulo ezinganamakghono . Idayagramu elandelako ikhombisa ukobana isigaba ngasinye semiphumela yokuphathwa kwephrojekthi nokulinganisa godu amagadango begodu nokobana umzombe awusiwo umjeje ngokwemvelo . Irherho elikhudlwana neliphumelelisako lamatjhuguluko nemibono emitjha , elikhambisana khudlwana namafemu asebenza eenkorweni ezilandela iqhinga letuthuko . Mema isiqhema esisodwa sizokwethula bese unikela ezinye iinqhema ithuba lokwenza iimphakamiso nemibono . Umbono ' ulibhudango ' lomphakathi , ziinkoro umphakathi ufisa ukuzifumana ukuphi . Kuthatha isikhathi eside ukuvumelana ngombono , khulukhulu lokho kubangelwa kukobana ibhudango lezakhamuzi lingahluka khulu ngendlela erarako ngenca yesendlalelo sezomnotho nehlalakuhle somuntu othile . Umtlamo lo ulindele ukubona iSewula Afrika lapho omunye nomunye umuntu azazizwa akhululekile kodwana asebenzisana nabanye abantu ; lapho omunye nomunye umuntu azakusebenzisa khona ikghono lakhe elipheleleko , inarha lapho ithuba lingaqali ukubelethwa komuntu , kodwana liqale ikghono , ifundo nokusebenza ngokuzikhandla . Nangabe sifuna ukuba nomphakathi onjalo , kuzakufanele sitjhugulule umnotho nemizamo enqotjhiswe ekwakheni amakghono wenarha . Nasifuna ukurarha ubuchaka nokuphungula ukungalingani , kufanele bonyana umnotho uhlume ngokurhaba nangeendlela ezihlomulisa woke amaSewula Afrika . Inturhu - dzubhula inturhu esekhe yakwenzakalela , emsebenzini , ekhaya , namtjhana ebujameni obunye nobunye . Isijamiso sesikhathi esingaphasi sikhombisa ezinye zezehlakalo eziqakathekileko ezithinta umphakathi we-Bloemfontein eFreyistati njengesibonelo . Ukwenza ngcono ikhwalithi yefundo etholakala eenkolweni nemakholiji weFundo eRagela Phambili nokuBandula ( ama-FET ) angasebenzi kuhle . Ukugcugcuzela amaqhinga wokwakhelwa izindlu ngendlela evangiweko nokuthuthukiswa kweendawo zemadorobheni ngendlela ehlangeneko ukusiza abantu bonyana bakwazi ukufumana iinkhala neentlabagelo zombuso , iinhlangano zombuso , nomsebenzi kanye namathuba wamabhizinisi . Isahlukwesi sithoma ngokuqala iinhlathululo ngokuhlukana kwazo . Iragelo phambili ngokutlhaga neengcenye zendlela ephumelelako yokuphatha ukuhlukana nezinye izinto eziqakathekileko ezithinta ukuphathwa kokuhlukana . Isahlukwesi siswaphelisa ngerhelo lokuhlola ngokwenziwa komtlamo wokuthatha igadango lokuhlukana . ISewula Afrika ingahlomula ekukhuleni ngokurhaba kweenarha ezithuthukako begodu lokho kungarholela ekutheni kube nefuneko yepahla namamakethe wabasebenzisipahla anabako . Begodu ngokunjalo , amatjhuguluko la aletha iintjhijilo eenarheni ezifumana ingeniso ephakathi ngesibanga sephaliswano elikhulu lokukhiqiza neminye imisebenzi yetheknoloji yelwazi . Begodu ukukhuphuka kwenani lamamakethe asathomako kukhuphula izinga lephaliswano leentjhabatjhaba , begodu lokho kugandelela imirholo yabasebenzi abanamakghono aphasi eenkorweni ezirhwebelana namazwe wangaphandle . Ihlangahlangano yegezi yomnyaka wee-2008 nokhunye okuvele mhlapha nje kuveze ukubhalelwa kweenhlangano ezihlobene namakhampani wombuso asebenza ngemithangalasisekelo yethungelelwano . Ukubalekela imiraro enjalo kutlhoga amalungiselelo weenhlangano , iimvumelwano zabosomatjhere ezitjhatjhalazisiweko , iindlela ezizwakalako zokuziphendulela kanye nemifuziselo yezeemali eyazisako ukuqinisekisa bonyana izinto ziragela phambili ngefanelo . Senza iimphakamiso emkhakheni ngamunye walemikhakha . Imithetho elawula ukukhanjiswa kwezinto ngefanelo ivamise ukuhlangahlanganisa izinto , ngombana uhlanganisa umgomo nomthetjhwana . Kuneendlela esiziphakamisako zokulungisa ubujamobu . Ukutlhayela kweensetjenziswa - isibonelo indatjana okukhulunywe ngayo ngehla . Ngonobangela wokutlhayela kokutholwa kwamanzi , kufakwe ipompo engazange isebenzeke kiwo woke umuntu , kunokugugunyeka ngayo . namtjhana isibonelo , kunokutlhayela kwezindlu begodu inturhu ingavela mayelana nokwabiwa kwezindlu kanye nendlela esetjenziswako lokha nakwabiwa izindlu . Ibhajedi kamasipala yomnyaka ibonisa bonyana imali kamasipala izakusetjenziswa kuphi begodu nokuthi njani . Lezi ziindleko zakamasipala . Ibuye godu iveze bunqopha bonyana urhulumende wekhaya uzalithola kuphi ingenisomali . Abahlanganyeli basebenza eenqhemeni leza zomSebenzi 1.1 bese batjheja ifundo-sehlakalo bese bathuthukisa iqhinga lokuthintana . Ukuragela phambili nokwenza ituthuko ekungezeleleni imirholo namazinga wokuphila , kufanele bonyana kukhuphuke nesilinganiso sokukhiqizwa kwemikhiqizo . Ikoro yezabasebenzi eSewula Afrika ivamise ukuba nokubangisana phakathi kwamafemu afumana inzuzo nabasebenzi ekubonakala babhadalwa kuhle . Imiphumela ebekwa eenkambisweni zokukhulumisana ngemirholo nobujamo babasebenzi benza bonyana kube budisi ukuqatjhwa kwabasebenzi abatjha . Ukurarulula amazinga aphezulu wokungasebenzi , khulukhulu kwelutjha , kutlhogeka amagadango angakajayeleki . Uburholi beenhlangano ezijamele abasebenzi buqakatheke khulu ekuqinisekiseni bonyana iinzuzo zamalunga ziragela phambili nokuba khona . Ukuphumelela kilokhu , isilinganiso sokukhiqizwa kwemikhiqizo kanye nemisebenzi kufanele sikhuphuke njalo . Indlela esetjenziswako yomtlamo womphakathi idinga ukutlanywa ngokucophelela nangokuhleleka ukuqinisekisa bonyana iyaphumelela . Ithatha isikhathi eside kanye nokuzibophelela begodu idinga isekelo leKomidi yeWadi , lamakhansela kanye neenkhulu zakamasipala . I-CBP ilithulusi elinamandla lokuphumelelisa umnqopho womThetho wamaHlelo kaMasipala , ka-2000 . Umbuso othuthukisako kufanele ube nekghono , kodwana umbuso onekghono awuphumeleli ngokukatelelwa mthetho , begodu awujanyiselwa imithetho nanyana wakhiwe ngeememezelo . Kufanele wakhiwe , ngesitina ngasinye ngasinye ngasinye , ngehlangano ngayinye ngayinye ngayinye , uphiwe umdlandla begodu urageliswe phambili ngeenkhathi zoke . Utlhoga uburholi , imigomo ezwakalako , abaphathi nabasebenzi abanamakghono , iindlela ezicacileko zokuziphendulela , amarherho afaneleko , nokusetjenziswa kwemithetho ngendlela engatjhugulukiko nelungileko . Cabanga bona uthintana / ukhuluma bunjani . UMBUZO 2 Kubayini iqakathekile ? Nikela iinqhema imizuzu ema-30 ukutlhama ibhajedi kamasipala yokusebenza . Kudingeka bonyana batlole phasi yoke imininingwana yama-ayithemu angenziwa ngeBHAJEDI YOKUSEBENZA ukufaka hlangana ama-ayithemu weendleko zokusebenza . Isigaba 2 sigcina ngomhlangano omkhulu lapho umphakathi ukghona khona ukubuyekeza , ukuhlolisisa kanye nokuqinisekisa ilwazi elihlanganisiweko . Begodu loke ilwazi elifunyenwe nakwenziwa koke lokhu kufuze libekwe endaweni lapho umphakathi uzakwazi ukulibona khona . Ngemva kwalokho kufuneka bonyana umphakathi ukhethe imiphumela emihlanu edinga itjhejontangi ukwenzela bonyana ukwazi ukutlama ngesikhathi nakwenziwa umtlamo . Tlola itheyibula elingenzasi phezu kwephrojektha esikhanyisi-magama namkha yedatha . Nangabe awunayo neyodwa yeentlabagelwezi , tlola itheyibula leli phezu kwetjhadi elilengiswako . INdlela yokuSiza ukuPhumelelisa imumethe iingaba ezihlanu ezizwisisekako . Isigaba ngasinye sirholela kwesilandelako . Idayagramu esekhasini elilandelako inikela ihlathululo efitjhazana yeNdlela yokuSiza ukuPhumelelisa . UKUQALELELA NGEENKAMBISOLAWULO EZIQAKATHEKILEKO , AMAMEKHENIZIMU KANYE NEENDLELAKAMBISO EZIDINGEKAKO NEZIZAKWENZA BONYANA ABOMASIPALA BAKWAZI UKUPHUMELELA EKUTHUTHUKISENI IMIPHAKATHI YENDAWO KWEZOMNOTHO NEHLALAKUHLE , KANYE NOKUQINISEKISA BONYANA BOKE ABANTU BAPHAKELWE IINSETJENZISWA EZIQAKATHEKILEKO ABAZAKWAZI UKUZIBHADALA . Lehlathululo efitjhani isirhunyezo esiqakatheke kwamanikelela somtlamo lo . Izahluko ezili-15 zikhuluma ngemimongo yemikhakha eqakathekileko ngokuzeleko , zinikela ubufakazi , iimphakamiso nemileyo yokuphumelelisa ecacileko . Mhlobo bani womsebenzi abomma abanengi abawenzako ? Khomba izinto ezivame ngokweqileko , imiraro ekhona isilinganiso somrholo abasitholako ngomhlobo lowo womsebenzi ? Laphaya eforomineli kunesibonelo sokobana lizaliswa njani . Omunye nomunye umnyango karhulumende kumele utlhame umTlamo wokwenza Ngcono ukweThulwa komSebenzi ( i-SDIP ) . Ama-SDIP aqakathekile endleleni yekambiso ye- IDP njengombana banqophe ukuphumelelisa , ukubanekghono begodu nokuba khona ukwethulwa komsebenzi ophumelelako nokuletha iinkambisolawulo zeBatho Pele entweni ephilako . Ngaphandle kwe-SDIP ukunikela amandla ukwethulwa komsebenzi . AmaKomidi wamaWadi ngebanga lalokho kumele azwisise ikambiso yokuthuthuka kwe-SDIP nokunikelwa komsebenzi . AmaKomidi wamaWadi kumele ahlale anelwazi ngezinto begodu azibandakanye ekuthuthukisweni , kweminqopho nekwethuleni kukamasipala . Ukuzibandakanya ekutlameni kokwethulwa komsebenzi kuqakathekile . Ukubandakanya ibubulo langeqadi ngokupheleleko ku-IDP ukwenza ngcono amaqhinga wokuthuthukisa umnotho wesigodi nowekhaya begodu itlhame isisekelo sengeniso-mali begodu neentlhabagelo zabomasipala . Ukuziphatha okungasebenzisi amezwi yindlela enamandla khulu yokuthumela umlayezo . Izenzo nje , njengokuvuma ngehloko , ukuqala umuntu ngemehlweni , ukusebenzisa ukukhuluma okunembako ngobuso , ukukhuluma ngezitho zomzimba kanye nokujama komzimba kanye nejamo lomzimba kungasiza ekukhulumisaneni . Ngesikhathi salesisiteji , ukuhlolwa kufanele kwenziwe ngamakghono neensetjenziswa ezikhona emphakathini ngokwawo . Ngokuqala amandla wamakghono wemiphakathi nokukhuluma ngemiraro yawo , amaphrojekthi abambelelako athoma ukusebenza begodu namandla wekhaya ayaqina . Tlhama irhelo lemibuzo okumele lisetjenziswe nakukhulunyiswana ubuso nobuso nabantu manqophana netuthuko yewadi . Imibuzo kumele ibuzwe ukwenzela ukukghonakalisa ikulumiswano evulekileko begodu nokusiza umphathikulumiswano ukuvala zoke izinto ezitlhogekako . Amaphrojekthi ahluleka ukwamukela ubungako bezinto eziphathelene nobulili ezifana nobuchaka , i-HIV / AIDS , nenturhu elwisana nabomma namkha ikghono labomma lokufumana iindingo ezisisekelo , iintlabagelo , umsebenzi namkha inarha elizakudinga okuzwisisekako okuzwisisekako komraro . Amaphrojekthi aphumelelako adinga ukuzwa bonyana iintjhijilwezi zinemirabhu emandleni anetjhebiswano elikhethekileko nelingafaniko eliphathelene nomphakathi elidinga ukutjhejwa ukuze likwazi ukulungisa umraro . Mema isiqhema esisodwa ukweethula itheyibula yabo emhlanganweni wokutlama . Emva kwalokho mema esinye isiqhema ukungezelela namkha ukuveza umbono . UmbikomThethokambiso yikambisolawulo etjengisa indlela okungazuzwa ngayo ibhudango lokuthuthukisa urhulumende wendawo ozibophelele ekwenzeni ngcono ikhwalithi yamaphilo wezakhamuzi kileyo ndawo nokuhlangabezana neendingo zazo ngokusebenzisana nabo ukobana bathole iindlela ezizakuragela phambili isikhathi eside ukwenza lokhu . Abomasipala babawiwa ukobana balawule ukuphatha kwabo , iinkambiso zokutlama nokubhajeda ngendlela etjheja qangi iindingo zomphakathi ezisisekelo . Iinkambisolawulo ezivezwe kumbikomThethokambiso ohlongozwako usekelwa mithetho ehlukeneko yepalamende . Ngiwaphi amalunga weWadi ekufuze anikelwe isibopho sokwenza imisebenzi ? Kuvele kobana umhlangano uyokubanjelwa kuphi kanye nesikhathi somhlangano ngaphambilini . Unobhala nguye ofuze enze lokhu . Ezingeni lamaziko , ukulawulwa kwetjhejo lezamaphilo kusebudisini . Mhlapha nje umNyango wezamaPhilo uhlome ihlelo lokuhlaziya ikghono lalabo abaphetheko . Amatjhuguluko angezelelako kufanele afake hlangana ukunikelwa amandla amanengana mayelana nokuhlinzekelwa ngestafu , nezakhiwo zamatjhuguluko kanye nomsebenzi wangamalanga wokuthengwa kwepahla nemisebenzi . Amakhoso ahlukahlukeneko wesenzo lapho kubandakanyeka ilawulo lephrojekthi angahlukaniswa ngeenqhema ezikulu ezihlanu ezitjhiwo ethebuleni elisephepheni elilandelako . Veza ukukwata kwakho nakufaneleko , kuvikelekile begodu kufanelekile ukwenza njalo . Ukubambezela ukukwata kungenza umraro ubhebhetheke . Thola ithuba elihle lokuveza ukukwata kwakho . Akukaqakatheki njalo ukuveza ukukwata namtjhana ukukunaka , kwesinye isikhathi umuzwa lo udlula masinyana . Ukwethula ihlelo lokondleka labomma abasidisi nabantwana abancani begodu nokungezelela imisebenzi yokuthuthukiswa kwabantwana abancani abangaphasi kweminyaka emihlanu . Qala amanothi wekhoso ( ikhasi lama-56 nelama-64 ) malungana nesisetjenziswa sakho esinqophileko bese ulandela indlelakambiso . Nangabe kuyakghonakala , iimpendulo zakho azeyame phezu kwamalemuko onawo mayelana newadi lakho . Ngiziphi iinhlangano zomphakathi nanyana iminyango yakamasipala enifuna ukuyimema kobana izokwethula / izokuveza ikghono kumaKomidi yeWadi nanyana ukuba khona emhlanganweni wesifunda sokubusa ? Isilinganiso esiphezulu sesisomali , lapho isisomali lombuso livumela khona ukukhula kwesisomali lekoro yangeqadi . Lokhu kuzokuya ngokuhlanganyela nekoro yangeqadi , ngokungabi nokuzaza ngemigomo nangokwakha ithemba ekukhuleni komnotho kwesikhathi eside . Kubuye kube ngenye indlela yokuzwisisa iindingo ezihlanganeko zomphakathi . Kukobana abantu bahlelwe ' njengabomndeni ' namkha ' abachakileko ' lapha ukuzicabangela kwenziwa khona ngabantu , njengabantu abamndeni owodwa , itsengo lobulili livumela ukuqalela eduze amaqiniso abantu abahlangabezana nazo . Yehlukanisa itsengo labobaba nabomma - imirarwabo , iindingo nekghono lokufumana amandla neentlabagelo . Nakufika umnyaka wee-2030 , iSewula Afrika kufanele bonyana ibe sele inerherho elipheleleko lokuvikelwa kwehlalakuhle okufaka hlangana iimbonelelo zehlalakuhle yomphakathi ezivela kurhulumende , iimali ezibulungelwa umhlalaphasi ezikatelelekileko , iinzuzo zeengozi ( njengeenzuzo zokungasebenzi , zokufa nezokukhubazeka ) kanye neemali ezibulungelwa umhlalaphasi ngokuzithandela . Ukuvula amathuba wemisebenzi amanengana ngokuthuthukisa zelimo , okuyame ekubuyekezweni kwemithetho yenarha nekuthuthukisweni kwenarha yokulima ethelelelwako nemikhiqizweni yenarha . Iphesentheji yebhajedi ekulu kamasipala ngokweqiniso isetjenziswa kumaphrojekthi amakhulu akhonjelwe umnyaka wemali othileko ngokuya kwe-IDP kamasipala . Umphathi we-CBP uhlathululela abahlanganyeli ngomtlamo , begodu uyabahlathululela bonyana wakhiwe bunjani , abanikele netlhadlhulo enabileko nangabe kunesidingo . Hlanganyela emibuzweni ephathelene nomtlamo wephrojekthi yohlobo elithize lamaphrojekthi imiphakathi ezakuthinteka ngawo . Ngokukhambela imihlangano yomkhandlu - ukwenziwa komthetho womkhandlu kudinga ukuba ngekokuphendulelwa , okuvulekile kanye nokuphendula emalungeni womphakathi . Umphakathi unelungelo lokuya emihlanganweni yomkhandlu . Ukuze wenze lelilungelo umphakathi udinga ukwazi bona umhlangano womkhandlu uzokubanjwa nini begodu uzokubanjelwa kuphi . Kufanele wazi godu umnqopho womhlangano womkhandlu . AmaKomidi weWadi angasiza umphakathi ukuwunikela ilwazeli . Amalunga wekomidi yeWadi kufanele aye emihlanganweni ukuze ahlale anelwazi njengabajameli bomphakathi begodu asizeke ngokunikela umbiko obuyako emphakathini . IRHEMISO-KAMBISO YOBULILI ITJHO BONYANA NANYANA NGILIPHI IGADANGO NAMKHA AMAPHROJEKTHI NAMKHA AMAPHROGREMU ATLANYWE MAKOMIDI WAMAWADI , UMZAMO OLUNGISELWEKO UYENZIWA UKUQINISEKISA BONYANA UBULILI BUYAFAKWA EMITLAMENI LE . Ukuhlela kokwenziwa komsebenzi ngokwehlelo - lokhu kubandakanya imininingwana yokuhlela epheleleko yokobana iphrojekthi izokwenzeka bunjani . Isethulo se-MSA sigandelela iphuzu ziinkoro urhulumende wemakhaya akakafaneli bonyana alwele ukubonelela zoke izakhamuzi ngeensetjenziswa , kodwana kufuze alwele ' ukuletha ituthuko esisekelo ' . Khombela abahlanganyeli bonyana bahlukane ngeenqhema ezincazana bese ubakhombela bonyana baqale iSWOT yeenqhema zehlalakuhle esekhasini lama-66 lamanothi wekhoso . Ukwanda kwemisebenzi ngendlela eragela phambili kutlhoga bonyana kube nomnotho okhula ngendlela emsinyana begodu kutjhidiswe izakhiwo eziziinqabo , njengefundo yekhwalithi engazisiko nanyana iindlela ekuhlelwe ngazo iindawo zokuhlala ezibandlulula inengi labantu . Lezi kuzizinto eziqakathekileko ekuphumeleliseni amazinga aphezulu wokusisa neentengo eziphasi , nekunabiseni imikhiqizo nokuthengiswa kwepahla eenarheni zangaphandle . Ikoro yamabhizinisi , yabasebenzi , imiphakathi nombuso kufanele zisebenzisane ukuphumelelisa ukukhula msinyana komnotho . Ubujamo bokwamukela , ukuthembeka begodu nepumelelo yenye nenye iphrojekthi kusezandleni zesekelo elivela emphakathini lowo iphrojekthi enqophe bonyana ibazuzise kungebanga lalokho , kubalulekile bonyana amaphimbo wabo boke abakhathelela ipumelelo ayezwakala ukuqinisekisa isekelo lephrogremu . Ungahlolwa bonyana abomma kuvamisile bonyana badinywe amaphrogremu la nakatlanywako namkha akhonjwa pheze ngokobana abanye abantu bacabangani ngeendingo zabo , kunesidingo sokobana imibonwabo , umcabango neemphakamiso kuzwakale ukwenzela iphrojekthi ithole isekelo lomphakathi . . . Ukuzilungiselela kungasiza ekususeni ukwesaba kokwethula emhlanganweni . Khumbula : umnyango wekhaya mkhakha abahlanganyeli abangaba nesabo khona khudlwana . Iimfundo-bandulo zilisizo njengobana zinikela ilwazi begodu ziveza itjhejo mayelana neendaba ezithile begodu zinikela ithuba lokuthuthukisa imithetholawulo nokuthatha iinqunto . Ivamisa zibanjwa eenqhenyaneni ukuze abahlanganyeli esifundweni-bandulo bakhulumisane ngendaba ngokujulileko . Abahlanganyeli bahlukaniswa ngeenqhema bese utjheja indatjana esekhasini lama-68 . Coca ngeengaba zokuphathwa kokwenziwa komsebenzi . Landelisa lokhu ngekulumiswano ngeendlela zekambiso yetjhejo begodu nokuhlungwa . UmThetho wamaRherho kaMasipala , womnyaka we-2000 unqophe ukutlama isiko kokuhlanganyela komphakathi begodu nokuthoma iindlela zokwenza , iindlela zekambiso begodu neenkambiso zokuqinisekisa lokhu . Inikela indlela yokuthi ilwazi lingadluliswa njani begodu nokujanyiswa komthetho ophathelene nesaziso somphakathi ngento ethize begodu nokwamukela ukubanjwa kwemihlangano yomphakathi nokobana umphakathi wekhaya ungawazisa ngayiphi indlela . Ukuqinisa imisebenzi yemitholapilo nokunabisa amahlelo wezamaphilo wesiyingi , njengamahlelo wabasebenzi bezamaphilo emphakathini newababelethisi , kanye nefundo yezamaphilo . I-Batho Pele inikela iphahla lokutjhugulula kokwethulwa kweensetjenziswa zomphakathi . I-Batho Pele , ' ebeka abantu mantanzi ' yenzelwe ukubeka iinsebenzi zombuso bona zisebenze begodu zilwele ukwenza ngeqophelo eliphezulu imisebenzazo . Ivumela amakhastama bona babambe ukuzibophelela kweensebenzi zombuso ngendlela ezenza ngayo umsebenzi . Ukuhlola kokwenza kungalinganiswa ngendlela iinKambisolawulo ze-Batho Pele zisetjenziswa ngayo lokha iinsebenzi zombuso zisebenza nomphakathi . Isikhathi - nakubanjwa umhlangano nanyana isifundobandulo , kumele siyelelwe . Nangabe kuzokuba malanga ntambama khulu nanyana ebusuku nanyana ngepelaveke lapha amalunga womphakathi azobe afuna ukwenza lokho akutlhogako , nanyana azobe asebenza , ukukhanjelwa komhlangano lowo kuzokudanisa . Isigabesi sirekhoda lokho okwenziwe mkghonakalisi / bakghonakalisi ukwakha lomtlamo nalabo ababandakanyiweko . Esigabenesi umkghonakalisi / abakghonakalisi utlola irhelo lemihlangano ebanjiweko kanye nebizo / nenani labahlanganyeli nabakghonakalisi . Kuyifuneko eqakathekileko ukobana iKomidi yeWadi iyabandakanyeka ekutlanyweni kweqhinga lokwakheka komnqopho wendlela yeenkambiso zakamasipala wendawo yabo esikhathini esingaba minyaka emihlanu . Ekhabo lakhona , lokhu kuyindlela iKomidi yeWadi ezakwazi ukutjengisa ngayo ikghonolayo . Abomasipala kufuze balungise i-IDP ethatha iminyaka emihlanu . Indlelakambiso yokutlama nokuphumelelisa ihlelwa ngeengaba ezihlanu ezendlalwe ngaphasi ngokufitjhani . Kuqakathekile ukujayela iingabezi ukuze ukwazi ukuhlobanisa imizombe ye-CBP neye-IDP . Umtlamo wokuthuthukisa ohlanganiswe ngokuzeleko uyindlelakambiso esetjenziswa bomasipala ukwenza umtlamo wokuthuthukisa weminyaka emihlanu . I-IDP imkhiqizo wendlelakambiso yomtlamo wokuthuthukisa ohlanganiswe ngokuzeleko . Umtlamo wegadango lokuhlukana ufuna imininingwana eminengi neendlela ezicatjangisisiweko zekambiso . Umtlamo kumele uthole indlela yokuthuthukisa ukuhlukana , ukulingana nokungasolisiko ngesikhathi kulungiswa indaba yebandlululo . UmThethosisekelo unikela godu iminyango eqinisa idemokhrasi yomthethosisekelo . Lokhu kwaziwa njengeminyango ' yesAhluko 9 ' njengobana indlalwe kumThethosisekelo esAhlukweni 9 . Ukutlama komphakathi kuphumelela lokha nangabe boke ababambisani bayahlanganyela . AmaKomidi weWadi asisakhiwo esamukelwe ngokusemthethweni njengesidlulisi esiqinisekisa bonyana ilizwi lomphakathi liyazwakala . Abakghonakalisi be-CBP kufuze basebenzisane nabo boke ababambisani ukwenzela bonyana indlelakambiso ikwazi ukusebenza . AmaKomidi weWadi angazithola asebujameni lapho kufanele aphendule enturhwini . tjheja amajamo alandelako nokobana kusetjenziswe yiphi indlela . Esahlukwenesi sizokuqala ehlangothini lephahla lomthetho okungilo elenza isendlalelo sokwethulwa kweensetjenziswa zomphakathi , indima okumele idlalwe maKomidi wamaWadi begodu namarherho adinga ukuhlonywa ukuqinisekisa ukwethulwa kweensetjenziswa zomphakathi eziyipumelelo . AmaKomidi weWadi akghonakalisa ukuhlanganyela komphakathi ekambisweni yokuthuthukiswa , ukubuyekezwa nekulawulweni kokwenziwa kwe-IDP . Ngalokho amaKomidi weWadi adinga ukuzethemba , ukuba nelwazi nekghono bona benzelele ukuzalisa umsebenzi lo . Ithebula liphethe isirhunyezo sabadlaliindima , imisebenzabo kanye nobudlelwana babo namaKomidi weWadi . Umehluko wobulili utjho umehluko phakathi kwabomma nabobaba akhethwa ngetjhaphuluko nangobugugu obungathathiko ihlangothi . Kodwana , ' umehluko ' omkhulu phakathi kwabobaba nabomma , nalapho ingabandakanya khona i-elemende yokukhetha ( isib. ongakumbatha ) kodwana nangaphandle kwalokho bafakiwe ezakhiweni zokungafani kobulili okuvame ukwehlisa igugu lokukhetha kibomma nokuthuwelelisa ukufumana okungalinganiko kwamandla neentlabagelo . Ikambiso eyakhiweko eyenziwa ekhotho yomthetho enejaji elingathathi hlangothi namtjhana umarhastrada obeka isiqunto samaswaphelo ngemva kokulalelwa kobufakazi kanye nokuphikisana okusemthethweni kwamahlangothi womabili . Isiqunto sakhe sinzinze ecaleni , emthethweni ojanyisiweko neentweni ezakhe zenzeka okuthathelwa kizo njengesibopho esisemthethweni . Iphrojekthi kukwethembisa ukwenza okuthileko ukuthuthukisa umsebenzi nanyana umkhiqizo ngesikhathi esibekiweko . Kumele kuthathelwe phezulu nanyana kwenze itjhuguluko elihle ngenye indlela . Iphrojekthi ibekelwe isikhathi esiquntiweko kunokuba yenzeke njalo nanyana kube yikambiso yasafuthi begodu inebhajede ebekiweko begodu kukwethembisa kokwenza okuthileko kwesikhathi esisodwa . Ekunikelweni kwemisebenzi yakamasipala , kunamaphrojekthi ahlala asenzeka njalo , njengokulungiswa kweendlela . Ebujameni obunjalo , indlela ehlathululwe ngenzasi le ayizokusebenza . Umkhandlu ungenza imithetho yokobana isaziso somthetho kamasipala sinikelwa bunjani emphakathini , kungaba ngamaphosta namtjhana ngeembikiindaba . Amalunga womphakathi angenza iimphakamiso ezitloliweko angazisa e-ofisini kamasipala . Umkhandlu kufanele wenze isiqalelelo esikhethekileko malungana namalunga womphakathi ekungenzeka bona azange aye esikolweni , namtjhana malungana nobunye ubudisi obungenza kube lukhuni kibo ukuthumela iincwadi ezitloliweko . UMSEBENZI OMKHULU WEKOMIDI YEWADI kukuqinisekisa bona umphakathi emawadinabo uyabandakanyeka ekwazini mayelana neenqunto ezithathwa mkhandlu nezithinta ipilwazo . AmaKomidi weWadi amamehlo neendlebe zomphakathi kanye nendlela eqakathekileko yokugcugcuzela ukuzwisisa hlangana komphakathi nomkhandlu . Lokhu kutjho bona iKomidi yeWadi kufanele ibonisane nomphakathi mayelana netuthuko kanye namahlelo womsebenzi . Ukuthintana kuqakatheke ekuqinisekiseni bona imibono yomphakathi ikhona eenquntwini ezimayelana nokwethulwa nokuthuthukiswa komsebenzi . Imisebenzi ethuthukisiweko yobuhlakani bezerhwebo ukusekela ukunaba kwetjhere yemakethe yeSewula Afrika ephasini loke . Isitjhijilo sokuthoma selawulo lephrojekthi kuqinisekisa bona iphrojekthi yethulwa hlangana nesikhathi esincitjhisiweko . Sesibili , okusitjhijilo esirhulutjhelweko kukwenza isiqiniseko sokobana okunengi kwenziwa ekwabiweni kwemali kanye nakwezinye iinsetjenziswa ezikhona ukuphumelelisa iminqopho yephrojekthi . Ukuhlela bona iphrojekthi ifanele yenziwe bunjani - lokhu kwaziwa godu njengesigaba sokwakha namtjhana isiteji sokutlama ukwenziwa njengobana kunqotjhiwe . Amajamo neendingo kuyatjhuguluka lokha abantu abatjha nabeza endaweni , kungenzeka bona iindingo ezindala sezitjhejiwe begodu sezikhona ezitja ezivelileko . Eendaweni zemadorobheni amalunga wamaKomidi wamaWadi kufanele ajamele iinqhema ezithileko , isibonelo , iinqhema zekolo , iinhlangano zabomma , iinhlangano zabantu abatjha , umkhakha wezamaphilo , iinqhema zemidlalo , umphakathi , neenhlangano zababhadeli bomthelo . Zoke izakhamuzi kumele ziphathwe ngehlonipho begodu nangokutjheja . Ipendulo : Kunokuba ivulelwe ukuba kuthendarwe , umkhandlu ukhethe ikontraga X ngombana uthi yona unamandla wokwenza njalo . Imisebenzi yeemali eqinisiweko ukwehlisa iindleko zayo nokwenza ngcono ukufumaneka kwamabhizinisi amancani naphakathi . Isigaba esinye nesinye sakhiwe ngezehlakalo ezinqophileko ezimbalwa ekungasetjenziswa kizo isisetjenziswa esisodwa nanyana ezimbili ze-CBP . Kufanele kube yihloso yeensebenzi zoke ezithuthukisako ( urhulumende , umasipala namtjhana iinsebenzi ezisizako zangaphandle ) ukwakha imiphakathi lokha nayilawula amaphrojekthi akiwo . Imiphakathi inikelwa amandla lihlobo lokuthuthukiswa okulungileko khulukhulu nabazibandakanya emaphrojekthini athinta bona . Nabafunda ukuphumelela ekuthuthukisweni komphakathi , imiphakathi izokusebenzisa izinto abazifundileko eengcenyeni ezithile zepilwabo . Bazokufunda ukuhlela ngepumelelo begodu amakghono woburholi azokuqiniswa . Inikelo-mandla- Lokhu kutjho ukuba nelawulo ekuphathweni kweenqunto nezinye izinto ezithinta ipilo yomunye umuntu . Kutjho ukujameleka endleleni yekambiso yokuthathwa kweenqunto nokulawula phezu kokwabiwa kweentlabagelo . Kudinga igadango langabomu okumele lithathwe ukutjhugulula ubujamo lapha abomma bangakajameleki ngokwaneleko ekuthathweni kweenqunto . Ukuhlanganyela ekutlameni endleleni yekambiso yokuthathwa kweenqunto kunenzuzo engezelelweko yokwandisa umkhumbulo wokuzibophelela ebunikazini beminqopho yomtlamo . UMBUZO 6 . Zisetjenziswa njani ? Zisetjenziswa ngubani ? Lungiselela ukutlolwa phasi kwemininingwana yomtlamo ntangi ngombana kungenzeka kube nesidingo sokuhlela imitjhiningqondo ephathwako nanyana iinkghonakalisi zokuthwathwaza ngomtjhiningqondo . Iphungule irhasi ekhutjhwako esilaphaza ibhoduluko begodu yenze ngcono ukusebenza kwamandla kweembaseli . Yenza isiqiniseko sokobana isiqhema sizwisisa umehluko hlangana ' nokuqakatheka ' kanye ' nokutholakala ' . Amagama la angatjhugululelwa elimini lendawo . Ukuhlinzekela ngezenzelo ezisisekelo ezenza bonyana abantu bakghone ukuthuthukisa amakghonwabo ukwenzela bonyana bakwazi ukuzuza emathubeni akhona enarheni , azabenza bonyana bakghone ukufaka isandla emiphakathinabo ngokuthumela iimali nangokudlulisa amakghono . Ukusukela eminyakeni yokuphela kwekhulumnyaka le-19 , iSewula Afrika isebenzise umnotho wayo wezenjiwa ngokukhathalela okuncani nanyana ngokungakhathaleli ibhoduluko layo . Kutlhogeka amatjhuguluko wokuvikela ibhoduluko ngesikhathi kuvunyelwa inarha le bonyana ihlomule kuzenjiwa zayo ezitholakala ngaphasi komhlaba . Ngaphezu kokuqakatheka komnotho wezenjiwa ongavuselelekiko , imithombo yemvelo yenarha ifaka hlangana amalwandlekazi wayo aseduze , ihlabathayo , amanzayo , imihlobohlobo yeentjalo neenlwana emabhodulukweni wemvelo , umkhanyo welanga kanye nomthala omude weligu . Akunazinto zokuzithabisa eWadini A . Lokhu kuthinta abantu abatjha abajama emakhoneni weentrada kwesinye isikhathi basela utjwala balwe nokulwa . Amasondo wekhaya vane ahlangane ukuzama ukurarulula umraro lo . Aye eKomidini yeWadi . Indaba le kukhulunyiswane ngayo eKomidini yeWadi lapho kuvunyelenwe khona bona ikhansela lewadi lizayethula emhlanganweni olandelako womkhandlu bese libawa umkhandlu bona ubize umhlangano nababambisani okufaka hlangana abosorhwebo bomphakathi , iinqhema zetja , iinhlangano zekolo njll . IKomidi yeWadi isize ngokuyokuhlangana nabahlanganyeli ukuyobazisa ngomraro nonobangela wokubizwa komhlangano wababambisani . Umhlangano wenziwe kwabese kuvunyelwana bona itatawu lezemidlalo kanye nendlwana yetlabha izakusiza ilutjha bona lihlangane . Imiphakathi yezekolo yavumelena ukusebenzisana bona ikwazi ukunikela ngamahlelo kanye nemisebenzi abantu abatjha abangahlanganyela kiyo . Amakomidi wamaWadi kumele godu anikelwe umbiko obuyako njalo njalo njalo ngemali kamasipala esesandleni esebenza njalo . ' Imali esesandleni esebenza njalo ' kutjho ukufaka nokukhupha imali kamasipala e-akhawundini yebhanga . Umsebenzi 3 khetha mabili wamagadango owakhombe emSebenzini 2 . Thatha isiqunto ngalokho ozokwenza ukusiza iKomidi yeWadakho ukuthatha amagadango . Ukungathembeki - Izakhamuzi kungenzeka zingabi nokubathemba abadosiphambili abakhethiweko , amalunga wekomidi yamaWadi begodu / nanyana iimphathiswa zakamasipala ukobana benze ngepumelelo amahlelo namaphrojekthi . Lokhu kungaba miphumela yelemuko lesikhathi esidlulileko nanyana ukutlhoga ilwazi . Amalunga wamaKomidi wamaWadi kufanele athole iindlela zokukhuthaza nokuthuthukisa ukuthembeka nokuzethemba ukubandakanyeka komphakathi okunomphumelakho nanyana ihlathululo . Ngehlangothini lezepolotiki , intando yenengi ithuthuke ngokungalinganiko . Imiguruguru yamhlapha nje yeTlhagwini Afrika isikhumbuzo seengozi ezidalwa kungabusi ngefanelo neenhlangano ezinganamandla ezivumela iinqhenyana ezikhethekileko bonyana zizinjingise ngeemali ekufanele zisize ngazo abantu . Iindawo eziphathelene nokwephasi ezakha iwadi , zikhanjelwa ukuthumela abajameli bazo abaphakamisiweko ukusebenza njengamalunga weKomidi leWadi . Rhunyeza ngokurhunyeza isigaba ngasinye . Inarha ekudanyana neligu yeSewula Afrika inamazinga aphezulu wobuchaka nokungasebenzi , begodu inemisebenzi ekhawulelweko kwezelimo . Irherho lebandlululo lakatelela inengi labantu be-Afrika bonyana bayokuhlala eendaweni zemakhaya ezingakhiqizi ukudla . Lokho kwabangela bonyana kube nekoro yokulimela irhwebo ethuthukileko begodu enemikhiqizo engafaniko ethembele ebasebenzini bemaplasini abarhola imali engazisiko nemiphakathini etjhonileko neminyeneko enamathuba akhawulelweko wezomnotho kanye nezenzelo zombuso ezingamukelekiko . Iimphakamiso zeKomitjhini mayelana nemithangalasisekelo yezomnotho zifaka hlangana ukusiza ngeemali , ukutlama nokutjheja . Lo mbiko wabonobangela abaqakathekileko bangaphandle ( izinto isiqhema sephrojekthi esingakghoni ukuzilawula ) laba abaqakathekileko epumelelweni yephrojekthi . UKUPHASISWA KWESABELO SEEMALI KUYINTO EQAKATHEKE KWAMANIKELELA EKUTHATHENI ISIQUNTO SOKOBANA IINDLELAKAMBISO ZE-IDP NE-CBP ZINGENZEKA NINI . Iminqopho etjhiwo kulogfremu , ihlanganiswa nomsebenzi , isisetjenziswa kanye namatjhejuli weendleko , inikela ilwazi lokusekela icozululo lendleko esizako . Umphakathi uthuthukisa ubunikazi mayelana namaphrojekthi asetjenzisiweko . Lokhu kungagcina ngokuthi kutlhogonyelwe khulu kuthuthukiswa komphakathi okufana namaphaga nanyana imakhiwo . IBatho Pele iyelelisa ikambiso karhulumende yamaqhinga wokutlama , umTlamo weTuthuko eHlanganisiweko , wokuphatha ukwenziwa komsebenzi nokuphatha iimali ezibhadalwako . Njengalokho kuqakathekile ukulungisa ibhoduluko lomsebenzi welinye nelinye ilunga lomsebenzi wombuso . Iminqopho yamaqhinga yeminyango yeliZwe kufanele yehlele phasi kumaqhinga weminqopho nemibono yayo yoke iminyango yamaphrovinsi norhulumende wendawo . Ngemva kwalokho imiPhumela yeeNdawo eziQakathekileko ( ama-KPI ) yabaphathi nayo kufanele yenze okufanako . Inengi labahlali lihlala ezindlini ezimametjhibhoksi nanyana emikhukhwini engemuva kwendlu . Izindlu ezinengi kilendawo azinayo igezi nanyana amanzi asatjalaliswa ngamaphayiphu . Lendawo ineenkolo ezintathu kanye nemitholapilo emibili . Amalemuko la akhombisa lokho okungenziwa ngepumelelo lokha nangabe abarholi nestafu bazibophelele ekusebenzisaneni ukwenza ngcono imisebenzi . Amabhajedi akukameli bonyana enziwe bukhobosi . Ukwakhiwa kwamandelaniso wezehlakalo kuqinisa umqondo wokuzikhakhazisa kwamalunga womphakathi ngokusebenzisa lokho okucabange ngokuhlanganyela . Ifundo eyenziwe ngcono , ngokwesibonelo , izakurholela ekutheni abantu basebenze ngobunengi begodu bafumane imirholo ephezulu , begodu ukukhula msinyana komnotho kuzakwandisa amathuba wabo boke abantu begodu kwakhe imithombo efaneleko yokuthuthukisa ifundo . Abajameli bamaKomidi weWadi bangazibandakanya kumaForamu we-IDP . Iforamu le inikela ababambisani ithuba lokujamela ikareko yomphakathi . Inikela ngesijamiso semikhulumiswano , ukubonisana kanye nokuthatha iinqunto ngokuhlanganyela hlangana komphakathi kanye nomasipala . Begodu inikela ithuba lokutjhejwa komtlamo kanye nokwenziwa komsebenzi we-IDP . Umbono weKomitjhini ngewokobana ekugcineni , abasebenzisi kufanele babhadale inengi leendleko zemithangalasisekelo yezomnotho , kodwana kufanele kuvikelwe imindeni etlhagako . Indima yombuso nemali yomphakathi kubeka imibandela efaneleko ukwenzela bonyana iindleko zikwazi ukubhadalwa kancani kancani kancani ngokukhamba kwesikhathi , begodu ngokwenza njalo amanani angakhanjiswa ngendlela efaneleko . Begodu umbuso kufanele bonyana uhlome imileyo efaneleko yokulawula nokubusa ukwenzela bonyana imithangalasisekelo ikwazi ukusetjenziswa ngepumelelo begodu amatharifu akwazi ukubekwa emazingeni afaneleko . Malungana nemithangalasisekelo engenisa imali , isikolodo esenziwe ekwakhiweni kweensetjenziswezo kufanele bonyana sibe sesitatimendeni sepahla neenkolodo zamabhizinisi wombuso nanyana samakhampani enza umsebenzi . Imibandela kufanele isetjenziswe ngokukhetha ukwehlisa iindleko zepahla nokufumana imali isikhathi eside . Isizo lemali lokwehlisa iindleko eliphiwa imindeni etlhagako kufanele bonyana linqophe begodu litjhatjhalaziswe ngendlela ekungakghonakala ngayo . Imithangalasisekelo yezehlalakuhle engangenisi imali - njengeenkolo nanyana iimbhedlela - kufanele isizwe ngeemali zesabelomali . Umphakathi kufanele uzibandakanye ekambisweni yokutjheja , ukulinganisa nokubuyekeza ukwenza , njengobana umasipala nakaqeda ukubonisana nomphakathi wekhaya kufanele uthuthukise bewenze iindlela namarherho begodu akhombe ikambiso yalokhu . Umasipala nangabe uzizwa akghona ukunikela umphakathi omkhulu umbono nokuhlanganyela komphakathi , angajamisa iforamu yokuhlanganyela komphakathi . Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi angaba khona kileforamu . Kumusebenzi welunga lomkhandlu ukujamisa iforamu yomphakathi . Ngikuphi okungenziwa msinyazana ? Iminqopho le izaliselela iminqopho eyendlalwe eHlelweni eliTjha lokuThuthukiswa komNotho . Nakutlhogekako umsebenzi onqotjhiweko awukapheli , kufanele kwenziwe imizamo yokusiza umuntu loyo ukobana azuze lokho akunqophileko . Nangabe ukungasebenzi kuhle kusaragela phambili yeke kufanele kube khona okwenziwako okufana nokujanyiswa nge-ofisini , iinkambiso zokujezisa nokupheliswa kwekontraga . Ukuze ilwazi libe lisizo lidinga ukutsengwa ngepumelelo . Imininingwana kumele irhunyutjhwe ngesizathu sokwenza iimphetho . Ukutjheja ukuthuthuka kwephrojekthi kuqakatheke khulu ukuze kuqinisekiswe kobana kuhlala kukhamba kuhle njalo nokuthi iingozi ezitjha nanyana iintjhijilo ziyatjhejwa bese ziyemukelwa ekwenzeni umsebenzi ongemva kwalapho . Iinqhema zamaphrojekthi zisebenzisa iinkomba ukuze zitjheje ituthuko . Iinkomba zizinto ekulinganiswa ngazo ezitjengisako kobana imibono ifinyelelwe . Amafreyimi welogo ngesinye isikhathi aziwa ngeleensetjenziswa ' ngokunqophileko ziinkomba eziqinisekisako ' iinkomba zifuze kobana zinembe , zanele , zinqophe , zilinganiseke , zingabizi khulu begodu zitholakale . Songa ngesifunjwana esincani esidzimelele ethebulini esekhasini lama-90 . Itheyibula linikela amaKomidi wamaWadi ngerhelo lokuhlola lezinto abanganqophana nazo begodu nabangadosela umphakathi kizo . Kilesisigaba umlamuli kufanele asebenzise umsebenzi wokurarulula umraro . Iphrojekthi ingahlathululwa njengelinye nelinye igadango elingathathwa ukuthuthukisa umsebenzi namkha umkhiqizo ngesikhathi esibekiweko . Lokhu kwengeze ubugugu namkha kulethe itjhuguluko elihle ngandlela thize . Iphrojekthi inesikhathi esilinganisiweko sokuba khona kunokuba yindendende namkha ibe nendlela yekambiso yasafuthi , inebhajedi ehlathululiweko begodu ivame ukuba negadango elilodwa . Ekwethulweni kwemisebenzi kamasipala kunamaphrojekthi aragela phambili , afana nokutjhejwa kweendlela , ezehlakalweni ezifana nalezi indlela yokwenza izinto ehlathululwa lapha angekhe kwaba ngefaneleko . Begodu ukumebha kunikela indlelambono yomphakathi mayelana nesakhiwo sakhathesi sesikhala , iindaba ezithinta iimphande ezahlukeneko , imithombo yemvelo , ibhoduluko lemadorobheni kanye namakhetho angaba khona wokwenza ngcono ibhoduluko lawo lokuphila . Ukwakha irherho letjhorensi yezamaphilo yenarha kumnqopho oqakathekileko . Kunezinto ezine eziziimfunekontangi lokha nalizakuphumelela : ukwenza ngcono ikhwalithi yetjhejo lezamaphilo lombuso , ukwehlisa iindleko ezihlobeneko zetjhejo lekoro yangeqadi , ukudosa abosobizelomsebenzi abanengana ekorweni yombuso nekorweni yangeqadi , nokwakha irherho lelwazi lezamaphilo elibandakanya abanikeli ngemisebenzi yezamaphilo bombuso nabangeqadi . Amatjhuguluko la azokuthatha isikhathi , azokutlhoga ukubambisana phakathi kombuso nekoro yangeqadi , begodu azokutlhoga imithombo ebonakalako . Emhlanganweni opheleleko wabahlanganyeli khombani iinkambiso eziqakathekileko zelizwe begodu nezesifunda esele zithuthukisiwe ukuqinisekisa bonyana amaphrogremu welizwe begodu nawesifunda ayahlanganiswa nezinto eziqakathekileko zakamasipala . Ngendlela sijwayele isithintela senturhu ngendlela siphendula inturhu . Kunamazinga athize enza umzombe wenturhu . Umzombe lo ungaba muhle begodu ube mumbi . Umzombe yindlela enesizo yokucabanga ngeendlela inturhu iphila ngayo eempilweni zabantu . Abahlanganyeli bafundisisa isigaba esinye nesinye , nanyana esikhundleni salokho umkghonakalisi angahlathulula isigaba esinye nesinye , anikele itlhadlhulo ezeleko nangabe kunesidingo salokho . Khuyini okungangisiza bona ngilalele ngepumelelo ? AmaKomidi wamaWadi adinga ukwenza imizamo elungiselelweko ukuqinisekisa bonyana zoke iinqhema zifaka phakathi eendleleni zekambiso yokuthatha iinqunto ezithinta umphakathi begodu nezifaka phakathi nemihlangano yemibiko ebuyako nokufaka phakathi begodu nezifaka phakathi nemihlangano yemibiko ebuyako nokufakwa phakathi kwemibonwabo , kungaba ziinqhema , zabomma , imiphakathi yabaphalali , iinqhema zabomma , imiphakathi yabaphalali , iinqhema zabomma , imiphakathi yabaphalali , iinqhema zezekolo , njll . Lokhu kungafuna umtlamo wamambala wokuthatha igadango elakhiwe ngokunqophileko ukufaka phakathi iinqhema ezitjhiywe ngaphandle . Kungenzeka bonyana abosiyazi be-CBP balibuthelele ngaphambili elinye lelwazeli . Buthelela ilwazi elisisendlalelo bese ulihlela ngefomede erhunyeziweko ekhombisa ilwazi . Qinisekisa neKomidi yeWadi bonyana ingabe ikhona eminye imithombo yelwazi elisizo begodu engasetjenziswa nanyana njani . Isiqhema , ngokurholwa ' bakghonakalisi ' , kufuze sendlale imisebenzi eqakathekileko kanye namaphrojekthi eyenziwa emphakathini waso nokobana bobani abanikeli ngemisebenzi . Umongameli uThabo Mbeki wagandelela bona ipi yokuphelisa umtlhago nokungathuthuki enarhenethu kuyinto eqakatheke eqakatheke ekuzuzeni umnqophethu welizwe wokwakha umphakathi otlhogomelako nodzimelele ebantwini . ' Le yindlela okumele sizwisise ngayo iBatho Pele . Kusezingeneli eliqakathekileko lokutjhugulula namatjhugululo lawo iBatho Pele engaba namandla namandla kiwo . AmaKomidi wamaWadi angenza iimphakamiso ezimayelana neendaba ezithinta iwadi kukhansela yewadi , nanyana ngokuzidlulisa kukhansela yewadi , zisiwe edorobheni nanyana kumkhandlu wendawo nanyana amakomidi wemikhandlu . Okungaphezulu ziinkomba zakazweloke ezikhitjhwe nguNgqongqotjhe ngemva kokubonana nosomkhandlu wesifunda mayelana norhulumende wekhaya ne-SALGA . Nanyana kunemilandu eziinkulungwana ephenyisiswako , kodwana iimbalwa esiwa ekhotho . Kufanele kuhlonywe iinqhema ezikhethekileko zabatjhutjhisi namakhotho akhethekileko . Ukuthuthukiswa kwelizwe loke azange kube yikambiso enqophileko , begodu umtlamo othuthukisako angeze waragela phambili nokukhanjiswa emthaleni onqophileko . Ngokunjalo-ke siphakamisa bonyana kube nomleyo oqalene namahlangothi amanengi ozakwazi ukuletha umzombetuthuko , othuthukisa ihlangothi elithileko , elizakusekela ituthuko yamanye amahlangothi . Begodu isayensi netheknoloji zingasetjenziselwa ukurarulula ezinye zeentjhijilo ezikulu zefundo nezamaphilo . Iingcenye ezinengi ze-Afrika ezingazange zibe nethuba lokufumana imitato ejanyisiweko njenganje zisizakala khulu ngamathungelelwano wabofunjathwako asebenza ngepumelelo begodu anikela imisebenzi eyahlukahlukeneko . Iincwadi zokufunda ziyakghona ukuthunyelwa bu-elekthroniki eendaweni ezingafikeleleki lula . Isayensi ilinga ngakho koke okusemandlenayo ukulwisana namalwele nokuphungula iindleko zokuhlanzwa kwamanzi . AmaKomidi weWadi angathola ilwazi emithonjeni yelwazi ehlukahlukeneko . Isibonelo , umasipala anganikela ilwazi ngenani lemizi endaweni , namtjhana amaPholisa weSewula Afrika anganikela ngelwazi lamastathistikhi wobulelesi . Begodu , iKomidi yeWadi ingenza layo iphenyo ngokuvakatjhela imizi ukuze ithole ilwazi . Ukuthuthukiswa kweensebenzi zomphakathi kungasiza ekutholeleni iKomidi yeWadi ilwazi . Ukuphumelelisa ukukhula msinyana komnotho , izinga eliphezulu lokusisa , nokusebenza kwabantu ngobunengi . Umsebenzi omunye nomunye kufanele wabele iinsetjenziswa ezifaneleko ( ngalokho kutjhiwo , iindleko zeemali neensetjenziswa ezinye ) ezizokudingakala ukuyiqedelela . Iinsetjenziswa ezidingakalako kufanele zitjhiwo ngokunembako . Abantu baphendula enturhwini ngeendlela ezahlukahlukeneko . Kanti abanye baphendula ngendlela efanako ngaso soke isikhathi , abantu bangasebenzisa iindlela ezinengi ngokuya ngobujamo benturhu . Umqopho omkhulu welawulo lenturhu , kusombulula inturhu ngendlela yokobana boke ababandakanyekako baneliseke ngomphumela ngaphandle kombango . Lokhu kungathiwa ubujamo BOKUTHUMBA / THUMBA . Iphesentheji yomndeni ethola ngaphasi kwe-R1 100 ngenyanga , izakukghona ukuthola imisebenzi eyisisekelo yasimahla . Ingabe iKomidi yeWadi idlale indima ekuthatheni isiqunto ekambisweni yomkhandlu ? Amaphrojekthi womphakathi amancani njengokukhulisa ukwenza kwesiqhema sebholo erarhwako namtjhana ukuthuthukisa iphrojekthi yengadi ongasizwa mumuntu kiyo , begodu nokufuna iinkambisolawulo zelawulo lephrojekthi ukuqinisekisa ukuthuthukiswa kweenhloso . Esikhathini esifitjhani , kufuneka bonyana umgomo ukwazi ukuvikela ibhoduluko lemvelo msinyana nangepumelelo nokuphungula ubungozi bokutjhuguluka kobujamo betlayimethi . Esikhathini eside , ngokusebenzisa amaqhinga wamambala nabonakalako nangokuhlanganyela nephasi loke , iSewula Afrika ingakghona ukutjhugulukela erherhweni lezomnotho elisebenzisa ikhabhoni ephasi khulu ngebelo elikhambisana neembawo ezenziwa mbuso emphakathini , ngaphandle kokulimaza imisebenzi nanyana ikghono lokukhiqiza nokuthengisa ipahla . Thoma ngokucoca ngalokho okulindelweko kanye nalokho okutshwenya i-CBP , kuveze bese uyatjho bonyana lokho kungena bunjani ekambisweni ye-IDP kamasipala , indima edlalwa siqhema esikghonakalisako kanye neKOmidi yeWadi . Khomba iinqhema ezahlukeneko zehlalakuhle ezisemphakathini . Ungasebenzisa isilinganiso sehlalakuhle esifana nalesisibonelo esingaphasi . Iziko lelwazi lekhaya - i-ofisi lakamasipala wekhaya yindawo ekungiyo okungatholwa kilo ilwazi . Kungaba ngendlela yesaziso ebhodini yezaziso . Ukuhlola : Imiphakathi nanyana abajameli bayo nabo bangadlala indima eqakathekileko ekuhlolweni kwabanikeli bemisebenzi abafaneleko , ukuzibandakanya kwemiphakathi ekunikeleni umsebenzi nekutjhejeni abanikela imisebenzi . Yamukela impendulo zeenqhema . Linga bewutjengise amagadango umsombululi-mraro awasebenzisileko . IKomidi yeWadi yikhathalisti eqakathekileko ekwenzeni umphakathi bona uzibandakanye eendabeni ezithinta umphakathi begodu ngalendlela kwenza imiHlahlandlela ebalwe ku-1.1.1 iqiniso . AmaKomidi weWadi angasebenzisa amaqhinga ahlukahlukeneko ekuphenduleni kweendingo zomphakathi . Kunabonobangela abahlukahlukeneko abazokulinganisa bona iphrojekthi ikghonakele begodu ukuhlela okuragela phambili kufanele kwenziwe . Kunamathulusi afanisiweko nathuthukisiweko ukuze kuhlonywe bona ngiziphi iinhloso zephrojekthi nokobana ziphumelele na . Abahlanganyeli basebenza ngeenqhema ezinamalunga amane ukuya kamahlanu begodu baphendula imibuzo engaphasi . Nangabe isiqhema senyula ukufundelwa umbuzo , funda umbuzo munye ngasikhathi sinye , khombela zoke iinqhema bonyana zicocisane ngombuzo , bese ngemva kwalokho ragela phambili ngombuzo olandelako . Nangabe usebenzisa ifliphutjhadi , nikela isiqhema esinye nesinye imibuzo emibili . Khumbula bonyana isiqhema esingaphezu kwesisodwa sizokuba nombuzo ofanako . Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi kungafuze aphendule imibuzo yabantu abehlukeneko nabaneenkareko ezahlukeneko . Iinkareko lezo zingehluka kumibono yamalunga weKomidi weWadi . Ukusebenza nokukhulumisana nabantu abaneenkareko kanye nelingemuva elahlukeneko kungenza kobana baphambane . UmTlamo wokuThuthukisa weliZwe Loke umleyo obanzi onamaqhinga aphumelelisako . Wendlala indlela ebumbeneko nepheleleko yokulwisana nobuchaka nokungalingani okunzinze phezu kwamatjhejontangi anqophileko nakhambelanako arhunyezwe ngaphasi . Umnqopho ophakathi weBatho Pele ' sisakhamuzi njengekhastama ' . Imigomo le ingezelela umbono walabo abathola imisebenzi yombuso njengamakhastama , ingasi njengezakhamuzi kwaphela . Ngalokho-ke iinsebenzi zombuso akukafaneli bona zibhaqe ngekambiso karhulumende , kodwana kufanele zibeke amakhastamazo phambili . Ilwazi elibuthelelwe ecozululweni eliphathelene neendlela zokuziphilisa lisetjenziselwa ukwenza iSWOT yeenqhema zehlalakuhle . Imiphumela efunekako yesiqhema ngasinye kufuze itlolwe ngokurhunyeziweko efliphutjhadini . Wazini ngamaKomidi weWadi ? Ukufana kukhathalela ukuziphatha komuntu ngamunye ngendlela efanako , ngaphandle kwemibandela . Kutjhiwo epathweni efanako yokwemibandela yokusebenza ngerhwebo , ubungako namkha amagugu . Ukufana kungadosela ekungafanini okungeneleleko eenqhemeni ebegade zisehlangothini elimbi ngendaba yerherho , elibhalelwa kuthatha ubujamo nobunjalo babo njengento etlhoga ubuziphendulelo . Ukuphathwa ngokulingana kuthoma ukuba nelungelo elifanako ebujameni bomphakathi , umrholo , neendlela zokusebenza ebujameni babomma nabobaba . Okokuthoma , umasipala kumele akhethe bonyana ngimiphi imisebenzi okumele yandiswe namkha yenziwe ngcono . Isibonelo : Kukangaki kubuthwa iinzibi ? Isibonelo semiphumela eneempendulo ngobulili . ( ukwandiswa kwenomboro yabasebujameni obumbi ngokweqileko abatloliswe ngokobulili begodu nokuhlala esikolweni , ( b ) Ukwandiswa kwamandla wokuthathwa kweenqunto mayelana neendleko zomndeni , ( c ) ukuhlanganyela ngokulingana kwabomma nabobaba ekuphathweni kweentlabagelo zemvelo . Zama ukusebenzisa ukulalela ngokuqophelela . Isibonelo , nakusakhulunywa ngokukwata , unga : hlathululi , thikamezi , nikeli abonobangela , hluleli namtjhana uhlunge . Lalela ngokuqophelela ngokutjengisa omunye umuntu bona ulalele begodu uzwelana naye . Esikhathini esinengi ukwazi bona kunendawo evikelekileko yokuveza imizwa kusiza ukusebenzisana njengabantu abakhulu esele banenqgondo . Ukusisa eenthuthini zomphakathi , okuyinto ezakuhlomulisa imindeni efumana imirholo ephasi ngokuyenza bonyana ikghone ukukhamba . Buza abahlanganyeli bonyana bayijayele i-IDP yakamasipala wabo nanyana njani . Thatha iimpendulo . Lokha nangabe abahlanganyeli bayijayele i-IDP yabo , babuze bonyana i-IDP imumethe ini . Rekhoda efliphutjhadini . Lokha nangabe unamakhophi we-IDP yakamasipala wabahlanganyeli , khombela abahlanganyeli bonyana baqale i-IDP bakwazi ukubona bonyana nangambala imumethe amaphuzu avezwe bahlanganyeli nanyana awa . Irhelo lokuhlola lingarhunyezwa , lenziwe lula begodu lenziwe likhambisane nobujamo bendawo kanye nesilinganiso somsebenzi womnikeli ngemisebenzi ekukhulunyisanwa naye . Ukukhulumisana ngconywana , ukuthembeka nokuzithoba khudlwana kwalabo abaphetheko kungasiza khulu ekwakheni umphakathi nekurarululeni imiraro ndawonye nangokuthula . Imitlamo yephrojekthi ngekhe ibe ngeyamambala nangabe abomma abakathintwa ngokuzeleko mayelana nomtlamo nokwenziwa komsebenzi ngokwesiqunto . Ingabe akhona amadamu nanyana amahlelo ahlonyiweko wokuthelelela ? Ingabe lokhu kube nomthelela onjani mayelana nokufumaneka kwamanzi nanyana nekhwalithi yamanzi ? Iimpendulo zingafaka hlangana : Ukutlhogeka kwesekelo lomphakathi begodu / nanyana lakamasipala , umhlangano wokutlama okwandulelako uyahlelwa kodwana abahlanganyeli abezi emhlanganweni , ukutlhogeka kweensetjenziswa zomphakathi kanye nabakghonakalisi bewadi ekufuze benze umsebenzi . Umrholi - umkghonakalisi uyaluleka abe alawule ikambiso , unikela ihlelo emhlanganweni namtjhana athathe ukuziphendulela emphumeleni . Isigaba 2.3.2 somBikomthethokambiso ( i-White Paper ) we-1998 sithi ukuthuthukiswa kwedemokhrasi yekhaya kufanele kubonakale njengendima eqakathekileko yakarhulumende kamasipala omunye nomunye . Sindlala imithethokambiso emine yokuzibandakanya efaka hlangana ukuvumela izakhamuzi , kungaba ngabanye namtjhana iinqhema ezinekareko , ukuba nemibono kwezepolotiki zekhaya nemisebenzini yabathengi ukuba nelizwi ngendlela imisebenzi yethulwa ngayo . Izungu lekhaya liyikundla lapho imiphakathi ihlanganyela khona ukuthatha iinqunto ukuze bakhe amabhoduluko wabo wepilo begodu benze bebakhulise namalungelwabo wentando yenengi . Yoke imithetholawulo esekelako yakhiwe ngokuthathela lokhu ehloko . Lokhu kutjho bona amalunga weKomidi yeWadi kufanele bathathele imibono le ehloko lokha nabacabanga ngokuzalisa indima abayidlalako njengendlela yokuthintana hlangana kwekhansela nabantu emphakathinabo . Ukuphumelela kwendlelakambiso kweyame ezingeni eliphezulu lokuhlanganyela kwamalunga wewadi emtlameni wewadi . Lokhu kuzokwenza bonyana umphakathi ukwazi ukuzenzela imitlamo yawo ngomuso , begodu ngokwenza njalo uzobe uphungula izinga lokuthembela ebakghonakalisini abavela ngaphandle . IKhansela leWadi liba ngusihlalo weKomidi yeWadi . Lingabawa kobana omunye alibambele umhlangano ekujamelekeni kwekhansela okupheleleko nanyana ngiliphi ilunga leKomidi yeWadi . Phendula imibuzo elandelako . Tlhama umutjhwana ongabamba umphakathi ongasetjenziswa njengokunanyathiselwako , amamemo , kanye neminye imatheriyali . Iqhinga - umkhandlu wendawo nanyana ihlangano ' yenza sengathi ' iyile ebantwini ukobana yenze ikambiso ibe semthethweni ngaphandle kobana kube nokubonisana kwamambala okwenzekileko . Isibonelo ihlangano nanyana ikhamphani nanyana umkhandlu uthi siyile ebantwini begodu umphakathi uyavumelana nalokho okwenzekileko nini abantu bazisiwe ukuthi kunesehlakalo esenzekako . Namhlanjesi abantu abasebenzako ( labo abaneminyaka yobudala eli-15 ukufikela kwema-64 ) benza amaphesende ama-64 wesitjhaba , begodu ingcenye yabantwana neyabantu abadala yincani khulu . Ngokweentjhabatjhaba , ubujamo bedemografi obufana nalobu buvamise ukuhlotjaniswa nemirholo ekhuphukako , ukukhula msinyana kwemikhiqizo , iimali ezibulungiweko eziphezulu kanye namazinga wokuphila akhuphukako . Ngakwelinye ihlangothi , ubujamobu bungarholela ekutheni kube nebhoduluko elihlangahlangeneko nelingakanzinzi begodu abantu abatjha babhalelwe kufumana imisebenzi , begodu bazinikele emigurugurwini , ebulelesini , etjwaleni nakwezinye izinto ezimbi emphakathini . Isilinganiso sepumelelo ngesokobana inarha ikghone ukuba nabantu abatjha abakghonako nabazimisele ukusebenza . Ukwenza lokhu kutjho ukubanikela ifundo namakghono , nokusiza abafundi abaqeda isikolo ukobana bafumane umsebenzi ozabenza babe majadu begodu bakwazi ukuphumelelisa iinkanuko zabo . Ingabe umkhandlu nekhansela baziphendulela bunjani ? Ukukhomba iindingo - ukwenza irhubhululo namtjhana ukwenza icozululo leendingo ukukhomba iindaba eziqakathekileko zomphakathi ngeendaba zokuthuthukisa , amabhajedi nokwethulwa kweensetjenziswa . THOLAKALAKO - liyatholakala yini izinga ngabasebenzi banje kilomnyango nangemibandela yamambala yanje namkha egadungileko yokwenza umsebenzi na ? Begodu kunendawo yabahlali abahlala ngokungasisemthethweni ethome iminyaka engaba mihlanu egadungileko . Amanzi wakilendawo atholakala eempompini ezintathu zomphakathi begodu kuneempompi ezintathu kwaphela kilendawo . Inengi labahlali abahlala kilendawo lirhweba ngokungasisemthethweni begodu abanye abahlali abanengi basebenze emaplasini ukufikela lapho baqothwa khona . Azikho iinkolo kilendawo . Irhelo lokuhlola lepahla lingadinga bonyana lihlaliswe ngendlela ezakukhambisana nendawo ekwenzeka kiyo i-CBP ( isib . indawo yemadorobheni , indawo yemakhaya , njll . ) . Amagadango alandelako athathwa ngokusebenzisa isiqhema esifanako sabantu abali-12 . Sithoma ngokwenza amalungiselelo wesitatimende somnqopho esiphathelene neminqopho eminye neminye esebenzako . Lomsebenzi kufuze wenziwe ngeenqhema ezincazana , esinye nesinye kufuze sibe nelunga leWadi yeKomidi nabantu abafaneleko abayisika begodu abanamakghono athize afunekako kanye nabanikeli ngemisebenzi . Ukuphumelelisa umtlamo lo ngepumelelo , inarha le kufanele bonyana ihlanganyele nemiphakathi yoke begodu isebenzisane ngomnqopho owodwa . Njenganje , iSewula Afrika inamazinga aphezulu wokungathembeki phakathi kweenhlangano ezikulu zabasebenzi nabaqatjhi . Umzombetuthuko wokwakha ukuthembeka nokuzibandakanya emikhulumiswaneni yokuqalana neentjhijilo ezirhabekileko uyadingeka - lowo onombono ozakusebenza isikhathi eside esizako . Bekukhona iindlela ezahlukileko zokwenza ? Nakunjalo bezihlukile begodu ziphumelelise ini ? Ngokusebenzisa iphepha lecozululo leendlela zokuziphilisa elizaliswe emsebenzini ogadungileko , khombela abahlanganyeli bonyana benze ithebula elinjengaleli elingaphasi . Ubunjalo bobulili kumele bungeniswe emiBandeleni yesiKhombisolwazi esilungiselelwe nanyana ngiliphi ihlungo . Izinto ezilandelako kumele zivalelwe emahlungweni begodu lapha kukghonakala khona , ngendlela yobulili obungakahlanganiswa ukwenzala bonyana kufikwe ekulinganisweni kwesimo kwamambala nokuzwisisekako ngemiphumela yamaphrogremu . Ukukhula kanye nesisomali lesikhathi eside kutlhoga umbono ohlanganyelweko , ukuthembana nokusebenzisana phakathi kwekoro yamabhizinisi , abasebenzi nombuso . Namhlanjesi , izinga lokuthembana liphasi , begodu ubudlelwano babasebenzi butjhubile ngendlela engamukelekiko ( begodu ngezinye iinkhathi bunenturhu ) . Akwenzeki bonyana irherho lezomnotho lingatjhuguluka lifune abasebenzi abanengi nangabe ubujamobu buyaphikelela . Ukugcugcuzela ukukhula ngokurhaba nangendlela ezakwazi ukwakha imisebenzi kutjho bonyana kufanele kusetjenzwe ngokutjhuba kwemimoyokhu ngendlela ethembekileko nevulekileko . Umbuso wedemokhrasi ukhethwa babantu ngokubamba amakhetho afaka boke abantu , atjhaphulukileko nangathathi ihlangothi begodu ngokuvowuda okuyifihlo . Qinisekisa bonyana umkhandlu uyaziphendulela emsebenzini wawo ogadungileko . AmaKomidi weWadi kungenzeka angabandakanyeki bunqopha emisebenzini kasodorobha kodwana angabandakanyeka njengabantu abanesibopho esipheleleko somkhandlu , iKomidi yeWadi yenza isiqiniseko sokobana usodorobha wazi zoke iindaba ezimayelana nomphakathi . Zama ukuthola bona ukukwathokhu kunqotjhiswe kuwe na . Abantu abanengi banemizwa yokukwata ngaphakathi kwabo ngaphambi kobana wena uze nakho . Ungaba endaweni engasiyo ngesikhathi ekungasiso . Amakhansela neKomidi yeWadi abize umhlangano wokuzokukhulumisana ngeemphakamiso zamaphrojekthi afanele ukufakwa ku-IDP elungiswako nje . Amanye amalunga womphakathi afuna umakhiwo womtholapilo wakhiwe hlanu kwalapha kunemikhukhu khona , njengobana abahlali bemikhukhu banganamali yokunande baya esibhedlela namtjhana kweminye imitholapilo ekude . Esinye isiqhema sabahlali sifuna i-IDP ifake ukuhlinzekelwa kokulungisa nokukhuliswa kwerenke yamateksi njengobana inganazo iindlwana zokuzithumela namtjhana indawo yabathengisako . Isiqhema sesithathu sifuna bona kungezelelwe amalanga wokuthuthwa kweenzibi abe mabili ngeveke edorobheni ngonobangela weenzibi eentradeni . Emhlanganweni kunokudosadosisana okunengi ngalokho ezinye iinqhema zikatelela bona iphrojekthi eziyikhethileko iqalelelwe kokuthoma . Kuqakathekile ukobana umbuso wedemokhrasi ugade amalungelo wabantu avikelwe ngaphakathi komThethosisekelo . Imigomo yeBatho Pele iqinisekisa ikambiso yokutjhugulula umsebenzi wombuso ukuze iziphendulele eendingweni zemiphakathi nokutjheja amalungelwazo . Ngokwenza lokhu imigomo iragelisela phambili ukwenziwa kwedemokhrasi eSewula Afrika . Umtlamo ohlanganyelweko nanyana umtlamo womphakathi unikela imiphakathi amandla wokobana ikwazi ukukhulumisana nokubandakanya amangenelelo afaneleko wokuphungula itjhono emiphakathini yayo begodu kufuze urholele ekutheni imitlamo nemisebenzi yebandla lendawo neyamanye ama-ejensi ibe ngcono . Ngokuqala ekhasini lama-33 lamanothi wekhoso , hlathululela abahlanganyeli iphuzu elinye nelinye . Thoma ngeengaba zomtlamo we-IDP . Sebenzisa imizuzu embalwa ukuhlolisisa iingaba ze-IDP , uhlathulule bonyana kuyafuneka ukuzijayeza i-IDP ngombana umzombe we-CBP uhlobana nalowo we-IDP . Ukuzibandakanya komphakathi kwenzeka emazingeni ahlukeneko . ITlhatlha lePhahla litjho ' ilere yokuzibandakanya ' eyatlhanywa nguSherry Arnstein ( ngomnyaka ka-1969 ) . Ilere itjengisa bona ungakhetha igadango linye ngesikhathi esisodwa . Isiqhema esibanzi somphakathi sihlangana ama-iri amabili , kungaba ngomGqibelo ntambama , nanyana ngesikhathi esilungele abahlanganyeli . Isiqhema sibuyekeza umbono , sikhetha iminqopho ekufuze inikelwe itjhejontangi malungana neqhinga elinye nelinye , iimphakamiso malungana neemali ezigade isimetjhe kanye nezethulo ezingeniswa ku-IDP . Kuyasiza ukufumana loke ilwazeli efliphutjhadini . Lokha nagabe unazo iintlabagelo , ilwazeli lingathwathwazwa ngomtjhiningqondo bese kwenziwa amakhophi . Inengi lomtlamo lo likhuluma ngamatjhuguluko wamaziko afunekako ukuphelisa ubuthakathaka obukhona ekorweni yombuso , khulukhulu lapho kutholakala bonyana ama-ejensi wombuso ayabhalelwa kuhlangabezana neembopho zawo eziphathelene nemiphakathi etlhagako . Iimphakamiswezi ziphathelene nokwakhiwa kwamatshwayo adingekako ekusekeleni umtlamo lo . Ukwakha amakghono wamaziko kuthatha isikhathi eside kanye nemizamo . Isahluko sokwakha umbuso onekghono nothuthukisako sinikela iinkomba zendlela ekufanele kusetjenzwe ngayo . Amaziko asebenza ngcono ngokufunda okuragela phambili kanye namagadango athuthukisako ; ngokudingida umraro omabhombo khulu , ngokuwurarulula nangokuyamela kwelinye itjhejontangi . Lokhu kutlhoga ukuphatha okuhle , ukuzinikela ekusebenzeni khulu , ukuqalana nomnqopho wokuziphatha ngendlela engathalazisiko kanye nokuzinikela ekufundeni ngelemuko . UMBUZO 1 Iyini ibhajedi ? Iimpendulwezi zingaba lisizo eendaweni neenkhathini ezithile . Esikhathini esinengi bakhandela ukulalela bese bamuka abanye amandla wokulalela . Bathi : awukalungi kangako , awusimuhle kangako , awukaqini kangako , ngimi owaziko . UMBUZO 5 . Ngiziphi iinkomba eziqakathekileko zokwenziwa komsebenzi ( ama-KPI ) ? Begodu kunendawo yabahlali abahlala ngokungasisemthethweni ethome iminyaka engaba mihlanu egadungileko . Amanzi wakilendawo atholakala eempompini ezintathu zomphakathi begodu kuneempompi ezintathu kwaphela kilendawo . Inengi labahlali abahlala kilendawo lirhweba ngokungasisemthethweni begodu abanye abahlali abanengi lisebenze emaplasini ukufikela lapho liqothwa khona . Azikho iinkolo kilendawo . Indima yamaKomidi weWadi kuqinisekisa kobana labo abanesibopho sokutlama iphrojekthi babandakanya imiphakathi nokuqinisekisa kobana izibandakanya ngokupheleleko kuphrojekthi . ISewula Afrika ifuna bonyana abarholi bomphakathi woke basebenzisane . Njengombana ukutjhuguluka kombuso webandlululo kwaba sisombululo esihlomulisa boke abantu kunokobana kube mzabalazo wokulwela amandla angeze aba namarhubhelo ngomuso , ukulwisana nobuchaka nokungalingani kuzokuba namarhubhelo emntwini woke - abanzima nabamhlophe , abanjingileko nabatlhagako . Ngokubona bonyana inarha le begade ihlukene ngaphambilini , kwesinye isikhathi abarholi basekela ubujamo obanelisa ihlangothi elithileko kanye neenrhuluphelo zesikhatjhana kunokobana baqalane nezinto ezibanzi nezizokusiza esikhathini eside esizako . Kuqakathekile ukuphuma emkhumbulweni onjalo nokufumana abarholi abazimiseleko nabakghona ukuzibophelela khudlwana ekurarululeni iintjhijilo zeSewula Afrika . Kwamambala ukulalela yinto eqakatheke kwamambala ekuthintaneni . Abantu vane bafuna ukuzizwa bona bazwiwe begodu balalelwa . Lokhu kudinga ukulalela kwamambala . Ukulalela kwamambala kutjho ukubona iphasi ngamehlo womunye umuntu . Kubandakanya ukulalela ngokukhulu ukutjheja nokuzwa imizwa ephekelelwa magama . Khombela isiqhema ngasinye bonyana sivumelane nombono womphakathi waso .
