Sihlathululele bonyana ukwakha umbono womphakathi kuyingcenye eqakathekileko yokwakha umtlamo wewadi ngombana umbono ' ulibhudango ' lomphakathi . Umbono uyaqala bonyana umphakathi ufuna ukuzibona ukuphi ngomuso . Sihlathululele bonyana lomsebenzi uthatha isikhathi eside begodu lokha nawusebenza nomphakathi ukwakha umtlamo wewadi kufuze kube nesikhathi esaneleko sokwenza lokho . Sikhombele bonyana siqale igadango loku-1 ukuya kwelesi-3 bese uyagandelela bonyana lamagadango anikela umkghonakalisi we-CBP isithombe sokobana bobani abamphakathi . Ngenca yokobana umphakathi wakhiwa ziinhlangano ezinengi zehlalakuhle , iinqhema zomnotho njll . Kuthatha isikhathi eside ukufikelela embonweni ofanako , ukubekezela kanye nokulawula isiqhema ngokucophelela . Ngakwelinye ihlangothi , inturhu ingakha ukubumbana kwesiqhema ngokuhlathulula ukungazwisisani begodu icacise iinkolelo . Ingaba sisekelo setjhuguluko begodu ingakha ubuhlobo obutjha njengabantu bathola begodu bafunda unobangela wenturhu . Amaphrojekthi amzombe ngokwemvelo begodu adinga ukuhluzwa okungatjhugulukiko nokuhlelwa godu njengobana enziwa . Itheminoloji yelawulo lephrojekthi iyahluka iya nge-ejensi eyenzako . AmaKomidi weWadi ajamele iindingo zemiphakathi emaphrojekthini azokuthinta bona begodu kufanele azibandakanye ekambisweni ngendlela akghona ngayo . Iinkambiso zelawulo lephrojekthi zilisizo emaphrojekthini amancani njengalokhu zilisizo kwamakhulu . Ukwaba likghono eliqakathekileko lepumelelo yeBatho Pele okumele boke abaphathi neensebenzi balizwisise . Kubaphathi kutjho bona ukuthemba amandlabo kwabanye ukuze basebenze ngokukhululeka kumphathi , kodwana nangabe kunemiraro isibopho sisala nomphathi . mayelana neensebenzi kutjho bona ukubanikela amandla nanyana ukubakhulisa , ithuba lokusebenza ngokukhululeka , ukwakha ukuzithemba begodu ngokuthembeka kunikela amathuba wokuthuthukisa ibizelo . Izenzelo zehlalakuhle yomphakathi kufanele bonyana zinabiswe , ngefundo nebandulo elingezelelweko mayelana nabosohlalakuhle nangokubuyekezwa kweemali zokusiza iinhlangano ezingasebenzeli ukufumana inzuzo . ILANDELELO NOMBIKO OBUYAKO : Phikelela ngokufuna imibiko ngamaprojekthi nemisebenzi kamasipala , emawadini ukuze izakhamuzi zibe nelwazi ngeragelo phambili nokufuna imiraro ekhona . Imibono eyakhako nethuthukisako ayivele , begodu lapho kukghonakala khona , umphakathi awaziswe ukurarulula ikinga . Nokululeka umbuso neenhlangano ezijamele abasebenzi nabaqatjhi mayelana nokuphumelelisa umtlamo . Iphesentheji yebhajedi kamasipala yamambala isetjenziswa ezweni ngokwesiqunto umtlamo wayo wamakghono wendawo yomsebenzi . Umbuso ujamisa indlela yokuziphatha komphakathi woke . Nangabe ikohlakalo ibonakala njengento eyamukelekako embusweni , izokuba nomthelela endleleni umphakathi oziphatha ngayo . Begodu lokhu kwenza bonyana kuqakatheke khudlwana ukobana umbuso ube namagadango owathathako mayelana nokulungisa amazinga aphezulu wekohlakalo etholakala ngaphakathi kwawo . UMBUZO 1 Khuyini umnqopho wokulalelwa kwebhajedi ? Khomba iindima ezahlukileko abobaba nabomma abazidlalako mayelana nokuphatha nokutjheja iindaba eziphathelene nomphakathi elevelini yeKomidi yeWadi . Amaphepha womqondo alinga ukuvumbulula okutjha , kodwana kufuze abonelele ngelwazi elaneleko ukwenzela bonyana umasipala akwazi ukuzwisisa iphrojekthi leyo begodu akwazi ukuthatha isiqunto sokobana ifanele itjhejwe nanyana njani . Nasele kwaziwa bona ngimiphi imisebenzi okumele yandiswe namkha yenziwe , isikhathi esicacileko begodu nemiphumela kumele itlhanywe ukwenzela bona umasipala akhethe iindlela ezingcono zokufinyelela iminqophakhe . Kumele godu ikhethe bona ngiziphi iintlabagelo- iimali , iintlabagelo kanye namakghono- atlhogekako ukufezekisa iminqopho . IKomidi yeWadi ingenza iphenyo lonyaka lokwaneliseka ukuze ibasize ekwenzeni imisebenzabo . Iphenyo kufanele lilawulwe malunga weKomidi yeWadi kuwadi ngaphasi kwelihlo lekhansela yewadi begodu ngesekelo lokuphatha lakamasipala . Izehlakalo zomsebenzi ezilungiselelwe yiKomitjhini zitjengisa bonyana inengi lemisebenzi emitjha kulindeleke bonyana litholakale emabhizinisini wangekhaya , nemafemini amancani naphakathi asakhulako . Nanyana inengi lemisebenzi lingakhiwa ngokunqophileko emafemini athumela ipahla eenarheni zangaphandle , kodwana iinkoro ezirhwebelana nephasi loke zivamise ukuba namandla khudlwana ekukhuphuleni iinzuzo zangekhaya . Njengombana iSewula Afrika inezinga eliphasi leemali ezibulungiweko begodu kunetlhogeko lokusisa ezingeni eliphezulu nje , kuqakathekile ukukhulisa ipahla ethengiselwa iinarha zangaphandle nokunabisa umphumela eenkorwenezo . Ubujamo bokurhwebelana beSewula Afrika abukayifezi iminqopho le eminyakeni eli-15 edlulileko . Nasifuna ukuthuthuka kufanele bonyana sihlanganyele nephasi loke emikhakheni yokuzihlomulisa ngamakghonwethu wokukhiqiza nokurhwebelana ngepahla , begodu nangokwakha imithangalasisekelo kanye namakghono atlhogekako . Qinisekisa bonyana amalunga womkhandlu ayayazi imiphakathi yawo , ivakatjheleni njalonjalo begodu lalela iinkinga neendingo zomphakathi . Ikulumiswano engakahleleki ngokupheleleko eyenziwa nabanikeli ngemisebenzi abakhonjwe ku-Venn diagram . Lokhu kuthatha isikhathi esingaba li-iri li-1 ukufikela e-irini li-1.5 . Ukukhonjwa kwezinto eziphathekeko nenzekako ekufuze zenziwe kuligadango eqakathekileko lokutlama . Lokhu kungafaka hlangana imisebenzi umphakathi ozibanfdakanya kiyo ngokunqophileko ; nanyana imisebenzi engasekelwa ngeemali zakamasipala ezigabe isimetjhe . Tlola igama elithi ' inturhu ' efliphutjhadini bese ubawa abahlanganyeli batjho igama abalicabangako nabahlangana negama ' inturhu ' . Iimpendulo zizokuvamisa ukungabi zihle . Veza bona inturhu ayisiyimbi ngamalanga . Ingaletha itjhuguluko isenze bona sicabange ngokukhetha nokobana sikwenza bunjani . Indlela esilawula ngayo inturhu iyisitjhijilo . Ukuzithemba namtjhana ukuba nomqondo ovulekileko -umuntu lo uvulela yoke imibono emitjha neemphakamiso , uyalalelisisa , akathathi ihlangothi , uyakghona ukuthatha isiqunto , uyazithemba begodu utjhaphulula abantu . Kunikelwe amalunga wekomidi i-ajenda ngaphambi kokuthoma komhlangano ukuze azi kobana umhlangano umayelana nani ukuze azilungiselele . Ngesinye isikhathi kuzokudingeka kobana kube nombiko okhethekileko ngeendaba zamaphothfoliyo , nakunjalo , nangabe umniniphothfoliyo akwazi lokhu , angabonisana nomphakathi ngendaba leyo bese ubikela ikomidi ngendlela enembako . Umasipala wamadorobha amakhulu kanye nowekhaya kufuze ahlome amaKomidi weWadi . Yesibili , ngeyokuqinisekisa bonyana abahlanganyeli bendlelakambiso ye-CBP bayajanyelwa ezehlakalweni ze-IDP ngokusebenzisa izakhiwo neenkambiso ezikhona khathesi ngaphakathi kweendlela zokusebenza kwe-IDP okuziindlela ezimumethwe yiPakana yomHlahlandlela we-IDP , khulukhulu iForamu yabaJameli ye-IDP kanye neenqhema zemisebenzi yephrojekthi . Ukunikela umphakathi umbiko obuyako nelwazi , nokubawa imibono yomphakathi kungomunye womsebenzi welunga leKomidi yeWadi . Lokhu kungafuna ikhansela leKomidi yeWadi liphathe umhlangano . Ukwenza isethulo somhlangano kungaba yinto elikhuni khulukhulu nangabe kudinga iinsetjenziswa ezifana nama-overhead projector namtjhana amamakhrofoni . Yoke iminyango le ilindeleke ukuthuthukisa ' imitlamo yengcenye karhulumende ' amaqhinga wokusebenza ukuqinisekisa ukunikelwa komthangalasisekelo ofaneleko kamasipala begodu neensetjenziswa zakamasipala ezingapheliko ngaphakathi kwengcenye karhulumende . Indlela yokwenza koke iyatlhogakala ukwenzela bonyana ukwazi ukwenza indima yokuhlobana hlangana kweengcenye zakarhulumende ziziphendulele begodu ziqinisekise bonyana zihlanganiswe ngokuzeleleko nendlela yekambiso yomtlamo woke kamasipala . Ukubuyekezwa Kwemisebenzi eyenziwe ngonyaka : Umkhandlu kufanele unande ubika kumaKomidi wamaWadi nemiphakathi ngebhajedabo nokubuyekeza imisebenzi , njengengcenye yemihlangano yomphakathi . Nangabe ikomidakho ayinande ithola umbiko wokwenziwa komsebenzi emkhandlwinakho , imeyara kufanele yaziswe bona iKomidi yeWadakho ilindele ukwenziwa ngcono kurhulumende wendawo okhethwe ngokwentando yenengi . IBhodo yomKhawulo kaMasipala imuthetho ozijameleko olinganisa imikhawulo kamasipala . Idorobha linebubulo elincani kwamanikelela kanye nomphakathi olimako ozombeleze idorobha . Inengi labantu alisebenzi edorobhenapho . Kunamaplasi amathathu anobunikazi obuhlanganyelweko begodu abasebenzi abasebenza emaplasini lawo bafumana isabelo seenzuzo . Imisebenzi yephrogremu ifakile yini isandla ekungezelelekeni kwekghono labomma lokufumana iintlabagelo ( ifundo , ibandulo , amakhredithi njll ) na ? Abobaba bona ke ? Idayagramu elandelako itjengisa kobana umkhakha ngamunye wemiphumela yokuphathwa kwephrojekthi ekuhloleni kabutjha amagadango kanye nomzombe awalandelani ngokwemvelo . Ukujamela umphakathi kumaforamu wokukhulumisana - iKomidi yeWadi kufanele ibe nelwazi mayelana nomphakathi begodu kufanele aphakamise iindabezi emaforameni wokukhulumisana . Amarherho wezomnotho weenarha ezinengi ze-Afrika akhule ngokurhaba eminyakeni elitjhumi egadungileko , begodu lokhu begade kukokuthoma esikhathini pheze esisiquntu sekhulumnyaka ukobana kuphunguke ubuchaka ngalindlela , begodu inarhakazi le izakhele igama eenhlanganweni zephasi loke . Iinqhema zidlula emibuzweni , zitshwaye izinto eziqakathekileko eziveziweko ngesikhathi sokucocisana kwabo phezu kwephepha lokugadangisa . Ukuthenga ubuncani bakhona ama-20 000MW wegezi evuselelwako ngomnyaka wee-2030 , ukungenisa enarheni le igezi evela esiphandeni , ukujamiselela i-11 000MW leentetjhi zegezi ezisebenzisa amalahle esele zizidala kanye nokungezelela amasisomali wamandla weembaseli . Tjheja umuntu namtjhana isiqhema okhuluma kiso kanye nesihloko okhuluma ngaso . Isibonelo , abantu abaphatheki kuhle lokha nakukhulunywa ngeendaba ezifana ne-HIV ne-AIDS , begodu isihloko esinje kufanele usingene ngokutjheja okukhulu . Iinkomba zobungako zitjho iinomboro namaphesende wabomma nabobaba namkha iinhlangano namkha ezithintekako kunofana ngisiphi isiqhema namkha umsebenzi . Iinkomba zobungako , zidoswe emarherhweni wemininingwana yobulili obungakahlanganiwa begodu namarekhodi ahloliweko ngesikhathi sendlela yekambiso yomthethokambiso namkha yomtlamo wephrojekthi . Ukuba khona kwemininingwana yobungako besisekelo-kambiso okutjho bonyana iinkomba zivame ukufaka phakathi ezinye zamalunga wehlelo eliqothelweko isibonelo : Abomma benza okungasenani amaphesende ama-33 wamalunga weKomidi yamanzi ekupheleni komNyaka wesi- 2 . Ngomnyaka we-2004 ukuhlola kwatjengisa kobana abomasipala abanengi bafunyana bonyana umThetho wezAkhiwo zakaMasipala we-1998 , kanye nomThetho wamaHlelo waboMasipala we-2000 , ayikhange inikele ngemininingwana ngokuthi ahlonywa njani amaKomidi weWadi . Kwagazedwa isede yemihlahlandlela ngomhlaka-24 kuJuni ngomnyaka we-2005 ( Igazede yenomboro 27699 ) ukusiza abomasipala ngokunikela ngeminingwana eminengi kobana lokhu kwenziwa njani . Umqopho womfanekiso womraro ulithulusi elinesizo eliqala iminqopho kunemiraro ethuthukisa ihlelo lephrojekthi . Umfanekiso womraro utjhugululelwa emnqopheni womfanekiso womraro ngokutjhugulula unobangela omunye nomunye esitatimendeni esithe tjha . Isilinganiso sokwenzeka kwento , itjhejuli kanye nelawulo letjhuguluko lentengo : ukulawula amatjhuguluko ngehla kwephrojekthi . ' Isilinganisi sokwenzeka kwento esinanabako ' kulokha amatjhuguluko amancani amanengi enzeka okuletha kokugade kungakalindelwa begodu esikhathini esinengi ngikho okwenza iphrojekthi ingasaphumeleli . Kuqakathekile ukuphungula okuthenjiswe ukunikelwa lokhu okugade kusehlelweni . Ngemva kokuphela kwalomhlangano omalungana nomnqopho omunye nomunye , kufuze kube nesede yelwazi elivunyelanisiweko ekufuze lisetjenziselwe ukutlama . Urhulumende wekhaya uqalene neentjhijilo ezimbalwa ezihlobeneko , ezifaka hlangana amakghono angasimahle , amarherho wokuphatha abuthakathaka , ukucabhela okungakafaneli kwepolotiki ekuthathweni kweenqunto ezibuthekniki nezokuphatha , nokungalingani kwekghono lokukhuphula ingeniso yokuthuthukisa umphakathi . IKomitjhini inekolelo yokobana ngaphakathi komleyo womThethosisekelo , kunekghonakalo enengi yokwabiwa kwamandla nemisebenzi ngendlela engalinganiko nokwahluka okunengi mayelana nendlela ekungaphunyeleliswa ngayo amatjhejontangi aphumelelisako . Ekuphumeleliseni lokhu , kutlhogeka amaqhinga wesikhathi eside , kufaka hlangana ukutjheja indaba yokutlhogeka kwamakghono , ukuvumela ukwenziwa kweentjengiso-mbono ezinengana eenhlanganweni kanye nokusebenzisana nombuso wenarha newesifunda . Namhlanjesi , pheze amaphesende ali-17 wesitjhaba seSewula Afrika ayakwazi ukufumana ithungelelwanohlanganiso - okulinani elikhuphuka pheze ngamaphesende ama-20 ngomnyaka . Ukusetjenziswa kwamathintanonomboro kutjhugulule umphakathi ngeendlela ezingezwisiseki ngokupheleleko . Kusepepeneneni , nokho , bonyana abantu abatjha bayazisekela iimbikiindaba ezitja , begodu le kuyindlela enamandla khulu yokubabandakanywa kwezehlalakuhle . Hlathululela abahlanganyeli umzombe wenturhu ngokusebenzisa amanothi wekhoso asesAhlukweni 5 ukuba akusize . Esigabeni ngasinye bawa abahlanganyeli bacabange ngabakwaziko . UNom . uMali ubuya eSomalia begodu uhlala kuWadi XYZ . Ufaka isinghonghoyilo kumasipala sokungenzelwa imisebenzi mayelana nokususa iinsila . Lokha nakaya kumasipala ayokunghonghoyila utjelwa bona akasuye umSewula Afrika yeke akanalo nakancani ilungelo lokunghonghoyila . Nokwenza irhubhululo mayelana neendaba eziqakathekileko ezithinta ituthuko esikhathini eside esizako . Ngemva kobana ufundisise amanothi wekhoso ukuthoma ekhasini lama-65 ukuya ekhasini lama-67 , bahlathululele bonyana kilomsebenzi bazokusebenzisa ilwazi elibuthelelwe ecozululweni leendlela zokuziphilisa ukwenza iSWOT yeenqhema zehlalakuhle . Amaphrojekthi azakuqalela phasi iinzathu ezimurabhu wokulimala lula , okufaka phakathi ubulili nokungalingani okuphathelene nomphakathi begodu nephetheni ehlonyiweko yobulili yobulili nobungalinganiko buzakuhlala beqiswa amehlo . Bawa abo-A baphumele ngaphandle . Hlathululela abo-B bona sekuyisikhathi sokwenza ukulalela . Kodwa-ke kufanele balalele ngokutjheja . Lokhu kutjho bona kufanele banqophe emntwini , babuze imibuzo yokuhlathululelwa , bese balalela abangani babo . Isithembiso esinzinze phezu kwesethulo somThethosisekelo kufanele bonyana sithuthukiswe begodu sisetjenziswe emibuthanweni yeenkolo . Isethulo kufanele bonyana sitjengiswe kizo zoke iindawo zokusebenzela . Pheze emkhakheni omunye nomunye wepilo , kwenziwa imizamo yokwakha umphakathi ongabandlululaniko , wokuphungula izehlakalo ezingakarisiko zomlando nokunabisa amathuba wabo boke abantu . ISewula Afrika ikghonile ukwakha iinhlangano ezidingekako ekuletheni umbuso wentando yenengi namatjhuguluko . UmThethosisekelo wethu umumethe indlela eyame phezu kwamalungelo begodu ulindele bonyana kube nombuso wentando yenengi onepumelelo , ongabandlululi ngokobuhlanga nangokobulili begodu ongewabantu boke . Ukupholisa amanceba wombuso webandlululo nokulungisa ukungalingani okwabangelwa makhulukhulu weminyaka yokubandlululwa ngokobuhlanga kuzizinto eziqakathekileko nezirhabekileko kumthethosisekelo wethu . Ukufunyanwa kweensiza kunatjisiwe , umnotho unzinzisiwe begodu umphakathi ongabandlululani ngokobuhlanga uthoma ukubonakala . Iingidigidi zabantu ebegade babandlululwa ngaphambilini njenganje bafumana ifundo , amanzi , igezi , itjhejo lezamaphilo , izindlu neembonelelo zakarhulumende . Pheze abantu abangaba ziingidi ezintathu nanyana abangaphezulu bayasebenza namhlanjesi kunangomnyaka we-1994 , isilinganiso sobuchaka sehlile begodu imirholo eyi-avareji ikhule ngokunzinzileko , nasikhuluma iqiniso . Ilawulo lokuphathwa kobungozi : Ukuphendula ematjhugulukweni wengozi ngesikhathi soke sephrojekthi . Iingozi zizokutjhuguluka namtjhana msinyazana zibe bufakazi iphrojekthi isaragela phambili . Umtlamo wokulawula ingozi kufanele uhlaliswe kuhle njengobana lokhu kwenzeka begodu umphathi wephrojekthi kufanele azise boke ababandakanyekako . Ukufikeleka - Ngokufanako amanye amalunga womphakathi angeze afikelela lula eenthuthini begodu nangabe indawo yomhlangano nanyana yesetjheni yombiko obuyako ayifikeleki lula angeze bakghona ukukhambela umhlangano njengombana isikhwelo kungenzeka sibize nesikhathi esisithathako ukufika kileyo ndawo lokho kungabakhandela ukobana bawukhambele . Iingaba zokulungiselela ibhajedi zibonakala ehlelweni elibizwa umzombe webhajedi . Amalunga womphakathi begodu namaKomidi wamaWadi adinga ukutjheja umzombe lo benzelele ukuhlanganyela okuzwakalako . Amabhajedi amathathu asebenza ngesikhathi sinye emkhandlwini kamasipala : ibhajedi yomnyaka ogadungileko , ibhajedi yomnyaka kamasipala akuwo begodu nebhajedi yesikhathi esiphakathi somnyaka ozako . Lokhu kubizwa ngokubhajeda kweminyaka-minengi . Bakhombele bonyana batlole lemiphumela emithathu ekufuze inikelwe itjhejontangi efliphutjhadini ngombana izokuba lisizo emsebenzini olandelako . Eminye imithetho isib . umThetho wakaZweloke wokuTjhuguluka komHlaba ukatelela amaphiko womnyango ukuhlanganisa amahlelwabo namaphrojekthi ku-IDP kanti-ke imithetho yamanye amaphiko ayihlangabezani neendaba ezinje . Akunamaforamu amatjha wakarhulumende wangaphakathi namtjhana iinhlangano zenziwe ngeenhloso zokubuyekeza i-IDP . Kusetjenziswe amaforamu akhona nabalwe ngehla . Ukwethula imigomo enesizo yemakethe yabasebenzi neenhlohlomezelo zokukhulisa izinga lemisebenzi , khulukhulu imisebenzi yabantu abatjha kizo zoke iinkoro eziqatjha abantu abanamakghono aphasi ngokwesilinganiso . Ukufunda ukulalela akusiyindaba yokufunda iimpendulo ' ezilungileko ' kodwana kukufunda ukuba nomqondo omsinya kizo . Ukuba nomqondo omsinya kutjho ukuzimisela ukulalela omunye umuntu nalokhu akucabangako , ukubeka imibono yakhe ngeqadi , indlela okuphendulwa ngayo neenjwayelo . Ukuba nomqondo omsinya kuyindlela yepilo yokwala . Yenza isiqiniseko sokobana amalunga womphakathi ayazwisisa ibhajedi yokugcina i-SDBID begodu nesivumelwano somsebenzi . Indima yeKomitjhini yemiSebenzi yomBuso ekusekeleni iinlinganiso namazinga , nokutjheja iindlelakambiso zokuqatjha kufanele kuqiniswe . Kwenzakeleni lokha nawuzama ukutjhidelisa umnganakho lapho egade ujame khona ? Ingabe ngiwaphi amatjhuguluko aba khona weenkhathi zonyaka malungana nokusetjenziswa kwemithombo ( idayagramu ephathelene nokwenzeka kokuthize ngeenkhathi ezithize zonyaka ingasiza lapha ) ? Bekufike ukuyela ekupheleni komnyaka we-1970 iSeymour bekuyindawo ethi nawuyilinganisako ibonakale iyidistrigi enokuthuthuka ngehlangothini lezokulima . Umnotho bewudzimelele khulu ebubulweni elenza amaplanka begodu nefemu eyenza igwayi esentha yedorobha . Igwayi amatafula begodu iinthelo zamasitrasi ngizo ebezitjalelwa irhwebo . Ungawubandakanya bunjani umphakathi ku-IDP ? Kukhona iKomidi ye Wadi emajadu emphakathini . imihlangano ngokuvamileko ibanjwa nge-iri lesi-6 entambama phakathi kweveke . Ngombana abomma ngokwekolelo balindelwe ukobana babone abentwana begodu balungisele indeni ukudla , ngalesosikhathi abomma abanengi bayabhalelwa kukuba khona . Abanye abomma bayalila ngokukhamba nokukhwela amateksi aya ekhaya sele kunzima ebusuku . Abanye babuye godu banghonghoyile ngokobana nangabe bakwazile ukuya emhlanganweni izinto neenghonghoyilo zabo azithathelwa ehloko . Kanti abanye bathi baqalene nabantu abahlala bakwatile begodu nabasebenzisani bembaji abatlhorisanako ngitjho nangokukhanjelwa kwemihlangano begodu nokungabi khona emakhaya . Kwanjesi iinkulumiswano ngokukhukhuthiswa kwelokitjheli sele kuthomile phakathi kweKomidi yeWadi norhulumende wekhaya . Abomma batjhiywe ngaphandle . Bafuna ukuthoma ihlanganwabo ephathelene nezakhamuzi ngebanga lakho lokhu . Abobaba abawufuni umkhumbulo ofana nalo , bathi abomma akutlhlogeki bonyana bahlangane babodwa ngombana abobaba banekghono lokwenza zoke izinto eziphathelene nomphakathi . Umkhandlu okhethiweko kusiqunto esithethwe yiforamu kuma-IDP . Indima yokuhlanganyela kudemokhrasi kukwazisa , ukubonisana nokwenza iimphakamiso ngeenquntwezo , lokha nakwenziwa ikambiso yokutlama / yokuthatha iinqunto . IMITJHINI KARHULUMENDE : KUDALA IMISEBENZI YOMPHAKATHI EPHAKATHI KWABANTU BEGODU ETJHAYELWA BABANTU , EBUNJWE NGOKULINGANA , IKHWALITHI , I-TIMOROUSNESS NEKHOWUDI EQINISEKISIWEKO YOKUZIPHATHA OKULUNGILEKO , UKUHLELELA KWEQOPHELO ELIPHEZULU LOKUZIPHATHA OKULUNGILEKO , BEGODU NOKWETHULWA KOMSEBENZI WEKHWALITHI . Ukusebenzisa imali enengana kumasisomali kuligadango lokuthoma kwaphela . Begodu iSewula Afrika kufanele yenze ngcono ikhwalithi yokusetjenziswa kweemali ngokutlama ngconywana , ngokusebenzisa amarherho amahle wokuthenga ipahla nemisebenzi nangokuphalisana khudlwana kwezomnotho . Kunefuneko yokusebenza ngekghono kizo zoke iindleko zombuso , ngombana kunekghonakalo yokobana imikhakha leyo yoke ingathuthuka kabuthaka esikhathini esiphakathi . Khulukhulu kufanele kutjhejwe ukulawulwa komthethomlingwa wemirholo yombuso , ukwenza bonyana kube nemithombo yamatjhejontangi amanye . Lokhu kubandakanya ukulinganisa amagandelelo atjhayisanako anjengokungezelela inani labasebenzi , ukurholisa abosobizelomsebenzi abanamakghono imirholo elingeneko nokwenza ngcono iinzuzo ekufanele bazifumane . Ingabe umkhandlwakho unayo i-PMS ? Ihlathulule . IKomidi yeWadi ingaveza ukunganeliseki ngokutlolela i-ofisi lakaspikha kumasipala mayelana nokungenzi umsebenzi kwekhansela yewadi . Umkhandlu ungathatha eminye imisebenzi uyinikele amaKomidi wamaWadi . Iphepha lomqondo wephrojekthi kufuze lizaliswe malungana nephrojekthi ngayinye edinga isekelo lakarhulumende , ama-NGO nanyana amabubulo wekoro yangeqadi . Leliphepha lomqondo lisekela iphrojekthi ngokuhlathulula amatshwayo wayo begodu lisiza ekwaluseni iragelo phambili kanye nekwenzeni bonyana abantu babenokuziphendulela mayelana nezenzo zabo . Nakutlanywako dosa ingcoco hlangana neBatho Pele emsebenzini . Buza imibuzo engenzasi bese utjheja iimpendulo ezisemgadangisweni wephephandaba . Ngokuya kwesivumelwano , umnikeli womsebenzi angazibophelela ngokwenza umsebenzi othileko kamasipala esikhundleni sakamasipala ngaphakathi kweenkathi ezinqophileko , ibhajedi nezinto eziqothelweko . Umnikeli womsebenzi angaba nesibopho sokunikela umsebenzi kiwo woke umphakathi namkha ihlangothi lomphakathi kwaphela . Kungenzeka godu azithole anesibopho sokunikela yoke namkha ihlangothi elithile lalokho okumele kunikelwe . Isibonelo , ihlangano edzimelele emphakathini ingenza isivumelwano neentaradeni begodu bazibeke eendaweni lapha iinlori zomkhandlu zizazithatha khona . Ukuzibophelela ekusebenziseni iindlela zombuso nekoro yangeqadi zokuthenga ipahla nemisebenzi ezikghona ukugcugcuzela amabubulo wangekhaya nokuvulwa kwamathuba wemisebenzi . Ukuqinisa amaKomidi wewadi ukwenzela bonyana akwazi ukusebenzisana ngokupheleleko nge-IDP njengomtlamo ovulekileko kamasipala . Khumbula bona iinqunto ezenziwa yiKomidi yeWadi azibopheleli ilunga lomkhandlu wewadi . AmaKomidi weWadi akanamagunya ngokomthetho mayelana neenqunto zekhansela . Ngalokho iKomidi yeWadi idinga ukuthuthukisa ubudlelwana bokubambisana nelunga lomkhandlu begodu nokusebenzisa amathuba andlalwe ngehla ukuqinisekisa bona umbono womphakathi uthathelwa phezulu . UmThethosisekelo neenHlangano zakaMasipala kanye nemiThetho yamaRhelo kaMasipala ubeka iphahla lokobana imikhandlu kamasipala kufanele idlulise bunjani imithetho kamasipala . Indima edlalwa yi-CDM mayelana nokuhlalisa kuhle kwabomasipala bekhaya mayelana ne-HIV / AIDS . Ukuthintana nengcenye yeenqhema - isibonelo , iinhlangano zabalimi zithola imibonwazo ngemitlamo emayelana nemakhethe etja . Imibono bonobangela bangaphandle abangaba nomthelela eminqopheni yephrojekthi . Zizinto esingakwazi ukuzilawula begodu zidinga ukuqalelelwa ngombana nange zahlala zinganakwa zingenza bona iphrojekthi ingaphumeleli . Isibonelo , nangabe ilanga lokwakhiwa kwesisekelo somakhiwo libekiwe , izulu line amalangana , lokho kuzokuliya ikambiso kodwana akusiyo into esingayilawula . Ngebanga , lalokho , irherho leendlela zokwenza zidinga ukufaka phakathi iinjayezo nokulamula kuwo woke amaleveli ukuqinisekisa ngerherho , umuntu opheleleko netjhuguluko elihlanganiswe ngokwamaqhinga wokuphumelelisa , lokhu kumele kubandakanye kiletjhuguluko emuntwini ngamunye , isiqhema , ihlangano begodu nelevelini yomphakathi . Woke amalunga womphakathi anelungelo lokuqala umhlangano okhethekileko womkhandlu lapha kukhulunyiswana ngebhajedi begodu ivowudelwa . AmaKomidi wamaWadi kumele aqinisekise bonyana ukuhlanganyela komphakathi kuyakhuthazwa ngokobana kwaziswe umuntu woke ngomhlangano . Ukukhamba uye ngehla kokubonisana begodu nokuhlanganyela ekwakheni ihlangano egcinekako ngokutlhama ithungelwano eliragela phambili begodu nokubonisana ngemibono emitjha nabantu abadlala iindima ezahlukahlukeneko . ImiPhumela yeeNdawo eziQakathekileko ( ama-KPI ) azizinto eziphathekako , aminqopho emedekako leyo iinsebenzi evumelene ukobana izuzwe ngesikhathi esithileko . Isisebenzi ngasinye kufanele sibe nekontraga yokuphatha ukwenziwa komsebenzi okungileyo emumethe ama-KPI , ikontraga le ingasetjenziselwa ukobana baziphendulele mayelana komsebenzi abawenzileko ngokukhambisana nama-KIP . Ukwenziwa kweqhinga lomthethokambiso we-HIV ne-AIDS kanye nomthethokambiso wemsebenzini . Iqhinga lokuthintana - Abomasipala benza amaqhinga wokuqinisekisa bona ukuthintana kucatjangwa ngeqhinga nokuhlaliswa kuhle eenkambisweni zakamasipala . Ematjhumini weminyaka ezako , njengombana amahlelo wezomnotho avumbukako azabe akhulisa isabelo sawo sokurhwebelana ephasini nokusisa , isilinganiso sokwehla kwamandla wezomnotho e-United States , e-Europe ne-Japan sizakuba nemiphumela ekhambisana naso mayelana nomthelela weenarhezi kwezepolotiki nesijoni . Lokhu kungarholela ekutheni kuhlelwe ngobutjha ukujanyiswa kwehlelo lezokubusa leentjhabatjhaba nobudlelwano bamazwe ngamazwe , elitjengisa amasentha amatjha wokurherha . Idayagramu ekhasini elilandelako ibonisa ukobana kwenzeka njani elevelini yomuntu oyedwa , ukuphathwa kokulamula ukuhlukana kumele kunqophe phezu kobana umehluko womuntu ngamunye uyithinta njani ukuzwa , iindlela umuntu aziphatha ngayo , iintjisakalo , iindingo nendlela evulekileko yokuziphatha . Lokhu kuzakubuye kuhlole isiphiwo somuntu ngamunye ukutjhugulula ikolelwakhe , ukuzindla , izinto ezinganamirabhu . Ukulawula kumele kutlanywe elevelini yesiqhema ukwenzela bonyana wehlise izinga lokuzindla nezinto ezinganamirabhu begodu bakhombe iinqabo ezingatholakala emasikweni emigomeni , emarherhweni begodu neenkambisweni ezikhona . Khamba uye ngaphandle bese uhlathululele u-A bona kufanele bacabange isitori esithize namtjhana isehlakalo abangabelana nabangani babo . Ukutjhuguluka kuqakathekile mayelana nokubandakanyeka komphakathi . Imiphakathi ingaba khona kwaphela kwesinye isikhathi begodu imitlamo ingatlhoga bona ikhutjhwe nanyana itjhugululwe ngokuya neendingo zabantu ezithintwa zizehlakalo , isib . Umtlamo wokutjhugulula ibhizinisi : ukutlamela ukobana imali-ngeniso ibe ibe etholakala epahleni eyamukelwako kanye nemisebenzi ekukhambeni kwesikhathi esibekiweko . Abakghonakalisi kufuze baqinisekise bonyana abajameli beenqhema ezilimala lula babayingcenye yeenqhema ezisebenzako begodu babanelizwi eenqhemeni . Abomasipala kufuze bahlele begodu balawule iindlelakambiso zabo zokuphatha , zokwaba iimali kanye nokutlama ukwenzela bonyana bakwazi ukutjheja ntangi iindingo ezisisekelo zomphakathi . Isigaba 74a no-b somThetho wezAkhiwo zakaMasipala , we-1998 undlala imisebenzi namagunya wamaKomidi weWadi ngokubophelela umsebenzi kumaKomidi weWadi ukuze ajamele umphakathi eendabeni zawo . AmaKomidi wamaWadi angenza umzamo okhethekileko ukuqinisekisa bonyana abomma bajamelekile emihlanganweni yemibiko ebuyako nokobana imibonwabo iyatholakala begodu iyafakwa phakathi embikweni obuyako phakathi komphakathi , umkhandlu nelunga lomkhandlu . Kufanele kwamukelwe indlela yokulawula kwaphela mayelana nokuqatjhwa kwabasebenzi abasezingeni eliphasi , begodu iinkhulu eziphezulu kufanele ziphiwe igunya elipheleleko lokuqatjha istafu eminyangweni yazo . Ngokwakha ubudlelwana namakhansela - AmaKomidi weWadi adinga ukwakha ubudlelwana bokubambisana nokusebenzisana namakhanselawo wewadi njengoba amakhansela kungiwo akha umkhandlu . AmaKomidi weWadi kufanele ajamise ikambiso eyakhiweko ukwenzela bona akwazi ukuhlangana njalo nekhansela lawo lewadi ukulazisa mayelana neendaba zomphakathi , ezivela ngemihlangano yeKomidi yeWadi begodu nokwenza isiqiniseko bona kwenziwa imihlangano njalo ukuze umphakathi uhlale unelwazi ngezinto zomphakathi . AmaKomidi weWadi kufanele enze isiqiniseko godu sokuhlanganyela namakhansela ukuze anikele umbono ekwenzeni ilawulo , ibhajedi kanye neenkambisweni zokutlama zetuthuko ehlanganisiweko . Khathesi hlathululela abahlanganyeli bonyana ngemva kobana umphakathi uvumelene ngombono , kufuze bonyana kuzwanwe ngeminqopho begodu kutlanywe namaqhinga womnqopho ngamunye . Qala amanothi wekhoso asekhasini lama-44 nelama-45 ukwenzela bonyana akwazi ukukusiza . Umkhakha A abomasipala ( bamadorobha amakhulu ) : La madorobho amakhulu , anamandla akhethekileko wesigungu sokubeka imithetho eendaweni zabo . Namtjhana kunganabudlelwana obunqophileko nosomlomo , kodwana amalunga weKomidi yeWadi anokuthintana ngemihlangano nemigidi yomkhandlu . Hlathulula bonyana iinqhema kumele zicabange ngabomasipala abajayelene nabo begodu batlhame ibhajedi yokusebenza kamasipala osemkhumbulweni . Ukusuka ekukhulumisaneni ukuya ekunikeleni amandla kugcugcuzela ubunikazi betuthuko yendawo begodu kwenza bonyana abantu bangathembeli kurhulumende . Ukunikela amandla wamakghono kubadlaliindima abahlanganyela kumaforamu wobujameli be-IDP bona bakwazi ukuzibandakanya ngepumelelo ekambisweni yokuhlela nokwenza umsebenzi ngokwesiqunto . Irherho laborhulumende abahlukahlukeneko lineengcenye ezinengi khulu , kodwana isitjhijilwesi akukafaneli sibe siviko sokuhlangahlangana kwamazinga wokuziphendulela . Ukuhlonywa komNyango wokuTjhejwa nokuHlungwa kwemiSebenzi kuligadango elihle lokuqinisa umzombe wokuziphendulela . Begodu iKomitjhini ikhombela bonyana iimvumelwano zabomabelwamatjhere namabhizinisi wombuso kanye neemvumelwano zomsebenzi ezenziwa nabongqongqotjhe beKhabinethi kufanele zaziswe umphakathi . Ukubalekela - ukubalekela inturhu ipendulo ejayelekileko begodu nethemba kukobana nawubalakela inturhu ' izokukhamba ' . Ukusebenza ngenturhu yindlela ehle edinga ikghono , ukuzitjheja nokuzimisela ukuzibandakanya . Ukwala yindlela ejayelekileko yokubalekela inturhu . Namtjhana singazizwa bona siphendula kuhle , ukubalekela inturhu kungaletha umphumela lapho abantu bazozithola bahlangahlangene , bakwatile , bakhubekile begodu badineke bacabange bona inturhu izokuphela . Ubujamo nabunjalo bujamo BOKULOBA / LOBA kizo zoke iinhlangano ezibandakanyekako enturhwini . Cabanga emva ngendlela okungenzeka ngakhona begodu ukhumbule isehlakalo lapha walemuka khona kokuthoma bonyana uhlukile ebesaneni nangabe umntazana , begodu mahlangothi womabili , lokhu kutjho bonyana bewulindeleke bonyana uziphathe ngendlela ehlukileko begodu uphethwe ngendlela ehlukileko . kumele utjheje umehluko ekuziphatheni ingasi umehluko wokomzimba . Yabelana indatjanakho nomnganakho . Urhulumende wendawo kufanele agunyaze begodu athathe isiqunto sendlela yokusebenzisa ingeniso-mali kanye neemali ezitholakeleko ukubhadala imisebenzi namaphrojekthi abafuna ukuwenzela umphakathi . Lokhu kubudisi ukukutjheja , ngaphandle kobana kube namabhajedi abekelwe ngeqadi abekelwe imisebenzi enqophileko ' yabomma ' , ' abobaba ' namkha ' ubulili ' . UKWENZA NGCONO UMSEBENZI WOMBUSO KURAGELA PHAMBILI NOKUBA SITJHIJILO ESIFUNA UKUZIBOPHELELA KWAZO ZOKE IINSEBENZI ZOMBUSO UKOBANA ZISEBENZE , INGASI UKUHLANGABEZANA NEMINQOPHO KARHULUMENDE KWAPHELA KODWANA ZANELISE LOKHO OKUFUNWA MALUNGA WOMPHAKATHI WOKUFIKELELA EMISEBENZINI esezingeni ELIPHEZULU NEPILO ENGCONO KIBO BOKE ABANTU . AYIKHO INTO ESINGABAMBELELA NGAYO EKUBHALELWENI KWETHU EKWENZENI LOKHU OKULINDELWEKO , NJENGOMBANA KUSEMTHETHWENI BEGODU KUHLE . Lokha nakuthoma ukuvela izinto ekufuze zinikelwe itjhejontangi , kungaba lisizo ukumema abanikeli ngemisebenzi abaphathelene nalemiphumela bonyana babekhona lokha nakutlanywako elangeni elilandelako . Amaminidi womkhandlu amhlangano okhanjiswa emphakathini . Ukwakha ibhoduluko elihle ekunikeleni imisebenzi- ku-1.2 sicocisane ngeentjengisi zedemokhrasi nesisekelo samalungelo wobuntu . Amalungelo akazijameli awodwa kodwana eza nesibopho . Ukukhuthaza umphakathi ukobana ube nesibopho mayelana nezehlakalo nemisebenzi ukuze amalungelo aqinisekiswe kumThethosisekelo nakuVikelomalungelo kufanele atjhejwe kuhle begodu akhuthazwe . Isibonelo ilungelo lokuba nendawo ehlanzekileko likhambisana nesibopho sezakhamuzi ukobana zibhadale amanani nemithelo ukuze imisebenzi ikghone ukunikelwa . Umtlamo godu utlhoga ukobana imisebenzi nalokho okwenziwako kunikelwe abantu abathileko bese bekwa isikhathi okumele umsebenzi ngamunye uphele ngaso . Ukubuyekeza isibonelelo sezindlu nerherho lemali yesizo yokwehlisa iindleko ukuqinisekisa bonyana iinsetjenziswa ezisetjenziswako zinqotjhaniswa namatjhuguluko amahle womgomo wokuhlaliswa kwabantu . Ukwenza ngcono ikhwalithi yefundo kutlhoga ilawulo elitjhejisisako nesekelo lawo woke amahlangothi anekareko kanye nesikhathi . Ukuya ngokwerhubhululo lamatjhuguluko wamarherho ama-20 wefundo elenziwe ngomnyaka wee-2010 , [ 1 ] iindlela ezizwakalako zokusebenza zithoma ukuba nemiphumela ngemva kweminyaka esithandathu yokusungulwa kwamatjhuguluko , begodu zibonakala zinamakhakhazela amahle esikhathini eside esizako . Irherho lokuhlola elingaphasi lingakusiza ekuhleleni ikulumiswano nomjameli womnikeli ngemisebenzi ngombana kuzokufuneka bonyana ilwazi latjelwe nabanye . Umtlamo lo uyisebenzisa ngokuzeleko yini imibono , amakghono wokuphaliseka namandla na ? Nangabe iinomboro ezilinganako azikghonakali qinisekisa bonyana okungasenani uyakghona ukuthola imasi enobujamo obumbi yabomma nabobaba okutjho bonyana okungasenani ama-30% ) . Woke lomsebenzi otlolwako wenziwa siqhenyana somphakathi esinikelwe isibopho sokuhlathulula ngokuzeleko umtlamo wamaswaphela . Uthonywa evekeni yokutlama begodu uqedwa evekeni elandelako . Ukulalelwa komphakathi okuvame ukubanjwa ngendaba ethize . Isibonelo , ukulalelwa komphakathi ukuthola umbono ngomthetho ophakanyisiweko . Lokhu kutjho bona iKomidi yeWadi , iyindlela engasetjenziswa miphakathi ukutjho iinghonghoyilo namtjhana ukuphakamisa iindaba namtjhana ukutjho iindingo ezithileko . AmaKomidi weWadi anomsebenzi omkhulu ezakhamuzini wokuthatha iinghonghoyilwezi bazise emkhandlwini ngendlela yepumelelo . AmaKomidi weWadi akukafaneli acabhele ukusebenza komkhandlu , lokhu kufaka hlangana ukunganikeli imilayelo eenkhulwini umsebenzaso kuwukusa iinqunto ezithethweko ekhanseleni . Kodwana banendima eqakathekileko abafanele ukuyidlala enjengohlanganiso yomphakathi nomkhandlu . Yenza isiqiniseko sokobana isiqhema siyawuzwisisa umehluko phakathi ' kokuqakatheka ' ' nokufumaneka ' . Lamagama angatjhugululelwa elimini elikhulunywa endaweni leyo . I-GEP inamanani ambalwa womtlamo wesekelo lokungenelela ukukusiza bona uhlele imihlahlandlela mayelana nokuphatha ibhizinisakho begodu nokulemuka nokubogaboga okungafuna itjhejo . Ungabeki phambili imibonwakho . Linda bewuzwe bona abanye abantu bathini bese emva kwalokho ungafaka neyakho . Abomasipala banikela ngeemadlana ezingatjho litho ukusekela ukuphunyeleliswa okurhabekileko komtlamo wewadi ukwenzela bonyana kungalahleki amandla wokutlama . Iinqunto ezimayelana nokukhutjhwa kwaleziimali zokulekelela kufuze zivele ekambisweni yokutlama , ikambiso yokukhetha kufuze yenziwe ngendlela esetjhatjhalazini begodu umphakathi kufuze ufumane umbiko obuyako . Umsebenzi otlolwako olandelako uyahlathulula bonyana singakhiwa bunjani isabelo seemali malungana naleziimali zokusekela zewadi . Umkhandlu wakamasipala ungaphadlhalaja iKomidi yeWadi nangabe iyabhalelwa kufikelela iminqopho yawo . Isahlukwesi sendlale iminqopho neenkambisolawulo zomtlamo womphakathi begodu saqala nokobana lendlela imumethwe bunjani yikambisolawulo yokuthuthukiswa kwaborhulumende bemakhaya . I-CBP iyingcenye eqakatheke kwamanikelela yokuthuthukiswa kwemiphakathi , yokukhuphula izinga leensetjenziswa nokusebenzisa imithethokambiso eyendlalwe emithethweni ejanyisiweko karhulumende wemakhaya kanye nokuqinisekisa bonyana umThethosisekelo wezakhamuzi uba yipumelelo . Izahluko ezintathu ezilandelako kubonelela ngamakghono enzekako wokusebenzisa i-CBP . Ikghono lokukhulumisana lingakhuphula indlela amalunga weKomidi weWadi asebenza ngayo namakhansela , iinkhulu zakamasipala kanye nabanye . Ukuphambana okunengi kungabalekelwa begodu kungaqalanwa nakho lula khulu ngokukhuphula ukukhulumisana . Ukurarulula umraro - le yingcenye eneselele ekambisweni yokulamula begodu kusesigabenesi lapho kufanele kuvunyelanwe ngesisombululo . Umlamuli usiza iinqhema bona zikhulumisane ngeensombululo ezingaba khona , zibeka iimphakamiso ngendlela eziqakatheka ngayo bese uthola isivumelwano esanelisa zoke iinqhema . Umlamuli angadinga ukusebenzisa iindlela ezahlukahlukeneko ukurholela iinqhema ephuzwini ezingavumelana ngalo . Lokhu kungafaka ukuvumela iinqhema ukuya entumbeni , ukusebenza nesinye isiqhema begodu nenye , ukulethe iinqhema ndawonye , kanye nokutlama isivumelwano esanelisa zoke iinqhema . Ngalesisikhathi sesigaba sokutlama , abadlaliindima kufanele bakhonjwe begodu neensebenzi ezifaneleko kufanele zibandakanywe ukwenza isiqiniseko sepumelelo yokwenziwa kwephrojekthi . Kwesinye isikhathi ilunga lesiqhema sephrojekthi lizokuthola kuqakathekile ukwenza isiqhema sokusekela ukuze liphumelelise imiphumela abonokuziphendulela kiyo . Isibonelo , ukuze uhlele ikhonferensi , ukuhlelwa kwekhambo labantu abathunyiweko kufanele kwenziwe . Ngalokho umphathi wephrojekthi angabeka isiqhema esisekelako esizokusebenza ngeendaba zekhambo . Isiqhema esisekelako sizokuhlathululelwa sizokuhlathululelwa siqhema sephrojekthi okuzokufaka hlangana iinkhathi ezibekiweko , imisebenzi , ukwabiwa kwemisebenzi namabhajedi . Ezinye iimali ezibolekwa ngaphandle zitholakala eemakethe ezikulu ezifana namabhanga wamarhwebo . Abomasipala abanengi akusibo abasezingeni lokunganikelwa isikwelede , okwenza bonyana kube budisi kibo ukobana bangakwazi ukuboleka imali . Urhulumende usadinga bonyana athole indlela yokulwisana nekinga efana nale . Itsengo lobulili kulithulusi elisebenzako ngombana lephula amastiriyothayiphu , liveza iindima esikhathini esinengi eziqalelwa phasi , lirhelebhe ukuqinisekisa ukujameleka kokuhlukana ekuphathweni kwebhoduluko begodu likhomba iinhlangano zekhaya ezisekela imiphakathi . Khumbula bonyana kuqakathekile ukukhulumisana nabanikeli ngemisebenzi ukuzwa imibono yabo malungana neendaba ezithinta umphakathi kanye nemisebenzi yabo ukwenzela bonyana bakwazi ukwamukela nokusekela umfakela womphakathi . Umsebenzi wekhansela kuqinisekisa kobana imisebenzi esisekelo iyanikelwa begodu nokukhuphula ituthuko eendaweni ezingaphasi kwalo . Amakhansela kanye neenkhulu kumele ziqinisekise kobana kunemali eyaneleko ukunikela ngemisebenzi nokukhuphula umtlamo wokuthuthukisa . Ukukatelela -isikhulumi esikatelelako sikholwa bona ' ngilungile mina ' , sinomkhumbulo omfitjhani , simlaleli ongalaleli kuhle , sifuna ukwenza koke , singulizwi lakhe , sikhuluma ngephimbo eliphezulu , siyathusela , asibekezeli . Ukubhajeda ngobudlabha namkha ungakatjheji ngemali esetjenziswa budlabha begodu nemali ebuthelelweko engakaneli , emaswapheleni ingadosela umasipala etjhonweni . Sebenzisa umtato owephukileko ukudlulisa isifundweni ngendlela ekarisako yokutjengisa kobana kulula kangangani bonyana ilwazi likhulumeke ngokunganembiko kanye nomonakalo obangwa ngilokhu njengombana kudala ukuhleba kanye neensolo . Imibiko yebhajedi kufanele inikelwe khonokho njengemibiko yokutjheja , ukubuyekeza nokuhluza . Kufanele itjengise ukubandamela kwephrojekthi njengalokhu kuvunyelenwe kubhajedi nokobana ngiliphi igadango elizokuthathwa ukubuyisela izinto emtlhaleni . Umkhandlu ingabe usebenzise indlela yiphi , umphakathi wona usebenzise yiphi ? Ngokuqakathekileko , itjhejuli yeensetjenziswa yibhajedi . Ukubhajeda kuqakatheke ngendlela yokobana kungatjho umehluko hlangana kwepumelelo nokubhalelwa kwephrojekthi . Nangabe kubhajedwe kancani , kutjho bona eminye imisebenzi angekhe yenziwe . Nangabe iindleko zilinganiselwe phezulu , kuzokuba budisi ukuba nemali eyaneleko yokwenza iphrojekthi . Sekusikhathi sokukhomba imiraro eqakathekileko kanye neenthiyo ebujameni obukhona , abonobangela bazo kanye nendlela ezinomthelela ngayo kwezinye iindaba kufanele izwisiswe . Ilemuko leSewula Afrika mayelana nokusebenzisana nephasi loke lifaka hlangana iinzuzo ezibonakalako kanye namanye amahlangothi amanengi . Isitjhijilo ngesokusebenzisa kuhle amathuba anjalo nokuvikela amaSewula Afrika - khulukhulu lawo atlhagako - eengozini ezikhambisana namaphethini amatjha wokurhwebelana kanye nokusiselana . Isibonelo , iSewula Afrika inezinga eliphasi lemali ebulungiweko begodu ithembele eemalini zeenarha zangaphandle ukusekela amasiso wazo ngeemali . Ukuthembela emasisweni weenarha zangaphandle kwenza bonyana irherho lezomnotho lekhayapha lizifumane lisengozini ekulu yokutjhugutjhuguluka . Ukukhula kabuthaka eenarheni ezithuthukileko kukhambisana nefuneko ekulu yeenarha ezisathuthukako , begodu lokho kusize ekutheni ukuthengiswa kwepahla yenarha le emazweni wangaphandle kube sesilinganisweni esikarisako . Begodu ngakwelinye ihlangothi itjhugulukweli liletha isitjhijilo kilabo abatlama imigomo kanye nebakhiqizini , ngombana ifuneko yanjenganje yamamakethe amatjha avelako akhiqiza kwaphela ipahla yerhwebo kanye nematheriyali engakasetjenzwa , kunokobana akhiqize imikhiqizo eyahlukahlukeneko efunwa ziinarha ezithuthukileko . Indabapikiswano ngeyokobana ingabe iSewula Afrika ingakghona ukubawa abantu abangasebenziko ukobana bazibandakanye ekukhiqizeleni amamakethe athengisa ipahla eenarheni zangaphandle . Abanye baveza ukuthi irherho lezomnotho aliphalisani ekukhiqizeni kwabasebenzi abanengi ngombana isakhiwo seendleko siphezulu khulu , isilinganiso sokurweyilelana sitjhuguluka ngokungakalindeleki khulu , imithangalasisekelo iyatlhayela begodu isakhelo samakghono sikhawulelwe khulu . Kodwana iSewula Afrika ingakghona ukuphalisana emikhakheni eyahlukahlukeneko nange imiraro le ingatjhejwa - begodu inengi layo lingatjhejwa . Ukutjhuguluka ngokungakalindeleki kwesilinganiso sokurweyilelana kuliya ipumelelo begodu umtlamo lo uphakamisa bonyana ukurarulula umraro weendleko zemithombo yangekhaya begodu ukuba khona kwamakghono kungaba nomthelela oragela phambili mayelana neendleko . Njengenarha enengeniso ephakathi , iSewula Afrika kufanele bonyana iphalisane ngemikhiqizo nangamatshwayorhwebo amahle khulu , begodu nangokuzibandakanya ngepumelelo emaqhingeni wokwaba wephasi loke . Lokhu kuzokutlhogeka ukuzibophelela khudlwana erhubhululweni netuthukweni begodu nekuyithengeni kanye nekuyithengiseni , okuligadango eliphumelelisako lamalojistiksi kanye nobuhlakani obuphumelelisako bezomnotho . Ihlelo lokufaka iimfundiswa ezineziqu emsebenzi neqhinga lokuthuthikiswa kwamakghono lakarhulumende wekhaya kufanele kwethulwe ukudosa abongikhethani bekhwalithi ephezulu . Ukwakha , ngesikhathi esifaneleko , iinkimu ezimbalwa begodu ezitja zamanzi ezizakwazi ukuphakela amasentha wemadorobheni namabubulo , amasentha amatjha wokuthelelela asendaweni yomlambo obizwa Umzimvubu nemafledzeni weMakatini , kanye nehlelo lenarha lokongiwa kwamazi ukwenza ngcono ukusetjenziswa kwamanzi . Ngomnyaka we-1992 iinhlangano zomphakathi zedorobha zatlhama iforamu yokuthuthukisa iSeymour edzimelele emphakathini . Yayakhiwe yi-SANCO ( okuyiHlangano yomPhakathi yeLizwe eSewula Afrika ) , I-ANC ( okufaka hlangana iLigi yabaTjha begodu neLigi yaboMma ) begodu neenqhema zaboTitjhere . Inembo-mbono yeforamu kwakukutlhama ubudzimelelo obubanzi beqhinga letuthuko ebeyinqophe ukuzuzisa woke umphakathi wendawo begodu iqinise nomnotho wekhaya . Kuzakuba nokutlhogeka kwethuba lokuhlanganyela nokudosaphambili kwabomma . Amaqhinga angekhe aqalane nokunikelwa kwabomma amandla , njengombana ituthuko yemisebenzi ephathelene nomphakathi , amarherho wokondla abentwana , amasentha wabomma nezinye iindawo eziphephileko . Ukulalela okukhutheleko kufuna izwelo begodu kufaka hlangana nokulalela ngomnqopho , ukurarulula / ukusombulula umraro , ukwabelana ngeenkareko . Jamela umuntu aqede lokho akutjhoko . Ungamngeni emlonyeni unikela wakho umbono . Hlathulula bonyana indlelakambiso ye-CBP idinga ukwakhiwa komtlamo wewadi ngombana umtlamo wewadi ulithulusi lokuqinisekisa bonyana imibono kanye namatjhejontangi wezakhamuzi ayafakwa ku-IDP . Tlola amaphuzu aqakathekileko emekaradeni amancani namtjhana encwadini yamanothi wenzelele ukunande uqala khona . Nanyana iintatimende zepahla , iinkolodo kanye nengeniso zizihle nje , kodwana inengi lamabhizinisi weSewula Afrika alisisi ngombana umnotho wephasi loke usese buthakathaka . Begodu amabhizinisi atshwenyekile ngamatjhuguluko womgomo nebhoduluko lokulawula elingaphakamisa iindleko . Kokhunye , izinga eliphasi lesisomali nalo lingunobangela lokutlhayela kwemithangalasisekelo ehlinzekelwa mabhizinisi wombuso . ISewula Afrika kufanele iphelise lomzombe wokuthuthuka kabuthaka nesisomali eliphasi . Umbuso unendima eqakathekileko ekufanele uyidlale ekwakheni ukuthembeka nokuzithemba ukugcugcuzela isisomali lesikhathi eside . Begodu ikoro yezamabhizinisi inendima ekufanele iyidlale - nangabe omunye nomunye usisa khudlwana , iinzuzo zomnotho zizakuhlomulisa ikoro yangeqadi . ISAHLUKWESI SITJHEJA ABADLALIINDIMA ABAHLUKAHLUKENEKO nobudlelwana babo ekusebenzeni kwamaKomidi weWadi . Begodu sitjheja amano afaneleko wokukghonakalisa angasiza amaKomidi weWadi ukusebenzisana nabadlaliindima . Nikela ipara ngayinye ikambisolawulo ( unganikela ipara edlula kweyodwa ikambisolawulo efanako , kodwana lokho kuya ngenani labahlanganyeli onabo ) bese uyatjheja bonyana bazoyisebenzisa bunjani ikambisolawulo emphakathini wekhabo . Nasele isitejesi sifike emaphethelweni , iphrojekthi ifanele ihlathululwe kuhle . Iindleko , iimbopho , ukukhetha into eqakathekileko kunenye kanye namatjhejuli kufanele azwisiswe begodu nababambisani kufanele bazwisise bona ipumelelo izokumedwa bunjani nokobana ubufakazi buzokubuthelelwa bunjani . Indima yeKomitjhini yokuTlama yeliZwe Loke kululeka umbuso nenarha mayelana neendaba ezithinta ituthuko yenarha yesikhathi eside . Lo mtlamo wenarha yoke , begodu woke amahlangothi womphakathi kufanele bonyana azibophelele ekuwuphumeleliseni . Ukuphumelelisa umtlamo lo ngepumelelo , iKomitjhini ikhomba umlandelande wamaphuzu aqakathekileko . Buyela emuva embuzweni ngamunye bese utjheja ngokurhunyeziweko bonyana iKomidi yeWadakho inakho ukungafani phakathi kweenqhema zekolo , zobuzwe namkha kungaba ngiziphi iinqhema na ? Ukwazisa - umphakathi unikelwa ilwazi elibuya kumkhandlu . Lokhu kungaba ngokombiko obuyako nanyana amaphetjhana . Iimphakamiso ezenziwa mphakathi angeze zathathelwa ehloko nanyana zitjhejwe . Ipendulo : Amakhansela avala umnyango lokha nakabona iwoma lisiza aphuma ngomnyango wangemva . Kuzakusiza godu amakomidi wamaWadi ukwenza imisebenzabo njengabantu abahlanganisa umphakathi nomkhandlu kanye nemikhandlwabo yamawadi nangabe banetlhatlha lokuzibandakanya . UKUZE KUQINISEKISWE UKUGCINEKA KWETUTHUKO , kuyatlhogeka ukuvuma ukuqakatheka kobulili obubili obunjengezinto ezizijameleko nezengezelelanako ngokwebhayoloji . Godu kuqakathekile ukuhlonipha ukulingana nokufana okuzeleko kweendima eziphathelene nomphakathi ukobana zithoma eempilweni zabobaba nabomma . Ngendlela abobaba nabomma abathathwa nabaphathwa ngayo ingenye yezinto eziziinkonkhonkhwani zelinye nelinye irherho lezepolotiki , eliphathelene nomphakathi begodu nezomnotho . Ngesikhathi esifanako , indlela esetjenziswa ngayo ingenye yamahlangothi abonakalisa ngokweqileko . isahlukwesi sihlola indlela engcono yokungenisa iinkambisolawulo zobulili ngokulingana kumaphrojekthi wetuthuko , Isahluko sivalwa ngekulumiswano yeenthijilo iSewula Afrika eqalene nazo nangabe ubunjalo bokubandakanyeka kobulili ingalandelelwa ngokukhuthala . Ukuqalana netjhejo lezamaphilo wabomma namasana . Ikambiso eyenziweko lapho umuntu wesithathu angathathi ihlangothi ukusiza ngokwekambiso ukuthuthukisa ikulumiswano hlangana nabantu ababandakanyekako , esikhathini esinengi ngendlela yomhlangano . Lokhu kwenziwa ngokuqondisa okumumethweko , ukugcugcuzela ilwazi ngokudlhegana , begodu nokusiza nokulawula ikambiso ukuze umsebenzi othile wenziwe ngobudisi obuncani . Abahlanganyeli basebenza ngababili begodu bafundisisa iinkambisolawulo eziqakathekileko eziphathelene nendlela yokuziphilisa okubambelelako . Ikomidi ephetheko namtjhana ikomidi ephetheko yakasodorobha ithola iimphakamiso emakomidini wephothifoliyo kanye nabaphathi bomkhandlu abazokwazisa nge-ajenda yomkhandlu . Ngiziphi izehlakalo nanyana iinqhelo ezikulu ezenzeke emphakathini wekhethu eminyakeni ema-30-50 egadungileko ( ngaphambi kokwenzeka kwamatjhuguluko amakhulu ? Ukulawula ikhwalithi : Ukutjheja iphrojekthi enqophileko kuletha imiphumela yokulinganisa bona ikhambelana nomthetho onqophileko wamazinga wekhwalithi , ukukhomba kanye nokwenza iindlela zokuqeda abonobangela ababanga ukunganeliseki . Indlela enzinze esiyingini yetjhejo lezamaphilo yemitholapilo iyingcenye yesigaba sehlahlubopumelelo setjhorensi yezamaphilo yenarha . Ukuphumelelisa lendlela , irherho lezamaphilo litlhoga abasebenzi abanengi ( kufaka hlangana abosobizelomsebenzi namapharamediki ) , imihlobo emitjha yebandla elilawulako , nezakhiwo zomthetho eziqinisiweko ezijamele umphakathi . Enye nenye iKomidi yeWadi kufuze iqunte ngemihlobo yamakomidi amancani kanye nemisebenzi efuna yenziwe kuwadi . Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi abelwe imisebenzi ekhethekileko . ISewula Afrika kufuneka bonyana iphumelelise kuhle amatjhejontangi wemigomo yayo wezomnotho . Ukubhalelwa kuthintana , isibopho esihlukanisiweko kanye namagunya alakanyeneko aliya ukuphunyeleliswa kwemigomo ekhona . Ikulumiswano yesiqhema nesiqhema esitlamako , iKomidi yeWadi nanyana iinqhema ezisebenzako ezikhulumisene ngokutlhanywa kwamaphepha womqondo wephrojekthi mayelana namaphrojekthi adinga isekelo langaphandle . Usidu -isikhulumi esidu sivumelana nomuntu woke , asithathi isiquntu , sikhuluma ngephimbo eliphasi , sicabanga bona asinamandla wokwenza umsebenzi namtjhana asikwazi ukuqalana nomunye umuntu namtjhana enza okulungileko . Indlela yokusebenza kwe-CBP ibonelela abomasipala ngeensetjenziswa zokuqinisa amaphuzu wokuhlanganyela we-IDP yabo . Ngalendlela , i-CBP isiza abomasipala ukuphumelelisa khudlwana iimfuneko zomThetho oHlongozwako nezomThetho wamaHlelo kaMasipala , ka-2000 . Zilinge ngamandla ukufumana amathuba wokuthuthuka , wokufunda , welemuko namathuba . Into etshwenyako kungakanzinzi kwemigomo . Nanyana kunezehlakalo lapho imigomo ekufuze itjhuguluke khona , kodwana umbuso uvamise ukunyaza umphumela othikamezako wamatjhuguluko amakhulu wemigomo mayelana nokuphakelwa kwemisebenzi . Kufanele bonyana kulinganiswe izinto begodu njenganje ukulinganiswa kwezinto akukho . Ikhambo elisebenzisa umtletlana wendawana eyisampula lithuthukisa indlelambono yomphakathi malungana nesakhiwo sakhathesi sendawo yomphakathi . Ihlanganyelo lemisebenzi kamasipala ( i-MSP ) kusivumelwana hlangana kukamasipala nomnikeli womsebenzi . Umnikeli womsebenzi kungaba ngomunye nomunye umphathi womphakathi ( ofana nebhodo yamanzi namkha idistrigi kamasipala ) ikhamphani yangeqadi , ihlangano engaphandle kukarhulumende ( i-NGO ) namkha ihlangano edzimelele emphakathini ( i-CBO ) . UmSebenzi 1 Khetha isiqhema esiphathelene nomphakathi emphakathinakho pheze onelwazi ngawo-isibonelo , abalimi , abahlali beendawo ezingakahleleki , abanikazi bamabhizimisi amancani , njll . Umthetho unikela iindlela ezinengi zokuhlanganyela kwezakhamuzi ekubuseni ngemva kwamakhetho . Amaforamu anjengemikhandlu elawula iinkolo , amakomidi wamawadi , iinhlangano ezitjheje ukuphepha komphakathi namakomidi wemitholapilo anikela izakhamuzi ithuba lokuveza amazizo wazo kanye namathuba wokuthuthukisa iinhlangano eziseduze khulu nazo . Begodu imiphakathi ingahlanganyela ngokutlama imitlamo yaborhulumende bekhaya . Ngaphandle kweendlelezi , kunokungakabambani okukhulako phakathi kwezakhamuzi nombuso . Ukuqubuka kwemiguruguru kutjengisa itjharagano elingakaphathelani kwaphela nokukhamba buthaka kwezenzelo zomphakathi , kodwana litjengisa nokutshwenyeka okukhona malungana nokungalalelwa kwemiphakathi ngokweqiniso . Yehlukanisa abahlanganyeli ngeenqhema ezisithandathu , unikele isiqhema ngasinye isigaba esisodwa se-IDP ukobana bacoce ngaso okufaka hlangana isigaba samalungiselelo . Abahlanganyeni ababelane ukutjheja kwabo neenqhema zoke . Ngaphasi komThetho wezAkhiwo zakaMasipala [ isiGaba 32 ] , umkhandlu unganikela amanye amandla kumakomidi wamawadi . Lokha nakuqakathekileko ukufaka amakomidi wamawadi eenkambisweni zokubonisana ezizakutjhugulula iinqunto , ukunikelwa kwamandla kutjhejwa ngokutlhogonyelwa . Iinqunto zomkhandlu kufanele zenziwe mkhandlu okhethwe ngokwedemokhrasi , owenza izinto tjhatjhalazi nonokuziphendulela . amakomidi wamawadi akasiwo amabhizinisi asemthethweni angenza iimvumelwano nanyana angasiwa ekhotho mayelana nemitjhapho yokubhalelwa kuphatha nanyana ubukhohlakali . Nanyana ngimiphi imiraro ebgangelwa ziinqunto ezmbi ezithathwako zizakuhlala ngokomthetho zimsebenzi womkhandlu . Itjhejuli engeneleleko izokufuneka , ezabe yendlala imininingwana yesehlakalo esinye nesinye , ezabe itjengisa inani lamalanga , ( avezwe enyangeni yetjhejuli epheleleko ) umsebenzi omunye nomunye ekufuze wenzeke malungana nesehlakalweso , izinga lokuqakatheka komsebenzi lowo , nokobana umsebenzi lowo kufuze wenziwe nobani . Usihlalo uzokuvula umhlangano bese amaphuzu we-ajenda ngokulandelana . Ukufakwa kwe-HIV ne-AIDS ku-IDP . Imiphumela yezamaphilo ethatha isikhathi eside ibunjwa maphuzu khulukhulu awela ngaphandle kwerherho lezamaphilo : indlela yokuphila , umudlokhetho kanye namazinga wokondleka , ifundo ukuziphatha ngokomseme , ukuzithabulula , iingozi zendlela kanye nezinga lemiguruguru . IKomitjhini yenza iimphakamiso mayelana nomkhakha ngamunye walemikhakha . Imikhakha ekufanele bonyana itjhejwe ntangi ifaka hlangana ifundiso ngezomseme , ukondleka , ukuzithabulula , nokukhandela ukubhema kanye nokuselwa kumbi kotjwala . Kuneembopho zehlalakuhle ekufanele zithathelwe phezulu ngesinye nesinye isakhamuzi , begodu ekufuze zigcugcuzelwe mindeni neenhlangano . Ukunikela ngemisebenzi kwethembele ekusebenzeni okuphumelelisako nokunekghono kwabasebenzi bakamasipala kanye nakumahlelo . Ukunikelwa okuphasi kwemisebenzi kanengi kungebanga lokuphatha okumbi nanyana lokusebenza kumbi . Ihlelo lokuphatha ngokomsebenzi libeka iminqopho kanye namaqhinga tjhatjhalazi ukwenzelela kobana ababambiseneko kanye nezakhamuzi zemiphakathi zizokwazi ukutjheja ituthuko bese zikwazi ukukhomba imiraro . Nanyana indlelakambiso yokutlama isungulwa beyihlanganiswe ngumasipala , ukuze umtlamo uphumelele , kufuze ube ngewewadi , begodu lijanyelwe yiKomidi yeWadi . Abomasipala banikela amakhansela wawo kanye namakomidi wawo amandla wokukghonakalisa indlelakambiso yokutlama ezakwenza bonyana ' ikomidi enye nenye ikwazi ukwakha igunya lokusebenza ngesikhathi sayo sokuphatha ' . Umzombe we-IDP uthome ku-National Cabinet Lekgotla naku-Provincial Exco Makgotla okumihlangano ebanjwa nakuthwasa umnyaka omunye nomunye . Lemihlangano yakha iHlelo lokuSebenza ( i-PoA ) lomnyaka lowo begodu lihlela iindaba ezinabileko zethemu ephakathi . Izehlakalwezi zilandelwa kukwethulwa kweKulumo yesiTjhaba , yethulwa nguMengameli , ukwethulwa kweenKulumo zeemFunda kanye nekulumo yesabelo seemali . Kuthatha isikhathi esingangani ngaphambi kobana amalunga weKomidi yeWadi anganeliseka ngendima yawo ? Ingabe iSewula Afrika izokuqaleka injani ngomnyaka wee-2030 ? Ekutjhugulukeni kwedemografi yayo , inarha le ifike ezingeni lapho iinlinganiso zokubeletha zehla khona nalapho isitjhaba sinzinza khona . Ukutjhugulukokhu kunemithelela emikhulu esakhiweni sesitjhaba , esilinganisweni sokukhula kwabasebenzi kanye nefunekweni yemisebenzi enjengefundo nezamaphilo . Umkhandlu yePumalanga Kapa ( ECAC ) izokusekela ukuqatjhwa komvumelanisi we-HIV / AIDS . Iinkomba zekhwalithi ziqakatheke khulu . Akukaneli ukuzwa bonyana abomma bahlanganyela emsebenzini ; ikhwalithi lokuhlanganyela kwabo begodu nelemuko nanyana emhlanganweni weleveli yomphakathi , ematlasini wefundo ephasi namkha njengabasebenzisi bezinto zomphakathi , koke lokhu kuqakathekile . Abantu abanengi bacabanga bonyana ukuhlukana kuqaliswe emehlukweni ekhona hlangana nabantu abavela ezendlalelweni ezahlukeneko zamasiko . Abantu babuye bahlobanise ukuhlukana nomehluko okhona ebulilini namkha eminyakeni . Ngaphezu kwalokho , ukuhlukana kuveza okungaphezulu kunomehluko nje hlangana kwabantu abazisekele phezu kwamasiko , ubulili namkha ubudala , abantu bayahluka ngemihlobohlobo yobujamo bezinto okufaka hlangana ubudala , ikolo , amasiko , isendlalelo zefundo , ilemuko , zepilo , indawo ngokwephasi , ingeniso-mali , ubujamo bombelethi , ubujamo be-HIV ikghono lomzimba njalonjalo . Umkhandlu yedorobha umemezele bona ibeke indawo eqadi kwendawo yokudlalela igalfu mayelana nezindlu ezibiza imali ephasi . Izakhamuzi zendawo le azikhathabi ngemitlamo njengombana zithi lokhu kuzakuthinta ubungako bepahlabo . Umphakathi loyo otlanyelwa ukwakhelwa izindlu ufuna bona ukutlanmywa lokhu kuragele phambili njengombana izindlu zitjhoda nje begodu indawo obekwe kiyo iyaphuphuma . Lesisigaba sokwenza sizokuba nokubuyekezwa , ukuhlalisa kuhle imitlamo kanye nokubika njalo . Ukuthoma ukusebenza , akutjho bona zoke izinto ebegade zicatjangwa ekuthomeni komzombe wephrojekthi zizokuhlala zinjalo ukufika ekupheleni kwephrojekthi . Kuqakathekile bona kwenziwe amatjhuguluko afaneleko begodu ababambisani babikelwe njalonjalo . Zoke izakhamuzi kumele zibe namathuba alinganako wokukghona ukufumana imisebenzi abanelungelo lokuyithola . LINGANISEKAKO -izinga lomsebenzi liyalinganiseka yini begodu ingenzeka ngeendleko nemzamo ozwakalako na ? Ukuhlangana - Imiphakathi ihlukene ngeenkareko ezihlukeneko , imibono nokutjheja . Iindlela zokurarulula irarano kufanele zibe khona ukuze imahluko le ibe ngeyakhako begodu inikele ematjhugululweni amahle neragelo phambili . UmThetho oHlongozwako wakaRhulumende wemaKhaya , ka-1998 umtlolo womthethokambiso owahloma isisekelo sehlelo elitjha lokuthuthukisa lakarhulumende wemakhaya . I-IDP ibuye izalise okufunekako ekubekwe kumThethosisekelo begodu ngemumva kwalokho kube mthetholawulo ( ofana nombikomThethokambiso ophathelene noRhulumende weKhaya , we-1998 ) owenzelwe bonyana abomasipala bajamise begodu balawule ukuphatha kwabo , nebhajedi neenkambiso zokutlama ukuze anikele iindingo eziqakathekileko kunezinye zomphakathi begodu nokuhlanganyela nakumaphrogremu wetuthuko weSizwe nawesifunda . Imihlangano ebanzi yomphakathi kanye neenqhema ezincazana ezifaka hlangana iKomidi yeWadi lapho kukhulunywa khona ngebhoduluko letuthuko lomtlamo wokwenza umsebenzi kanye nesirhunyezo samaphrojekthi ( esingatlolwa efliphutjhadini begodu siqaliswe ) . SINGAZUZA IMINQOPHETHU KWAPHELA YOKUPHATHA KUHLE LOKHA UMUNTU NGAMUNYE , IMIPHAKATHI NEENHLANGANO ZEPOLITIKI , KANYE NALABO ABANEENKAREKO EZIHLUKENEKO , ABAKHOLELWA KIZO BEGODU BASEKELA IMIKGHWA YEDOMOKHRASI YEENHLANGANO " IKULUMO KAMENGAMELI UMBEKI AYETHULA KUFORAMU YOMNYAKA WAMAKOMITJHINI WAMAKHETHO WE-SADC , EDAR ES SALAAM , ETANZANIA NGENYAGA KAKHUKHULAMUNGU NGO-1999 . Usihlalo kumele alawule umhlangano kulandelwa i-ajenda etlolwe ngibo boke abahlanganyeli . Ilwazeli lifuneka malungana nokukhomba iindingo zomphakathi . Ilwazeli lifaka hlangana amastathistikhi nemibiko enikela isendlalelo sewadi . Umsebenzi 4 Iyini imiphumela yesigabesi ? I-CBP ibandakanya ukukhomba nokubandula abakghonakalisi abazokusebenza nemiphakathi bayisize begodu bayisekele lokha nayihlanganyela emtlameni womphakathi . Lokhu kuyafuneka ngombana kuzokusiza bonyana ukwazi ukukhomba iindingo zomphakathi . Sirekhoda iinqhema ezahlukeneko zehlalakuhle emphakathini , imihlobo yeendlela zokuziphilisa , ukuthi ngiziphi iinqhema ezilimala lula khulu emphakathini , imisebenzi eqakathekileko nokuthi bobani abanikeli ngemisebenzi . Imiphumela , iiNkomba kanye neZinto zobuFakazi ( imisebenzi , isisetjenziswa neendleko ) inikela umleyo wokulungiselela imibiko yeragelo phambili lephrojekthi ( ukumadanisa lokhu okuhleliweko nalokhu okuphumeleleko ) . I-CBP yindlelakambiso eyenziwe lula ehlelelwe ukuqinisekisa bonyana imibono yomphakathi iyafakwa ekuthuthukisweni komphakathi . Isiqhema esiqakathekileko ubuncani bakhona esinabakghonakalisi ababili iwadi ngalinye esisebenza neKomidi yeWadi yendawo siyindlela yokusebenza engaletha ipumelelo . Isiqhema kufuze sifake hlangana ubuncani bakhona umkghonakalisi oyedwa ovela ewadini namunye ovela kumasipala , begodu nomunye umkghonakalisi wewadi ongezelelako ovela kwelinye iwadi . Eqinisweni abakghonakalisi bewadi kufuze bathathwe eenkorweni ezahlukeneko , ukuqinisekisa bonyana iinkoro ezahlukahlukeneko zakamasipala zikwazi ukuba nelemuko le-CBP , begodu nokuthola umuntu ozokuba mthintanisi we-CBP ekorweni enye nenye yomnyango . Ikulumiswano yeKomidi yeWadi ephathelene nebhoduluko letuthuko lomtlamo wokwenza umsebenzi kanye nomtlamo ogadungileko wokwenza umsebenzi . Indlela yaboMma beTuthuko yokwenza okuthileko inqophe ekuthini abomma bangahlanganiswa njani ngcono ngaphakathi ' kwephaseli elikhona lokwenziwa bobaba ' , begodu neensungulo zetuthuko ezikhambelanako . Indlela le yokwenza iqothele umkhiqizo womsebenzi , wabomma otjhiya ngaphandle umkhiqizo womsebenzi begodu uhlathululwa njengephrojekthi yabomma ekhiqiza ingeniso-mali ngaphandle kokulungisa irherho leenzathu lokungafani kobulili . . UmThetho oHlongozwako omalungana noRhulumende wemaKhaya , ka-1998 umtlolo womthethokambiso owakha isisekelo sehlelo elitjha lokuthuthukisa lakarhulumende wemakhaya . Lelihlelo elitjha lizibophelele ekusebenzisaneni nezakhamuzi , neenqhema kanye nemiphakathi ukubonelela ngepilo yekhwalithi nokuhlangabezana neendingo zemiphakathi eziphathelene nezehlalakuhle , zomnotho kanye nalokho okuphathekako . Lokhu kutjho bonyana abomasipala kufuze bahlele begodu balawule iindlelakambiso zabo zokuphatha , zokwaba iimali kanye nokutlama ukwenzela bonyana bakwazi ukutjheja ntangi iindingo ezisisekelo zomphakathi . Amatjhuguluko weentjhabatjhaba neemphande athinta iSewula Afrika ngeendlela ezahlukahlukeneko . Umbonwethu ngewokobana ngemva kokutjhejisisa woke amaphuzu , amatjhuguluko wephasi loke angaba nemithelela emihle etuthukweni yeSewula Afrika , nanyana kunobudisi obunengana obubonakalako . Ukuzwisisa nokuthatha amagadango afaneleko malungana neentjhijilo ezahlukahlukeneko zephasi loke kumsebenzi wokuthoma wokutlama . Abomasipala abakha urhulumende wekhaya banikelwe amandla athileko kanye nemisebenzi . Imikhakha yaborhulumende belizweloke kanye naborhulumende besifunda nabo banawabo amandla kanye nemisebenzi . Abahlanganyeli kufanele banikele abonobangela bokutjhejula imisebenzi ngaleyondlela benze ngayo ngokutlola etjhejulini , etjhadini lebha namtjhana ngokunikela iimbonelo . Begodu umtlamo womphakathi ungarholela ematjhugulukweni aphathelene neendlela abomasipala baphakela ngazo iinsetjenziswa emphakathini . Isibonelo , umasipala angacabanga ukuhloma ihlanganyelo nesiqhema esithile somphakathi bonyana siphakele isisetjenziswa esithile emphakathini . Ukuzibandakanya komphakathi ekuphakeleni iinsetjenziswa sele kuthomile ukwenziwa eendaweni ezinjengeKwaZulu-Natal nePumalanga Kapa lapho umphakathi uzibandakanya khona ekuboneleleni ngamanzi nehlwengiso kanye nezamavakatjho . Esigabeni sokuthoma seNdlela yokuSiza ukuPhumelelisa i-CBP , isiqhema esitlamako sibuthelela begodu sicozulule ilwazi elikhona elivela emphakathini . Lokho siikwenza ngokubamba iinkulumiswano ezahlukahlukeneko nangokusebenzisa amathulusi ahlukahlukeneko we-CBP . Icozululo elingenelelelo laledatha linikela isiqhema esitlamako isendlalelo esinemininingwana epheleleko kanye nebonelophambili malungana nobujamo bomphakathi , imiraro , amasiko , imikhuba , amahlelo kanye namagugu . Lokhu kwenziwa nesiqhema somphakathi obanzi ovangeneko begodu kumhlobo othize weqhinga . Kuthatha isikhathi esingaba ma-iri amabili begodu idayagramu isetjenziselwa ukuqedelela iphepha lecozululo . Isigaba 152 - iminqopho karhulumende wendawo kukhuthaza ukubandakanyeka kwemiphakathi neenhlangano zomphakathi eendabeni zakamasipala wendawo . Bawa abahlanganyeli benze umsebenzi ongenzasi . Ngokuqinisa ukusebenza kwekoro yezabasebenzi ukwenza ngcono ukufunyanwa kwamakghono , ukumadanisa labo abafuna imisebenzi neenkhala , nokuphungula ukungazwani . Khumbuza abahlanganyeli bonyana lomsebenzi siwenzela ukulemukisa abahlanganyeli ngeentjhijilo zokwakha umtlamo wewadi begodu nokobana asinaso isikhathi sokuhlathulula yoke imininingwana yesigaba ngasinye . Bahlathululele bonyana ngebanga lalokho , sizokukghona ukusebenzisa imizuzu eli-10 ukufikela kweli-10 egadangweneli , kodwana iinqhema kufuze ziphakamise umbono ngaphakathi kwalesisikhathi esijanyisiweko . Nangabe azikghoni ukuqedelela umbonwazo , kufuze zilinge ngamandlazo woke bonyana ziwuqedelele . Ukuphatha kumasipala nokuthuthukisa kusitjhijilo begodu kufaka hlangana izinto ezinengi ezihlukileko . Njengombana ekuthomeni ufaka abantu , iindingo zabo , iimphakamiso , begodu ufuna ukobana kufanele uphathwe ngendlela inengi leenzuzo labantu abanengi liyazuzwa . Yeke , imiphakathi ibunjwe ziinqhema ezihlukeneko ezineenkareko ezihlukeneko begodu ingasi bona zoke iinqhema zinganeliswa ngesikhathi esisodwa . Ukusiza iimphathiswa zakamasipala nabadosiphambili abakhethiweko ekuphenduleni kuhle izakhamuzi eendaweni zazo , ukubandakanyeka komphakathi nokubandakanyeka kuqakathekile . amaKomidi wamaWadi adlala indima eqakathekileko ekwenzeni bona lokhu kwenzeke . Ngiyiphi ipendulo oyizwako lokha nawukhuluma nomuntu okuzwako ? Lo msebenzi wesiqhema wesampula yabahlali abajamele umphakathi ngobubanzi bawo obandakanya ukudwetjwa nanyana ukwakhiwa komebhe . Zinikele ama-iri amabili mayelana nomsebenzi wokumebha . Ezingeni lenarha , amakghono aqakathekileko afaka hlangana iinhlangano zomthetho kanye nezinye iinhlangano , imithangalasisekelo ( ithintaniswanoliqha , amanzi , igezi neenthuthi ) , irherho lefundo nebandulo , ukulawulwa kwebhoduluko ngendlela ebambelelako , amarherho wemibono emitjha namaphethini wokuthuthukiswa kweendawo zokuhlalisa abantu . Amakghono wabantu afaka hlangana ifundo , zamaphilo , ukuvikelwa kwehlalakuhle yomphakathi kanye nokuphepha komphakathi . IKhomitjhini yobuLili ithuthukisa ukuhlonipha ukulingana ngobulili begodu isebenza ukuvikela , ukuthuthukisa nokuthola ukulingana ngobulili . Amalunga weKomidi yewadi kufanele azijayeze nge-ofisi yesifunda yalamakhomitjhini benzelele ukutjela imiphakathi mayelana nama-ofisi la . Begodu kuyirhuluphelo yekoro yezamabhizinisi ukobana kuphungulwe izinga lokungalingani . Ukungalingani kukhuphula iindleko zokusebenza kwebhizinisi , kutjhigamisa isakhiwo semakethe begodu ekugcineni kukhawula amathuba wetuthuko . Begodu kubanga ukungathembi nokutjhuba kwemimoya . Imirholo ephezulu yalabo abaphetheko ayiwakhi umphakathi obandakanya boke abantu lapho omunye nomunye ahlomula emakhakhazeleni wetuthuko khona . Nanyana ukubeka umthetho malungana nemirholo kungakghonakali , kodwana abarholi kufanele baqinisekise bonyana amabhizinisi asebenza ngokuzibophelela . Indlelakambiso ye-CBP iyamukela bonyana amalunga womphakathi anamabonelophambili aqakathekileko nahlukileko kunamanye malungana netuthuko yawo begodu igandelela khulu leziindlelambono . Emsebenzini olandelako kusetjenziswa iinkulumiswano nabantu abayisika abanamakghono wokwenza izinto ezithile ukukhombela imibono yabo malungana neensombululo eziqakathekileko . Ukuziphendulela kuqakathekile embusweni wentando yenengi . Kunobuthakathaka obumbalwa emzombelezweni wokuziphendulela , ovamise ukuba nesiko lokusulelana ngeensolo . Umzombelezo wokuziphendulela kufanele bonyana uqiniswe ukuthoma phezulu ukuya phasi . Kokuthoma , ukuziphendulela kwepalamende kubuthakathaka , ngombana iPalamende iyabhalelwa kudlala indima yayo esisekelo yokulungisa imitjhapho eyenzeke ngokungakatjheji . Imiphumela yefundo angeze yaba ngcono nangabe akukaqiniswa ukuziphendulela erherhweni loke , ukuthoma emiphumeleni yabafundi ukuya ekwethulweni kweencwadi zokufunda . Ukukhuphuka kwesibalo semitjhagalo yezenzelo zomphakathi kukhombisa bonyana umbuso nawo kufanele wenze kube lula ukobana izakhamuzi zikwazi ukuveza ukutshwenyeka kwazo . Lokha nangabe izakhamuzi zingena emakhiweni wombuso , kufanele bonyana zikwazi ukubona imisebenzi ezingayilindela , lapho ekufanele zitjhinge khona nomuntu ekufanele zikhulume naye nangabe azikaneliswa . ImiHlahlandlela ye-Batho Pele izokusiza ekuphenduleni emalungeni womphakathi lokha nakangaveza bona umsebenzi abanikelwa wona ziinkhulu awusisezingeni elinikelwa mHlahlandlela we-Batho Pele . Umasipala kufanele abeke iKomba eQakathekileko yokwEnziwa komsebenzi ukuze akwazi ukulinganisa ukwenza kwayo begodu kufanele abandakanye umphakathi . Lokha nakwenziwa umsebenzi olandelako kubanjwa iinkulumiswano nabanikeli ngemisebenzi ukubona bonyana amandla wabanikeli ngemisebenzi akhonjwe emsebenzini ogadungileko angangani bonyana angakghona ukusiza ekuphumeleliseni , ekuhloleni imiraro abaqalene nayo , kanye nokubandakanya ekambisweni yokutlama . Lokhu kuzokusiza ekwakheni imitlamo yamambala nengaphunyeleliswa . Khumbula ukuhlela leziinkulumiswano ngesikhathi esifaneleko . ISewula Afrika yoke yehlukaniswe ngabomasipala . Kunemikhakha emithathu yabomasipala eyehlukeneko . Nangabe iSewula Afrika ifuna ukurhabisa ituthuko , iqinise intando yenengi begodu yakhe umphakathi ongabandlululaniko , kufanele itjhugulule itjhaphuluko yezepolotiki ibe yihlalakuhle yezomnotho yabantu boke . Abantu abasebenzisa ipompo le abayivali kuhle amanzi ahlala athonta njalo . Lokhu kubangela idaka nabonompopoloza . UNom . Nkosi uzicabangela yena kwaphela kunabanye abantu emphakathini . UNom . Nkosi wabona bonyana umphakathi awumcabangeli ngombana umndenakhe utlhagiswa mamanzi wepompo engavalwako . Ingabe zikhona iindawo zeemila ezazisako ekufuze zitlhogonyelwe nanyana abantu bazithabise ngazo , isib . iindawo zemvelo ezinamatshwayo akhethekileko njengemithi edosa abantu nenemithunzi emihle ? Hlukanisa abahlanganyeli ngeenqhema ezintathu ( 3 ) . Bawa isiqhema ngasinye kobana sicabange besitlole phasi kobana uyini umsebenzi wakamasipala ngamunye . Kumele bacabange ngomasipala wendawo abahlala kiyo lokha nabaphendulako . Emhlangwaneni wokutlama coca nabahlanganyeli ngeminqopho yomtlamo odzimelele emphakathini , ngokusebenzisa amanothi wekhoso ( qala itheyibula elisekhasini lama-38 ) njengeseluleko . IKomidi yeWadi inayo yini indlela yokwakha umthamo wabasebenzi ukuthembisa itsengo lobulili kumthethokambiso , iphrogremu neleveli ngokwehlangano begodu namandla wokutlama nokwenza amaphrogremu asekela ukufana kobulili na ? Nangabe akhona ngimaphi ? Amazinga aphezulu wekohlakalo ahlangahlanganisa ikghono lomphakathi lokusebenza ngefanelo nangepumelelo , kanye nekghono lombuso lokwenza imisebenzi ethuthukisako . Ukuya ngokweembalobalo zekohlakalo yephasi loke zabakwa-Transparency International , phakathi komnyaka wee-2001 newee-2010 , izinga lekohlakalo likhuphukile . Ikohlakalo ivame ukubandakanya abahlanganyeli bombuso nekoro yangeqadi . Umbono ngamazinga aphezulu wokwenziwa kwezenzo ezingasisemthethweni emazingeni aphezulu wombuso kwenza bonyana ukulwisana nekohlakalo kube budisi khudlwana . IKomidi yeWadi kanye nabakghonakalisi be-CBP basebenzisa iSWOT ephathelene neendlela isiqhema esiziphilisa ngazo kanye nelwazi elivela esiGabeni soku-1 malungana nekulumiswano yesiqhema ethatha ama-iri asithandathu . Umsebenzi 5 nikela iimbonele ezinembako ukobana umphakathi wakho ungabandakanyeka njani esigabenesi se-IDP , begodu nezakhiwo ezikhona ukuthuthukisa ukuzibandakanya komphakathi . Lokha nakwakhelwa phezu kwedatha ebuthelelwe esigabeni sokuthoma , isigaba sesibili sona vane sibandakanye ukucozululwa nokuhlanganiswa ngokupheleleko kwaledatha . EsiGabeni sesibili , idatha ebuthelelweko iyacozululwa bese bese bese kucocwa ngayo eenqhemeni ezincani . Lendlelakambiso ihlanganisa amacozululo weendlela zokuziphilisa zeenqhema ezahlukeneko zehlalakuhle , amathulusi we-CBP ( imebhe , i-Venn , umtletlana wendawana eyisampula , ukwenzeka kwezinto ngeenkhathi ezithize zomnyaka , iinqhelo eziragela phambili kanye nelandelaniso lezehlakalo ) , kanye nalokho okufunyenwe nakukhulunyisanwa nabanikeli ngemisebenzi nebantwini abayisika begodu abanamakghono wokwenza okuthize . Ekupheleni kwesigaba , umphakathi ubuyekeza , uhlolisise begodu wamukele ngokusemthethweni ilwazi elihlanganisiweko . Ngemva kwalokho lokhu kwethulwa ewadini bese lona kufuneka bonyana linikele imiphumela emihlanu eqakathekileko itjhejontangi ukwenzela bonyana likwazi ukutlama . Isigaba 39 somThetho wamaRherho kaMasipala , we-2000 sinikele usodorobha omkhulu , ikomidi ephetheko namtjhana ikomidi ekhethekileko yamakhansela ilawulo lokuthuthukiswa kwe-PMS bese liyisa emkhandlwini . I-PMS kufanele itjho ngokucacileko imisebenzi neembopho zabadlaliindima abanye nabanye . Ukuhlungwa kobujamo bephrojekthi kuyakufaka phakathi ukubuyekezwa kobujamo babomma ngokwezomthetho , okuphathelene nomphakathi nakwezomnotho na ? Okhunye ( nanyana iindaba ) ezivumbuka kumaminidi agadungileko - iphuzweli lifaka hlangana iindaba okwakhulunywa ngazo emhlanganweni owagadungako amalunga wekomidi abika ngazo . Kanengi kuyabonakala lokho okuwela ngaphasi kweendaba iindaba ezivumbuka emaminidini ngokuqala lokho ebekumele kwenziwe babantu . Imisebenzi enikelweko iyalinganiseka yini ngamazinga na ? Ikoro yezabasebenzi esebenzisa kuhle amathuba wezomnotho . Lokhu kutlhoga ukufunda ipilwakho yoke nokuthuthuka ngokwebizelo ; ukunzinzisa ibhoduluko labasebenzi , ukuqinisa iinhlangano zokurarulula imibango ; ukubuyekeza imithetjhwana namazinga wamabhizinisi amancani naphakathi ; ukutjheja itjhebiswano labasebenzi bombuso ; ukuqinisa ukusetjenziswa kwamazinga amukelekako ebasebenzini , ama-ejensi wedoselomsebenzi kanye nabaqatjheli ; ukuqinisa imigomo esebenza ngamandla yekoro yabasebenzi nemadaniselomsebenzi ; nokukghonakalisa ifudukelo lamakghono . Umtlamo wenziwe kodwana-ke udinga bonyana utjhugululwe ube mtlamo wokwenza umsebenzi ukwenzela bonyana ukwazi ukuphunyeleliswa . Nasi indlela yokuwenza . Ukwenziwa kweemphakamiso ngokuzinikela ikhansela lewadi mayelana nenye nenye nenye indaba ethinta iwadi nanyana ngokuzinikela ikhansela lewadi bonyana lizidlulisele kumasipala . Emzombeni ogadungileko wama-IDP , ababonisani badlale indima ekulu - eenkhathini ezinengi kutholakele imiphumela enemiraro . Ababonisani be-IDP kanye nabatlami bakamasipala bagcina sele bazenza abosonjiniyera nanyana abatlami bedorobha , begodu ngebanga lalokho babandulelwa ukuqalana nezinto ezibonakalako , neendaba eziphathelene nomthangalasisekelo nanyana eziphathelene nesikhala , kunokobana baqalane namatjhuguluko wendlelakambiso nanyana nokuthintana nomphakathi . Lomraro uvunywe ngokubanzi njengoliqiniso yi-dplg begodu ibandulo eliphathelene nama-IDP elabanjwa ngo-2001 lalinga ukuqinisekisa bonyana abantu bezwisisa ngokunabileko ituthuko kunokutlama okubonakalako . Umkhakha B abomasipala , nanyana abomasipala bekhaya / bendawo . Laba bomasipala ababelana ngesigungu kanye negunya lokubeka imithetho nomkhakha C nanyana abomasipala besiyingi . Boke abomasipala bekhaya / bendawo bawela ngaphasi komkhawulo wesiyingi sabomasipala . UmThethosisekelo weSewula Afrika unevikelamalungelo eqinisekisa ukuvikeleka kwamalungelo . Esinye nesinye isakhamuzi sinesiqiniseko sokuvikelwa kwamalungelo wobuntu . Amalungelo la afaka hlangana ilungelo lebhoduluko ' elingasiyingozi emaphilwenazo nanyana eempilweni zazo ' ' nokuvikela ukuthuthukiswa kuhle kwezinto eziphathelene nebhoduluko nokusetjenziswa kwemithombo yemvelo lokha nakuthuthukiswa umnotho ofaneleko nokuthuthukisa zehlalakuhle . ' Umthetjhwana 24 weVikelomalungelo , amaKomidi wamaWadi adlala indima eqakathekileko njengabaphenyi bendlela mayelana nalokho okufunwa mphakathi woke okufanele kwethulwe ku-IDP nokwenza isiqiniseko sokobana imitlamo yezehlalakuhle neyomnotho mayelana newadi zenziwa ngendlela ehle engathandwa mphakathi wokana . AmaKomidi weWadi ahlobana nomphakathi ngeendlela ezintathu , kokuthoma njengabajameli bomphakathi , kwesibili ukwakha ubudlelwana nomphakathi bese kwesithathu ukuziphendulela ngokupheleleko . PHENDULAKO - izinga liyaziphendula yini iindingo zezakhamuzi ezizuzako emsebenzini lo na ? Ukuthuthukisa ukubandakanyeka komphakathi ngokuthuthukisa imisebenzi yomphakathi nemizamo ukuze ukghone ukuziphendulela kilokho okudingwa mphakathi . Lokhu kungafaka hlangana ukulungisa amaphepha namaphetjhana okumele azise umphakathi ngezehlakalo . Umrhatjho womphakathi uyindlela enamandla khulu yokufaka hlangana umphakathi ezehlakalweni . Isibonelo , amalunga weKomidi yeWadi angahlungwa ngezehlakalo ezenzeka emphakathini , nanyana umrhatjho womphakathi ungasetjenziselwa ukwazisa abantu ngezehlakalo nanyana ukubawa umbono ngephrojekthi etlanyiweko . Sebenzisa irhelo lokuhlola lepahla malungana nekulumiswano ehlelwe ngokungakapheleli ephathelene neendlela zokuziphilisa zesiqhema . Rekhoda iimpendulo . Isibonelo serhelo lokuhlola lepahla singakusiza kilomsebenzi ukuqinisekisa bonyana ufumana loke ilwazi olidingako . Lokhu kwenziwa njengekulumiswano yesiqhema begodu kuthatha pheze ama-iri amabili ukuya kamathathu . Abahlanganyeli bathathwa esiqhemeni esibanzi samalunga womphakathi , afaka hlangana abajameli bazo zoke iinqhema zehlalakuhle . Sebenzisa i-PowerPoint nangabe unedathaphrojektha , nanyana hlathulula ngokuzeleko isigaba esinye nesinye esisefliphutjhadini bese ukhombela abahlanganyeli bonyana baqale idayagramu esemanothini wabo wekhoso asekhasini lama-35 . Ikombamphandemitato - lungisa ikombamphandemitato yeenhlangano zomphakathi , okufaka hlangana imininingwana yokuthintana kanye nomuntu omayelana nomsebenzi othile ukuze wenze isiqiniseko bona boke ababambisani bahlale baphelele ngakho koke ngomkhandlu . Amandla wepolotiki aqakathekile ekuqedeni ikhwekhweli . Amandla wepolotiki alinganiswa ngokuhlola inani lemali esetjenziselwa ukulwisana nekohlakalo , ibuthelelo leenkhali elisemthethweni lamaziko alwisana nekohlakalo , ukuzijamela kwamabandla alwisana nekohlakalo ekubeni angacajelwa yipolotiki nangokungatjhuguluki kwendlela ekusetjenziswa ngayo umthetho . Ukuba nemithetho ethambileko mayelana nemilandu emincani , nanyana ube nemithetho eqine ngokungakajayeleki ekohlakalweni ebandakanya iimbangi zepolotiki , kutjho ukungakhambisi umthetho ngendlela efanako . Yenza ibhoduluko elisekelako nelisiza abantu bona bazigedle bese banqopha eendabeni . UmThethosisekelo , we-1996 ujamisa urhulumende wekhaya njengephiko elahlukanisiweko kurhulumende omayelana nokwethulwa komsebenzi . Umphakathethu ufaka hlangana abantu abahlukaneko ahlukeneko wamagugu ahlukeneko , iindlela zokuphila , ikolo , amalimi , ubujamo obuphathelene nobulili , iintayela zokuvunula neendlela zokuvezwa komzimba womuntu . Nangabe senza imahluko le ngendlela eyakhako singatjho bonyana ' yenza iphasi libe ngelikarisa kwamanikelela begodu iyasinjingisa ; . Ukuphila ngokuhlukana kusitjhijilo nesidingo samaKomidi wamaWadi , sokwazi ukuphendula iintjhijilwezi ngokwakhako . Iinqhema hlangana nomphakathi zineendingo ezihlukeneko ezilindelweko . Njengombana anesibopho wamaWadi anesibopho sokuqinisekisa bonyana iindingo zomphakathi zifakwe hlangana emtlameni nemaphrogremini kamasipala , badinga ukulimuka ngeenqhema ezihlukileko ezisemphakathinabo begodu nokuqinisekisa bonyana iinqhema zizizwa zifakiwe hlangana eendleleni zekambiso yokuthathwa kweenqunto . Zama ukukhomba okungasenani igadango linye elinobudlelwano nombuzo ngamunye kwengehla . Gcugcuzela abanye abantu bakhulume ngokukwata kwabo beze kufike lapha kungasabalawuli -kunalokho bona balawula khona .
