Ithulusi lelogfremu limtlolo otjengisa iingcenye eziqakathekileko zomtlamo wephrojekthi ngokulandelana . Imininingwana ezeleko yesigaba , iyazaliswa emsebenzini kanye nakumatjhejuli weesetjenziswa ( ahlathululwa esigabeni esilandelako ) akhamba woke nelogfremu . Indlela esikhulumisana ngayo ingaliya nanyana ikhuphule ubujamo . Cabangani ngabantu enibaziko abaziinkhulumi eziphuma phambili bewutjengise kobana ngikuphi okubenze kobana babe ziinkhulumi eziphuma phambili . Iindlela zekambiso yokuvala - kuqinisekisa bonyana koke kwephrojekthi okulindelweko kuyafezakaliswa , ukubuyelwa ngokutloliweko ukutlikitla okuvela kubabambisani abafaneleko , abenza ukuqedwa kwephrojekthi kube ngokomthetho ngokukhiqizwa kwelwazi begodu nokurhatjhwa kwalo ukuqedwa nokulungiswa kwamakontraga okufaka phakathi ukulungiswa kwezinto ezisaleleko . Umtlamo womphakathi awuzenzakaleli . Ukutlama akusiyo into eyenziwa ngusiyazi . Kuyinto eyame ekuhlanganyeleni naphezu kweenkambisolawulo zedemokhrasi yepolitiki . Ukuhlanganyela kufuna bonyana boke ababambisani bamenywe bazokuhlanganyela , lokho kufaka hlangana urhulumende , umphakathi , amabhizinisi , ikoro yezabasebenzi kanye nezinye iinkoro zomphakathi . Gcugcuzela ukukhuluma ngokutjhaphuluka -ungathathi ihlangothi lokha abantu nabaveza amazizwabo . Ingahluka kuneyakho . Kuqakathekile ukuthatha isiqunto ngaphambili bonyana lokho okufunwa ziinqhema ebegabe zidinywe amathuba ngaphambilini bonyana kutjhejwe ntangi , kuzakutjhejwa ntangi nanyana njani . Isibonelo , kungenzeka bonyana kuzwenwe ngokuthi isiqhema esisodwa kwezihlanu kufuze sivele kileziinqhema . Khuyini abakwenzako okwenza bona kube lula bona ukhulume ? Bamba imihlangano nemiphakathi begodu nababambisani abathintekileko . Ukubambisana hlangana nemikhakha , nanyana yehlukene , yeyame phezu komunye beyihlobene . Abakghonakalisi : I-CBP ifuna isiqhema sabakghonakalisi esizinikelako nesibandulwe ngefanelo esizakuzwisisa ngokuzeleko indlelakambiso begodu siyenze ngekghono nangepumelelo . Bawa iinqhema ezahlukahlukeneko zikhombe isikhulumi bese bayazethula batjho bona bajamele ubani . Umjameli weKomidi yeWadi kanye nelunga lomkhandlu bayazethula kanye nabalingani babo . Vumelanani ngemithetjhwana neenhlangano zoke . Isibonelo : vumela isiqhema esinye nesinye sihlathulule isibawo saso ; khuluma ngokuqalisa kumlamuli , ungabizi umuntu ngegama njll . Itjhebiswano nehlangano yamateksi ekileyo ndawo bese lisiza ukwazisa abantu ngomhlangano okungezinye zeendlela itjhebiswano elingasiza ukukhuthaza ilizwi lomphakathi . Ibandlululo yindlela yokuziphatha eyakhiwe ngepatho yomuntu namkha isiqhema engakafaneli edzimelele phezu kwehlangothi lobunjalo besiqhema sabo begodu kufaka phakathi ukwalela umuntu ilungelo lakhe lokuragela phambili . Amakomidi wasafuthi akhambisana neminyango kamasipala begodu angajanyiswa mkhandlu nangabe kunesidingo . Ukwakha ikghono lombuso lokudlala indima ethuthukisako neletha amatjhuguluko . Esikhathini esinengi amaKomidi wamaWadi akhethwa emihlanganweni yemiphakathi ukobana asebenze ithemu yinye nanyana amathemu amabili . Nangabe ilunga liyabhalelwa kukhambela imihlangano , kufanele ilungelo lijanyiselelwe ngelinye . Amalunga wamaKomidi wamaWadi akhethwa ngendlela ehlukileko emaplasini nemadorobheni . Umhlangano wabizwa , ikhansela lewadi lahlathulula bona lesi siphakamiso sanje ekusakhulunyisanwa ngaso nokobana umhlangano wezakhamuzi uzokubizwa . Ubuye watjho abonobangela besiphakamiso sokususwa , okufaka hlangana iphuzu lokobana umhlaba lapho kuhlala khona abahlali awukalungeli ukufakwa kwesoritjhi , ngalokho indawo le angeze yakwazi ukuthuthukiswa njengendawo yanaphakade . Okwanje abahlali abanengi bagulela futhi , bathola umgomani namakhaza . Abahlali abaphethwe sifuba abakghoni ukuba ngcono nabahlali abaphila ne-HIV / AIDS abakwazi ukuthatha iinhlahla zabo ngendlela efaneleko ngaphandle kweensetjenziswa ezaneleko . Ukutjhuguluka kobujamo betlayimethi sekunomthelela omumbi eSewula Afrika , ngenca yokutjhugutjhuguluka okukhona kwamazinga wokutjhisa nokuna kwezulu kanye nokuphakama kwamazinga welwandle . Umbuso uzokuba nesibopho sesabelo esikhulu seemphakamiso ezisemtlameni . Njengendlela yokuphumelelisa iimphakamiswezi , ufanele bonyana uqinise umzombe wawo wokuziphendulela , wenze ngcono amakghonwawo , uzimisele ukuthatha iinqunto ezibudisi begodu usebenzisane nabanye emphakathini ukurarulula iintjhijilo . Lokhu kutjho ukukhulumisana ngokuthembeka nangokweqiniso nomphakathi , begodu wenze bonyana izakhamuzi zibe nokuziphendulela mayelana nezenzo zazo . Abarholi , khulukhulu embusweni , nabo kufanele baqalane nokuthatha iinqunto ezibudisi kanye nokulahlekelwa ngokhunye ukuze bazuze okhunye . Uburholi obuqinileko buphathelene nokuthatha iinqunto ezinjalo nokwenza bonyana umphakathi ulandele indlela yamambala . Imali ekghona ukwenza umsebenzi kamasipala ngepumelelo . Abahlanganyeli abaqale amanothi wekhoso andlala imithombo eyahlukahlukeneko yenturhu . Abomasipala bangangena emithonjeni esemiphakathini . Imiphakathi inamakghono ahlukeneko amanengi nelemuko elingenza bona umasipala azuze . Ingonga imali kamasipala njengombana imithombo le seyikhona iyatholakala . Ukuthuthukisa iindawo zokuhlala ezingakahleleki nezingasisemthethweni enarheni ekwakhiwe kiyo ngendlela efaneleko . Ukubuyekezwa kwaqobe mnyaka - umkhandlu kumele ubikele iKomidi yeWadi ngebhajede yawo kanye nangeminqopho yokwenziwa komsebenzi . Imvelo le kokuphathwa kokuphathwa kwephrojekthi idosele ekukhonjweni kweendlela zekambiso ezihlathululiweko ezidabuka zoke iingaba zephrojekthi . Isekelo elibanzi lomphakathi woke liyadingeka ekuphumeleliseni umtlamo lo ngepumelelo . Embusweni wentando yenengi onamandla netjisakalo isekelweli liqakathekile . Imikhulumiswano engeneleleko iqakathekile ekwakheni iimvumelwano zenengi kanye nobunikazi obubanzi bomtlamo lo . Imikhulumiswano eyakhako isiza ekwakheni isitjhaba ngokwenza bonyana amaSewula Afrika akghone ukuzwisisa ngconywana nokwamukela ubunikazi bamatjhejontangi wabo . Iingcenye ezihlukileko zomtlamo zifuna ukwamukelwa nokuzinikela kweenkoro ezahlukeneko . Nangabe kuba khona ukwahluka ngemibono , kuqakathekile bonyana kukhulunyiswane ngeenzathu zokwahluka begodu zihlathululwe ngokuzwakalako , ukwenzela bonyana kube nokuvumelana mayelana nendlela etjhinga phambili . IKomitjhini yokuTlama yeliZwe Loke ingasebenzisa amandlayo wokubiza umhlangano wabahlanganyeli ukukghonakalisa ikulumopendulwano nokuletha iinsombululo . I-CBP ithuthukisa amaphuzu womthethokambiso karhulumende njenge-Letsema neVuk'uzenzele , begodu igcugcuzela imiphakathi nezakhamuzi bonyana zilawule ibhoduluko lazo ngokusebenza ngokuzinikela . Ukubuyekeza ukwenziwa komsebenzi qobe mnyaka - Umkhandlu kufanele ubike kumaKomidi wamaWadi nemiphakathini mayelana namabhajedawo neminqopho yokwenziwa komsebenzi . IKomidi yeWadi ingazisa imeyara nangabe ayiyitholi imibiko okumele inande iyithola . Abonobangela ngaphandle kwephrojekthi bangatjhuguluka kwesinye nesinye isikhathi , ngalokho kuqakathekile bona ukuhlolwa kwengozi kwenziwe kiwo woke umzombe wephrojekthi . IRHERHO LOKUPHATHWA KOKWENZIWA KOMSEBENZI KAMASIPALA LIMUMETHE IPHAHLA ELIHLATHULULA BELIJAMELE BONYANA UMZOMBE NEKAMBISO KAMASIPALA NENDLELA YEKAMBISO YOMTLAMO WOKWENZIWA KOMSEBENZI , UKUTJHEJA , UKULINGANISA , UKUBUYEKEZA , UKUBIKA BEGODU NOKWENZA NGCONO KUZAKULAWULWA , KUHLELWE BEGODU KUPHATHWE , OKUFAKA HLANGANA UKUKHETHA IINDIMA EZAHLUKENEKO ZABADLALIINDIMA . Ezingeni lemakhaya , i-Local Government Makgotla mhlangano obanjwa ngoNtaka begodu ukhanjelwa yi-Municipal Exco kanye nabaphathi ukwenza amalungiselelo wehlelo lomnyaka weemali . Begodu urhulumende wemakhaya uthoma ngokwakha i-IDP yeminyaka emithathu . Urhulumende wekhaya njengomsunguli : Urhulumende wekhaya angasebenza neminye imikhakha yakarhulumende ukuveza ikghono lendawo emikhawulweni yakamasipala . Lokhu kuzokusiza bekwazise imitlamo kanye namaqhinga angakhuphula ukukhula komnotho wendawo . Nayifuna ukuletha ituthuko erhabekileko , iSewula Afrika kufanele ifumane isekelo elikhulu kizo zoke izakhamuzi , eburholini bazo zoke iinkoro ezizimisele ukutjheja zoke iinkareko zenarha ntangi kunokobana ziqalane neminqopho emincazana begodu yesikhatjhana , kanye nokusebenza kombuso ngendlela ethuthuke khulu . Kokhunye , kungaba nesidingo sokutjhugululwa komgomo , kodwana emikhakheni eminengi lokho kumayelana nokufumana amalungelo asisekelo , ukuphumelelisa amahlelo wombuso , ukwenza bonyana abantu babe nokuziphendulela malungana nezenzo zabo begodu nokufumana iinsombululo ezinamaqhinga amatjha zeentjhijilo ezihlangahlangeneko . Iinqhema zabelwa imisebenzi eyenziwako . Iinqhema zinikelwa imizuzu engaba li-10 ukuya kweli-15 ukobana zicoce ngalokho okwenziwako bese zabelana ngeempendulo zazo ekutlameni . AmaKomidi wamaWadi nabantu ababajameleko banelungelo lokulindela ukwethulwa komsebenzi . Nanyana kunjalo kumele kukhumbuleke nokho ukobana umphakathi nawo uneembopho zokuqinisekisa ikhwalithi nobunengi bemisebenzi ehlathululwa emazingeni womsebenzi . Isibonelo , kumele banikele ilwazi ngokunembako , bahlathulule ubujamo babo ngokwethembeka begodu bathembise nokuziphatha okuhle nokunehlonipho ebanikelini bomsebenzi njll . Katelela umbiko obuyako nohlelekileko ovela emkhandlwini oya eKomidini yeWadi . Hlathulula ngeendlela ezinengi ezingasetjenziswa ukuqinisekisa ukufakwa koke , kutlole etjhadini . Abahlanganyeli banikelwa ithuba lokungezelela ngananyana ngiliphi ilwazi elitjhiywe lokha nakwenziwa ukuvumelanisa kokuthoma . Iinhlangano ezikhonjwe esiGabeni 1 zinqotjhaniswa nomqopho onikelwa itjhejontangi . Begodu umhlangano unethuba lokungezelela ngelwazi eliphathelene neenkulumiswano kanye nemisebenzi yomnikeli ngemisebenzi bese uhlola begodu uhlolisise imiphumela ngokuyihlobanisa nesirhunyezo se-IDP , nephepha lehlalakuhle yeenqhema zehlalakuhle kanye nephepha ledatha yebhoduluko nendawo yokubekeka kokuthize . Landelani amaminidi - qalani kobana alirikhotho elinembako lalokho okwatjhiwo emhlanganweni owagadungako . Woke amalunga kumele avumelane kobana amaminidi ayanemba njengobana amaminidi alirikhotho elisemthethweni lomhlangano . Amakomidi wamawadi akasizo izakhiwo zakarhulumende ezihlelekileko ezinamandla . Amakomidi wokuyelelisa abunjwe ngabantu abazi indawo kuhle begodu abangasiza ikhansela ukubonisana ngefanelo , bayabika begodu batjele abantu bese bathatha iinqunto ezingcono kukhansela , ingcenyabo kanye nomphakathi . Umphakathi kumele uthole ithuba lokuphefumula ngomtlamo ngaphambi kobana i-IDP ithole imvumo . AmaKomidi weWadi afaka hlangana amakhansela wewadi njengosihlalo kanye namalunga womphakathi angafika etjhumini ( 10 ) . Ikhansela lewadi liba ngusihlalo wekomidi . Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi angabhadelwa ukunikela ngemisebenzi kuKomidi yeWadi . Isehlakalo esinye nesinye seNdlela yokuSiza ukuPhumelelisa kufuneka bonyana sitlanywe ngokucophelela . Abakghonakalisi be-CBP kufuze bakwazi abafuna ukukwenza ngombana lokhu kwenza bonyana umphakathi ube nethemba kilokho okwenziwako . Ilwazi elingezelelako lifaka hlangana ilwazi elirekhodwe ngaphambi kwesigaba sokutlama . Ilwazeli lifaka hlangana amastathistikhi , imibiko , kanye nemizuzu yemihlangano nama-athikhili , iincwadi zamarekhodi waborhulumende bemakhaya kanye nedemografiki . Imihlangano yomphakathi inikela amathuba mayelana nombiko obuyako kanye nokwaba kwelwazi njengobana ivame ukuba nabantu abanengi , kunethuba elincani lokubamba ngokungenelelekileko ekulumiswaneni neendabeni . Kuqakathekile ukubika ngemisebenzi yomkhandlu namtjhana ngeendaba ezivezwe emhlanganweni ogadungileko . Sebenzisa imibuzo ukuthola ilwazi nanyana hlathulula lokho okutjhiwo ngomunye . AmaKomidi weWadi angeze akwazi ukulawula iphrojekthi enomsebenzi omkhulu emawadinawo , lokhu kuwela ngaphasi komsebenzi kamasipala . Ukuhlanganyela kilabo abathola lemisebenzi kuqakathekile ukuqinisekisa ipumelelo yokwethulwa komsebenzi begodu nokuthuthukisa idemokhrasi . Eendaweni ezineendawo ezimaqalanga ngokwejiyografi nanyana ezinabantu abanengi , amakomidi amancani ayahlonywa ngokwamaphothfoliyo . Ngaleyondlela , amaKomidi weWadi angaba nokubonisana okungeneleleko nemiphakathi ngeendaba eziwuthintako . Lokhu kungaqinisa umphakathi kanye nokuzibandakanya kwamaKomidi weWadi eenkambisweni zokuthatha iinqunto . Ngaphandle kwengqugquthela yeenhlangano / amaforamu wokuthintana nomphakathi njengamaKomidi weWadi namaForamu wabaJameli be-IDP , abomasipala bangakhetha ukunabisa ububanzi bokubonisana nokuthintana nemiphakathi hlangana nendawabo yomkhawulo . Bangajamisa ihlanganyelo yababambisani lapho baletha ndawonye ababambisani ababuya eenqhemeni ezinerhuluphelo ezihlukahlukeneko ezikhambisana nerherho lehlanganyelo njengoba kunjalo kumaphothifoliyo ahlukahlukeneko . Amakomidi wephothifoliyo - yiba nerhelo elizeleko lamakomidi wephothifoliyo wekhansela kanye nemininingwana yokuthintana yamalunga wekomidi yephothifoliyo ukuze ukwazi ukubanikela ilwazi laqobe nombono eendabeni ezimanqophana nekomitabo . Bawa amakhophi kumasipala wakho nangabe uyawadinga . Ukuvala - lobu bujamo obulikhuni bekambiso yokulamula begodu umlamuli kufanele enze isiqiniseko sokobana isivumelwano sirekhodwe ngendlela eyanelisa iinqhema begodu kufanele sitlikitlwe ngizo zoke iinqhema . UmbikomThethokambiso uphakamisa godu nokobana aboMasipala kufanele bathuthukise iindlela zokuqinisekisa ukubandakamyeka kwezakhamuzi ekuthomeni umgomo nekuwubumbeni , kanye ne-M&E ekuthatheni iinqunto nekwenzeni . Abeluleki kwezobuthekhiniki bangakghona ukudlala indima eqakathekileko begodu bayayidlala ngombana babonelela ngamakghono nangelemuko umphakathi onganalo , ngebanga lalokho kuqakathekile ukuletha abeluleki / abanikeli ngemisebenzi abavela emazingeni aphezudlwana karhulumende wemakhaya , ama-NGO nanyana ikoro yamabubulo wangeqadi . Ukuhlanganyela kwabeluleki kwezobuthekhiniki kufuze kusize indlelakambiso ngokunikela imifakela efaneleko malungana nendlelakambiso , ngaphandle kokulawula bonyana imiphumela kufuze ibe njani . Isibonelo , ukubandakanyeka kwabeluleki kwezobuthekhiniki kulisizo lokha nangabe imiphakathi ikhetha amaqhinga namaphrojekthi ukuphumelelisa iminqopho yayo , ngalokhu kutjhiwo ilanga lesine lokutlama . Ukuhlanganiswa ngokuzeleko komzamo nokuthintanisa okusezingeni eliphezulu kuyatlhogeka ukwenzela bonyana Imisebenzi yerhemiso-kambiso lobulili liyaqinisekiswa njengendlela epheleleko enqophe ekutjhugululweni kwezakhiwo ukwakha nokuthuwelelisa ukufana kobulili nokunqopha ekungeneni phakathi phakathi phakathi phakathi . Ezinye izinto ezifana nobuhlanga / nobuzwe , itlasi / ifuzo nobudala kunalo itjhayisano ngendlela abomma baphenduleka ngayo . Ukungafani kobulili , ngekhe kulungiswe ngendlela eyaneleko ngaphandle kokuthi ukungafanokhu okuvela ezintweni ezinye ezitjhugutjhugulukako nakho kulungiswe . Ukwakha iminqopho kuligadango elilandelako ngombana lihlathulula ngokuzeleko bonyana umphakathi uzowuphumelelisa bunjani umbono wawo . Iminqopho kufuze icace begodu inqophe , ibe ngeyamambala begodu ibe ibe ukwenzela bonyana abantu bakwazi ukuhlomula kiyo . Isikhathi samambala esijanyisiweko sokubeka iminqopho minyaka emithathu . AmaKomidi wamaWadi adinga ukwenza isiqiniseko sokobana zoke iinqhema neengcenye zomphakathi zifakwa phakathi ekuqinisekiseni nekuqiniseni ukuhlanganyela komphakathi . Inturhu ingathathwa ngendlela engasingiyo begodu ingenza amajamo anobungozi ebantwini . Isibonelo , ubujamo benturhu bungaba nomphumela wepi , abantu balimale begodu yenze ukugandeleleka nokwesaba . Ukuhlanganyela komphakathi kuqakatheke ekuhlangabezeni iimfuneko zomthetho ezitjhiwo emThethweni wamaRherho kaMasipala , we-2000 kanye nomThetho wezAkhiwo zakaMasipala , we-1998 . amaKomidi weWadi enza njengendlela yokuthintana hlangana kwababambisani ofanele ukwenzeka ; ngalokho kufanele bazijayeze ngokukhulumisana kwekambiso ephumelelisako . I-PMS kamasipala kumele ifake hlangana izinto ezikhonjwe mkhandlu njengombana zihlobana manqopha neendawo eziqakathekileko zokwenza umsebenzi wakamasipalabo . Ama-IDP kamasipala akhomba amaphrojekthi ngamalanga wokumukela umsebenzi kanye neenkomba zeragelo phambili . Amalunga womkhandlu anendima eqakathekileko yokutjheja ukwenza kwakamasipala ngokuya ngalokhu okqakathekileko okufanele bakwethule . AmaKomidi weWadi kufanele enze isiqiniseko sokobana bazijayeza ngama-KPI nabomqothelwa bokwenza abaku-IDP yabomasipalabo ukuze bakwazi ukuhlola iragelo phambili . Isibonelo esingenzasi sitjengisa bona i-KPI ihlangabezana bunjani neemfuneko zemiThetjhwana . Iinkambiswezi zibandakanya ukutjheja nokulinganisa iragelo phambili nokuqinisekisa bona kuhlangatjezanwa neminqopho yephrojekthi , kukhonjwe nokuhlukileko emtlameni kwenzelelwe bona kulungiswe . Begodu ibandakanya isenzo sokuvikela ngaphambili . Ibandakanya nokumadanisa ukwenza kwamambala nokwenza okutlanyiweko . Ngubani obhadalela imithangalasisekelo yezomnotho ? Eminye imihlobo yemithangalasisekelo inikela iinzuzo ezinabileko zomnotho nehlalakuhle . Kodwana ukuletha isizo lamsinya kutjho bonyana iimbadalo kufanele bonyana zikhuphuke esikhathini esifitjhani ukuya esikhathini esiphakathi ukuze imisebenzi ikwazi ukwenzeka ngepumelelo ngokweemali . Iphuzu lokobana isitetjhi esisodwa begodu esitjha segezi ( esikhiqiza igezi ezi-4 800MW ) pheze sibiza kabili inani elipheleleko lokwehla kwamatjhere agunyaziweko weentetjhi zamandla wegezi ezikhona ( ezikhiqiza igezi ezi-40 000MW ) litjengisa isitjhijilo . Ngaphezu kwalokho , amazinga aphezulu wokungasebenzi nokungalingani enza bonyana inengi labantu libhalelwe kuthenga eminye yemisebenzi le ngaphandle kwalokha nangabe abantwabo basizwa ngeemali zokwehlisa iindleko . Amaphuzu aqinileko wehlalakuhle nawo adlala indima . Imibono yokobana isakhiwo sezomnotho asikalungi , ukungalingani ngokwepolotiki kanye nemihlobo emitjha yokuthuthukisa ehlomulise abantu abatjhidelene ngokwepolotiki irhagalisa isiko lokuthuwelela kwekohlakalo , embusweni nekorweni yezamabhizinisi . Lamaphuzu asisekelo wezehlalakuhle kufanele bonyana alungiswe njengengcenye yepi yokulwisana nekohlakalo . Nikela iinqhema isikhathi esingaba mizuzu eli-15 ukudlulisa ukufunda ngesehlakalo . Abahlengi esele bathathe umhlalaphasi kanye nabalawuli bayafuneka ukuzokusiza kilephrojekthi bese balawula ukusatjalaliswa kwamaphasela wokudla emindenini efaneleko . Umtlikitlo kufanele utholwe nakwamukelwa amaphasela wokudla namaphepha ekutlolelwa kiwo amavakatjho enziwe batlhogomeli . Igadango 1 - Vumelana ngehlelo lesikhathi , umtlamo womzombe , ukuvalwa kweenkathi zokubika . Ababambisani bafaka hlangana amakhansela wewadi , iinkhulu zakamasipala , iinsebenzi ezithuthukisa umphakathi , amalunga womphakathi neenqhema ezinekareko . Nikela esinye nesinye isiqhema munye wemisebenzi elandelako . Indlela enzinze ekuhlanganiseni inikela amaziko ahlukahlukeneko namtjhana iinqhema ithuba lokuhlangana ndawonye bona zikwazi ukusebenzela emnqopheni ofanako . Amaziko ahlukahlukeneko kanye neenqhema zihlangana ndawonye ukwenzela bona zikwazi ukusebenzisana ephrojektheni ethize . Ngiliphi ilwazi esilitlhogako ukwenzela bonyana sikwazi ukulemuka amaqhinga wokwenza okuthile ? AmaKomidi wamaWadi kuzakutlhogeka bonyana alawule ukuhlukana eendaweni ezinengi , ukusukela ekuhlukaneni phakathi kwamalunga weKomidi yeWadi ukuya ekuhlukaneni komphakathi . Imojuli le inqophe ekwahlukaneni emphakathini begodu nokobana inamandla angangani webuthano phezu kwetuthuko . Boke abahlanganyeli abazibandakanya kurhulumende wendawo kufanele babe nelwazi elisisekelo likarhulumende wendawo , iinhloso zabo , iminqopho kanye nendima nomsebenzi . AmaKomidi weWadi angasiza ukunikela ilwazeli emphakathini . Khuyini okwenzako ekwenza kube lula ukukhuluma nabo ? Ukuphathwa kwakamasipala kufaka hlangana iinkhulu zakamasipala . Iinkhulu zakamasipala kwezokuphatha ngizo ezinesibopho sokuphakela umphakathi ngemisebenzi yakamasipala . Iinkhulu , khulukhulu lezo ezineenkhundla eziphezulu zokuphatha , ziqatjhwe ukuya ngamakghono kanye nelwazi lazo . Icozululo leendlela zokuziphilisa lilithulusi elisisekelo lendlelakambiso ye-CBP ngombana lakha ukuzwisiswa kweendlela zokuziphilisa zeenqhema ezihlukileko zehlalakuhle emphakathini , zifaka hlangana ipahla yazo , iintjhijilo , imiphumela kanye namathuba afunwako . Iintjhijilo kanye nemiphumela yakha isisekelo zomtlamo . I-ofisi letuthuko : Lokhu mhlawumbe kwakungomunye wemiphumela eqakatheke kwamanikelela wokwakhiwa kweMasincedane Development Corporation . IMasincedane inikela ituthuko begodu nesekelo leensetjenziswa emphakathini , okufaka hlangana ideske yamarhwebo amancani , isentha yokusekela iingadi zomphakathi begodu nesentha yezeluleko enikela irhelebho langokomthetho labakhubazekileko begodu nesekelo eliphathelene nokuhlalisana komphakathi . Ubujamo balo lokuba yikhamphani yesiGaba 21 buyikghonakalise ngekulu ipumelelo ukukhuthaza ekutholakaleni kweemali ukuphathwa kweentlhabagelo begodu nokulinga ukwenza ngcono ubujamo bekhayapha . Ukungezelela kulokho ukuba khona komakhiwo wakhona esentha yedorobha kwenza bonyana kube yindawo yokuthintana hlangana nama-ofisi wangaphandle kwemisebenzi wetuthuko begodu nomphakathi wekhaya . Ngebhadi , ukutlhogakala kweemali emnyakaneni le eseduze kube nomthelela ekusebenzeni kwalo . Ukutlola abakhona / abakhambele umhlangano . Ukwenza ituthuko ebonakalako , emsinya nebambelelako ekuphunguleni ubuchaka nokungalingani eminyakeni ematjhumi amabili ezako , iSewula Afrika kufanele ilungise ingomuso layo , ukuthoma namhlanjesi . Umtlamo lo wendlala indlela etja yokuthuthukisa elinga ukubandakanya imiphakathi , ilutjha , abasebenzi , abantu abangasebenziko kanye nekoro yezamabhizinisi ukobana ihlanganyele nombuso onekghono khudlwana . Umnqopho kukwakha amakghono wabantu newenarha , ukwenzela bonyana kwakhiwe amathuba wabo boke abantu . Khulukhulu , umtlamo lo ugandelela ifuneko erhabekileko yokuletha ituthuko emsinya emikhakheni embalwa ukuphungula ubuchaka nokungalingani ngendlela eragela phambili . Ukwenza iimbawo - iimbawo eziphathelene neendingo ezinqophileko zomphakathi zingenziwa ngokuthuma amakhansela wewadi bona azidlulise namtjhana ngokuzisa bunqopha emkhandlwini . Nangabe ucabanga bona nawe ube nesandla ekukwateni , ungahlathululi , bawa ukulitjalelwa namtjhana phendula beze kuthi abanye baveze ukukwata kwabo . Ngaphandle kobana lokhu kwenzeke , angeze kube khona ikulumiswana ehle . Itjhebiswano -umphakathi kanye nekhansela bayabambisana bese ngokuhlanganyela banikela ekutlameni nekuthatheni iinqunto . Ekugcineni umkhandlu ngiwo onelizwi lokugcina . Tjengisa imikhakha lapha umasipala wangekhenu afaneleka khona . Tlama amaforamu womphakathi wokukhulumisana . Kubiza imali engangani ukudlulisa amakhetho ewadini ? Ukwenza imisebenzi yamapholisa ibe phrofetjhinali . Indlelakambiso yokuziphatha kwamapholisa kanye nendlelakambiso yephrofetjhinalizimu kufanele zihlanganiswe nokukhutjhulwa nokuzilawula ngefanelo emsebenzinabo . Ijima lokungeniswa esipholiseni kufanele lidose abosobizelomsebenzi abanekghono namakghonofundwa ngokusebenzisa irherho eliindlelambili ; elinye ngeleemphathiswa eziphetheko begodu elinye ngeleemphathiswa ezingakaphathi . Isekelo lobuthekhniki lokusiza le-GEP lizakusiza bona wenze okhunye ozicabangela khona ngekusasa lebhizinisakho . Lokhu kufaka hlangana ukwenza irhubhululo elihlelekileko lawo woke amaphuzu afunekako kanye nedatha . Ukubuthelela umtlolo ofunekako osemthethweni begodu nokuhlola iingozi ezikhambisana nokuraga ibhizinisi ngendlela efaneleko . Nikela abahlanganyeli imizuzu eli-10 ukuya emizuzwini eli-15 ukutjheja imibuzo . Kufanele bonyana kwenziwe amakhetho abudisi . Ukugcugcuzela ukwakhiwa kwemisebenzi eminengi , ukusebenza kwekoro yezabasebenzi kufanele kwenziwe ngcono . IKomitjhini yenza iimphakamiso ekunqotjhwe ngazo ukusiza abantu abatjha bonyana bangene ekorweni yezabasebenzi , ngokwenza bonyana imithetho yamabhizinisi amancani ibe lula , ngokuphungula ukutjhuba kwemimoya nokulwa , nangokuhlathulula iinkambiso zokuqotha nokuziphatha kumbi . Begodu kufanele kutjhejwe khudlwana ukubandulwa okuragela phambili kwabasebenzi abakhona ukwenzela bonyana boke abasebenzi babe namabizelo abazibandakanya kiwo . Urhulumende wendawo kumele ubikele umphakathi ukobana imali abanayo bayisebenzise njani . Benza lokhu ngokwenza bona iintatimende ezi-odithiweko zitholakale . Ilunga / amalunga weKomidi yeWadi angenza bonyana woke amalunga wengcenye ethileko yomphakathi ibakhohlisi begodu kungebanga lalokho umbono omunye nomunye abawenzako ngokwethulwa kwemisebenzi yomphakathi namkha amaphrojekthi kumele eqiswe amehlo . Amakhansela babantu abakhethwe bavowudu begodu ajamele abavowudu labo kumkhandlu wabomasipala . Akhethwa njalo ngemva kweminyaka emihlanu kobana ahlale kumkhandlu wabomasipala . Imindeni nemiphakathi . Ukondleka nomudlokhetho ofaneleko , khulukhulu wabantwana abangaphasi kweminyaka emithathu , uqakathekile mayelana nokukhula kuhle ngokomzimba nangokwengqondo . IKomitjhini yenza iimphakamiso mayelana nokondleka kwabantwana , ukusiza ababelethi nemindeni ukurarha ubuchaka , nokunikela amalungiselelo amahle khulu mayelana nabantwana abancani - kufaka hlangana isiphakamiso esithi umntwana omunye nomunye kufanele ubuncani bakhona afumane iminyaka emibili yefundo yekulisa . UMBUZO 3 Unayo na ibhajedi yenyanga ? Abanikeli bomsebenzi bakhethelwe amaprojekthi athileko , isib . Ukwakhiwa kweendlela , begodu badinga ukuthintwa nokuthi bahlale baziswa ngeendingo zomphakathi . Umsebenzi wabo kunikela umsebenzi abawukontrageleko . Umhlangano wokutlama okwandulelako wenziwa ngendlela yokukhulumisana nabajameli abavela emphakathini , lokho kufaka hlangana amakhansela , iKomidi yeWadi , abarholi abasiza ngemibono , abarholi bendabuko kanye nabanye ababambisani abafaneleko . Kilesisigaba umlamuli uvala ikambiso . Isingeniso - umnqopho wesigabesi kuthuthukisa ukuzithemba kwabantu ababandakanyekako ekambisweni . Esigabenesi boke abantu ababandakanyekako ( okufaka hlangana umlamuli ) bavumelana ngemithetjhwana ebekwako yekambiso . Isibonelo , abantu ababandakanyekako bavumelene ngokuthi abanye abantu nabethula ihlangothi lendababo , abakwenze ngaphandle kokuthikamezwa . Umlamuli - umkghonakalisi mumuntu okghonako begodu angakghona ukungena hlangana ukwenza isiqiniseko sokobana ikambiso ithola imiphumela efaneleko . Umkghonakalisi usesemrarululi womraro . Isigaba 195 ( e ) - ngokutjho kobungako obusisekelo nemigomo karhulumende yokuphatha umphakathi - iindingo zabantu kufanele ziphendulwe , begodu umphakathi kufanele ukhuthazwe ukobana uzibandakanye ekwenzeni imigomo . Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi nabakghonakalisi be-CBP esele baqedile ngamaphepha wecozululo leendlela zokuziphilisa babamba ikulumiswano yesiqhema . Ukubhajeda okungcono kuthuthukisa ukwethulwa komsebenzi . Umtlamo ohlanganisiweko , ukubhajeda begodu nokutjhejwa kwendlela yokwethulwa kweensetjenziswa okuqinisa ukuhlangana phakathi kweensetjenziswa ezinikelwa minyango begodu iinzuzo neendleko zazo isetjenziswezi . Amagadango wokwenza enza ngcono ukuba sepepeneneni begodu nokuzibophelela ngokuphathwa begodu nokusetjenziswa kweentlhabagelo zomphakathi ngokwepumelelo . Isigaba 3 siqalene nokwakhiwa kwamambala komtlamo . Ngokusebenzisa indlelakambiso ezwakalako yokuthatha amagadango alandelana ngefanelo , umphakathi uthatha ilwazi elihlanganisiweko kanye nemiphumela enikelwa itjhejontangi bese ukhiqiza umbono , umnqopho , isitatimende , amaqhinga , amaphrojekthi kanye nemisebenzi ukwenza ngcono ipilo yomphakathi . Ukunabisa amahlelo wemisebenzi yombuso ukufikela esigidini sinye sabahlanganyeli ngaphambi kokuphela komnyaka wee-2015 begodu ukufikela eengidini ezimbili zabahlanganyeli ngaphambi kokuphela komnyaka wee-2020 . Thoma ngemiraro emimbi khulu , isibonelo , ngiwuphi umnyaka obe mumbi khulu , ngibaphi abantu abangacoca ngezinye iimbonelo ukuya ngobumbi bazo . Ukuziphendulela : Ukutjengisa bona iinsetjenziswa zisetjenziswe ngendlela engiyo begodu ngendlela iphrojekthi iphakanyiswe ngayo emathomeni neemvumelwano zokusekelwa ngeemali . IKomidi yeWadi ibunjwe yikhansela yewadi nabantu abalitjhumi ababavowudi ngewadini begodu abakhethwe mphakathi abawusebenzelako . Amalunga wamaKomidi wamaWadi kufanele ajameleke ngokunabileko ajanyelwe mikhakha ehlukeneko yomphakathi ( abomma , abantu abatjha , imiphakathi egade idinywe amathuba phambilini , njll ) . Ubulunga babo kwezepolotikiakukafaneli buthikazise ukukhethwa kwabo . Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi azibandakanya ngokuzinikela ngokuthanda kwawo . Ukuhlaziya iphrojekthi - ukutjheja nokubuyekeza ngokusebenzisa ukuqinisa ngaphambili kweentjengiso ukulinganisa bona iphrojekthi iraga bunjani , ngiziphi iintjhijilo ezivelileko nokobana ukwenziwa kufanele kuhlaliswe bunjani . Iindawo zemikhukhu zakhiwe eduze nesitetjhi . Amalunga wabantu abahlala emikhukhwini banomraro wokuphathwa ziinhloko nokuba nokuvaleka esifubeni . Bayazaza ukusuka lapho batjhide ngombana baseduze nemisebenzinabo . Ipendulo : IKomidi yeWadi yabawa umkhandlu bona ubize umhlangano lapho ekuzokukhulunyiswana ngendaba le begodu kukhonjwe umkghonakalisi ozijameleko azokulamula indaba le . Umkhandlu wavuma . Umhlangano waba khona ama-iri ambalwa kodwana emaswapheleni womhlangano bavumelana bona ikontraga kufanele inikelwe isaziso senyanga bona iqedelele begodu ngaleso isikhathi ithendara lizokulungiswa bese abosokontraga benze iimbawo . Umjameli wamalunga weKomidi yeWadi , amakhansela kanye neensebenzi zomkhandlu zibekelwe ukubamba ama-inthaviyu nokutjheja amathendara . I-ajenti yetjhuguluko - iKomidi yeWadi ibandakanya umphakathi ekukhetheni imithetholawulo karhulumende wekhaya kanye nemitlamo njengobana ukubandakanyeka komphakathi kuqakathekile ekulinganiseni iindingo zomphakathi kiwo woke amazinga wekambiso yokuhlela . Yaba abahlanganyeli ubenze iinqhema ezincani begodu unikele esinye nesinye isiqhema umbuzo lo otlolwe ngenzansi . Njengombana kunemibuzo emithathu kwaphela , ezinye iiqhema nazo zizakunikelwa imibuzo efanako . Amanye amaphrojekthi akhonjwe ngesikhathi nabegade kwenziwa i-CBP kufuze enziwe abe ziimphakamiso ezithunyelwa ku-IDP ngombana amumethe ilwazi eliqakathekileko eliphathelene neemfuno zomphakathi kanye neensombululo ezakhako ezifumaneka emphakathini . Kodwana kungenzeka abe makhulu khulu bonyana angaphunyeleliswa ezingeni lewadi . Isirhunyezwesi sinikela ihlathululo malungana nekufuze kwenziwe lokha nakwakhiwa izethulo ze-IDP . Ukukhonjwa nokukhetha okuqakathekileko kwamahlelo namaphrojekthi kuqakathekile ukuvikela imiphumela ezokuba lisizo khulukhulu emphakathini . Ingabe iKomidi yeWadi ifuna ukujameleka kimaphi amaforamu , njengezepilo nanyana iinhlangano zomphakathi ? Isivumelwano somsebenzi kusivumelwano hlangana kukamasipala nomnikeli womsebenzi ukunikela umasipala ihlangothi elithileko lomsebenzi ngesikhathi esifitjhani ( ngomnyaka owodwa namkha emibili kwaphela ) . Umasipala unikela ibhajedi begodu atjheje nokusebenza komnikeli womsebenzi ukuqinisekisa bonyana umsebenzi onikelweko uba ngowekhwalithi ehle begodu uwela ngaphakathi kwebhajedi enikelweko . Ikomidi yesigungu ehlangeneko ikhethwa mkhandlu nekomidi kasodorobha ekhethwe ngusodorobha womkhandlu ophetheko . Womabili amakomidi la , aphethwe ngusodorobha . Amakomidi la enziwa makhansela anemisebenzi ethize enqophileko . Abatlhogomeli badinga ibandulo ibandulo iingulani ezigulela ekhaya . Nasele babanduliwe kufanele bathole umrholo kanye namaphasela wokudla . Umbuso othuthukisako urarulula abonobangela bamambala bobuchaka nokungalingani . Umbuso othuthukisako weSewula Afrika uzakungenelela ukusekela nokuhlahla ituthuko ukwenzela bonyana umphakathi woke ukwazi ukufumana iinzuzo ( khulukhulu abantu abatlhagako ) , begodu ukwazi ukwakha isivumelwano senengi ukwenzela bonyana irhuluphelo yelizwe loke yesikhathi eside ikwazi ukuba sebujameni obungcono kunokutshwenyeka okungabandakanyi boke abantu . Engcenyeni yokuthoma yesiGaba 4 , abahlanganyeli be-CBP banikelwa imihlahlandlela malungana neemphakamiso abangazethula ku-IDP kanye namaphepha wemiqondo yephrojekthi aphathelene namaphrojekthi adinga isekelo langaphandle . Begodu kukhulunywa nangokwakhiwa kwesabelo seemali zewadi ezigabe isimetjhe esikghonakalisa umphakathi bonyana ukwazi ukuragela phambili ngomtlamo wawo ngaphandle kokumorosa isikhathi . Ingcenye yesibili yesiGaba 4 igandelela ukuqakatheka komtlamo wamagadango onemininingwana ezeleko malungana nokuphumelelisa umtlamo . Begodu yendlala indlela amaphrojekthi ekufuze ahlukaniswe ngayo ngamagadango alandelanako womtlamo wamagadango . Begodu ihlathulula indlela ekufuze isetjenziswe mayelana nokutlolwa kwemininingwana ezeleko yomtlamo . Isigaba siphetha ngokwethulwa komtlamo oqedelelweko kumphathi we-CBP bonyana aphasise isabelo seemali ezigade isimetjhe . Lokhu nasele kuphasisiwe , kufuze bonyana kuhlelwe umhlangano wokunikela umphakathi umbiko obuyako malungana nelwazi elitjha elifunyenweko . Iintlabagelo zakamasipala zisetjenziselwa ukuhlanganisa iindawo zemakhaya nezemadorobheni begodu nokudlulisela iinsetjenziswa ebantwini abatlhagako . Abahlanganyeli babelana ngelemuko abalitholako babelana ngelemuko abalitholako mayelana nokwethulwa komsebenzi , kungaba ngobumbi namkha okuhle . Vumela munye namkha babili abahlanganyeli bonyana babelane ngelemuko labo begodu babuze nokobana khuyini okumele kwenziwe ukwenza lokhu ngcono , nangabe ilemuko bekungelimbi . Sebenzisa amanothi wekhoso asesAhlukweni 2 , 2.2 azokusiza ngemva sewuthole umbiko obuyako obuya eenqhemeni . Zinengi iindlela ezehlukileko zokuphathwa kwephrojekthi ezisetjenziswako ngehlangothini letuthuko . Lokhu kuvamise ukuhluka eembonelweni ezisetjenziswa ephasini elisebenzisanako . Nazo zivamise ukuhluka phakathi kweenarha . ebujameni beSewula Afrika asikho isbonelo sengcenye yomphakathi esizinganisiweko begodu kungaba nomehluko naphakathi kweembonelo ezisetjenziswa eninyangweni ehlukileko karhulumende . Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi kumele ajayele umzombe wokuphathwa kwephrojekthi ngombana lokhu kusibonelo esisetjenziswako esikhathini esinengi . Ukuhlukaniswa namagama weenteji namkha iingaba zomzombe wephrojekthi kungahlukana ngokwethembela e-ofisini elisekela ngemali namkha emnyangweni karhulumende . Izakhamuzi zidlala indima eqakathekileko eenquntweni ezithinta iimpilo zazo nekwenzeni isiqiniseko sokobana abadosiphambili bazo abakhethiweko badlala iindima zabo ngendlela efaneleko begodu benza nemisebenzabo . Lokhu kuba ngaphezulu kokuvowuda emakhethweni . Ukuzibandakanya kuhle kwezakhamuzi kutjho bona abantu badlala indima eqakathekileko hlangana namaklhetho . Kiyo yoke imikhakha yombuso izakhamuzi kufanele zenze isiqiniseko sokobana ziphosela lobubodlhana nakucocwa mayelana nokubunjwa kwemithetho emitjha ngokukhambela imihlangano yokulalelwa kwemibono yomphakathi nanyana ukuthumela iimphakamiso . UMBUZO 1 Iyini indima oyidlalako njengelunga leKomidi yeWadi endleleni yekambiso yebhajedi ? Thatha iimpendulo . Emtlameni beka woke amatheyibula avela kizo zike iinqhema phezu kweboda bese ukhupha amaphuzu ajayelekileko etheyibuleni usebenzise imibuzo ecocako yoMsebenzi wesi- 4 . Umtlamo kufuze ufake hlangana ilwazi eliphathelene nomphakathi , izehlakalo zomphakathi kanye namathulusi neendlela ezingasetjenziswa ukufumana ilwazi elifunekako . Ekhasini elilandelako kunesibonelo somtlamo nokobana kufuze uhlathululwe bunjani . Lokhu kwenzelwa ukunikela isithombe malungana nalokho okumumethweko ekufuze kufakwe emtlameni wewadi . ISewula Afrika inamatjhere amanengi ephasini loke emkhakheni weplathinamu neensimbi , wegolide , wedayimani , wemanganisi , wamalahle , welitje lesimbi neyuraniyamu . Kodwana eminyakeni elitjhumi egadungileko , umsebenzi wangekhaya wokurhweba ngezenjiwa ubhalelwe kukhambisana nokukhula kwephasi loke okuvame ukuba khona mayelana nokuthengiswa kwezenjiwa eenarheni zangaphandle ngenca yemithangalasisekelo engasimihle , ekhambisana nemileyo yokulawula nemigomo eliya isisomali . ISewula Afrika ingahlomula khulu ngenca yefuneko ekhulako yeempahla zerhwebo e-Asia . Nangabe ifuna ukwenza lokhu , kufanele yenze ngcono imithangalasisekelo yayo yamanzi , iinthuthi namandla wegezi begodu kufanele yenze bonyana abasisimali bangabi nokuzaza ngemigomo nokulawula . Lokhu kuzokwenza bonyana ikoro yemisebenzi yokurhweba ngamaminerali ikwazi ukuthumela amakghono , imithombo , ilwazi nemali ekhona , begodu lokhu kuzakwenza bonyana umbuso ukwazi ukukhuphula ingeniso yomthelo kunangendlela esebenza ngayo njenganje . Ukutjhugulula irherho lokutlama ukurarulula isibopho esimakghedlhukghedlhu sokutlama embusweni wenarha , ukutlama kwemibuso okungakahlanganiswa kuhle , ukuhlukana kwemingcele yabomasipala nobuthakathaka bemitlamo yokuthuthukisa ehlanganisiweko . Ihlangano yabahlali igcugcuzela ituthuko nokubumbana komphakathi . Emiphakthini eminengi etlhagako , iinhlangano ezingasizo zakarhulumende eziqalene nehlalakuhle kanye nezinye iinhlangano ezinzinze emphakathini zethula amahlelo aqakathekileko wezehlalakuhle nemisebenzi . Ukunabisa amahlelo wemisebenzi yezehlalakuhle nemisebenzi yomphakathi , ukwenza bonyana umbuso ukghone ukusebenzela nokusekela imiphakathi etlhagako , khulukhulu leyo enamazinga aphezulu wobulelesi nemiguruguru . Ngiziphi iinhlangano zomphakathi nanyana iminyango kamasipala esifisa ukuyimema bonyana izokwenza izethulo ekomidini yewadi nanyana emhlanganweni wesifunda sekhetho ? Amalanga umasipala azabe abambe ngawo imihlangano yokukhulumisana ongafisa ukuhlanganyela kiyo , njenge-IDP kanye nesabelo seemali saqobe mnyaka . Ukwethulwa kwemisebenzi okunepumelelo yomthangalasisekelo okugcinekako kudzimelele ekuzwisiseni kweendima nemisebenzi yababambisani ekuqalelelweni komthangalasisekelo . Ukuzibophelela ekuphathweni kokwenziwa komsebenzi kusezandleni zomphakathi kamasipala . ISewula Afrika itlhoga irherho lezomnotho elihlomulisa boke abantu , elinamandla nelizakuba namakhakhazela ahlukaniselanwa ngokulinganako . Ngomnyaka wee-2030 , irherho lezomnotho kufanele libe seduze nokuqatjha boke abantu , ukuhlomisa abantu ngamakghono abawatlhogako , ukuqinisekisa bonyana ubunikazi bemikhiqizo buhluke khudlwana begodu buyakghona ukukhula ngokurhaba , begodu bunikela imithombo yokubhadalela ukusisa ebantwini nepahleni . Imithombo : Ikhophi yomTlamo wokuThuthukisa oHlanganiswe ngokuZeleko kamasipala , uumHlahlandlela 2 womTlamo womPhakathi ne-IDP ( i-AICDD nemiSebenzi yokuThuthukisa ) , i-PowerPoint ( ayikakateleleki ) . Indima edlalwa mizamosisungulo yemisebenzi yombuso , efana nehlelo lemisebenzi yombuso , nayo kufanele bonyana itjhejwe . Nanyana iSewula Afrika iphumelela ekufumaneni ukukhula kwe-GDP ngamaphesende angaphezu kwamahlanu ngomnyaka begodu imisebenzi ikhuphuka ngokurhaba eminyakeni elitjhumi ezako , kodwana kusazokuba nesidingo samahlelo anjalo . Ukusebenza ngabo bonabo abangababili abahlanganyeli benza iphosta erhunyeza imihlobo yemitlolo yemigomo nemithetjhwana ebumba itlhatlha mayelana nokuthuthukisa urhulumende wendawo . Abahlanganyeli godu ngokufitjhazana bacoca ngelwazeli kumawadabo bese bahlathulula indlela umgomo nebhoduluko lemithetjhwana elinamandla ngakhona phasi . Lapho kuthonywa khona kuthola ihlobo lenturhu . Inturhu akusiyo into embi . Ngokweqiniso inturhu ingasebenza njengesilethitjhuguluko . Igama elithi inturhu livela kwelesiLathini ' conflictus ' elitjho ' ukulwa ndawonye ' . Isibonelo , nawukghona ukutlwebha iintlhogwana ezimbili zomlilo ukghona ukwenza umlilo wokupheka namtjhana wokufuthumeza . Ngendlela siphendula ngayo enturhwini kuzokulinganiswa kukobana inturhu iyabhebhetheka namtjhana iyehla na . iinturhu ezinengi azirarululeki kodwana ukukhuluma ngeendingo zabantu ababandakanyekako kungasiza ekwenzeni ubujamo ngcono . IKomidi yeWadi ingahloma ikomidi encani nanyana amakomidi amancani bese ibandakanya iinhlangano zomphakathi emakomidini amancani la . Boke ababambisani ewadini bayakhuthazwa ukuzibandakanya kumakomidi amancani akhambisana nalokho abanekareko ngakho . Nangabe ufuna ukurarulula umraro okubangela bona ukwate , sebenza ngokukwata engcenye bese nomraro nawo wodwa . Balekela ukwenza iinqunto eziqakathekileko lokha nangabe ukukwata kuyakulawula . Umphakathi ohlala emikhukhwini ehlanu kwedorobha usiwe endaweni yezindlu ezakhiweko ekungaba ma-20km ukusuka edorobheni . Esinye seenzathu esenza bona abahlali bemikhukhu basuke lapho bakhe khona kukobana abanye babahlali banikelwe iindawo zasafuthi abaziqatjhisako . Abahlali abanengi bakwatile ngombana babe serhelweni lesigiyani isikhathi eside ngalokho bathi akukalungi kilabo bahlali abanikelwe izindlu bese bona bayaziqatjhisa ngombana bakhandela abanye abantu ukuthola amakhaya . Khonapho bathi abafuni ukusuka ngombana kude nedorobha begodu abanye babo basebenza edorobheni begodu abanamali yeenkhwelo . Abahlali bathi abasuki . Lokha nabegade akhulumisana nababikiindaba , usihlalo wekomidi yabahlali uthe nakibe bebathintwe mantanzi ngaphambi kokuthoma kwamahlelo la bebazokwazi ukuhlathulula bona kubayini bangafuni ukusuka kanye nonobangela wokunikelwa kwabanye amakhaya , abaqatjhisako kungombana kuyabiza ukuya emsebenzini ngamalanga . IKomitjhini isekela umtlamo wamaphuzu alikhomba ovezwe lirherho lobulungiswa bobulelesi , ekucocwa ngalo ngokuzeleko esahlukweni se-12 . Umtlamo lo usekela umnqopho wombuso wokutjhugululela kancani kancani kancani imithombo yombuso kumasisomali azakwazi ukubuyisela irherho lezomnotho esigeni , ukunabisa amathuba nokukhuphula amakghono . Ngesibanga salokho , ezinye iingcenye zesabelo seemali selizwe loke kuzakufuneka bonyana zikhule khudlwana ngendlela ebuthaka . Khuthaza ingcoco ngemva kobujamo ngabunye lapha abahlanganyeleko bacabanga khona ngeendlela abangahlula ngazo ubujamobo bese benza isiqiniseko sokobana kuba nokuhlanganyela komphakathi . Ukukwata mumuzwa wemvelo ovela navane umuntu azizwa asilingeka namtjhana ahlaselwa . Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi angahlangabezana namajamo lapho bahlangana nesiqhema sabantu esisilingekileko namtjhana umuntu ngamunye khulukhulu njengamaKomidi weWadi enza ngendlela hlangana kwakamasipala , ilunga lomkhandlu nomphakathi . Abahlali bangahlangahlangana bese bayakwata eentweni ezifana nokwethulwa kweensetjenziswa ezibuthakathaka namtjhana bajame ereyini lokufayila amatleyimu namtjhana ukuthola imitlolo . Ukuthintana okuphumelelisako kufaka hlangana indlela yokwazi ukusebenza ngokukwata nokuthusela . Njengobana lesi siphetho salemojuli , buyelela woke amaphuzu aqakathekileko walesisahluko bese urhunyeza ngokubuthelela ilwazi kizo zoke izahluko ukuze abahlanganyeli bazwisise ikambiso ngokupheleleko . Hlola amanothi wekhoso bona akusize . Indima yokululeka - ukululeka nokusiza amakhansela bona atjheje iindaba zomphakathi begodu iindabezi zisiwe emkhandlwini . Ukulingana emsebenzini namanye amagadango wokulungisa lokho okungakhange kukhambe kuhle ngaphambilini kufanele bonyana kwenziwe ngepumelelo ngokuqalana nebhoduluko ekuthuthukiswa kilo amakghono . Ukulingana kukhathalela ukufana kwemiphumela . Kutjhiwo Kutjhiwo Kutjhiwo Kutjhiwo ubulungiswa nokungasolisi begodu nokobana kungadinga ipatho eyehlukileko , namkha amagadango akhethekileko kwabanye abantu namkha iinqhema . Ukulingana kuvumela ubujamo obunqophileko namkha imikghwa yomuntu ngamunye isiqhema , ubulili , itlasi , ikolo namkha ubudala . Kutlhoga ukwehliswa kwazo zoke iinqabo eziya emnothweni nemathubeni wezepolitiki begodu nokufumaneka kwefundo nemisebenzi esisekelo , ukwenzela bonyana , abobaba nabomma babo boke ubudala , ubujamo neenkhundla bathabele amathuba la bebazuze ngawo . Ukulingana ngokobulili kutjho ukuphathwa okungasolisiko kwabomma nabobaba , ngokuya kweendingo zabo . Lokhu kungafaka phakathi ukufana kwepatho engafaniko kodwana etjhejwa njengelinganako ngokuya kwamalungelo , inzuzo iimbopho namathuba . Bacabangele phambili begodu / bakhombe neesetjenziswa zomphakathi wabo emnyakeni ombalwa . Ama-IDP kaMasipala akhomba amaprojekthi anamalanga acacileko wokugcina neragelo phambili leenkomba . Indima eqakathekileko yamalunga wekhansela kutlhogomela ukusebenza kukamasipala ngokuya ngezethulo ezibekiweko . AmaKomidi wamaWadi kumele enze isiqiniseko sokobana bazijayeza ngeentjengiso zomsebenzi nemiphumela yemisebenzi ebekwe ku-IDP kamasipala wabo ukuze bakghone ukuhlela iragelophambili . Lokha nangabe iwadi likhavara indawo ekulu , hlela imihlangano endaweni engaphezu kweyodwa ukwenzela bonyana zoke iindawezi zibe nelemuko ngalokho okwenzakalako . AMALUNGA WEKOMIDI YEWADI ASEBENZA EDUZE KHULU namakhansela begodu nomphakathi . IKomidi yeWadi ingakhetha ukwabela amalunga weKomidi yeWadi imisebenzi / amaphothifoliyo . Lokhu kwenza ukusebenza nomasipala kube lula khulu begodu nokujamela imiphakathi eendabeni eziyithintako . Indima yeKomidi yeWadi kufaka hlangana ukukghonakalisa nokwenza ngcono amandla womphakathi wokuphumelelisa iinhloso zephrojekthi abayenza bona ngokwabo . Iinqhema zokwenza namtjhana amakomidi ahlonywe emphakathini bona enze amaphrojekthi athize azokusizeka ngokuthola ilwazi elisisekelo lelawulo lephrojekthi . AmaKomidi wamaWadi ahlonywe ngokwesiqunto esenziwe mkhandlu . Imisebenzi yamaKomidi wamaWadi ilawulwa kuphasiswa kweenqunto zomkhandlu ezizwakalako . Le yikambiso eyakhiweko neyokuhlanganyela isiquntu esithathwako lapho abantu ababandakanyekako bahlangana , ngesizo namtjhana ngaphandle kwesizo lomuntu wesithathu , ukufinyelela esisombululweni esamukelekako ebantwini boke ababandakanyekako bese kusetjenzwa iimvumelwano namtjhana kurarululwa kwamambala namtjhana kubonakale ukwahlukana . Ilandelela nemibiko ebuyako : Ukuphikelela emibikweni ehlala yenziwa kumaphrojekthi kamasipala nemisebeni kuKomidi yeWadi nemihlanganweni yomphakathi kumawadawo ukuze izakhamuzi zinande zaziswa ngeragelo phambili / nanyana imiraro . Iimphakamiso ezakhako mayelana nokwenza ngcono kufanele yenziwe , begodu lapha kukghoneka khona , umphakathi ungafakwa ekuraruleni umraro . AmaKomidi weWadi kufanele adlale indima enokuzinikela mayelana nokulawula ukwenziwa komsebenzi njengobana i-PMS ilithulusi elilisizo lokukhamba emzileni weragelo phambili lokwenza lakamasipala elimayelana nabomqothelwa bokwenza kanye neenkomba eziqakathekileko zokwenza umsebenzi ezibekele yona . Lokhu kudinga ukusebenzisana okubandamelene nelunga lomkhandlu elilindelwe ukubonisana namaKomidi weWadi kizo zoke iinteji zelawulo lokwenza . Yoke iminyango karhulumende , yelizwe neyamaphrovinsi , ifuneka bona ngokombiko mThethokambiso wokuTjhugululwa komSebenzi womPhakathi , ka-1995 ukobana ithathele phezulu ukwenziwa komsebenzi . Incwadi yeBatho Pele izama ukunikela abaphathi bemisebeni ilwazi elizabenza bona basebenzise iinkambiso ezithileko , iinkambiso eziqakathekileko zokwenziwa komsebenzi . Urhulumende uyame ngomkhakha womphakathi ukobana wenze imisebenzi efunekako kuhle nethembekako . Lesi ngesinye seenzathu esenza iBatho Pele ihlale ikhona kurhulumende , yazise ngazo zoke iinkambiso ' ukusukela kumaQhinga wokutlama , nazo zoke iingaba zokuThuthukisa umTlamo oHlangeneko , ukuPhatha umSebenzi nokuPhatha imiRholo begodu kufanele ibe nobufakazi ngaso soke isikhathi lokha isisebenzi sombuso nasisiza isakhamuzi . Imibono akukafaneli bonyana ibe ngileyo engakanqophi nenganayo imininingwana , kodwana kufuze bonyana ihlukaniswe ngemisebenzi elandelana ngendlela efaneleko . Lokha nangabe imisebenzi ayibandakanyi imininingwana enqophileko angeze yenzeka . Lesi sigaba samaswaphela sokwakha umtlamo wewadi begodu kufuze sitjheje indaba yesabelo seemali esiphathelene neemali ezigade isimetjhe esifuneka ukuragelisa phambili umtlamo , okusisabelo esivela kurhulumende wendawo . Begodu kufuze sitjheje namaphrojekthi ekufuze ethulwe ku-IDP bonyana ikwazi ukuwatjheja . Mhlambe umukghwa oqakathekileko okufanele ukhunjulwe mayelana namazinga welawulo lephrojekthi nakanjani , kukobana akavumeli iphetheni ethe thwi enezinga elilodwa elirholela kwelilandelako ngaphandle kokubuyelela kweenteji zemathomeni . Amanye amazinga ahlukahlukeneko abuyekezwa njengoba umzombe wephrojekthi usiya . Isibonelo , izinga elinye nelinye lidinga ukuqedwa ngaphambi kokuthoma elinye . Amandla wezakhamuzi -abantu bazibophelela ezenzweni zabo begodu abayami komunye umuntu ukobana abenzele . Isibonelo umgodi osendleleni uvulekile begodu uyingozi . Umphakathi uthatha isiqunto sokobana uhlangane bese ukhetha ikomidi ukobana ikhambe iyokukhulumisana nomkhandlu wedorobha . Okwesikhatjhana kubekwa itshwayo eliyelelisa izakhamuzi ukobana ziyelele . Bakhulumisana ngendaba le bekufike isikhathi lapha umkhandlu liyitjheja khona . Khuluma kabuthaka bona woke umuntu ezwe . Sebenzisa ilimi abamukelilwazi elibanelisako nakungasinjalo angekhe basaba nomdlandla walokhu okutjhoko . IKhomitjhini yamaLungelo weLimi , amaSiko nezeKolo ithuthukisa ihlonipho yamalungelo la begodu ithuthukise beyikhulise ukuthula , ubungani , ubuntu , ukubekezela nebumbano lesizwe . Ngokusebenzisa idayagramu esekhasini lama-35 lamanothi wekhoso ( sebenzisa i-PowerPoint nangabe ikhona , nanyana usebenzise amanothi wekhoso njengomtlolo ongakusiza bese wakha idayagramu efliphutjhadini uthome ngesigaba ngasinye ngasikhathi sinye ) , hlathulula bonyana umzombe we-CBP kufuze uhlobane nalowo we-IDP . Gandelela bonyana isizathu salokho kukobana i-CBP ilinga ukuqinisekisa bonyana iindingo zomphakathi ziyakhonjwa begodu zifakwe ku-IDP . I-CBP ne-IDP ziindlelakambiso ezizombelezako begodu ngebanga lalokho kufuze zikhambisane . Umtletlana wendawana eyisampula ufana nengcenye esikwe emphakathini ekufuze ikhethelwe ukugandelela imisebenzi yendawo malungana nendawo leyo . Ukhomba iindaba ezinqophileko zesikhala eziphathelene nokutlama ituthuko umphakathi wewadi ozithatha njengeziqakathekileko . Iinkambiso zombiko obuyako - Iyini ikambiso ekhona ukwenza isiqiniseko bona umphakathi uthola umbiko obuyako qobe , mayelana neendaba zomkhandlu kanye nelwazi elenziwa ngeenkhathi ezifaneleko lomkhandlu kanye nombiko obuyako womphakathi ? UKUTHUTHUKISWA KWEQHINGA LOKUHLANGANISA ITUTHUKO NGOKUZELEKO ngumasipala kusidingo sakaRhulumende weKhaya : UmThetho weRherho lakaMasipala , we-2000 . Isahluko sesi-5 se-MSA , somnyaka we-2000 sibawa bonyana omunye nomunye umasipala . . . . . amukele elilodwa iqhinga elihlanganisiweko begodu namano wokuthuthukisa umasipala ( isigaba 25 ( 1 ) . Ihlelo lithatha iminyaka emihlanu begodu liliphahla elibanzi letuthuko ngaphakathi kwendawo le . Libuyekezwa kanye ngonyaka . I-IDP ihlahla indlela yomtlamo wokwenza kwakamasipala begodu kumele ( ngokomthetho ) ithuthukiswe ngokuthintana nomphakathi wekhaya . Ukungalingani kobulili kungalungiswa nje kwaphela ngokobana abomma nabobaba bathathe amagadango wokutjhijila indlela abaziphatha ngayo , ilungelo elikhethekileko nendlela yokwenza izinto . Yoke iminyango yelizwe neyamaphrovinsi kufanele iveze kuhle begodu ibeke neenkhathi mayelana neragelo phambili lokufikelelwa kwemisebenzabo mayelana nalabo abangazange bayithole ngaphambilini . Qinisekisa bonyana amalunga weKomidi yeWadi ayabandakanyeka emaforamini wokubonisana . Ukusekelwa kwamabhizinisi amancani ngokuwathintanisa ngconywana nama-ejensi aphatheleneko , neenhlangano zeemali zokuthuthukisa , namahlelo wombuso newekoro yangeqadi wokuhlomulisa umphakathi . IBatho Pele ihlose ukwenziwa komsebenzi okufaka hlangana ukuthokozwa kweendingo zamakhastama ngokupheleleko nokuhlanganisa ' inani loke lokufakwako ' leempendulo neensombululo . IBHAJEDI IHLELO LEZEEMALI . Ibeka epepeneneni imisebenzi yomnyaka weemali ozako ngokunikela iindleko zemisebenzi le begodu nokuthi ingenisomali yokubhadela zoke iindleko izakubuyaphi . Ukwakha isiko lokuziphendulela , ukuvuleka nokuba pepenene ekuphatheni umphakathi nanyana ekulawuleni amandla womphakathi nanyana ukwenziwa komsebenzi womphakathi , ngokunikela umphumela elungelweni lesenzo sokuphatha . IBatho Pele yenzelwe ukujamisa kuhle ubujamo bomsebenzi wombuso ukuqinisekisa bona ubungako beBatho Pele kuragelwa phambili nabo kuhle emisebenzini eyenzelwa izakhamuzi zenarha . Kuyithatha isikhathi esingangani iKomidi yeWadi ukuphumelelisa indima yawo ? Iinkulumiswano eziqakathekileko zabanikeli ngemisebenzi - iinkulumiswanezi kufuze zibanjwe ntangi ukuqinisekisa ukuhlanganyela okunabileko . Ukuthintana kuyindlela yekambiso lapha abantu ababelana ngemibono . Ukuthinana ngokuphumelelisako , abantu kufuze bahlele imicabango yabo , bazethule kuhle bazwakale begodu balalele ngendlela enqophileko . Ukuthintana okungakaphumeleliswa kungenza kobana kuphambanwe . I-jenda yomkhandlu ihlathululwa entumbeni yehlangano mayelana neenkhundla zepolotiki zeenqhema ngeendaba eziku-ajenda ngaphambi komhlangano womkhandlu . UmThetho wamaHlelo kaMasipala , ka-2000 wendlala amahlelo wangaphakathi wabomasipala ekufuze abenza bonyana bakwazi ukusebenza ngendlela ezakuthuthukisa imiphakathi yendawo ngokwezomnotho nehlalakuhle begodu bakwazi ukuqinisekisa bonyana boke abantu bafumana iinsetjenziswa eziqakathekileko ngentengo engalilisiko . Ukufunda isifundo : umbiko ohleliweko wokuthuthukisa ngesikhathi somzombe wephrojekthi uzokunikela isisekelo sokuraga ngokubuyekeza , kanye neemfundo zephrojekthi ezokuthathwa ngomuso . Iindlela zemitlamo yephrojekthi zingafanela ukutjhuguluka begodu kuqakathekile ukuba nesilululwazi okuzakunande kuyiwa kiso ngomuso . Isahlukwesi sibonelela ngomleyo ekwenzelwa ngaphakathi kwawo umtlamo womphakathi . Abahlanganyeli kufuze batjheje iminqopho , imithelela ebonakalako yokuthoma i-ICBP , iinkambisolawulo kanye nesendlalelo somthethokambiso malungana nalendlela . Isahlukwesi sinikela abahlanganyeli isisekelo sokuhloma i-CBP . Ukubeka ngeqadi libandlululo elenziwa kutjhiya ngaphandle umuntu namkha isiqhema sabantu ekubeni yingcenye yommongo wabadlali abathatha iinqunto . Khuyini okucabanga bona kwenziwe siqhema sakho okusebenze kuhle ? Sele kuziinyanga ezihlanu soloko amalunga weKomidi yeWadi babe nomhlangano . Amalunga womkhandlu athi wona amatasatasa ngalokho amalunga weKomidi yeWadi abona inga akhutjhelwa ngaphandle . Kwadaleka ukwahlukana hlangana kwamalunga weKomidi yeWadi kanye nekhansela . Amalunga womphakathi nawo abona bonyana amakhansela akawathathi njengabantu abancamileko njengobana ikhansela lihlala lingekho ukuzobahlangabeza namtjhana ukuphendula iinghonghoyilo zawo . Umphakathi wahlela umtjhagalo usiya emkhandlwini uyokunghonghoyila . Isakhelo esinabileko samakghono ngokusebenzisa ifundo engcono nokuthwasiselwa umsebenzi . Yabakghonakalisi bakamasipala - bangavela eenkorweni ezahlukeneko zakamasipala nanyana kungaba ziinkhulu zobuthekhiniki zakarhulumende ezivela esiyingini nanyana eminyangweni yesifunda . Umsebenzi 4 Qala kumThethosisekelo begodu utjengise umnqopho ubudlelwano hlangana kwakarhulumende obambiseneko kanye netjhebiswano laborhulumende . Itjhebiswano nomrhatjho womphakathi okileyo ndawo lizakusiza amaKomidi weWadi ukobana anikele umphakathi ilwazi bese athola imibiko yawo ebuyako . Igadangweli liveza isithombe somphakathi , bobani abamphakathi , ngalokho kutjhiwo , iinqhenyana zehlalakuhle , imithombo kanye nemihlobo yeendlela zokuziphilisa zomphakathi , imisebenzi eqakathekileko yomphakathi neyabanikeli ngemisebenzi . Isigaba somtlamo wewadi sihlukaniswe iingcenye ezintathu . Yokuthoma , ikhuluma ngesendlalelo somphakathi kanye neenqhelo eziqakathekileko ; yesibili ikhuluma ngokuthi bobani abamphakathi ( iinqhema zehlalakuhle ) nokobana basebenzisa ziphi iindlela zokuziphilisa ; begodu ingcenye yesithathu ikhuluma ngemisebenzi neensetjenziswa . Kungani ucabanga kobana ibhajedi yakamasipala kufuze inikelwe umphakathi / izakhamuzi ? Zinengi iindlela zokuphatha / zokulawula ubujamo bokuphambana ngemibono . Esahlukweni lesi siqale indlela evamileko yokurarululwa komraro . Ababambisani abahlukileko bephrojekthi kufanele bakhonjwe nekghono labo lihlolwe . Lokhu kutjho bona isiqhema sephrojekthi sizokuba nelwazi lokobana khuyini okuhloswe ukuphunyeleliswa yiphrojekthi nokobana khuyini okufuna mbambisani ngamunye mayelana nokubika nehlobo lesizo namtjhana iinsetjenziswa ezinganikelwa ephrojekthini . IBatho Pele akusiyo ikambiso engeqadi ehlukileko , imgomo begodu kufanele ibe mgomo oyelelisako kiyo yoke imisebenzi eyenziwako . Yeke , nanyana ngikuphi ukubandakanyeka , kungaba ngokwengcenyeye- ofisi engemva nanyana i-ofisi yangaphambili elawulako nanyana ukuthintana ngaphakathi nanyana ngaphandle , kufanele kuyeleliswe ziinkambiso nomoya we-Batho Pele . Amaphrojekthi ayakghonakala , okutjho bona iminqopho ingaphunyeleliswa ngepumelelo hlangana nesikhatjhana sebhoduluko eliphilako kanye nobukghoni bama-ejensi bokwenziwa komsebenzi . Ngokuhlanganyela emakomidini nemaforamini - imikhandlu ingajamisa ubululeki kanye namanye amakomidi namaforamu , njengeforamu yokuthuthukisa ehlangeneko . AmaKomidi weWadi angasebenzisa iinhlanganwezi ukunikela umbono weenqunto ezithinta umphakathi . Imiphakathi yeendaweni zemakhaya yeSewula Afrika kufanele bonyana ibe namathuba amanengana wokuhlanganyela ngokupheleleko kwezomnotho , kwezehlalakuhle nakwezepolotiki yenarha , ngokusekelwa ngefundo yekhwalithi ehle , ngetjhejo lezamaphilo , ngeenthuthi neminye imisebenzi esisekelo . Ukuphumelela kokubuyekezwa kwemithetho yenarha , kokwakhiwa kwemisebenzi nokukhuphuka kwemikhiqizo yezelimo kuzokusiza ekwakheni irherho lezomnotho weendaweni zemakhaya elibandakanya boke abantu . Ukutjheja : Imiphakathi ingabawa umasipala ukobana akhethe abajameli bekomidi yomphakathi ukobana itjheje iinkambiso kanye nokuyelelisa umasipala kilokho okunyulwako mayelana nokungezwa komsebenzi kanye nokwenza ngcono . Amalunga wamaKomidi wamaWadi angasebenza godu njengamalunga wekomidi . Ukungezelela ipahla ethunyelwa eenarheni zangaphandle , ngokuqalana nemikhakha iSewula Afrika esele inemikhiqizo yayo kanye nenzuzo emadanisekako , njengomkhakha wemisebenzi yokurhweba ngezenjiwa , wokwakha , wokukhiqiza amakghono aphakathi , wezelimo nokukhiqizwa kwemikhiqizo yezelimo , wefundo ephakemeko , nezamavakatjho kanye nemisebenzi yerhwebo . Iinkomba ngokunqotjhiweko okwenza bona ukutjheja , ukubuyekeza nokuhlaziya kwephrojekthi kuphumelelisile iminqopho nofana awa . Kuziinkomba ezizokutjengisa bona iindingo zokuhlela zifanele ukuhlaliswa kuhle begodu ziqinisekise bona kufundwa isifundo sangomuso sokwenziwa kwephrojekthi . Ukuhlukana : Indlela yokuhlanganyela komphakathi okuhlelwe ngakhona kufanele kunikele indawo eyaneleko yokuhlukana , okutjho bona mayelana nemihlobo yeentayela ezihlukeneko yokuzibandakanya namasiko wokuhlanganyela ahlukeneko . Lokha nakufanele kube nesakhelo esilawulako mayelana nokuhlanganyela okuhleliweko enarheni , isakhelwesi kufanele sinabe khudlwana mayelana nesilinganiso sendawo esinqophileko okumele senziwe maphrovinsi nabomasipala . Ithulusi lelogfremu linikela isirhunyezo seengcenye zephrojekthi eziqakathekileko ngefomede ejayelekileko . Ngalokho lisiza labo abamayelana nokuhlola nangabe ububanzi nokunqopha kuyalandelana namtjhana isisomali elihlongoziweko . Hlathululela abo-A abasele ngekamarweni bona bazokulalela abangani babo nababuyako . Lokha nabalalelako kufanele batjengise ukungabi nerhuluphelo . Bangenza lokhu ngokurasisa iintulo zabo , baphazamise , babonakale babhorekile , baqophe amazipho , babubule njll . IInkomba nezinto zobufakazi zinikela iphahla lokuTjheja okungeneleleko kanye nokuHluza iHlelo elifanele lakhiwe belenziwe baphathi bephrojekthi . Ikhwalithi : Kumele bakhambisane nekambiso yelizwe ngokuya , ngokweziqu begodu nelemuko . Ukuhlanganyela kwababambisani kusitjhijilo kumasipala , kumakhansela wamawadi nakumaKomidi wamaWadi . iPaka yomHlahlandlela we-IDP iveza iinkambisolawulo zokuhlanganyela . Iinkambisolawulwezi zingasiza amaKomidi wamaWadi ekusekeleni umasipala ukuze wamukele indlela ehle bese ubeka imikhakha efaneleko ukuqinisekisa ukuhlanganyela okunepumelelo . NASELE UKUKHONJWA KOKUTHOMA KWEPHROJEKTHI KWENZIWE isiteji esilandelako kutlama , ngokungeneleleko bona iphrojekthi kufanele yenziwe bunjani . Kwesinye isikhathi lomtlamo ubizwa umleyo weLawulo lomZombe wePhrojekthi . Uthuthukisa umtlamo wokwenza othonywe esaHlukweni 2 , isiGaba 1 , emtlolweni osebenzako ohlathulula ngokuzeleko bona khuyini , kwamambala ekufanele kwenziwe , kwenziwa ngubani begodu kwenziwa ngasiphi isikhathi esibekiweko begodu kwenziwa ngawaphi amabhajedi . Ithulusi elisetjenziswa ukusiza ukucabanga nokuthuthukisa umleyo obizwa iThulusi lePhahla eliNqophileko , begodu libizwa ilogfremu . Ngokusebenzisa lamagama-mmongo , abahlanganyeli bakha isitatimende sombono . Funda isibonelo sesitatimende sombono esingaphasi . Hlathulula bonyana irhemo lokutlolwa kwamagama wombono kufuze litjengise irhemo lemiphumela yewadi enikelwa itjhejontangi . UmTlamo wemiThombo oHlanganisiweko unentengo oyibekako yekhabhoni . Ukubuyekezwa kwemithetho yemali yomphakathi okungezelelako kuyafuneka ekunabiseni intengo yekhabhoni ukugcugcuzela ukusebenza ngekghono kwerherho lomnotho woke kanye nesisomali kumatheknoloji wokutjala . Yazi unobangela wokukwata kwakho . Zama ukukhomba imizwa eminye oyijayeleko enjengokusaba namtjhana ukuhlangahlangana . Ukuphumelelisa ikanuko yombuso onekghono nothuthukisako , inarha le kufanele iqinise indima yePalamende yokutjheja imitjhapho eyenzeke ngokungakatjheji , inzinzise ubujamo bepolotiki nokuphatha , ikhambise umbuso ngokwemithethokambiso yamakghono nebandulo , ithuthukise amakghono begodu ithuthukise ukuhlangana . Begodu itlhoga indlela ephathekako nenebonelophambili lokulawula irherho laborhulumende abahlukahlukeneko ukuqinisekisa bonyana isibopho sikwazi ukukhambisana nekghono . Ngokulinganako , umbuso kufanele bonyana uzimisele ukulingelela , ukufunda ngezehlakalo ezikhe zavela ngaphambilini nangokwamukela amaqhinga ahlukahlukeneko ukwenzela bonyana ukwazi ukufikelela eminqopheni efanako . Iinqhema zenza imisebenzi bebaqinisekise bonyana bayavumelana babodwa ezintweni eziqakatheke khulu begodu nombiko opheleleko obuyako . Nikela isiqhema ngasinye amaphepha wetjhadi begodu neemeregi ezisetjenziselwa ukwenza umsebenzi lo . Umasipala kufanele athuthukise ama-KPI wawo woke amayunidi , iinsebenzi kanye nabanikeli msebenzi . IKomidi yeWadi akusiyo indawo yezepolotiki namtjhana yehlangano yezepolotiki , aboonkhetheni namtjhana isiqhema esinerhuluphelo engayisebenzisa . IKomidi yeWadi inikela indawo yokuvulela ikulumiswana ukwenzelela ukwendlala isisombululo namtjhana ihlelo elizokuba lisizo emphakathini . Iindleko eziphunguliweko zokuthobela imithetjhwana , khulukhulu zamafemu amancani naphakathi . Amakomidi weWadi adlala indima eqakathekileko ekuhlwengiseni begodu nekubuyekezweni kwe-NSDP njengombana idzimelele emibonweni evela kurhulumende wekhaya . Ilogfremu inikela umleyo wokuhluza , njengobana kutjhiwo okufanele kuphunyeleliswe ( okungukuthi yimiphumela nomnqopho ) , nokobana ipumelelo le izokuqinisekiswa bunjani ( IiNkomba neziNto zobuFakazi ) nokobana iyini imibono eqakathekileko . Kuqakathekile ukukhumbula bona amalunga womphakathi abuya esikweni , ebuzweni , elimini namtjhana ikolo , eenqhemeni zeminyaka engafaniko namtjhana eenqhemeni ezinerhuluphelo ezahlakahlukeneko . Nawukhulumako kufanele utjheje bona ngibuphi ubujamo obuthathwa njengobokumukela esiqhemeni esithize . Sebenzisa ilimi abalaleli abalizwisisa ngcono nakungasinjalo bazokuphelelwa lithando lalokhu okutjhoko . INgogwana yeNtumbantonga / iNtumbantonga ( i-HIV ne-AIDS ) ibe nomthelela omumbi khulu esitjhabeni , ikhuphule khulu inani lokuhlongakala kwabantu ukusukela emnyakeni wee-2000 begodu yaphungula ingcenye yabomma abaseminyakeni yokubeletha . Kunamatshwayo wokobana inarha le seyithomile nokho ukutjhugulula ubujamo obumbobu ngokuzibandakanya ejimeni lokufunda ngobulwelobu nangokuzelaphisa . Isilinganiso sokutshwayeleka ngomulwana we-HIV sinzinze pheze ngamaphesende alitjhumi . Ukutshwayeleka okutjha ngomulwana lo ebantwini abatjha kwehlile begodu isikhathi sokuphila siyangezeleleka . Ngaphandle kweenzuzwezi , lisazokubakhona idlanzana leentandani ezibangelwe yi-AIDS kanye nabantwana abadinga isekelo elikhulu embusweni nemiphakathini eminyakeni ematjhumitjhumi ezako . Iinkomba kumele zithuthukiswe ngokuhlanganyela neenqhema zabazuzi . Kuyakghonakala kwaphela ukubeka abaqothelwa betjhuguluko lobungako nangabe imininingwana esisekelo-kambiso ikhona . Eminyakeni embalwa ezako , irherho lezomnotho lephasi lilindeleke bonyana likhule ngebelo elilingeneko . Ebujamenobu , amabhizinisi weSewula Afrika kufanele acabangisise kuhle bonyana akhiqiza ini , ayikhiqizela maphi amamakethe , begodu asebenzisa maphi amakghono . Njengerherho elincani nelivulekileko lezomnotho , iSewula Afrika ingakhiqiza imikhiqizo emincani yekhethelo . Ukufumana isabelo esincani salokho okufunwa liphasi loke emikhakheni lapho kungaphalisana khona amafemu wekhaya kungaba negalelo elikhulu . Isibonelo , iSewula Afrika ingaba mrholi wephasi loke mayelana nepahla ekhiqizwako kanye nemisebenzi yebubulo lokurhweba ngezenjiwa , lapho inelwazi elibonakalako khona . Lokhu kungaba nomfakela oqakathekileko ekuthuthukisweni kwamabubulo emakethe ekhiqizela iphasi loke imikhiqizo emincani nekhethekileko . Isigaba 1 sithoma ngokubuthelela loke ilwazi elikhona eliphathelene newadi ukwenzela bonyana kuthonywe kwenziwe umtlamo . Lokhu kufaka hlangana amatjhejontangi we-IDP , iindawo ekungenzeka umasipala azisekele ngeemali kanye nelwazi eliphathelene nabanye abanikeli ngemisebenzi . Isirhunyezo esingaphasi sendlala indlela ekufuze isetjenziswe nakubuthelelwa ilwazi . Kghonakalisa umbono ophathelene nendlela yokuhlanganyela nomphakathi kubomasipala , begodu neejamiso ezihlonyiweko zokuhlanganyela nomphakathi . AmaKomidi weWadi asetjenziswe khulu njengendlela yokuhlela ubudlelwano bakamasipala nomphakathi . Malungana nokubuthelela i-IDP , amaKomidi weWadi adlala indima eqakathekileko mayelana nokunikela imifakela yomphakathi kanye nehlolo yeendingo zawo elungele i-IDP . Begodu adlala indima eqakathekileko ekwenzeni lula ibuyekezo lomphakathi elimayelana nokuphunyeleliswa kwe-IDP kanye nokusebenza kukamasipala mayelana ne-IDP . Amandla anikelweko -iinqunto wendawo leyo inesibopho sokuthatha iinqunto nokubhadalela amaphrojekthi . Bangathatha eminye imisebenzi bayinikele umjameli / abajameli bomphakathi ukobana babasize NGOKWENZIWAKO . Ezinye zeendima eziqakathekileko iKomidi yeWadi enazo kuthola imibono evela emphakathini mayelana ne-IDP begodu nokwenza isiqiniseko sokobana umasipala unelwazeli . Lokhu kungenziwa ngokubanjwa kwemihlangano yomphakathi namtjhana ngokwenza iphenyo lokukhamba ngomzana ukuyokukhomba iindaba eziqakathekileko kunezinye emphakathini . Lesi sigaba esifuna isenzo ngendlela yokuphendula namtjhana ngendlela okuphendulwa ngayo . Isibonelo , ipendulo ingabandakanya ukukgharameja namtjhana ukubetha namtjhana ukukhuluma namtjhana ukukhetha ukusukela ubujamo . Abantu baphendula inturhu eyenziwe ziindlela abathatha izinto ngayo kanye neenkolelo . Lokha nawumadaniswa namazinga amahle khulu weentjhabatjhaba , umthangalasisekelo we-ICT weSewula Afrika mumbi khulu . Umthangalasisekelo welwazi onekghono begodu ogcugcuzela ukukhula komnotho kanye nokubandakanywa kwenengi utlhoga ithungelelwano eliqinileko lezizwambiko ezinabileko zeentetjhi zommoya nethintaniswanoliqha , kanye neentengo eziphasi . Iinzuzo zomnotho nomsebenzi zidlula iindleko . UKUHLOLA KOKUTHOMA KWEMIGOMO EKHONA KWAQINISEKISA BONYANA ISEWULA AFRIKA INEMIGOMO EQINISEKISA UKUGCINEKA UKWETHULWA KOMTHANGALASISEKELO BEGODU NEENSETJENZISWA . UKUQALELELWA KOMTHANGALASISEKELO WEENSETJENZISWA ZAKAMASIPALA EZINGAKAGCINEKI NGALOKHO AKUKGHONAKALI BONYANA KUNGAYANYANISWA NOKUNGABI KHONA KOMTHETHO . Ukungezelela emthethwenilawulo ongehla , kunemiThetholawulo embalwa engasiza amaKomidi weWadi ekwenzeni imisebenzayo njengobana kutjhiwo emThethweni weenHlangano zakaMasipala , we-1998 kanye nemThethweni wamaRherho kaMasipala , we-2000 . Ngaphezu kokwenza bonyana abantu bahlanganyele ngobunengi , umhlangano ulithuba elihle lokwenza bonyana umphakathi woke uzwisise iinzuzo zendlelakambiso ye-CBP . Iinqhema ezincazana zabantu ababili ukufikela ebantwini abathathu abanekareko nanyana amakghono mayelana nomnqopho / neqhinga / nephrojekthi enikelwe iphepha lomqondo . Udinga isikhathi esingaba li-iri elilodwa ukuya ema-irini amabili mayelana nephepha ngalinye lomqondo . UMTHETHO WAMARHERHO KAMASIPALA , WE-2000 , izAhluko 4 nese-5 , ufuna bona imikhandlu kamasipala yenze amaqhinga wokubandakanya umphakathi neenhlangano zomphakathi . Lokhu kusekelwa liPhahla lokuPhunyelelweko kweLizwe loke mayelana nokuHlanganyela komPhakathi , we-2005 okuhlathulula ukuhlanganyela komphakathi njenge ' kambiso evulekileko , nenokuziphendulela lapho umuntu ngamunye kanye neenqhema hlangana nemiphakathi ekhethiweko zingakhulumisana ngemibono bese zithatha isiqunto ' . Isahlukwesi sifuna amano wokukhulumisana angasetjenziswa ukusiza amaKomidi weWadi ekugcugcuzeleni nekwenzeni ukuzibandakanya kube sezingeni eliphezulu . Zomnotho : lokhu ngokungasetjenziswa babantu ukuziphilisa , njengemali , ukubulunga imali , iintolo zesiphila , ifuyo , amathulusi neensetjenziswa . Iindawo zemakhaya zingaba namawadi amakhulu anabantu abamaqalanga kiyo yoke imizi kanye namaplasi . Kuneenhlangano ezimbalwa ezikhutheleko . Umuzi nanyana isiqhema ngasinye esakhele amaplasi singakhetha umjameli ukusebenza kuKomidi leWadi . Ngaphambi kokuthoma ngegadangweli , abakghonakalisi kufuze babe nekhophi ye-IDP ukwenzela bonyana bakwazi ukukhomba woke amatjhejontangi we-IDP . Nangabe abahlanganyeli banekhophi ye-IDP , banikele imizuzu emihlanu bonyana batlole imininingwana ezeleko evela emalungeni wabo , kurekhode lokho bese ngemva kwalokho ukhomba itjhejontangi elilodwa le-IDP yabo . Hlathulula bonyana isigabesi somtlamo wewadi sirekhoda lokho okwenziwe bakghonakalisi ukwakheni umtlamo nalabo ababandakanyiweko . Nikela isiqhema ngasinye imizuzu embalwa yokurekhoda amabizo ' wabakghonakalisi ' kanye namabizo wabanye abahlanganyeli abamalunga womphakathi . Yitjho bonyana ngiyiphi imisebenzi edinga iinsetjenziswa ezinengi ezivela ngaphandle nanyana ezingasetjenziswa ngcono kibomasipala . Lokhu kufuze kwethulwe ku-IDP . I-CBP ithembele ekuhlanganyeleni komphakathi lokha iinsetjenziswa nazizakuphumelela ngendlela efaneleko . Izinga kanye namandla wokuhlanganyela aqakathekile lokha i-CBP nayizakusebenza . Ifuna bonyana ababambisani bazibophelele ekuhlanganyeleni ngokukhuthala ukwenzela bonyana lokhu kube sisenzo somphakathi begodu esizawunikela amandla . IKomidi yeWadi ifaka hlangana iKhansela leWadi kanye nabantu abalitjhumi ( 10 ) ababavowudu ewadini begodu abakhethwe mphakathi abawujameleko . Amalunga weKomidi leWadi kufuze ajameleke ngokunabileko ziingcenye ezahlukeneko zomphakathi ( abomma , ilutjha , imiphakathi ebeyibekelwe ngeqadi , njll . ) . Ukuthi malunga waziphi iinhlangano akungathikamezi ukukhethwa kwawo . Amalunga weKomidi leWadi azibandakanya ngokuzithandela . Iindima ezidlalwa bulili ziziindlela zokuphatha ezifundwa emphakathini othileko nezinye iinqhema zomphakathi . Iinjamiso zemisebenzi neembopho zibonwa njengezabobaba namkha zabomma . Baphathwa njengabendabuko , kodwana abasibo . Ubulili budlala iindima ezithintana nobudala , itlasi , ubuhlanga , ubuzwe nekolo , begodu nangokuphathelene nokwephasi , ummnotho nebhoduluko lezepolotiki . Batholakala godu esikhathini esinengi babagandeleli kibomma . Isibonelo , ubulili bomuntu wengubo benza kube msebenzakhe ukumunyisa umntwana . Kodwana umntwana sele alumulile kuhlala kumsebenzi kanina ukumupha ukudla ngombana umphakathi ulindele lokho kuye . Lokhu kuyindimakhe ayidlalako ngobulili . Ubaba naye angase awenze umsebenzi lo ngombana akukho neyodwa into ngokwebhayoloji emkhandelako ukobana angakwazi ukuthenga , ukupheka ukudla nokupha umntwana ukudla . Abobaba abanengi abawenzi umsebenzi wangekhaya ngombana kubonakala kumsebenzi wabomma . Abahlali beWadi A babe nomraro wobulelesi obunengi . Namtjhana babike ubulelesobu emapholiseni , kodwana busaragela phambili . Abahlali banghonghoyile ngobujamobu elungeni leKomidi yeWadi yekhaya elibikele iKomidi yeWadi emhlanganweni wamaswaphelo ababe nawo . iKomidi yeWadi nekhansela lewadi yakhetha ukubiza umhlangano wabahlali . Emhlanganweni kwenziwe iintjhukumiso ezimbalwa zokuzama ukwenza ngcono ubujamo bokuphungula ubulelesi . Amaphuzu amakhulu okuvunyelenwe ngawo kwaba kukuya emkhandlwini wekhaya bona ungezelele amakhandlela wendawo njengobana ubulelesi obunengi benzeka ebusuku begodu nokujamisa iForamu yesiPholisa somPhakathi ( CPF ) . Umhlangano wavumelana ngekomidi encani yokutjhayela enamalunga amabili weKomidi yeWadi , ilunga lomkhandlu nabahlali ababili . Abahlanganyeli bakha eenqhemeni ezinabantu aba-4 ukuya kwaba- 6 begodu baqeda umsebenzi 1 . Ukuqinisekisa bonyana esinye nesinye isiqhema sikhethe isiqhema esahlukileko somphakathi esivela emphakathinabo . I-Oditha Zombelele inomsebenzi woku-oditha woke amaphiko karhulumende neminyango elawula iimali zomphakathi . Ezinye zeendima i-ofisiseli elizidlalako mayelana norhulumende wekhaya kuwuku-oditha imiphumela yokulawula ukwenza kwakamasipala omunye nomunye . UmTlamo wokuThuthukiswa kweliZwe Loke unzinze erhubhululweni elibanzi , ekubonisaneni nekuhlanganyeleni . Nanyana ungasimuhle kangako nanyana ungakapheleli , kodwana wendlala iimphakamiso eziqinileko zokurarulula imiraro yenarha le , nezokuqinisa ukuhlanganyela kwamaSewula Afrika avela emazingeni ahlukahlukeneko womphakathi ekwakheni ingomuso lethu . Imithangalasisekelo enekghono nengabiziko . Imithangalasisekelo yokukghonakalisa umsebenzi wezomnotho ohlinzekela ngobujamo obuhle betuthuko nokwakhiwa kwemisebenzi . Kufanele bonyana kwakhiwe iqhinga lokuqinisa imisebenzi eqakathekileko enjengemisebenzi yeenthuthi zerhwebo , yamandla wegezi , yethintantaniswanoliqha namanzi , begodu kufanele kuqinisekiswe bonyana ayibizi begodu iragela phambili isikhathi eside . Ukwakha umzila wamalahle omutjha ukwenzela bonyana kuvuleke amalarha wamalahle e-Waterberg , anabise imizila yamalahle ekhona ekabeni yendawo leyo begodu athuthukise umzila wamalahle otjhinga e-Richards Bay kanye nomzila welitje lesimbi otjhinga e-Saldanha . Izakhiwo zakarhulumende wendawo zinomsebenzi omkhulu wokuphatha , ngokwendlela yekambiso ephezulu yokuphatha ( kufakwe hlangana imeya nabanye abaphathi baboke ) kanye nomthetho wokulawula ngokwemikhandlu . Ikambiso karhulumende wendawo eqakathekileko yokuphatha ayivulelwa umphakathi , kodwana kuba yikambiso yomthetho . Umfanekiso karhulumende wendawo wokuthuthukisa osetjenziswako ugandelela itlhogeko lokwenza izinto zibe pepenene , kube nokuziphendulela , kubonisanwe , kube neenkghonakalisi zokubandakanyeka komphakathi namatjhebiswano . Ingabe amanye amapara awenze njani umsebenzi lo ? Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi afuna amakghono wokukhulumisana amahle ukuqinisekisa kobana ayazwisisa kanye nokwakha ithemba phakathi komphakathi kanye nomkhandlu . Lokha nasele umkhandlu uqedile ukubuyekeza isabelo seemali ezigade isimetjhe begodu nasele uvumile nokunikela isekelo , kuhlelwa umhlangano omkhulu ukunikela umphakathi umbiko obuyako ngaphambi kokuphumelelisa . Ukuhlela lokhu okunqotjhwe ukuphunyeleliswa ngephrojekthi - lokhu kwesinye isikhathi kubizwa imiphumela yokuhlela begodu kubandakanya yoke imisebenzi elungiselelweko begodu ilinganisa bona iphrojekthi izokwenzeka nanyana njani . Kuqakathekile ukutjhugulula iinqondo-hlaliso begodu nemizindlo ephikisanako , iindlela zekambiso yomcabango namkha izinto ezinganamirabhu ngesinye nesinye isiqhenyana nangabe sifuna ukuhlonipha ukuhlukana ngokwamasiko . Imizindlo ingena ngamafektha ambalwa . Tjheja ilwazi elingenzasi nokobana amaKomidi wamaWadi ayitjhugulula njani imizindlo le ngendlela engaphendula ngayo izinto eziqakathekileko . Umma uSmith ube neenghonghoyilo kumasipala amahlandla ambalwa anghonghoyila ngomgodi owenjiweko esitradeni sakhe . Kumnyama akunamkhanyo esitradeni sakhe sekube mahlandla amathathu abantu abatjhayisa ebusuku ngombana kumnyama bawela ngaphakathi komgodi , nanyana bapheze bawela kiwo . Umphakathi utshwenyekile ngombana munye wabantwababo angawela ngaphakathi komgodi lo okungabangela bona abe ahlongakale . Ufaka isinghonghoyilo kumasipala . Indaba le isikinyelwa phezulu msinya . Ukwakha iindlela zokuthintana ezisemthethweni nezingathathi ihlangothi begodu nokwakha ihlanganyelo elinetjhebiswano phakathi komphakathi nomkhandlu . Umkhandlu uthethe isiqunto sokobana uzokufaka amamitha wamanzi ngemva kokubona bona amanzi ayamotjheka . Ikontraga kufanelwe iqatjhwe ukwenza umsebenzi lo . Ikomidi yewadi kamasipala we-ABC ihlala iya emhlanganweni womkhandlu . IKomidi yeWadi yenze ihlelo elinamagama wamalunga weKomidi yeWadi kanye namalanga wokuya emhlanganweni womkhandlu . Amalunga la athola amakhophi wamaminidi bese abelana ngelwazi namanye amalunga . Amalunga weKomidi yeWadi asebenzisa amaminidi wekhansela ukuhlola bona iinqunto ezithathwako ziyalandelwa na . Umthetho wamhlapha kamasipala wokuhlanganyela komphakathi nekoro yamabubulo wangeqadi utloliwe begodu amalunga weKomidi yeWadi ahlela umhlangano womphakathi ukukhulumisana ngeendaba nokuletha umbiko obuyako emkhandlwini . Ukusekela ngemali engenako nephumako yepilo yoke yephrojekthi ( ihlelwe qobe ngekota ukufaka iminyaka yeemali ehlukahlukeneko yemithombo ehlukahlukeneko esekela ngeemali ) . Amanothi aku-3.2.1 bekufike ku-3.2.5 . Abahlanganyeli bahlukaniswa ngeenqhema zamalunga amane isiqhema ngasinye . Tlola imibuzo phezu kwetjhadi elilengiswako . Abahlanganyeli basebenza ngababili ( bakhuluma nomuntu oseduze nabo ) begodu batjhukatjhukana neempendulo ( banikezwa imizuzu eli-10 ukuya kweli-15 ukobana batjheje imibuzo ) . Usodorobha ukhethwa mkhandlu bona enze umsebenzi womkhandlu . Usodorobha wenza yoke iminyanya eqakathekileko nemisebenzi ayinikelwa mkhandlu . Usodorobha omkhulu unamagunya woke amakhulu . Hlathulula bona ibhajedi ifaka hlangana IINDLEKO NENGENISO . Nangabe akuthintanwa nabo boke ababambisani begodu kuhlolwe iindingo zabo ekuthomeni kwephrojekthi , iphrojekthi ingaba sengozini yokungasaphumeleli . AmaKomidi weWadi angadlala indima ekulu kilesisiteji njengobana azi ubujamo babamukeli bephrojekthi nokobana ziyini iindingo zabo . Azokwazi godu ukusiza ngokuhlola kabutjha ukucozululwa kwababambisani ngesikhathi somzombe wephrojekthi ukuqinisekisa bona kuhlangatjezanwa neendingo zabambisani ngepumelelo . Ngiwaphi amaphrojekthi ikomidi yewadi efisa ukuwenza ? Tjheja izinto ezinjengamaphrojekthi wokuthuthukisa zomnotho , ukubandula abatjheji beengulani ezigulela emakhaya ? Ingabe lamaphrojekthi singakghona ukuwenza nezinye iinhlangano zomphakathi ? Cabanga ngeminyango / imikhakha emithathu yakarhulumende nokuthi izakhamuzi zingazibandakanya njani kwelinye nelinye ileveli . Mukela bewuqinisekise imizwa yokukwata yabanye abantu . Khumbula bona kulungile ukukwata . Ilwazi lokwenziwa komsebenzi wokwethulwa komsebenzi kumele unikelwe emuva kubanikeli bomsebenzi nakulabo abazuzako ekwethulweni komsebenzi . Nangabe ikhwalithi yokwethulwa komsebenzi kuthuthukisa isidingo somphakathi ukobana bangalindelani begodu nokuthi khuyini ekhona kibo . . . Ukwenza bonyana izakhamuzi zikghone ukuhlanganyela embonweni weenkambiso zokufaka abantu eendaweni zokuhlala kanye nokutlama . Kunabantu abanengi abathengisa eqadi kwesitetjhi . Kube neenghonghoyilo ezivela kubanikazi beentolo zokobana abantu abathengisakwaba ababhadali irende yeke bathengisa iimpahla zabo ngemali ephasi begodu batjhiya iinsila phasi lokha nasele baqedile ukubutha nabakhambako . Sebenzisa IPHAWAPHOYINTHI A ukuveza iingaba ze-IDP . Ukujamiselela lokhu ungadlulisela abahlanganyeli ekhasini le-18 emanothini wekhoso begodu utlole esinye nesinye isigaba etjhadini . Ukusekelwa kwamarhwebo amancani : Ngomnyaka we-1994 i-ofisi lerhelebho le-Britain lanikela ngemali yokutlhama ideske le-LED . Umnqopho wedeske le-LED kunikela ibandulo , isekelo lamarhwebo amancani begodu nokubolekwa kwemali . Ngaphandle kokungena phakathi lokhu , amarhwebo amancani endaweni le ahlangabezana nezinye eliphezulu lokubhadelwa ngebanga lokutlhogeka kwemakethe yemikhiqizo edorobheni le , ingenisomali eliphasi lezakhamuzi ezinengi , ukutlhogeka kweenthuthi ebantwini abakhiqizako ukwenzela bonyana bakwazi ukuthengisa kwezinye iindawo begodu nokutlhogeka kwebandulo kuwokewoke . Yenza ilwazi lakho libe lula begodu linemba . Ingcenye yeqhinga lethu lokuvikelwa kwehlalakuhle ngelokusebenzisa isibonelelo sehlalakuhle , esifaka hlangana iinkolo ezingabhadelisiko , izenzelo ezisisekelo zasimahla neenthuthi zomphakathi ezisekelwa ngeemali zokwehlisa iindleko . Ngaphezu kokwakha imisebenzi eminengi ekorweni yangeqadi , ukunabiswa ngendlela ebonakalako kwamahlelo wemisebenzi yombuso kungasiza ukuqinisekisa bonyana kuba mindeni embalwa ephila ngaphasi kwezinga lengeniso elibekiweko . Ilunga / amalunga weKomidi yeWadi angenza bonyana woke amalunga wengcenye ethileko yomphakathi ibakhohlisi begodu kungebanga lalokho umbono omunye nomunye abawenzako ngokwethulwa kwemisebenzi yomphakathi namkha amaphrojekthi kumele eqiswe amehlo . NQOPHILEKO - izinga lomsebenzi liyatjho yini ngokunqophileko bonyana khuyini okulinganiswako na ? Kwamaswaphelo , lingabandakanya ukuqeda iphrojekthi , lihlole ikhwalithi yomkhiqizo opheleleko namtjhana umsebenzi bese liqedelela amakontraga kanye namabhajedi .
